prayojanam nanu ca heyataddhetū na prastotavye niṣprayojanatvāt hānaprayuktaṃ hi śāstraṃ tadupāyabhūtā vivekakhyātir eva vaktavyā na hi kaṇṭakaviddhacaraṇatalasya tadapanayanaṃ muktvā duḥkhataddhetū sādhyaṃ hānasyāpi vivekakhyātir eva sādhanam iti sādhyasādhanayor itaretaraniyama eva na anyasambandhaḥ tad yathā bhaiṣajyasya ārogyam eva phalaṃ ārogyasyāpi bhaiṣajyam eva sādhanam itītaretaraniyamaḥ sa ca śāstrād iti tasmāt sasaṃbandhaprayojanaṃ yogānuśāsanam nanu ca yadi hānaṃ prayojanaṃ tadupāyaś ca vivekakhyātir iti tatra vaktavyam atha vivekakhyātyanuśāsanam iti kim artham atha yogānuśāsanam iti sūtritam tadupāyatvād yogasya upāya eva vaktavyaḥ syāt upeyopapradarśane hi upeyam upāyaṃ prati sākāṅkṣam eva iti upāyaḥ sāṅgakalāpaḥ punar api vaktavyaḥ syāt tasmiṃś cābhihite sarvam eva abhihitam iti kathaṃ tad upāyatvam yata āha sūtrakāraḥ yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād aśuddhikṣaye jñānadīptir āvivekakhyāteḥ iti nirvicāravaiśāradye adhyātmaprasādaḥ ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā iti ca tathā bhāṣyakāro apy āha yas tv ekāgre cetasi sa bhūtam arthaṃ pradyotayati iti bhūtārthāvagatiś ca vivekakhyātiḥ tasmād yuktaṃ tad upāyayogānuśāsanam eva ādau sūtritam iti nanu ca yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād vivekakhyātiḥ tatra vaktavyaṃ atha yogāṅgānuśāsanam iti na phalenopakramāt yogāaṅgānuṣṭhānasya hi phalaṃ yoga iti tadupakramo yuktaḥ yady evaṃ hānena upakramyeta na tasya upeyatvāt upeyam eva hi tat yogaḥ punaḥ svāṅgānām iti yogānuśāsanam iti yathā śiṣyo anuśiṣyate viśiṣṭapravṛttinivṛttiniyamadvāreṇa tathā viśiṣṭasādhyasādhanatadaṅganiyamamātrasādṛśyād antevāsyanuśāsanavad yogā anuśāsanam ity ucyate anuśiṣtṭir putraśabdasyārthaḥ pitā tathā ihāpy ārambha evābhidhīyate ānantaryaṃ tu pratīyate ata eva ca vṛttād anantarasya prakriyā arthao dṛṣṭaḥ ity ucyate yadi cānantaryārtho abhaviṣyat tadā vṛttād anantaye nirodhe viṣayaviśeṣe cittaṃ nirudhyate tadā hi viṣayitvān nivartate prigaṇanānupapattiś ca na hi kṣiptādayaḥ pancā eva saṃyamasya viṣayāḥ teṣām ānantyāt nanu cānyathā yogaṃ kecid icchanti tathā ca āhuḥ indriyamano arthasannikarṣāt sukhaduḥkhe tadanārambha ātmasthe manasi sa śarīrasya sukhaduḥkhābhāvaḥ prāṇamano vinigrahāpekṣaḥ saṃyogo yoga iti tad iti prakṛtāpekṣam yo asau sukhaduḥkhayor ātmendriyamono arthasannilarṣo hetuḥ tasya anārambhaḥ tadanutpattiḥ sa kathaṃ bhavati ātmasthe manasi nendriyasthe saśarīrasyāviśīrṇaśarīrasya tadā kāraṇābhāvāt kāryābhāva iti sannikarṣābhāve sukhaduḥkhayor apy abhāvaḥ tasyām avasthāyāṃ yo asau vibhor ātmano manasā saṃyogaḥ sa prāṇamano vinigrahāpekṣaḥ saṃyogaviśeṣo yoga iti atra ucyate ātmasthe manasīty ayuktam sarvadā ātmasthatvān manasaḥ indriyādisannikarṣānārambhāpekṣayā ātmasthe iti cet tadanārmbha ity eva siddhatvād ātmasthe manasīty anarthakaṃ syāt kiṃ cānyat muktasyāpi manasa ātmasthatvād indriyasannikarṣābhāvāc ca yogaḥ prāpnoti tasyāpi hi sarvagatatvāt manasaś ca nityatvāt sarvadā ātmasthatvam eva kiṃ ca ātmanaḥ pradeśābhāvād ātmastha ity ayuktam na cāpy upacaritātmapradeśasaṃyogaḥ paramārthasya yogasya hetuḥ syāt upacaritasya mithyātvāt kiṃ cānyat mano arthasannikarṣābhāva ity eva sddheḥ siddhaṃ indriyagrahaṇam anarthakaṃ syāt atha indriyair vinā mano arthasannikarṣābhāvāt tadanārambha iti prāptyabhāve pratiṣedho na yukta iti cet naitad evam vinā indriyair mano arthasannikarṣo nāstīty arthāt sannikarṣapratiṣedhaṃ kurvatā viṣayaprāptir indriyadvārā pratipāditā syāt kiṃ cānyat sarvaprāṇabhājām indriyamano arthasannikarṣāt sukhaduḥkhapratilambhasya prasiddhatvād ātmanaḥ saṃbandhasya ca nityatvāt sukhaduḥkhābhāvo yoga ity eva siddheḥ tatra sūtra śeṣo narthakaḥ syāt athāpi syād indriyamano arthasannikarṣagrahaṇād ṛte sukhaduḥkhābhāva ity etāvati sati muktasyāpi sukhaduḥkhābhāvād yogitvaprasaṅga iti tannivṛttyarthaṃ sūtraśeṣagrahaṇam iti tac ca na muktasya sukhaduḥkhaprāptyabhāvāt prāptipūrvapratiṣedhasya nyāyyatvāt yasya sukhaduḥkhaprāptiḥ tadviṣayaḥ sukhaduḥkhābhāva eva yoga iti sūtraśeṣapratyākhyānaṃ yujyate kiṃ cānyat upātte api saśarīragrahaṇe muktād vinivṛttir na śakyate kartum niṣprayojanatvāt sukhaduḥkhābhāvaś ced yogaḥ vidyamānam api śarīraṃ kāryākaraṇād anarthakaṃ syāt kāryānapekṣāyāṃ hi muktāmuktayor aviśeṣa eva kiṃ cānyat prāṇamano vinigrahāpekṣa ity api na ghaṭate vidhārakasya prayatnasya ātmasamavetatvād avidyamāne api manasaḥ kriyāvattve indriyeṇāsaṃyujya manaḥprāṇa mano nigrahau na kartuṃ paryāpyate indriyasaṃyoge ca manasaḥ tadanārambha ity ayuktam manasaś ca prāṇanigrahe vyāpṛta vyāvṛtatvād anārambhānupapattiḥ na cāsatīndriyavāyu sannikarṣe prāṇanigrahaḥ na cānigṛhīte prāṇe yogaḥ ātmasthavidhārakaprayatnadvārā mano gatakriyāsaṃbandhahetutvāt prāṇanigrahasya athāpi syād yogaḥ samādhir iti tac ca na niṣkriyatvād ātmano nityasamādhānam eva sthitiś ca samādhir ity ucyate tasmād yuktam abhidhīyate sa ca sārvabhaumaś cittasya dharmaḥ iti yady evaṃ samādhiś ced yogaḥ sa ca sārvabhaumaś cittadharmaḥ sa ca sarvajanānām ayatnasiddhiḥ kṣiptādyanugatatvāt tathā ca sati yathā eva śvāsapraśvāsādīnāṃ prayatnād ṛte siddhitvāt tatkaraṇam allakṣaṇam anarthakam evaṃ yogānuśāsanam apy anarthakaṃ prāptam ity ata āha tatra vikṣipte anavikṣipte cetasi vikṣepopasarjanībhūtaḥ samādhir na yogapakṣe vartata iti kṣiptādyanugatasya yogapakṣa anabhipretatvāt na hi kṣepādyanugataḥ samādhir bhūtārthāvadyotanādikṣamaḥ kṣepādipradhānatvāt vikṣepaniṣedhenaiva hi pradhānamallanibarhaṇanyāyena kṣiptamūḍhayor api niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ pradhānatā ca vikṣepasamādher adhikārayogyatvāt vikṣepasthaṃ hi cittam apakṣapātād iṣtaṃ viṣayam upanetuṃ śakyate na hi viṣayāsañjanādinā kṣiptam iṣtaviṣayaviyogādinā vā mūḍham anyathāupanetuṃ pāryate yogapakṣa iti samādhitve saty api kāryākaraṇāt pakṣa ity ucyate yathā gacchataḥ pratipadaṃ vidyamānāpi sthitiḥ sthitikāryākārān na sthitir ity ucyate vikṣepopasarjanī bhūtatvaṃ vikṣepasthaikasamādhivyaktyabhiprāyeṇa sārvabhauma iti tu prādhānyaṃ sāmānyena sarvabhūmiṣu vṛtteḥ yady upasarjanī bhāvaḥ samādhipakṣāvṛttau kāraṇam ihāpy ekāgre ekāgratā upasarjanatvaṃ syāt tataś ca yogapakṣāvṛttir iti ced ata āha yas tv ekāgra iti naikāgratāyāṃ bhūmyupasarjanatvam kutaḥ kleśakarmāprabalatvāt kleśakarmāprabalatve na hi vikṣepādīnām udayaḥ ekāgratā bhūmau samādhir yaḥ sa bhūtam arthaṃ yathā ātmānaṃ pradyotayati avagamayati ayogyarthajñānam ayathā bhūtatvagandhitam eva iti bhūtagrahanam kṣiṇoti kṣapayati pañcaparvaṇo vidyādīn kleśān karmabandhanāni karmāṇy eva bandhanāni dharmādharmavimiśrakarmajātāni janmādinibandhanāni abhyarhitatvād asamprajñātasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ yuktam iha vaktum iti samprajñātam upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāma ity ucyate itaś cāsamprajñātasya lakṣaṇam ihaiva vaktavyaṃ samprajñātanirapekṣo py asamprajñātaḥ para prakṛṣṭa vairāgyavirāmapratyayābhyāsābhyāṃ sidhyatīty etat pradarśanārtham iha samprajñātalakṣaṇābhidhāne taduttarakāle ca asamprajñātalakṣaṇābhdhāne samprajñātāpekṣayaivāsamprajñātasamādhāv adhikāra ity āśaṅkā syāt tasmād upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāma ity āha sarvavṛttinirodhe tv asaṃprajñāta iti tuśabddo vadhāraṇā arthaḥ tasyaivaṃvidhasya samādher asaṃprajñātasyaiva kevalasya lakṣaṇābhidhitsayā idaṃ sūtraṃ pravavṛte pravṛttaṃ yogaś cittavṛttinirodhaḥ i tī ti vaktavyam nanu ca tasya lakṣaṇam abhidhātum etat sūtraṃ pravṛttaṃ tathā ca sati yogasya cittavṛttinirodhaḥ iti vaktavyaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na yuktam na hi lakṣyam eva lakṣaṇaṃ syāt cittavṛttinirodhalakṣaṇa iti vā vaktavyam naiṣa doṣaḥ lakṣye lakṣaṇādhyāsāt yathā yaṃ piṇḍo devadatta iti lakṣye lakṣaṇam adhyasyate pratyasyate nanu ca sarvavṛttinirodhe tv asamprajñātaḥ tasya cedaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tataś ca yogaḥ sarvacittavṛttinirodhaḥ iti vaktavyam na ca uktam ato tivyāpi lakṣaṇam sarvaśabdāgrahaṇe tāvat kāraṇam ucyate yadi sarvagrahaṇaṃ kriyate tadā ekadeśanirodhanimittasya saṃprajñātasya yogatvaṃ nivartitaṃ syāt tan mā abhūt iti sarvaśabdāgrahaṇam astu tarhi saṃprajñātāsaṃprajñātayoḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ viśeṣānupādānāt naiṣa doṣaḥ yoge prakṛte punar yogagrahaṇāt viśeṣāvivakṣāyāṃ hi yogagrahaṇaṃ nārthavat syāt nanu cānuśāsane nyag bhūtatvād yogasyeha yogagrahaṇe asati cittavṛttinirodha ity ukta anuśāsanārthatā bhavet sūtrasya naivaṃ yogānuśāsanasya prastutatvāt yogānuśāsanaṃ hi prārabdhaṃ nāyogānuśāsanaṃ tallakṣaṇābhidhāne hy atiprasaṅgaḥ padārthāsaṅgatiś ca na hi cittavṛttinirodho yogānuśāsanam iti padārthaḥ saṅgacchate evam api yogagrahaṇāt kuto asaṃprajñātasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ na punaḥ saṃprajñātasya lakṣaṇaṃ syāt yogagrahaṇasyāviśiṣṭatvād iti ucyate avyabhicārāt vyabhicarati na tat tasya lakṣaṇaṃ nirodhas tv asaṃprajñāte api vartata iti saṃprajñātaṃ vyabhicarati na hi viṣāṇitvaṃ gor liṅgaṃ mahiṣyādibhir vyabhicārāt nanu cāsaṃprajñātam api vyabhicarati saṃprajñātasyāpi heyavṛttinirodhatvāt satyam evaṃ kiṃ tu na nirodhād anyena lakṣayitum asaṃprajñātaḥ śakyate nirodha eva tu tasya lakṣaṇam anyasyābhāvāt saṃprajñātasya tv asādhāraṇavitarkādilakṣaṇalakṣyatvāt yathā sparśalakṣaṇam ity ukte vāyur evāsādhāraṇyāl lakṣyate sparśavattvena atha ca vidyata eva sparśavattvaṃ tejaḥprabhṛtiṣv api evaṃ ca sati yogagrahaṇam anuvādamātram ata eva ca sarvagrahaṇaṃ na kṛtaṃ sūtre nirodhagrahaṇenaivāsaṃprajñātalakṣaṇatve siddhe yadi sarvagrahaṇaṃ kriyate tatsaṃprajñātasya yogatāṃ nivārayet tasmād asaṃprajñātasyaiva idaṃ lakṣaṇam tathā ca upasaṃharati bhāṣyakāraḥ na tatra kiṃcit saṃprajñāyate ity asaṃprajñātaḥ sa yogaś cittavṛttinirodha iti cittavṛttitannirodhavyācikhyāsayā cittaṃ hītyādi bhāṣyaṃ kimātmakaṃ punas tac cittaṃ yasya vṛttinirodhe yoga ity ata āha cittaṃ hi prakhyāpravṛttisthitiśīlatvāt triguṇam iti tatra cittaṃ triguṇam iti vyākhyāyate prakhyāpravṛttisthitiśīlatvād iti hetuḥ prakhyā prakhyānaṃ prakāśanaṃ sa hi sattvaguṇasya dharmaḥ pravṛttiḥ pravartanaṃ vyāpāraḥ sa hi rajo dharmaḥ sthitiḥ sthānaṃ varaṇaṃ pratibandha iti sa ca tamo dharmaḥ evaṃ śīlā hi sattvādayo guṇāḥ cittaṃ ca prakhyā ādiśīlaṃ tasmāt trayāṇāṃ guṇānāṃ pariṇāmaś cittaṃ bhavitum arhati tasya ca prakhyā ādihetor asiddhaṃ āśaṅkya āha prakhyāsvarūpam hi cittasattvam iti hiśabdaḥ prasiddhāvadyotanārthaḥ prasiddham hi loke śāstre ca sarvāvabhāsakatvaṃ cittasya cittam eva sattvaṃ cittasattvaṃ sattvapradhānaguṇapariṇāmatvāt atha vā anyasaṃsargaviyogābhyām anekavṛtti khyātimātraṃ ca cittaṃ spaṣṭaṃ darśayituṃ śakyata iti bravīti prakhyāsvarūpam hi cittasattvam iti idānīṃ vṛttayo vyākhyāyante tāsāṃ cānekatvaṃ rajas tamasor udbhāvibhavanimittaṃ viruddhatvaṃ cety āha rajas tamobhyāṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ sampradhānābhyāṃ yadā saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tadānīṃ aiśvaryaviṣayapriyaṃ bhavati prītiḥ rāgaḥ aiśvaryaviṣayarāgayuktā vṛttayo bhavantīty arthaḥ tat tamasānuviddhaṃ tad eva prakhyāsvarūpam cittaṃ yadā guṇabhūtarajaskena udbhūtena tamasā anuviddhaṃ tadānīm adharmādicatuṣṭayaviṣayā vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭā jāyante tad eva prakṣīṇamohāvaraṇām iti nyag bhūtatamaskaṃ tamaḥ kṣayād eva jaladhrāpagamād iva pari ravibambaṃ sarvataḥ pradyotamānaṃ rajomātrayā rajo leśenānuviddhaṃ yadā tadā dharmādyupagataṃ dharmādicatuṣṭayaviṣayā vṛttayo akliṣṭā bhavanti yadā tad eva rajo leśa malāpetaṃ svarūpapratiṣṭhaṃ kevalena svena prakhyārūpeṇāvasthitaṃ tadā sattvapuruṣānyathākhyātimātraṃ bhavati sattvaṃ cittaṃ puruṣo bhaktā tayor anyatā viviktatā tatkhyātiḥ tadavagamaḥ tanmātragrahaṇaṃ kleśādyabhāvapradarśanārtham dharmameghadhyānopagaṃ bhavati dharmamegho nāma samādhiḥ tad eva prasaṃkhyānabalād rajas tamasī tiraskṛtya kevalena khyātyātmanā puruṣasvarūpamātradarśanenāvasthānaṃ dhyānaṃ prasaṃkhyānam ity ācakṣate dhyāyino yoginaḥ evaṃ vṛttisvarūpe vyākhyāte tannirodhapradarśanārtham āha citiśaktir ity ādi citir eva śaktiḥ citiśaktiḥ yathā pacyādayah śaktayaḥ śaktimadapekṣāprāpaṇīyajanmāno na svayaṃśaktayaḥ citiḥ punaḥ svayam eva śaktiḥ nārthāntaram apekṣate tena nityāvasthitatvam citiśabdasya cinmātrābhidhyāyinaḥ śaktiśabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ avikṛtarūpāyā eva citer viṣayitvapradarśanārtham yasmād evam ato apariṇāminī vyavasthite dharmiṇi dharmāntaratiro bhāvena dharmāntaraprādur bhāvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ na pariṇāmituṃ śīlam asyā ity apariṇāminī ata evāpratisaṅkramā pariṇāmina eva cittāder viṣayādau pratisaṅkramadarśanāt ata eva darśitaviṣayā darśito antaḥkaraṇena viṣayo asyā iti tenaiva śuddhā ata evānantā deśataḥ kālataś ca pūrvapūrvam uttarasya uttarasya hetutvena draṣṭavyam vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ cittam indriyāṇi ca sattvaguṇātimikā sattvam eva guṇaḥ sattvaguṇaḥ tasya iva ātmā svarūpam avabhāso yasyāḥ sā iyaṃ sattvaguṇāatmakā avabhāsasvarūpā ity arthaḥ vṛttyaviśiṣṭavṛttitvād vā sattvaguṇātmikā ity ucyate yadi vā khyātyā saṃbandhyate khyātiḥ sattvaguṇātmikā iti ataḥ citiśakter uktalakṣaṇāyā viparītā vilakṣaṇā vivekakhyātiḥ pariṇāmādimatī yasmāt puruṣād utkṛṣṭāt pariṇāmādiguṇarahitān nikṛṣṭā priṇāmādiguṇayuktā ataḥ svarūpadoṣadarśanāt tasyāṃ viraktaṃ aparaktaṃ tām api khyātiṃ ātmano niruṇāddhi tad avasthaṃ nirodhāvasthaṃ saṃskāropagaṃ saṃskāramātrāvaśeṣam niruddhāsu vṛttiṣu vṛttijanitāḥ saṃskārā evāvaśiṣyante etasyāṃ nirodhabhūmau yaḥ samādhiḥ sa nirbījaḥ nirgataṃ bījam atra kleśādibījaṃ sarvam utsannam asminn iti tasmād asaṃprajñātasamādhilakṣaṇārthaṃm eva sūtram ity upasaṃharati sa yogaś cittavṛttinirodha iti yogaś cittavṛttinirodha ity uktaṃ tatra boddhṛtvena eva puruṣasadbhāvādhigamaḥ viṣayabhūtavṛttinirodhe ca viṣayiṇo api boddhuḥ puruṣasya nirodhaṃ kaścid āśaṅketā api tathā ca sati tatkaivalyaprāptyupāyasyāpi vivekakhyāter anarthakatvaṃ manvīta yogānuśāsanasyāpi tadarthasya niṣphalatvaṃ pratipadyeta tasmāt puruṣasya vṛttinirodhād anirodhaṃ darśayitu kāmaḥ khyāteś cāpi phalaṃ sākṣād darśayann āha tadavasthe cetasītyādi tadavasthe nirodhāvasthe svaviṣayābhāvāt svaviṣayaś cittavṛttis tadabhāve abhāvāt buddhibodhātmā buddhiṃ vṛttirūpena pariṇatāṃ budhyata iti buddher boddhā puruṣaḥ tadbodhanam eva hi puruṣasya svaṃ rūpaṃ nānyo boddhā nānyad boddhanam boddhuś ca bodhanād anyatve sati vikriyātmakatā syāt tataś ca darśitaviṣayatvaṃ ca na syāt tathā ca karaṇāntarāpekṣitvaṃ puruṣasya prasajyate tasmād bodhanaṃ boddhṛtvaṃ copacaritaṃ tadvṛttisārūpyeṇa tathā ca vakṣyati draṣṭā dṛśimātraḥ iti tasmād āha buddhibodhanam evātmā svarūpam yasya sa buddhibodhātmā puruṣaḥ kiṃsvabhāvaḥ kiṃ naśvarasvabhāvaḥ sadbhāve vā kiṃsvabhāvaḥ kathaṃ vā sadbhāva iti tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe avasthānam yadā niruddhā vṛttayaḥ svarūpapratiṣṭhā tadānīṃ citiśaktiḥ svarūpapratiṣṭhety arthaḥ yathā kaivalye tadā sadbhāvaṃ tu na tatsvābhāsaṃ dṛṣyatvāt ity evamādinā vakṣyati tatra siddhe sadbhāve tata ākṛṣya prāptāśaṅkānivṛttyartham ucyate svarūpapratiṣṭhā iti siddhavadvyākhyātam sūtraṃ tatra idaṃ prasaktam itaratra na svarūpapratiṣṭhā iti anyathā hi tadā iti viśeṣaṇānarthakyaṃ syāt na ced anyatra svarūpapratiṣṭhā tatrāvasthāntarayogāt pariṇāmitvād adoṣaḥ prāpnotīti tat parijihīrṣaya āha vyutthānacitte tu sati tathā api bhavantīti anena anyatrāpi svarūpapratiṣthatvaṃ darśayati na tathā ity anena tadā iti viśeṣaṇasyārthavattvaṃ khyāpayati itaras tu tathā api bhavanty anena cet svarūpapratiṣṭhatvam ucyate na tathā iti ca svarūpapratiṣṭhatvaniṣedhaś ced ekasya vastunas tathābhāvaś cātathā bhāvaś ca virudhyata iti vīkṣāpannaḥ pṛcchati kathaṃ tarhi iti itara āha vṛttisārūpyam itaratra iti kasmāt punar vṛttisārūpyam darśitaviṣayatvāt ubhayatra svarūpapratiṣṭhatvāviśeṣe api vṛttisārūpyāsārūpyakṛto viśeṣa iti na tathābhāvātathābhāvavirodhaḥ nanu ca vṛttisārūpyayoge sati avasthāntarayogāt pariṇāmitvādidoṣaḥ prāpnoty eva na darśitaviṣayatvena parihṛtatvāt cittavṛttyadhyāropitaṃ hi tat na svataḥ sphaṭikādyupadhānoparogavat vyutthāna iti nirodhād anyatra yaś cittasya kliṣṭādayo vṛttayaḥ tābhir aviśiṣṭā sadṛśī vṛttiḥ svarūpam asya cittavṛttivyatirekeṇa svarūpavtyatirekeṇa ca puruṣasya vṛttyabhāvāt sadā jñātaviṣayatve pariṇāmānupapatteś ca tathā ca pūrvācāryasūtram ekam eva darśanaṃ buddhipuruṣayoḥ kiṃ tad ity āha khyātir eva darśanam buddhivṛttir eva darśanam khyāyate puruṣeṇa iti ca khyātiḥ khyāte nayā ca buddhipuruṣayoḥ svarūpam iti khyātiḥ sā evārthākāratayā arthākāro nayā gṛhyata iti karaṇaṃ svena ca khyātirūpeṇa gṛhyata iti karma ca bhavati tathā dṛśyata iti darśanaṃ dṛśyate neneti ca jñāyata iti jñānaṃ jñāyate neneti ca sarvam evamādi drṣṭavyam yat tu khyātikartṛtve cittasya tad eva jñāyate jānāti ceti jñānād iti ceti jñānāntarakalpnā vaiyarthyaprasaṅga iti tasya na tatsvābhāsaṃ dṛśyatvāt ity atraiva parihāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ nanu ca yadi cittaparvijṛmbhitam evedaṃ sarvaṃ paruṣaś ced udāste katham asau bhokteti na kārakavaicitryāt kānicid vyāpriyamāṇāni kārakāṇi kānicid vyāpārād ṛte sannidhimātreṇa kartṛtvaṃ pratipadyante yathā pacatīty adhiśrayaṇādiṣu vyāpriyamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ kartety ucyate sthālī sambhavadhāraṇābhyām avyāpriyamṇaiva pacatīty ucyate tathā sthālī madhyagatam ākācam avakācaṃ dadāti na tasya vyāpāraṃ pratīmaḥ yathā ca rājā darśanamātreṇa eva kartā sarvāṇi ca kārakāṇi sveṣu vyāpāreṣu kartYṇi na ca ādityaḥ prakāśayan karaṇāntaram apekṣate vyāpriyate vā na hi prakāśanam avidyamānam utpādayati gamanādivat prakāśātmatā eva hi tasya sadbhāvaḥ tathāpi dṛśimātreṇa ghaṭādīnāṃ prakāśarūpeṇābhivyakteḥ prakāśayatīty ucyate evam ihāpi dṛśimātreṇa puruṣeṇa dṛśyamānāṃ cittavṛttīnāṃ cidātmanā vyāpyamānatvāt draṣṭā puruṣa itīmam arthaṃ darśayati cittam ayaskāntamaṇikalpam iti yasyāpy ātmamanas saṃyogāt jñānam utpadyate tasyāpi jñānena jñeyaṃ vyāpnuvan nātmā jñātety ucyate na vyāpriyamānaḥ jñānasyāpi jñānam api guṇatve sati niṣkriyatvād ātmana evārthaṃ darśayati nāpi kriyān abhyupagamāt jānātītyādi na upapadyate jñānena hi jñeyaṃ vyāpnivan jānātīty ucyate kiṃ cānyat ātmamanas saṃyogād apūrvajñānotpattau saty ātmamanas taj jñānaṃ na manasaḥ ātmā eva jñnāti na mana iti ko hetur bhavet athāpi syāt ātmanaḥ samavāyikāraṇatvād iti na etad evaṃ asiddhatvāt yathā eva jñānam ātmana iti sādhyaṃ evam āātmana eva samavāyikāraṇattvaṃ na manasa iti sādhyam anātmasvarūpatve saty ubahayasaṃyogajatvābhyupagamāt athāpi syāt jñānāhitasaṃskārasyātma naḥ smṛtyekakartṛtvena pratisandhānadarśanād iti na tasyāpi sādhyatvāt tatrāpi jñānasaṃskārasmṛtipratisandhānādīny ātmana eva na manasa iti sādhanīyāni phalena samānāśrayatvād icchādīnām iti cet na tatrāpi tulyatvāt saṃyogajatve saty ātmanaḥ phalecchādīni na manasa iti duḥsādham eva kiṃ cāsya jñānasyāpi jñeyatvābhyupagamād anavasthāprasaṅgaḥ na hi jñānam anyena karaṇabhūtena jñānena vijñātuṃ śakyaṃ tad apy anyena tad apy anyenety aniṣṭhaprasaṅgāt athānavasthāprasaṅgaparihārāya dūram api gatvā kiṃcij jñānam ādyaṃ vā jñānāntareṇa na gṛhyate svayam ātmanā eva gṛhyata iti tathā jñānavad arthasyāpi svayaṃ grahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ atha dīpavat svayam avabhāsate cāvabhāsayati ca avabhāsātmakatvāt arthasyānavabhāsātmakatvād adoṣa iti cet tathāpi prakāśasvarūpeṣv artheṣu vijñānenāgrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ atha jjānasya ātmasamavetatvāvabhāsanarūpābhyāṃ svayaṃ grahaṇaṃ bahiḥprakāśātmakānāṃ tu jñānaviparītadharnatvād adoṣa iti cet tac ca na yadi ca ātmasamavetatvaṃ prakāśātmakatvaṃ ca jñānasya svayaṃgrahaṇe hetuḥ syāt sarve sarvajjāḥ prāpnuvanti atha grāhyākāratvam api kāraṇaṃ cet tac ca nānyasya jñānasyānyākāratayā karaṇatvaṃ yathā tathā jñānasyāpi grāhyasyānyākāreṇānyad eva jñānaṃ karaṇaṃ syāt tathā cānavasthā duṣpariharā eva kiṃcānyat na hi kaścit svayaṃgrāhyagrāhakatvaprasādhanāya dṛṣṭānto vidyate pradīpasyāpi cakṣur ādigrāhyatvāt na cāpy aṃśadvayam asti jñānasya niravayavatvāt saty api cāṃśadvaye tayoḥ prakāśātmakatvān nānyonyagrāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ pradīpayor iva dvayoḥ kiṃ cānyat jñānasya grāhyagrāhakatvābhyupagame saty ātmasadbhāvo api dussampāda eva tasmād arthākārajñānasmṛtipratisandhānaprayotnecchā ādīnām anātmadharmatvaṃ grāhyatvāt rūpādīnāṃ iva parārthatvāc ca saṅghāt āśrayatvaṃ rūpādinidarśanena eva tathā āśrayavattvād anityatvāc ca prayatrapūrvakatvāc cety evamādibhyo anātmadharmatvasiddhiḥ ayaskānatamaṇikalpam ayakāntamaṇir eva yathā ayakāntamaṇir ayasaḥ svātmavyāptiṃ pratyupakaroti sannidhimātraṇa tathā cittam api citsvarūpasyātmanaḥ svātmavyāptiṃ pratyupakaroti dṛśyatvena nartakīva darśitaviṣayatvād antaḥkaraṇenety uktam tatra darśayitṛtvaṃ cittasya draṣṭṛtvaṃ ca puruṣasya kiṃkṛtam svasvāmitvakṛtam kathaṃ punaḥ svasvāmitvam vastu svabhāvatvāt katham it ced uktaṃ cittam ayaskāntamaṇikalpam iti atha cittavṛttīnāṃ bodhe ko hetuḥ puruṣasya iti ucyate yasmād evaṃ sannidhimātropakāri cittaṃ dṛśyatvena tasmāc cittavṛttīnāṃ bodhe puruṣasyāyaṃ hetuḥ bhavati yo sāv anādisambandaḥ tāḥ punar niroddhavyāḥ bahutve api sati cittasya yābhir vṛttibhiḥ vyutthāne sārūpyam uktaṃ puruṣasya kasmāt punaḥ niroddhavyā ity āha yato vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭākliṣṭāḥ nanu ca bahutve sati na śakyā niroddhum ity ata āha pañcatayya iti yady api kliṣṭākliṣṭā vṛttayo nantāḥ tathāpi pañcatayyaḥ pañcavidhāḥ pañcakulā eva tataś ca pañcaprakāravṛttipratipakṣabhūtābhyāsavairāgyaprayogād eva nirodhopapatteḥ pratyavayavanirodhasādhanāprayojakatvād vṛttīnāṃ tad bahutve na nirodhācakyatvaprasaṅgaḥ kleśahetukāḥ kleśanimittāḥ avidyādipañcakleśaprayuktaṃ hi cittaṃ vṛttibhir ātmānaṃ punaḥ punar āvedayati karmācayapracaye karmāṇi kuśalākuśalavimiśrāṇi tāny evāphalapradānāc cherata iti karmāśāyaśabdavācyāni teṣāṃ pracaya itaretaraguṇapradhānabhāvena saṃhananaṃ tasmin karmāśayapracaye nimitte avidyādikṣetrībhūtāḥ kliṣṭāśrayā ity arthaḥ satīṣu hi tāsu karmāśayo vipākābhimukhī bhavati khyātiviṣāyāḥ khyātyāspadāḥ guṇānām sattvādīnām adhikāraḥ saṃskārapravṛttiḥ tadvirodhinyaḥ khyātiviṣayatvād eva tā ākliṣṭāḥ apavargahetutvāt atha kliṣṭapaṅktimadhya m ānu janmāno kliṣṭā vṛttayaḥ kiṃ kliṣṭā eva kṣīrakubhaprakṣiptāmbubinduvat evam akliṣṭapravāhapatitā api kliṣṭāḥ kim akliṣṭā eva kiṃ cātaḥ yadi kliṣṭapravāhagatā akliṣṭāḥ kliṣṭāḥ syuḥ tadā vṛttisaṃskārānuvidhāyinī smṛtiḥ tadanurūpa eva vyavahāraḥ sa cāpi na sidhyati svarūpavyabhicāre tasmād āha kliṣṭacchidreṣv apy akliṣṭāḥ akliṣṭā eva bhavanti akliṣṭacchdreṣu api kliṣṭāḥ kliṣṭā eva yasmād evaṃ tasmāt tathā jātīyakāḥ saṃskārā vṛttibhir eva kriyante yady api kleśādayo api saṃskāram ārabhante tathāpi vṛttidvārā eva teṣām api saṃskāra iti vṛttibhir eva ity eva kārārthaḥ tathā saṃskārair api vṛttayaḥ svānurūpaṃ kriyanta ity evaṃ vṛttisaṃskāracakram aniśam anavaratam āvartate tad evaṃ bhūtaṃ cittaṃ evaṃ hetu hetumadvṛttisaṃskāradharmakam avasitāvakāraṃ uvivṛttāvidyāhetu pravṛttikaṃ hetu mātrāvasthatvāt ātmakalpena puruṣakalpena khyātimātreṇa eva kañcit kiñcit kālam avatiṣṭhate pārabdhasaṃskāraśeṣānuvṛttyā pralayaṃ vā gacchati saṃskāṛāvasānād iti kāḥ punas tāḥ kliṣṭākliṣṭāḥ pañcakārā vṛttaya ity āha pramāṇaviparyayavikalpanidrāsmṛtaya iti etāvatya eva vṛttayaḥ tatra pratyakṣānumānāgamāḥ pramāṇāni pramāṇākhyā vṛttis tridhā eva bhidyate tatra pramāṇākhyāyāś cittavṛtteḥ prathamo bhedaḥ pratyakṣam atas tal lakṣaṇam evābhidhīyate tat pūrvakatvāt bhedadvayasya indriyapranāḍikayā indriyam iti śrotrādipañcakaṃ na karmendriyaṃ tasya cittavṛttyahetutvāt kriyārthaṃ hi tat tasmād indriyaśabdasya sāmānyārthatve api cittavṛtter upavyācikhyāsitatvāc cchrotrādiviṣāyatā eva vṛttyarthatvāc ca śrotrādīnām indriyam eva pranāḍikā dvāraṃ śabdādyākāravṛttirūpeṇa parigamānasya cittasya atas tat tena indriyadvāreṇa sāmānyaviśeṣātmakabāhyavastvākāratayā pariṇamamānam uparajyate tasya taduparāgād hetoḥ cittasya yā mudrāpratimudrāvat vṛttiḥ sāmānyaviśeṣātmakavastūparoge api viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānā sā eva pratykṣaṃ pramāṇām atha svaviṣayasāmānyaviśeṣāvabhāsanasāmarthaye śrotrādīnāṃ cittasya ca kiṃkṛtaṃ viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānyam iti ucyate viśeṣapratibandhatvāt hānopādānādīnāṃ viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānanatety āha pradhānanateti na sāmānyaṃ nāvadhāryate guṇabhūtaṃ tu gṛhyata eva yathā nīlaṃ rūpam iti nīlāvadhāraṇapradhanye saty api rūpameva nīlam iti guṇabhūtam avadhārayati yathā duḥkhaśabdaḥ sukhaśabdo mūḍhaḥ śabda iti tathā ca viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānā vṛttir iti hy upapadyate kiṃ ca saṃśayaviparyayanimittatvāc ca sāmānyoplabdheḥ sāmānye hy upalbdhe bubuhutsitaviśeṣasya saṃśayo jāyate samupalbdhasāmānyasmṛter vā viparyayaḥ samadhigataviśeṣasya tu saṃśayaviparyayau na sthitim upāśnuvāte iti viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānatocyate yatrāpi sāmānyam evāvadidhārayiṣitaṃ gaur iti vā aśva iti vā tatrāpy anyataraparityāgenānyatarāvadhāraṇeti viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānatā eva sarvam eva hi vastu vastvantarāpekṣayā sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś ca yasya punaḥ sāmānyam avastvadhyāropitam evoṣarāmbuvat nendriyaviṣayam iti tasya pratiniyatasāmānyāshyāropaṇānupapattiḥ na hy anupalbdhapūrva sukhye saṃbhavaty adhyāropaṇā smṛtyasaṃbhavāt na kadācid adṛṣṭamukhyodakasya salilādhyāropaṇam ūṣareṣu vidyate athāsmarann apy adhyāropayet rūpasvalakṣaṇe śabdatvādy apy adhyasyet athendriyāntaraviṣayatvād rūpasvalakṣaṇe śabdatvādy adhyāso viruddha iti cet nāvastutve saty aviśeṣāt viśeṣābhyupagame ca vastutvaprasaṅgaḥ śabdasvalakṣaṇād iva rūpasvalakṣaṇasya kiṃ cānyat deśakālānyaviśiṣṭapratyakṣā na abhyupagame samastalokavyavahāravilopaḥ syāt na hīdam aham amuṣminn avakāśe kāle cāsminn adrākṣam etasmān nimittād evaṃ viśeṣaṇam iti ca smṛtyupapattiḥ na ca pratyakṣa adṛṣṭeṣu viśeṣyavad viśeṣaṇeṣu smṛtiḥ saṃbhavati na ca kalpanāpoḍhena vyavahāragocarātīten vyavaharamāṇo dṛśyate tasmāl lokaprasiddhapratyakṣānusaraṇam eva nyāyyam nanu ca yogināṃ nirvikalpasamādhijaṃ darśanaṃ tasyānevaṃ lakṣaṇatvāt tathā sukharāgādivijñānasya cānindriyapranāḍī pūrvatvāt pramāṇāntaratvam abhyupetavyaṃ pratyakṣatvaṃ vā vaktavyam ucyate pratyakṣasya na pramāṇasya puruṣapratyayāpekṣatvena parihṛtatvāt na hy apratyayā vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam caitanyodayahetor eva sapratyayāyāḥ pratyakṣatvam tathā cāha phalaṃ tadaviśiṣṭaḥ pauruṣeyaś cittavṛttibodha iti evaṃ ca sati sukharāgādijñānasya kliṣṭākliṣṭarūpasya tadaviśiṣṭapuruṣapratyayaphalāvasānatvāt pratyakṣatā siddhā eva indriyapranāḍikāgrahaṇaṃ laukikapratyakṣodbhavānuvāda eva anyathā hīndriyanirapekṣasya yogīśvarayor jñānasyāpratyakṣatā syāt asti hi kleśādipratibandhābhāve sarvārthena cittasattvena sarvaviṣayeṇa yugapatsūkṣmavyavahitādigrahaṇam tathā tārakaṃ sarvaviṣayaṃ sarvathāviṣayam akramaṃ ceti vivekajaṃ jñānam iti tasmān nāvadhāryate indriyapranāḍikayaivety bāhyavastu uparāgād iti viparyayanivṛttyartham viśeṣāvadhāraṇapradhānatvena saṃśayanivṛttir iti tatra keṣāṃ cit phalaṃ tad eva pramāṇam apareṣāṃ tu pramāṇād anyatra anyat pramāṇavyaktyantare antaram yathā ghaṭavijñānasya pramāṇāsya hānopādānāpekṣā buddhayaḥ phalam iti guṇadoṣatad ubhaya vad abhava śūnyatvaviṣayatvād upādānādibuddhīnāṃ pramāṇabhūtaghaṭavijñānād atyantabhedaḥ tataś cānyaviṣayasya pramāṇasyānya prameyasya viṣayapramāṇa ṇe vyaktyantaraṃ re phalam iti na hi khadir cchedanasya khadiropādānaṃ tat parityāgo vā phalaṃ bhavituṃ yuktam api vi yogasabandhaphalatvāt tyāgopādānayoḥ na ca phalasya phalaṃ sambhavati dvaidhī bhāvaphalavyavahitatvāc ca kiṃ ca phalasya cet phalaṃ kriyā anapekṣāprasaṅgaḥ phalārthaṃ hi kriyā apekṣyate tac cet phalaṃ vināpi kriyayā phalād api sidhyati ato hy tato na hy anekāyasāpekṣitaniṣpattikriyām anutiṣṭhet sādhanānveṣaṇānupapattiś ca kriyāyā abhāvāt nāpi kriyā eva phalaṃ kriyā anupraramaprasaṅgāt phalāvasanā api hi kriyā kriyāyāś ca phalatve phalānabhilāṣitvaprasaṅgaḥ tasyā duḥkhatvāt tasmānnityā na pramāṇasvarūpam eva phalam nāpi tadvyatiriktapramāṇāntaram ity āha phalaṃ tadaviśiṣṭa ity ādi tadaviśiṣṭaḥ tayā pramāṇākhyayā vṛttyā aviśiṣṭaḥ tulyaḥ tadākāratvena pauruṣeyaḥ puruṣasyāyaṃ bodha iti puruṣasya hi vṛttyākāratā tasmānnityā nākriyājaṃ dravyasvarūpamātraṃ phalaṃ kiṃ tarhi dravyasyaivāvasthāntaraviśeṣa ḥ kriyājā jaḥ kriyāparyavasānakālaḥ kriyā uparamopapatteḥ phalam phalaniṣpattāv eva hi kriyā uparama upapadyate evaṃbhūtasya mukhyaphalatve pradhānakriyāviprakṛṣṭāyāḥ vyavahita kriyāyā dravyaṃ dravyasya vā kriyā phalam ity anyonyapratyupasthāpakatvena pradhānaphalābhimukhīkaraṇāt phalatvopacāro na virotsyate nanu ca bhavato apy upacritam eva phalam vṛttyaviśiṣṭāyāḥ phalatvenābhupagamāt puruṣasya ca śuddhatvāt tadākāratayā anṛtatvam na hi sphaṭikamaṇer alaktakopadhānākāratā satyā bāḍham tathāpi tv etad eva phalaṃ mukhyam dṛṣṭatvāt mukhyaphalāntarādarśanāt sarvasyaiva kriyākārakajātasya etatphalārthatvāt etadavasānaṃ hi tat sarvam tathā ca pradarśitam nanu ca mithyā bhūtasya eva mukhyaphalatvaṃ vṛttyākārasya tathā ca tadabhilāṣānupapattiḥ bāḍham mithyā bhūta eva vṛttyanugato bhogaḥ tathā cāha sattvapuruṣayor atyantāsaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyayāviśeṣo bhogaḥ iti bhāṣyam api tayoḥ svarūpopalmbhe sati kuto bhoga iti ata eva ca samyagdarśanād ātyantokī nivṛttir upapadyate yeṣām amithyā phalaṃ teṣāṃ vairāgyakāraṇābhāvāt samyagdarśanānveṣaṇānupapatter mokṣābhāvaḥ na ca kriyāpariniṣpādyo mokṣaḥ anityatvaprasaṅgāt atha buddhiboddhṛtvaṃ puruṣasya sattvaṃ cāsiddham iti cet āha pratisaṃvedī boddheḥ puruṣa ity upariṣṭāt pravediyiṣyāma iti ye ca api indriy arthasannikarṣasya pratyakṣatvam abhyupayanti na teṣām api samyag abhyupetaṃ sannikarṣasya kriyāphalatvāt sannikarṣaś ca saṃyogaḥ sa ca kriyājas tair iṣyate yato yad upajāyate tat tasya pramāṇam tac ca tasya phalaṃ yad upajāyate phalam api sannikarṣī jñānaṃ prati pramāṇam iti cet tac ca na jñāpakapramāṇaprastāve kārakapramāṇa upanyāsasya ayuktatvāt sannikarṣī hi jñānasya utpādako na tasya jñāpakaḥ prameyādhigamāya hi pratyakṣādīny yas tāni na jñāna utpattikāraṇam tat prakriyāyāma yānya prakṛtaṃ prakriyeta atha api syāt jñānasya api prameyatvāt tac ca apy utpadyamānaṃ pramīyata iti tadytpattikāraṇasya sannikarṣasya jñāpakatvam eva iti tac ca na jñānaṃ jñanena eva jñāyeta teṣāṃ tathā abhyupagamāt na ca sannikarṣo jñānam jñāna utpādakatvena abhyupagamāt atha jñānasya jñāne sannikarṣo nimittatvāt pramāṇam iti ced adṛṣṭa īśvara icchā viṣayanimeṣādīnām api nimittatvāt pramāṇatve kaḥ pradveṣaḥ na ca jñānasya jñeyatve ātmanaś ca svabhāvacid rūpatv anabhyupagame śakyā anavasthā parihartum athātmasamavetamātratayaiva jñānasya jñeyatā na jñāna antaram apekṣyate yena atiprasajyeta iti cet asya apy anyat pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ vācyam anindriyasannikarṣādilakṣaṇatvād ātmani jñānasamavāyatvasya sannikarṣasya ca jñāna utpattiphalatvāt tadutpattivyavadhāne sati tasya jñānasya na ānantaryam tasmāt tad ānantaryeṇāpi na sannikrṣaphalatvaṃ jñānasya tathā hānādibuddhīnām api rūpādijñānaphalatva anupapattir uktā vyabhicārāc ca yathā ekasminn aṅganādipiṇḍhaviṣaye jñāne samāne bahūnām utpanne kasyacid upādānabuddhiḥ anyasya heyabuddhiḥ kasyacid ubhaya abhāvaḥ tatra hāna upādānabuddhir vyabhicarati anyataratra ekam eva jñānaṃ tad eva uhayaṃ vyabhicaraty upekṣakasya yac ca yad vyabhicarati na tat tasya phalam kiṃ ca hāna upādāna bhāvamātratvād abhāva eva upekṣā na ca abhāvaḥ pramāṇasya vatunaḥ phalaṃ bhavitum arhati rādadveṣābhyāṃ ca upādānaparityāgabuddhī tadabhāvāt kāraṇa abhāve kārya abhāva iti pramāṇavijñāne saty api hāna upādānabuddhyabhāva eva upekṣa iti vyabhicārān na hāna ādibuddhiphalatvam kiṃ ca rāgadveṣatadabhāvānām apy upādānādibuddhiphalatve pramāṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ pauruṣeyacittavṛttibodhatve tu na kiñcid viruddhyata iti nanu ca cittavṛtteḥ saṃvedyatvam asiddham na hi karaṇam eva karma bhavati na hi dātram eva lūyate na eṣa doṣaḥ kriyākārakayor bhinnadharmatvāt kriyānivṛttim prati sambhūya kārakāṇi vyāpriyante parasparaṃ viṣayaviṣayibhāvena kriyā tu sattāmātreṇa eva phalahetur iti karaṇatvam asyām upacaryate na kārakavat kurvad hi kārayed iti kriyā adhikārakaṃ syān na bhūtaṃ bhavyāya upadiśyate kiṃ ca anavasthāprasaṅgaś ca kriyā cet karaṇaṃ syāt tannivṛttyayā ca anyayā kriyayā bhavitavyam na hy anyāṃ kriyām antareṇa tasyāḥ kāraṇa karaṇa tvaṃ ghaṭate yā api ca anyā sā api kāraṇaṃ syād anyasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sā apy anyasyā ity anavasthā tataś ca kriyāsantāna anuparamāt phala anabhinivṛttiḥ tatra antyā cet kriyā antareṇa vinā phalahetur bhavet prathamasya tathātve kaḥ pradveṣaḥ cittavṛttes tv abhivyañjakatvāt samvedyate ty adoṣaḥ dṛśyate ca abhivyañjakānāṃ svarūpasaṃvedyatā eva karaṇatvaṃ pradīpādīnām tathā cittavṛtter api cakṣur ādiṣv abhivyañjakatve api agrahaṇad vyabhicāra iti cet samāna cetanasamāna jātīyasaṃkarāt katham yeṣāṃ tāvad bhautikāni indriyāṇi teṣāṃ cakṣuṣas taijasatvāt bāhyena ālokena tulyajātīyena vyatibhedāt gṛhyamāṇasya eva avivekaḥ yathā pradīpānāṃ bahūnāṃ prabhāvyatibhedāt kasya kā prabhā iti na vivicyate tathā śrotrādiṣv api yeṣām apy abhautikāni teṣām apy abhivyañjakatvena samānajātīyatā vṛtter abhivyañjakatvād agrahaṇam iti tan na prāptacaitanya upagrahatayā vibhāvyatvād avyavahitatvāc ca sarvagatatve apy ātmanaḥ sūkṣmatvena svaccharatvena ca cittena avyavadhānāc ca saṃvedyamāna eva phalam iti siddham yeṣāṃ punaḥ pratyakṣeṇa asaṃvedyo cittavṛttis teṣāṃ phalagrahaṇapramāṇābhāvaḥ phale ca gṛgīte jñāna asiddhatvasya arthāpattiḥ na ca phalaṃ gṛhyate pramāṇavyāpāra anabhyupagamāt tadabhyupagame ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ yat phala avagrahaṇāya pramāṇam abhyupagamyate tasya apy anyat phalaṃ tat pramāṇasya apy anyad iti na kvacid avatiṣṭheta atha na pramāṇavyāpāras tasya tadā pramāṇa abhāvāt phalasya asattvaṃ prasaktam yatra hi sadupalambhakāni pramāṇāni na vyāpāraṃ gacchanti tan nāstīty abhyupagacchāmaḥ teṣām athāgṛhyamāṇam api tad eva jñānaṃ phalasya apīti cet na abhivyañjakadharmavyatikramāt na hy abhivyañjakaṃ gṛhyamāṇam abhivyañjayad dṛṣṭam na hy ulkā giriśikhare api nijaṃ dharmaṃ atikramati athābhivyañjayad eva phalaṃ praty api pramāṇam iti cet siddhaṃ tarhi īpsitam asmākam rāgādīnāṃ vṛttiviśeṣaṇatvena grahaṇa upapatteḥ rakto haṃ dviṣṭo ham iti yady ahaṃ pratyayaviśeṣaṇaṃ tad api vṛttibhāva abhāvitvena eva grahaṇād vṛttiviśeṣaṇānāṃ rāgādīnāṃ grahaṇam upapadyate ā tenā nyathā rūpādivan mānāntarāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāt tataś cānavastheti tasmāt pramāṇaphalānabhijñānam abhimānamātram eva kevalaṃ paṇḍitaṃ manyānām ity upekṣaṇīyam iti anumānam atha ucyate anumeyasya tulyajātīyeṣv anuvṛtta iti anumeyasya jijñāsita dharmaviśiṣṭasya tad dharmavattayā tulyajātīyeṣv anuvṛttaḥ sadbhāvamātreṇa bhinnajātīyebhyaḥ tadviruddhadharmakebhyo vyāvṛttaḥ teṣv asan ity arthaḥ sambandha iti kaḥ sambandhaḥ kayor vā na hi sambandhināv anāpekṣya sambandhaḥ sambandhatāmiyāt yad asau prasiddhavac ca ucyate ya iti nanu cānumānasya prakṛtatvāt liṅgaliṅginoḥ sambandhaḥ prasiddha eva nāgamakatvāt na kevalaḥ sambandho gamakaḥ ucyate liṅgasya eva sambadho vyāvṛttyanuvṛttyoḥ kaḥ punar asau liṅgam eva na hi liṅgād anyad anuvṛttaṃ vyāvṛttaṃ ca tac ca gamakam nanu liṅgam api na eva gamakaṃ liṅgisambandhānapekṣaṃ yadi ca anapekṣitaliṅgisambandhaṃ gamakaṃ yadvṛttibhūmijayakrameṇa ubhayākṣepapūrvako kiñcid gamakaṃ syāt tasmāt liṅgaliṅgisambandho vaktavyaḥ na uktatvāt anumeyasya tulyajātīyeṣv anuvṛttaḥ ity ādinaiva uktatvāt na hy anumeyena asaṃbaddhaṃ liṅginā tat sadṛśajātīyeṣv anuvartate bhinnajātīyebhyo vā nivartate tasmāt ya iti ca prasiddham eva saṃbandham anuvadati tadviṣayā evam anvayavyatirekavośiṣṭasambandiviṣayā vṛttiḥ sāmānya avadhāraṇapradhānā liṅgasāmānya avadhāraṇapradhānā anumānam yathā deśāntaraprāpter gatimac candratārakaṃ caitravad iti yady api lakṣaṇa abhidhānamātraṇa tad abhivyaktih tatjā apy udāharaṇapratyudāharaṇapradarśanād atitarām ity udāharaṇapratipādanam tatra gatimac candratārakam iti candratārakasya gatimattvam anumeyam tatsumanajātīyeṣv anuvṛttā deśāntaraprāptir gatimatsu caitrādiṣu bhinnajātīyebhyaś ca agatibhyo vindhyādibhyo vyāvṛttā ity avyabhicarantī nityaṃ gatimatā sambandhāt bhavatu tāvad aviruddhānāṃ nityasambandhād deśāntaraprāptyādīnāṃ gamyagamakatā vadhyaghātakādīnāṃ tu sambandh abhāve katham ity ucyate gamyagamakabhāvaḥ bhāvvena tatrāpi nityasambandhād adoṣaḥ na hy atrāpi prāptilakṣaṇaḥ sambandho abhipreyate sāmānyatodṛṣṭā nu bhāvaprasaṅgāt na hi candratārakādiṣu deśāntaraprāpteḥ prāptilakṣāṇasambandhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate agṛhyamāṇaś ced gamakaḥ sarvaṃ sarvasya gamakaṃ syāt na hi kiṃcit kenacid asambaddham ākāśādīnāṃ sarvatra bhāvāt tasmād ganyagamakabuddhyutpattihetur eva sambandho anumānavisaye tathā ca badhyaghātakayor apy anyatara rā bhāvadarśane nyatarabhāvo gamyata ity anumānam eva yasya apy ucite deśe abhāvadarśanād anyatra bhāvo gamyate yathā ghātakadarśanena badhyābhāvo numīyate caitrasya jīvato gṛhe abhāva gṛhyabhāva darśane bahirbhavaś ca iti nanu cābhāvārthāpattī ete nānumāne na lakṣaṇāsaṅgateṅ gavādivat na yathā uktalakṣānopapatteḥ badhyaghātakayor virodhalakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ yatra yatra ghātakabhāvas tatra badhyā bhāva eva ity avinā bhāvaḥ na hi badhyasya abhāvaṃ ghātaka kā bhāvo vyabhicarati badhyasya vā bhāvo ghātakā ka bhāvam agnibhāvam iva dhūmabhāvaḥ kathaṃ punar avagamyate ghātakabhāvadarśanad eva tad gocare badhyasya abhāvabuddhir iti na punaḥ sadupalambhakapramāṇānāṃ ghātaka iva badhye vyāpārābhāvād iti ucyate ghātakabhāve vyāpṛ pyāvṛ tapramāṇasya eva badhyā bhāvabuddhiupapattiḥ dhūmabhāve vyāpṛ vṛ tatapramāṇasya badhyaviśeṣābhāvabuddhyutpattiḥ dhūmaviśeṣavyāpṛ vṛ tapramāṇasyeva agniviśeṣabuddhir iti abhāvapramāṇavādinas tu sarvatra pramāṇābhāvasya aviśiṣṭatvād virodhiviśeṣadarśanānuvidhānaṃ virodhyantarābhāvadarśanasya anupapannaṃ liṅgaviśeṣa anuvudhānam iva liṅgiviśeṣadarśanasya na hi sadupalambhakapramāṇavyāpārābhāvasya kaścid viśeṣaḥ yena viśeṣabuddhis tad viśeṣam anuvidhīyate atha jajñāsite viśeṣe sadupalambhakapramāṇa abhāvād iti cet tan nāsataḥ smṛti icchādisahabhāva apekṣanupapatteḥ na hy asat sahāya apekṣaya kāryaṃ nirvartayad dṛṣṭaṃ śaśa Viṣāṇādi dṛṣṭam iha iti cet na vipratipattisthānatve dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt tulyam iti cet na ghaṭādeḥ sato pekṣādarśanāt na cāpi nirvyāpārasyāvastutvād abhāvasya pramaṇabhāvo yoktaḥ na hi nirastavyāpārakaṃ kiṃcit kāryārambhakaṃ dṛśyate loke tasmād vyāpārarūpapramāṇajanitā prameyābhāvabuddhiḥ prameyaviṣayatvat ghaṭādibuddhivat tathā ca vastutvāt pravṛttinivṛttihetutvāt vipakṣaḥ śaśaviṣāṇādiḥ tathā abhāva pramā pramāṇā ṇa bhāvajanitā na bhavati yathā bhihitahetu dṛṣṭāntadarśanāt nena ghātakadarśanaṃ badhya abhāvabuddher liṅgaṃ tad bhāvitvād agnyādibuddhinimittadhūmādibuddhivat saṃśayanivartakatvāc ca badhyā bhāvabuddhir vā liṅgajanitā niścayarūpatvād agnibuddhivad iti iha gaṭo nāstīti kila nānumānaṃ liṅgaliṅgisambandhāgrahaṇāt na hi yathā agnyādibuddheer dhūmadiliṅga anveṣaṇaṃ tathā iha nāsti ghaṭa ity atra liṅgānveṣaṇam asti prāg eva liṅgānveṣaṇāt buddhyutpatteḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ ihapratyaya ākārasya eva liṅgatvāt na hi prathamam eva liṅgabuddhu upajanane sati liṅgānveṣaṇaṃ bhavati iha ityākāra uparañjitā buddhir liṅgam umuparañjakavyatiriktaghaṭādyabhāvabudder ghātakabuddhivad eva virodhalakṣaṇa eva ca atra api sambandhaḥ yatra punar aviruddhāny uparañjakāni tatra astitvabuddheḥ etena eva arthāpatter anumānatvaṃ vyākhgyātam avinābhāvena sambandhena tatra api jīvato hi devadattasya gṛhābhāve bahir bhāvaḥ yadā gṛhe bhāvaḥ na tadā bahir bhāva ity anyatareṇānumānam sākṣāt dṛśyamānabahir bhāva abhyantarābhāvatvaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ vṛttyuparañjaka anuparañjakatvena hy abhāvagrahaṇasya abhihito hetuḥ agnyādāv api dhanādiśaktigrahaṇam anumānam eva kāryanirvartakayor avinā bhāvasambandhasya ātmani dṛṣṭatvād bhujyādau dṛśyate hi pratyagātmani śakto ham idaṃ kāryaṃ kartum aśakto ham ity ātmavad ātmaviśeṣaṇasya śakter grahaṇam śaktinirvartyam eva dahanādikāryam api ity anumānasiddhiḥ nanu cābhāvasya pratyakṣatām upagāyanti kecit yathā kilādarśakena pradīpādinā sati gṛhyamāṇe vastuni na tad avayavini yad upalbhyate tan na asti ity evaṃ sataḥ prakarśakaṃ pramāṇam asad api prakāśayati tathā ca udāharanti anaṅkitaṃ vāsa ānayety praviśya bhāṇḍāgāram aṅkitānaṅkitavāsas sannidhāv aṅkitavāso grahaṇena eva pratyakṣeṇāṅkitābhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ vāsa upalabhyanayati tasmāt pratyakṣa evābhāvo lakṣaṇāntara anupapatter iti tan na buddhyākāreṇārthāvadhāraṇānṛtatvaprasaṅgāt yadākārā hi buddhis tasya pratyakṣa avadhriyamāṇātmatābhyupagamyate yathā nīlaṃ vastu pītam ity atra api viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasambandhapratyayo mithyā prāpnoti tadyathā iha ghaṭo nāsti itīhapradeśasya ghaṭābhāvena asati sambandhe sambandhapratyayah na hi ghaṭābhāvasya ihapradeśasya cā prāpta prāptilakṣaṇaḥ samavāyābhidhānovā sambandhas tair abhyyathā iha devadatta iti tasmād abhāva ve pratyayavā yā n nīlaṃ vastv iti viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasambandhapratyayo api sambandhapratyayatvān mithyā prasajyeta yathā ca asty api ihadeśaghaṭa abhāvasambandhe sabandhapratītis tathā eva anīle api vastuny asaty eva nīlatvasambandge nīlatvasambandhapratyayaḥ prāpnoti tathā sambandhiṣv api atha asty eva sambandhaḥ dviṣṭhatā viruddhyeta sambandhasya abhāvasya avastutva abhyupagamāt atha apy ekaśataṃ ṣaṣṭhyarthā iti yāvat ṣaṣthyarthāḥ sambandha iṣyeta tadā dvividha eva sambandhaḥ samavāyākhyaḥ samyogākhyaś ca iti na yujyate athai tathai kaśatasya api ṣaṣṭhyarthānāṃ ubhayāntaḥpātitvam ucyeta nābhāve anyatarasya apy asambhavāt kiñcā ntva nyat iha nabhasi kusumaṃ na asti iti sambandhino nabhaso apy apratyakṣatvāt gaganakusuma abhāvasya apratyakṣatvaṃ prāpnoti atha apratyakṣatvam eva iti ced āpatitaṃ gaganakusuma abhāvavad apratyakṣatvam iha bhū pradeśe ghaṭa abhāvasya api viśeṣo vaktavyaḥ atha vyomno pratyakṣatvād iti tan na puṣpasya patato nabhasy astitvadarśanād vyoma apratyakṣatvam ahetuḥ yathā eva nipatatkusumasadbhāve vyoma apratyakṣatvam ahetus tathā sadbhāvaviruddhagrahaṇe apy ahetuḥ syāt atha ākāśāpratyakṣatvād eva iti cet asambandham api yat kiṃcid vyavahitāpratyakṣatvādi so api hetuḥ syāt atha nabhaḥ kusuma abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa iti cet indriya arthasannikarṣa anarthakyaṃ sarvatra prasajyate tathā ca saty asannikarṣṭa upalabdheḥ sarveṣāṃ sarvajñatvaṃ prasaktam atha anumeyaṃ tatreti cet nabhaḥ kusuma abhāvavad iha ghaṭābhāvasya aviśeṣād anumānikatva kīya m eva siddham evaṃ ca saty abhāvapramāṇavādino api vyavahitaviprakṛṣṭodakādāv analādy abhāvasya anumeyatvād iha ghaṭābhāvo api tatsāmānyād anumānagrāhya eva iti niścetuṃ yuktam vindhyāś cāprāpter agatir iti ca prayogāntaram agatir vindhya iti pratijñānam aprāpter iti hetuḥ caitravad iti kākalocanavad ubhayatra sambadhyate gatimac candratārakam ity anena sādharmyeṇa vindhyāś cāaprāpter ity anena vaidharmyeṇa sambandhaḥ evaṃ ca saty anvayavyatirekā ka darśanakṛto na doṣaḥ atha vaitasmin prayoge vyatirekaviparyayadarśanena doṣābhāva ity upanyastam lakṣaṇasya ca lakṣyaviśeṣeṇa ūhyatvād adoṣaḥ āptaḥ parānujighṛkṣāprayukto doṣarahito dṛṣṭānumita arthaḥ tena dṛṣṭo vā anumito vārthaḥ paratra śrotṛviśeṣe svabodhasaṅkrāntaye svādhigamasaṃkramaṇāya śabdena śabda iti vākyaṃ tato viśiṣṭārthapratipatteḥ tasmāt tadupadiṣṭād vākyāt tadarthaviṣayā vākyārthaviṣayā yā cittavṛttiḥ sā anumānavad eva sāmānyāvadhāraṇapradhānā ittham āptyādidharmagrahaṇapūrvakā śrotur āgamaḥ na vaktuḥ dṛṣṭānumita artho hi vaktā tasya laiṅgakam aindriyakaṃ vā taj jñānam śrotur eva tu śravaṇapūrvakaṃ niścitaṃ vijñānaṃ laiṅgikaindriyakavyatiriktam sa āgamaḥ na pratyakṣam indriyā viṣaya viṣayatvāt yathā abhihitaliṅgaliṅgisambandhanirapekṣatvāc ca nānumānam na hi svargāpūrvadevatādiśabdā bde arthānvitaṃ jñānam āsāditaliṅgaliṅgisambandhapurassaram upajāyate phalaṃ tu sarvatra pauruṣeyo vṛttibodha eva yasya āgamasya vaktā āgama ākhyavṛttyutpattinimitte śabdoccāraṇāt āgamasya prayogopanyāsena pratipāditaṃ phalaṃ tu pūrvavad eva yadā apy eka eva prayogas ta thā dā api sādhyasādhana abhāvamātrasya vivakṣitatvān na viparītavyatirekadarśanād ity ucyate aśraddheya arthavaktrabhihitatvena āgama eva viśiṣyate katham asāv aśraddheya artho vaktā ity ata āha na dṛṣṭo numito vārthaḥ tena vaktā śiṣṭaleka prasiddha anyathā pratipādanāt buddhārhata ādiḥ na hi rāgādidoṣānupahatāntaḥkaraṇaḥ prasiddham anyathā nirvarṇayati sa āgamaḥ plavate ābhāsī bhavati yady api pratyakṣa anumānaviṣaya ābhāsadarśanaṃ svaśabdena na kṛtaṃ tathā apy āgama ābhāsa upadarśanena eva pūrvatrāpi yathābhihitalakṣaṇaviparītatvena pratyakṣānumānābhāsādi draṣṭavyam arthād uktam mūlavaktari tu ādyavaktarīśvare tann nimitto ya āgamaḥ sa viplavanimittābhāvānnirviplavaḥ syāt yathā artha ya vaktṛvat upamānaṃ mānaṃ śabdapūrvakaṃ tadāgama antaḥpātitvān na pramṇāntaram yathā gaur iva gavaya iti vanecarabhihatād eva vākyād avadhṛtasādṛśya punar vane gavayadarśane api pūrvaśrutavākya upasthāpitasādṛśyasmaraṇamātram eva nādhikam sādṛśyaṃ tu vākyād eva pūrvapratipannam na api saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhapratipattita eva mānaṃ tasyā api tadvākyād evāvagatatvāt na hi gaur ity etāvatānavagatagavayanāmakasya vanagatagavayadarśino api gavayo yam iti saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhāvabodho bhavati tasmād gaur iva gavaya iti gavayaśabdo api tadvākye pekṣitavyaḥ tathā ca sati pūrvaśrutād eva sarvaṃ pratītam athāpi syād ayaṃ dasya gavaya iti na pūrvabuddhiviṣayam iti tad api tatrabhavatām api paricodanaparihāram ava pa śyatām api pīḍitakaivale kaule yakavṛttikoṇo vasthānam iva lakṣyate tathā hi deśakālasannikarṣaviprakarṣādibhedenanekopamānabhedaḥ prasajyeta tathāstv iti cet tat pūrvadhiyā eātatvam antar nihitasamastaviśeṣam eva hi vā neyau pūrvam upapāditam na hi gaur ity ukte deśakāla ādiviśeṣābhāve na go śabdād arthapratipattiḥ kiṃ cānyat na hi saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhapratipattir upamānaṃ yena hy apamīyate tadupamānaṃ sādṛśyajñānaṃ hi tat na hi nāmināmasambandhapratipattyā kiṃcid upamīyate uttarakālatvāt avadhṛtasādṛśyasya hi paścād ā sya yaṃ gavaya ity evaṃ so api nipatati evam tarhi syād aśabdapūrvakaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ yathā gavayadarśanād etat sadṛśo gaur iti grāmīṇasya buddhiḥ tad api na prameyābhāvāt sati hi prameye sadupalmbhakatva abhimatasya pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ na hi go gavayayor vyāvṛttam anuvṛttaṃ ca vastutaḥ sādṛśyaṃ nāmaikam asti nanu ca sādṛśyabuddhir asty eva nāsau nirālambanā bhavitum arhati satyam evaṃ tatra eva vicāraṇā kim asau vanayūthādipratyayavat atha ghaṭādibuddhivad iti kim cātaḥ yadi vanapratyayavad bhavet tadā yathā eva viśiṣṭasanniveśānugatā mahīruhā eva ātmavyatirekeṇāvidyamānavanapratyayahetavas tathā eva go gavayāvayavā eva dvayadarśanasmṛtyapekṣayā svātmavyatirekeṇāsataḥ sādṛśyasya pratītau kāraṇam iti prāptam avastutvam atha punar ghaṭādipratyayavad vastutvaṃ pramāṇatvaṃ ca tadā syād iti tatra kīdṛśaṃ vastv iti vicāryate kiṃ go gavayayor anuvṛttam ekaṃ sādṛśyaṃ gotvagavayatvābhyām anyat te eva vānyonyaviśiṣṭe yadi vā tābhyāṃ bhinne go gavayādhāre dve sādṛśye parasparānupekḍe sāpekṣe vā kiṃ vyaktir eva sānyatarajātiviśiṣṭā vā kiṃ jātiḥ sācānyataravyaktiviśiṣṭā vyaktidvayaviśiṣṭā vā sambandho vaiteṣāṃ yathā vikalpayogam ity ekaikānyonyaviśiṣṭaviśeṣaṇatvādinā bhūyāṃso nye api vikalpā udbhāvayitavyāḥ tatra yady ekaṃ sādṛśyam ubhayagataṃ tadā na upameyatvam ekatvāt yathā gaur iva gaur iti atha tenānyataravyaktir upamīyate na etad api svātmagatatvāt gaur iva gotvena atha tadvatyā vyaktyā vyaktyantaram upamīyate na etad api na hi gotvvaṃ khaṇḍamuṇḍa upameyatvakāraṇam atha dharmāntarāpekṣayā sādṛśyaṃ tadbuddheḥ kāraṇam iti naṣṭaṃ tarhi sādṛśyaṃ sa evāstu dharmaḥ tadbuddheḥ kiṃ te sādṛśyahatakena kalpitena kiṃ ca sa cāpy apekṣyamāṇo dharmaḥ kim ekaḥ sādṛśyavad ubhayatrātha bhinna ity evam ādivikalpāḥ syur ity asambhavaḥ pūrvavad eva atha bhinnam ṃ sādṛśyam ucyate tac ca na bhedād eva na hi bhavati gaur ivāśva iti yathaivaikaikatvād aghaṭamānatā tathā bahubhir apekṣyamāṇaiḥ etena jātivyaktisambandhādayaḥ pūrvavikalpitāḥ pratyuktāḥ atha buddhyutpattyanyathānupapattyā sādṛśyakalpanā saty evaṃ vanavivarapūrvadakṣiṇottarādibuddhiyogānyathānubhavāt nyathānupapattyā vastutvaṃ kiṃ na kalpyate syād eṣā tava buddhir vṛkṣādaya eva tatra tadbuddhijanmahetava iti yady evaṃ mithyāpratyayo gavayena sadṛśī gaur iti vanabuddhivat atha ye vyāvṛttāḥ ka iha upamārthaḥ gaur ivāśva iti atha ubhaye api te vayavā vyāvṛttanuvṛttātmānas tadbudhdihetavaḥ tathāpi vanapratyayavad eva prāptam tasmāt parikṣyamāṇaṃ nātivimardanakṣamam iti ta evāvayavā ubhayatra upalbhyamānā bhūyāṃsaḥ sādṛśyabuddheḥ kāraṇaṃ vanabuddher iva pādapāḥ iti na upamānaṃ nāma prmāṇāntaram iti siddham nāpi premeyadvitvāt pramāṇadvitvakalpanam kutaḥ pramāṇavaśād arthapratīteḥ na hy arthavaśāt pramāṇakalpanā yadi cārthavaśāt pramāṇakalpanā syāt adhunā tan na śakyaṃ jānānām asarvajñatvāt caityavandanāt svargo bhavati ity atra caityavandanasya svargahetutvabuddheḥ pratyakṣanumāna aviṣayatvān mithyātvaṃ syāt tad arthaṃ vā pramāṇāntarakalpanam atha sā buddhir anmānaphalam iti cet pramāṇād anyatra phalaprasaṅgaḥ evaṃ canirmokṣaḥ ka raṇatrayādivākyārthaviṣyabuddhir apīti nāpi cātra pramāṇalakṣaṇanirūpaṇatātparyaṃ prasiddhapramāṇādivṛttinirodhābhyupāya abhipradarśanaparatvāt ata eva na sūtrakāraḥ sūtrayāñcakāra bhāsyakāreṇa tu kiñcit prasiddhānuvādamātram avalambitam iti tad anusareṇena kim api jalpitam iti pramāṇākhyāṃ vṛttim vyākhyāya viparyayābhidhānaṃ vṛttim idānīm upavyācikhyāsamāna āha viparyayo mithyā jñānam iti nanu nirodhasya prakṛtatvāt tasya ca hānatvād dhānasya ca heyāpekṣatvād dheyasya ca avidyamūlatvād avidyā ca viparyya iti sa eva prādhānyena niroddhvayaḥ tat prabhavatvād dheyasya kāraṇanirodhe hi kāryam arthād eva niruddhaṃ syāt tasmād viparyayaḥ prādhānyāt pramāṇāt pūrvaṃ vyākhyātavaya satyam evam asyeva prāthamyaṃ viparyayasya nirodhanīyatayā tathāpi guṇadoṣajñāna apekṣatvān nirodhaṃ prati puruṣapravṛtteḥ pramāṇam eva hi guṇadoṣajñānam na hy apremāṇena viparyayasya duṣṭatvaṃ gamyate nirodhatat phalasādhanāni vā jñāyante tasmāt pramāṇavṛtter eva prāthamyaṃ yuktam jñāyete ca guṇadoṣau pramṇena iti tad anantaraṃ viparyaya abhidhānam vṛttyantara apekṣayā tu viparyayasya prāthamyam tan mūlatvāc ca vṛttyantarāṇāṃ tannirodhapūrvam evānyanirodhopapatteḥ viparyayo mithyā jñanam iti paryāyakathanam atad rūpapratiṣṭham iti lakṣaṇoktiḥ tasya rūpaṃ tad rūpaṃ yad ābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ tasya vijñānasya ca sā pratiṣṭhā ālambanam agṛhītaviśeṣasya sāmānyamātrabuddhir upalabdhapūrvānyavastu smṛtyupasaṃhitā niścayākāreṇopasaṃhitā niścayākāreṇopājāyamānā viparyayaḥ saṃśayo hy ubhayor idaṃ sāmānyam ity evaṃ gṛhītasāmānyasya viśeṣam eva bubhutsamānasya jāyata iti smṛtāv evāntarbhavati yathā sthāṇuḥ kiṃ vā purusa iti gṛhītapūrvasya eva viśeṣasya smarataḥ saṃśayo jāyante na tathā viparyayaḥ anyatarasmaraṇamātreṇa evāvasitatvāt tad yathā sthāṇau purastād avasthite pariṇāhārohaṇādisāmānyamātropalambhena samupajātapuruṣas araṃasya puruṣa evāyam iti niśtirā buddhir utpadyate sā yady apīndriyamārgeṇopalabhyamānavastu sāmānyapradhānā tathāpi smaryamāṇātadvastupratiṣṭhatvān na pramāṇam smṛtyavasānā hi sā yataḥ pramāṇena prabādhyate ā ā bhūtārtha arthādi viṣayatvāt ity ataḥ pratiṣṭhatvād ity etat abhūto hi smaryamāṇo rthas tadā yady evaṃ smṛtir eva prāpnoti na viśiṣṭatvāt upalabhyamānaṃ vastu nimittīkṛtyānyatra smṛtir jāyate yathānubhūtavastu viṣayā na viparyayas tathā sannihitasāmānyamātre deśakālādiviśeṣānugate vastuni smaraṇaparyavasānatve saty apy ayam iti viśeṣarūpeṇa viparyayapratyayo jāyate tasmād evaṃ na pramāṇadharmo nāpi smṛtir dharma iti vṛttyantaratvam tatrāmramāṇasya pramāṇena bādhasaṃdarśanārtham udāharaṇaṃ darśayati tad yathā dvicandradarśanam iti yathā kācakāmalādyupahatadarśanasyābhūtārthaviṣayatvād dhi dvicandradarśanasya sadviṣayeṇa bhūtārthaviṣayeṇa ekacandradarśanena dvitīyacandrābhāvopapattijñānasmṛtyanugṛhītena bādhanam nanu ca dvicandram iti dvipūlī paṇcapūlītivat dvigusamāsatvāt dvigur ekavacanam iti pratibandhe tadbhāvāt akārāntottarapado dviguḥ striyām iṣṭaḥ iti dvigor akārāntāt iti dvicandraśabdād īkāraḥ prāpnoti naiṣa doṣaḥ pātrādipratiṣedhāt tatra ca ādiśabdāsya prakāravacanatvāt prakārasya ca śiṣṭaprayogānusāritvāt dvicandre api pātrādiṣu draṣṭavyaḥ dvau candrau yasmin darśana iti bahuvrīhiḥ ekacandraśabdasyādvigutvād eva caodyābhāvaḥ sā ca pañcaparvā avidyāḥ sā viparyayavṛttir avidyā paṇca parvaṇi asyā iti kāni punas tānīty āhāvidyā asmitā ityādi ata eva avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ svasaṇjñabhiḥ svābhiḥ śāstrāntaraprasiddhābhis tama ādisaṃjñabhiḥ viśiṣṭāḥ vittamalaprasaṅgenābhidhāyiṣyante dvitīyapāde idānīṃ vikalpaṃ darśayati śabdajñānānupātī vastuśūnyo vikalpaḥ śabdasya jñānaṃ śabdajñānam vācyavācakaniyamena sādhvasādhuśabdajñānaṃ tad anupatituṃ śīlam asya iti śabdajñānānupātī vastuśūnya iti yathāvācyārthaśūnyāḥ yasya śabdasya jñānam anupatati tasya śabdasya yathābhūtābhidheyena śūnya iti yāvat yathā bhūtārthavyatirekeṇa hi vikalpanaṃ vikalpaḥ tasya hi śabdajñānānupātitvād āgamāntaḥpātitvaṃ prāptam ata āha sa na pramāṇopārohīti na pramāṇāntaḥpātī vastuśūnyatvāt na hy āgamasya śabdajñānānupātitve api vastuśūnyatā yataḥ śābdārth viṣayā vṛttir āgamaḥ vikalpas tu vastuśūnyatvān na pramāṇam kiñ ca vaktṛśrotroś ca tulyo vikalpaḥ dvayor api śabdād uccaritād vikalpeaiva hi buddhir jāyate na tathā āgame śrotur eva hy āgamaḥ vaktā tu dṛṣṭānumitārthaḥ kiñ ca nirvitarkasamāpannasya vikalpo nirvartate nāgamaḥ tasmānnityā na pramāṇopārohī yady evaṃ vastuśūnyatvād viparyayāntaḥpātitvaṃ prāptam ata āha na viparyayopārohīti kutaḥ śabdajñānānupātitvāt na hi vastuśūnyatve api viparyayaḥ śabdajñānam apekṣate yataḥ viparyayo mithyājñānam atad rūpapratiṣṭham ity uktam pramānapariddhedyapratyayaṃ pratyariguṇabhūtatvāc ca vikalpasya na hi yathā sarveṣāṃ viparyayo virodhād bādhyate tathā vikalpaḥ pramāṇapratyayaguṇabhāvād eva tasmād vastuśūnyatvagrahaṇena śabdajñānānupātitvagrahaṇena ca parasparasaṃbandhena pramāṇaviparyayābhyāṃ pramāṇaviparyayagandhamātrānuliptam api bhinnaṃ vikalpākhyaṃ vṛttyantaraṃ darśitam tadvadgandhānulepanād eva tad ānantaryeṇa vikalpasyārambhaḥ nāpi smṛtitvam smṛteḥ kevalānubhūtāspadatvāt atha na tv īdṛśī cittavṛttiḥ prasiddhā na hi svabhāvaṃ kiṃcid vṛttinimittam iti ced āha vastuśūnyatve api śabdajñānamāhātmya mātra nibandhano vyavahāro dṛśyata iti mātragrahaṇaṃ śabdajñānavyatiriktakāraṇābhāvakhyāpanārtham kva dṛśyata iti ced āha tadyathā caitanyaṃ puruṣasya svarūpam iti citiśaktir apariṇāminīty uktatvād caitanyam eva puruṣaḥ tad eva ca svarūpam iti vyatirekābhāvād vyatirekopanibandhano vyapadeśo na syāt puruṣasya caitanyam iti tathā cemam evārtham upaśritya śabdavidā vārttikakāreṇoktam siddhaṃ tu vyapadeśivadbhāvād iti tathaivehāpi yathā sati vyatireke caitrasya gaur iti tadvad eva caitanyaṃ puruṣasya iti na hi yathā gor anyaś caitro vyapadeśahetuḥ tathā citer arthāntaram puruṣo sti yena vyapadiśyeta nāpi citiḥ puruṣārthāntaram vyapadiśyeta tathā api vyatirekasaṃbandhaviṣaye bhavati caitanyaṃ puruṣasya svarūpam iti vyapadeśe vṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhavastudharmeti vastuno dharmo vastudharmaḥ pratiṣiddho vastudharmo sya iti pratiṣiddhavastudharmā dharmād anic kevalāt itivacanāt samāsāntaś cintyasamādhiḥ vastuśabdena sattvādiguṇā ucyante teṣāṃ dharmāḥ pratiṣiddhā asya iti na hi pratiṣiddhāḥ sattvādidharmāḥ pratiṣiddhatvād evāsya puruṣasya sambandhino bhavanti yena te puruṣeṇāsya iti vyapadeśyeran tad abhāvamātram eva tu tatrārthaḥ tathāpi yathā citrā gāvo sya iti vyapadeśe buddhiḥ tathā pratiṣiddhā vastudharmā asya iti vyapadeśe buddhiḥ nirgatā kriyā asmād ity atrāpinirgatir apāyaḥ apāyaś ca sambandhapūrvaḥ yathā caitrān nirgatā kriyā na ca evaṃ puruṣe kriyāyā asambhavān nirgatih puruṣāt sambhavati tathā api niṣkriyaḥ puruṣa iti vyapadeśe bhavati vṛttiḥ tathā nutpattidharmā puruṣa iti na vidyate utpattidharmo sya iti pūrvavad eva atra svayam evārtham ācaṣṭe bhāṣyakāraḥ utpattidharmasyābhāva jñāna mātram ava matra gamyate yathā nirguṇo nirañjano niṣkala ity evam ādīny apy udāharaṇāni ātmaviṣayānekodāharaṇapradarśanam ātmatattvanirdhāraṇārthatvāt tiṣṭhati bāṇa iti lokaprasiddhodāharaṇapratipādanam aprasiddhyāśaṅkānivṛttyartham tiṣṭhatīti gatinivṛttir gatyabhāvaḥ na cābhāvasya kālatrayayogo bhavati nāpi bāṇasya kriyānirapekṣasya dravyasya nāpi cābhāvena gatinivṛttyā bāṇasya vastunaḥ sambandhaḥ tiṣṭhati bāṇaḥ sthāsyati sthitaḥ ity evaṃ trīṇy udāharaṇāni gatinivṛttau dhātvartha iti nanu gatinivṛttir eva dhātvarthaḥ tatra kathaṃ gatinivṛttāv ity ādhāraḥ ata evodāharaṇāntaram etat asati vyatireke ādhārādheyabhāvasyābhāvāt asti ca gatinivṛttau dhātvartha iti vyapadeśe śabdasāmarthyasamutthāpitā buddhir ādhārādheya bhāva sambandhāv almbinī tasmād itthaṃ jātīyaṃ vikalpa viṣayam anekam udāharaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam nidrākhyāṃ vṛttim idānīm ācaṣṭe abhāvapratyayālambanā vṛttir nidrā jāgradviṣayatvāt prāg uktasya vṛtti trayasya tadupamardena ca nidrāsamudbhava iti tad anantaraṃ nidrākhyā vṛttir vyākhyāyate abhāva iti jāgradviṣayābhāvaḥ na tv atyantābhāva eva tatra pratyayānupapatteḥ abhāve pratyayaḥ abhāvapratyayaḥ sa eva ālambanaṃ yasyāḥ sā vṛttir abhāvapratyayālambanā sā nidrā suṣūptāvasthā nanu ca svapnāvasthā Pi nidrā eva na eṣa doṣaḥ svapnanidrājñānālambanaṃ vā iti sūtrakāreṇa bhedena upadiṣṭatvāt iha suṣuptāvasthā eva nidrābhipretā kiṃ cābhāvapratyayālambanatvāc ca suṣuptam eva na hi svapnasyābhāvapratyayālambanatā smṛtitvāt smṛteś cānubhūtaviṣayatvāt tathā bhāṣyakāraḥ svapne bhāvitasmartavyā iti smṛtitvaṃ darśayati kiñ ca svapnasya cittavṛttitā svasaṃvedyeti nāśaṅkā eva upapadyate tathā ca cittavṛttitām āśaṅkyāha sā tu ca sam prabodhe pratyavamarśād ity ādi tasmāt pratyayaviśeṣo nidrā na hy asati pratyayaviśeṣe parāmarśo yaktaḥ asti cāyaṃ prabuddhasya pratyavamarśaḥ sukham aham asvāpsam ityādiḥ pratyavamarśo nāma kim apy anvabhūvam iti pratyayālocanā nānubhavābhāve sā bhavet nāpi tadviṣayāḥ smṛtayo yuktāḥ nidrāyā apratyayatve prajñāṃ viśāradīkaroti manaḥ manasaḥ kartṛtvaṃ satyānaṃ stimitam akarmaṇyam gurugurūṇīti prakāre guṇavacanasya iti dvir vacanaṃ guruprakārāṇi alasaṃ muṣitam iva mallenāpahṛtam iva etāni pratyayānubhavakāryāṇi na syuḥ kāś cana smṛtayaḥ kānicit kāryāṇi kecana pratyavamarśāḥ tad etat trayam api bhāṣyakāropanyastaṃ pratyayaviśeṣatva evopapadyate kiñca garbhagṛhādiṣu cādṛṣṭabāhyanimittānām asati viśeṣe ciram ahaṃ suptavān kṣiptam iti ca parāmarśo nyathā na yujyate nanu ca nātra smṛtayaḥ smṛtīnām anvabhavam ity evaṃ viśiṣṭatvāt na hi suṣuptād utthitoviśeṣaṃ smarati atrocyate bālasya iha janmany ananubhūtastanyasambandhasya janmānantaram eva tasyābhilāṣo dṛśyate na ca sa svābhāvikaḥ abālānāṃ smṛtipūrvapravṛttidarśanāt tathā ihāpi tasmāt pratyayapūrvakaḥ suṣuptotthitasya gātragauravādi kāryaṃ duḥkhādy anubhavapūrvaṃ gātrādiviṣayagauravādikāryatvāt prasiddhaduḥkhānubhavagārtagātragauravavad iti pratyayaviśeṣo nidreti siddham smṛtim idānīṃ vyācaṣṭe anubhūtaviṣayāsampramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ smṛteḥ pramāṇādisarvavṛttikāryatvād ante niveśaḥ anubhūtaś cāsau viṣayaś cānubhūtaviṣayaḥ yo asāvānandamahodanvattaraṅgāyamāṇaḥ anubhūtaḥ sa eva viṣayaḥ na punar yo viṣayaḥ sa evānubhūta iti tathā ca smṛter aśabdāditvāt smṛtiviṣayāyāḥ smṛter asmṛtitvaṃ prāpnoti iti iṣyate ca smṛtivisayā api smṛtiḥ svasaṃvedyatvāt anubhūtavisayasyāsaṃpramoṣo napaharaṇam atiro bhāvaḥ pārokṣye api sādṛśyādinimittāpekṣayā anubhūtasya viṣayasya dṛśyamānavad avabhāsaḥ smṛtiḥ tatra pratyayasmaraṇayor visayākārāvabhāsāviśeṣāt kiṅkṛtas tayor bheda iti tad vivekaṃ pradarśāyitukāma āha kiṃ pratyayasya cittaṃ smaratītyādi yady apy anubhūtānubhūyamānaviṣayatvena vivekaḥ tathāpi sādṛśyanimittāṃ bhrāntiṃ tayoḥ kāryakāraṇatvapradarśanāya nirvaratayati etad eva ca vaināśikānāṃ bahir arthānupapatter buddhikāraṇam kiṃ pratyayasya smaratīti karmaṇy ubhayatra ṣaṣṭhī cittaṃ smaratīti puruṣakartṛtvaṃ nivārayati smṛtipratyayayor ekakartṛtvapradarśanārtham na hi puruṣasya pratyayakartṛtvaṃ smṛtikartṛtvaṃ vā dṛśyatvāt pratyayānām dṛśyānāṃ ca svātmātiriktadṛśyatvaṃ ghaṭādivad iti vakṣyāmaḥ kiñcātaḥ yadi viṣayasya smarati pratyayasyāpi viṣayaviṣayatvād anarthāntaraṃ smṛtiḥ pratyayāt atha pratyayasya smarati tadā tv idam ayuktam anubhūtaviṣayāsampramoṣa iti tadā hy anubhavāsampramoṣa iti syāt tatrāha grāhyoparatktaḥ grāhyo viṣaya ālambanam tena uparaktaḥ lākṣādyuparaktas phaṭikavat grāhyagrahaṇobhayākāranirbhāsaḥ grāhyasya ca ghatādeḥ pṛthubudghnādyākāreṇa svena cāvabhāsarūpeṇopajāyamānatvād ubhayanirbhāsaḥ sa ca pratyaya utpadya vinivartamānaḥ svāśraye pratyayini saṃskāram ādadhāti sa ca saṃskāraḥ kāraṇānuvidhāyitvād ubhayā pāta kāra eva svavyañjakāñjana iti saṃskārādhyinaḥ pratyayasya hetubhūtaṃ yat karma dattaphalaṃ tattulyajātīyaṃ yatkarmāntaraṃ phalapradānāyābhimukhībhavati tat svavyañjakam tathā ca vakṣyati tatas tadvipākānuguṇānām evābhivyaktir vāsanānam iti tatkarma pratyupanītaṃ vā sādṛśyapraṇidhānādi svena vyañjakenābhivyajyata iti svavyañjakāñjanaḥ grāhyagrahaṇātmikāṃ smṛtiṃ janayati anyathā tadvyañjakasya karmaṇo vipākānupapattiḥ tatra grahaṇākārapūrvā buddhiḥ grahaṇam svī karaṇaṃ svīkaraṇam eva pūrvaṃ prathamam utpdyamānasya pratyayasya na hi viṣayaviśeṣam apekṣate pūrvam iṣṭāniṣṭagrahaṇāt nirbhagnaghaṭapradīpavinirgataprabhā jālavat grāhyākārapūrvā smṛtiḥ anubhūtāpekṣatvāt yadi ca grhaṇapūrvikā smṛtiḥ pratyayavad abhaviṣyat anubhūtaṃ nāpaikṣiṣyata apekṣate tu tasmād grāhyo viṣayaḥ pūrvo syā na grahaṇam tathāpi tūbhayātmikā eva smṛtisaṃskārayor ekarūpatvāt nāpy anyatarapratyākhyānena sambhavati tathā cānubhūtaviṣayāsampramoṣa ity upapadyate smṛtipratyayayor api amāna viṣayatvāt grahaṇatvasya ca sarvatra sambhavāt tasmāt pakṣadvaye apy abhihitadoṣo na dṛśyata iti sā ca dvayī katham hāvitasmartavyā bhāvitaṃ paraniṣpannaṃ asakṛdbhāvitatvāt yathā dravyāntareṇāsakṛdbhāvitaṃ tailādi asakṛdbhāvitatvād eva praṇidhānādiprayatnāntaraṃ nāpekṣate bhāvitaṃ smartavyaṃ praṇidhānādiyatnāntarā na pekṣayā yasyāḥ sā svapne bhāvitasmartavyā jā gṛ grat samaye tv apekṣate praṇidhānādiyatnāntaram iti tadviparītā sarvāś ca pramāṇādivṛttipañcatayānubhavād udbhavanti sarvāś ca etāḥ sukhādyā rasattvādyā tmikāḥ tadātmakaś ca saṃsāraḥ sukhaduḥkhamohāś ca kleśeṣu vyākhyātāḥ sūtrakāreṇa sarvaṃ duḥkhaṃ vivekinaḥ iti hi vakṣyati taddhānaṃ ceha vivakṣitam tasmāt sukhaduḥkhamohātmakatvāt niroddhavyā vṛttayaḥ kiñca āsāṃ nirodhe samprajñāto vā samādhir bhavaty asamprajñāto vā atha āsāṃ nirodhe ka upāya iti upāyaṃ pravedayati abhyāsavairāgyābhyāṃ tannirodha iti abhyāsavairāgye vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇe tābhyāṃ yathā uktalakṣaṇānāṃ vṛttīnāṃ nirodhaḥ viroghāt nirodha upaśamaḥ abhyāsavairāgyayor viṣayavivekapradarśanārtham etadbhāṣyam cittanadītyādi cittena nady eva saṃsāriṇaḥ satataṃ viṣaye pariṇīyante saṃsāraprāg bhārā saṃsārāvasānā samudrāvasāneva khilīkriyate pratibadhyata iti uddhāṭyate pravartyate uddhāṭaḥ kriyata ity uddhāṭyate anyathā mitvāt ghaṭādayo mitaḥ iti hatu mitāṃ hnasvaḥ iti syāt evaṃ ubhayatantra ity arthaḥ tatrābhyāsasvarūpam pratipādayiṣyann āha tatra sthitau yatno bhyāsaḥ tatra tasmin nirodhe sā ca nimittasaptamī nirodhanimittā cittasya yā sthitiḥ yatnasya phalabhūtā tasyā nimitto ttabhūto yo yatnaḥ so bhyāsaḥ tathā ca āha avṛttikasya praśānta paṅkakara ṅga ñjasyevābhyāsaḥ praśāntavāhitā prasannarūpata ya pariṇāmo niruddhavṛttikasya cittasya yatno vīryam abhyutsāha iti paryāyāḥ sthitisaṃpipādayiṣayā yamaniyamādiyogasādhanānuṣṭhānam abhyāsa iti sa tu kathaṃ sthirībhavatīty ata āha dīrghakālanairantaryasevitaḥ dīrghakāla tv avarjito vā nairantaryavarjito vā na dṛḍhabhūmir bhavaty abhyāsaḥ tasmād ubhayor api viśeṣya viśeṣaṇatvam eva saṃskārāsevita iti tv abhyāsa eva viśeṣyate dṛḍhabhūmir ity asya vyākhyānaṃ vyutthānasaṃskāreṇeti vyutthānajena saṃskāreṇa drāg iti sahasā nābhibhūyate vairāgyapratipādanārtham āha dṛṣṭānuśravikaviṣayāvitṛṣṇasya vaśīkārasaṃjñā vairāgyam viṣayaśabdaḥ pratyekam abhisaṃbandhyate vitṛṣṇaya iti ca drṣṭaviṣaya Vitṛṣṇasya ānuśravikaviṣayavitṛṣṇasya ceti dṛṣṭaś cāsau viṣayaś ca tasmin kaḥ punar asau striyo nnaṃ pānam aiśvaryam iti vyaktyapekṣayā śabda ādīnām ānantye api rāgaprabalatvam eteṣv atitarām iti stryādigrahaṇaṃ prādhānyāt atra hi prabalataro rāgaḥ sa prayatnatareṇa niṣeddhavyaḥ evam ānuśravikaviṣayaḥ ānuśraviko nāma āgamika iha sa ca svargādiprāptyānubhavanīyaḥ prakṛtilayagatabhogyo vaidehyāprāptāv upabhogyaś ca nanu ca vaitṛṣṇyam eva vairāgyam tathā rāgas tṛṣṇā garddhaḥ iti hi vakṣyati nāvasthā viśeṣasya vivakṣitatvāt tathā ca yatamānasaṃjñā vyatikrāntasaṃjñā ekendriyasamjñā vaśīkārasaṃjñeti catasṛṣṇām āsāṃ sāmānyasaṃjñā vairāgyam iti evaṃ sati dṛṣṭanuśravikaviṣayavitṛṣṇasya ity etad uktaṃ bhavati abigatapūrvāvasthātrayasya caturthīṃ yā avasthā sā tv iha vairāgyam iti vivakṣitaṃ tasmād iha vaitṛṣṇyād anyavairāgyam abhipretam tathā ca darśayati viṣyadoṣadarśinaḥ doṣadarśanasya viṣayanicṛttihetutvāt tad guṇadarśanaṃ hi rāgakāraṇam prasaṃkhyānabalāt tad doṣadarśanābhyāsabalāt anābhogātmikā viṣayavyatikarātmikā divyādivyayoḥ samprayogo api heyopādeyaśūnyā rañjanāvamuktasyeva sphuṭikasya viṣayarāgavimuktasya cittasyāvasthānam vaśīkārasaṃjñā vaśīkartuṃ śakyante syām avasthāyāṃ sarve gauṇāḥ padārthāḥ vaśīkartavyatvena saṃjñāyante vaśīkṛtāni ca tasyām avasthāyām indriyāṇi saṃjñāyante vaśīkaraṇaṃ vā saṃjñāyate syām iti tac ca dvividham paraṃ cāparaṃ ca viṣayanimittabhedena aparaṃ vyākhyātam adhunā param ucyate tat paraṃ puruṣakhyāter guṇavaitṛṣṇyam tad iti vairāgyaṃ parāmṛśyate param iti pūrvoktavairāgyād uttarakālabhāvīti yadi vā tasya viṣayanimittāmhuām utkṛṣṭanimittaviṣayatvāt kaivalyasya vā pratyāsannataratvāt param utkṛṣṭam kiṃ nimittam asya ity āha puruṣakhyāter nimittāt kiṃ viṣayam ity āha guṇavaitṛṣṇyam iti kuṇeṣu sattvādiṣu vaitṛṣṇyam dṛṣṭānuśravikaviṣayadoṣadarśīti pūrvavairāgyanimittaviṣayaparāmarśanam asya viṣayanimittabhedavivekārtham puruṣadarśanābhyāsāt nimittāt tacchuddhipravivekāpyāyitabuddhiḥ tad iti puruṣadarśanaṃ parāmṛśyate tasya śuddhiḥ tacchuddhiḥ nirṇiktakleśādimalatvam atha vā tasya puruṣasya śuddhis tacchuddhiḥ tacchuddhes tadālambanadarśanaṃ pravivicyate tat pravivekenāpy āyitā buddhir asya yoginaḥ guṇebhya iti viṣayapratipādanam pūrvas tu dṛṣṭānuśravikaviṣayebhyo api viraktaḥ eṣa tatkāraṇebhyo guṇebhya eva vyaktāvyaktadharmakebhyaḥ mahadādisaṃsthitā vyaktadharmakāḥ pradhānāvasthitā avyaktadharmakāḥ tebhyo virakta iti tat dvayaṃ vairāgyaṃ pūrvam idaṃ ca tatra yad uttaraṃ puruṣadarśananimittaṃ guṇaviṣayaṃ tajjñānaprasādamātram puruṣadarśanasya eva paraḥ praviveka iti yāvat puruṣadarśī hi heyopādeyaśūnyacitto bhavati tad āha prasṃkhyāne apy akusīd asya sarvathā vivekakhyāter dharmameghaḥ samādhiḥ iti yasya udaye yasya vairāgyasyodaye pratyuditakhyātiḥ pratyutpannadarśanaḥ evaṃ manyate prāptaṃ prāpaṇīyam ity ādi etasya hi nāntarīyakaṃ kaivalyaṃ tataḥ paraṃ sādhanānapekṣatvāt vairāgyasya jñānaprasādamātratve jñānavairāgyayor ananyatvāt tadviparītayoś ca rāgājñānayor anarthāntaratvam eva siddham evaṃ sati rāgo apy avidyāyā evāvasthāntaram iti pañcaparvā avidyety upapannam bhavati nanu ca evaṃ buddher aṣṭaguṇatvaṃ bādhyeta ṣaḍ guṇatvaṃ hi dhyānāvasthābhedābhyupagamāt jñānatve api vairāgyasya prasannataratvābhyupagamaḥ rāgo apy ajñānasyāvasthāntaraviśeṣaḥ nanu ca evaṃ sati jñānājñānayor anekāvasthābhedād aṣṭaguṇatvaṃ punar api na prāpnoti na eṣa doṣaḥ phalavattvapratyanīkatvaniyamāt jñānāvasthācatuṣṭayasya phalavattvena bhedaniyamaḥ tathā ajñānāvasthācatuṣṭayapratyanīkatvenādharmādicatuṣṭayaniyama ity aṣṭaguṇatvasiddhiḥ dharmādipratidvandvina eva hi guṇatvena niyamyante nājñānabhedāḥ sarva eva uktaṃ purastāt samprajñātaḥ samādhir vitarkādy anugata ity upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāmaḥ iti so vasaraprāpta idānīṃ lakṣyate upāyadvayena niruddhavṛtteḥ vairāgyadvataṃ parāparatvena vyākhgyātam abhyāsasyāpi dvitvaṃ sāmarthyād avasīyate katham viśiṣṭam asamprajñātasamādher abhyāsaṃ sūtreṇa eva vakṣyati virāmapratyayābhyāsapūrvaḥ iti tena sālambanaviṣayaḥ pūrvābhyāsa iti niścīyate vakṣyati ca tatpratiṣedhārtham ekatattvābhyāsaḥ iti bhāṣyakāro apy avadīt vairāgyeṇa viṣayasrotaḥ khilīkriyate vivekadarśanābhyāsena kalyāṇasrota uddhaṭyate iti nāvocata vṛttisvarūpatiraskāram eva samprajñātasamādheḥ vṛttinirodhaprabhavatvam aniṣṭaviṣayapravṛttyuparamottarakālabhāvitvāpekṣayā vṛttiviṣayaviśeṣānugata eva hi saḥ tathā ca dvitīyasūtre samprajñātasya nirodho na lakṣaṇam iti vyākhyātam ataḥ pūrvokt Bhyāsavairāgyopāyadvayena niruddhavṛtteś cittasya katham ucyate kathaṃ lakṣaṇam ucyata iti yāvat vitarkavicārānandāsmitārūpānugamāt samprajñātaḥ anugamaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ saṃbandhanīyaḥ vitarkānugamād vicārānugamād ānandānugamād asmitārūpānugamād iti rūpaśabdo mātrārtho vitarkādipūrvadharmatrayavarjitatvakhyāpanārthaḥ vitarkaś cittasyālambante sthūla āmogaḥ sthūla api miśrī bhāvaḥ prathamam ālambanākāreṇa pariṇamamānasya cittasya ya ālambanavyatikaraḥ sa vitarkaḥ sūkṣmo vicāraḥ āmogaḥ sūkṣma iti saṃbandhaḥ ānando hlādaḥ vicāraḥ sūkṣmatara ābhogas tṛtīyaḥ sānandatā viśeṣaḥ ekarūpātmikā saṃvid asmitā svasyāṃ prakṛtāv asmitāyāṃ samāpannasyāsmitā pratyayamātratā ekarūpātmakatvam tathā codāhariṣyati tam aṇum ātmānam anvavaityāsmīty etāvat saṃjānīta iti nanu cāsmitā kleśeṣu paṭhiṣyati dṛgdarśanaśaktyor ekātmatevāsmitā iti tat katham ivāsmitārūpeṇa kleśena samādhir anugamyata iti satyam evaṃ prakṛṣṭasvakāraṇākārāvabhāsakatvād anyaviṣayavinivṛttātmakatvāc cāsmitāyāḥ mamādhirūpatve apy adoṣaḥ yadi vā asmitārūpasyālambanasyāvisyātve api na yogipratyayasyāvidyātvam na hi khalu paracittavividiṣāyāṃ parasyāvisyātvam na hi khalu paracittapratyayaṃ gṛhṇan parakīyāvidyāpratyayarūpālambanadoṣeṇa svayam avidyāvān bhavati yaḥ punaḥ kleśaḥ sa viparyayaviśiṣṭa eva yathā ahaṃ gacchāmi kṛśo ham iti yogicittasya tannyagbhūtaṃ rajastamasī iti na tathā tatra pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ svakīyottarottaradharmānugataḥ paraḥ paras tu pūrvapūrvadharmavikalaḥ yasmāś ca etad dharmacatuṣṭayānugata evāyaṃ samprajñātaḥ samādhid tasmād etal lakṣaṇa iti lakṣaṇārthaṃ sūtram loke api yo yad asādhāraṇadharmānuyātaḥ sa tal lakṣaṇaḥ yathā sāsnādilakṣaṇo gaur iti asmitāmātragrahaṇān nirālambanatām eṣāṃ samādhīnām mā kaścid āśaṅkiṣṭety āha sarva ete sālambanā iti yaḥ punar manyate nirvikalpatvam asmiteti tat asataḥ asmitāśabdasyāhaṅkāre prasiddhatvāt tathā ca āha asmibhāvo smitā athāsamprajñātaḥ yogaś cittavṛttinirodha ity upapāditalakṣaṇaḥ kim upāyaḥ kiṃ sādhanaḥ kenopāyenopetya ity arthaḥ kiṃ svabhāvaḥ kiṃ svarūpaḥ kim avastha iti svabhāvaviśiṣṭasādhanasaṃbandhapradarśanārtham āha virāmapratyayābhyāsa pūrvaḥ saṃskāraśeṣo nyaḥ virāma pratyayābhyāsapūrva ity etāvatā sādhanasambandham ācaṣṭe saṃskāraśeṣa iti tu svabhāvavyākhyānam anya ity anantaroktalakṣaṇāta samprajñātād anyo ayaṃ nirbījaḥ asamprajñātaḥ anya ity ubhābhyāṃ saṃbandhyate virāmapratyayābhyāsapūrvaś ca saṃskāraśeṣaś ca ko sāv ubhyaviśiṣṭa ity āhānya iti viramaṇaṃ viramaḥ virāmaś cāsau pratyayaś ca virāmapratyayaḥ virāmarūpatvāt sa eva pratyayo virāma ity ucyate sarvaviṣayebhyo vinivartamānasya vinivartanakāle prāg apratyayāpatteḥ pratyayarūpatvam etad yathā pāvakasya jvalataḥ prakṣīyamāṇedhanasya śanaiś śanair upaśāmyataḥ prāg aṅgāratāpatter jvālātmakatā tasmād virāmarūpaḥ pratyayo virāmapratyayaḥ tasyābhyāsaḥ pūrvo mukhyaṃ yasya saḥ virāmapratyayābhyāsapūrvaḥ saṃskāra eva śeṣo yasya sa saṃskāraśeṣaḥ pratyayoparame tu pratyayasaṃskāra evāvaśiṣyate viṣayapratyayebhya uparataṃ cittaṃ saṃskāraśeṣam eva ity arthaḥ tasya paraṃ vairāgyam upāyaḥ tasya samādheḥ param uttaram nanu ca paraṃ vairāgyaṃ ceti vaktavyam abhyāsavairāgyābhyām vṛttinirodhasyābhipretatvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ virāmapratyayābhyāsasya sūtropāttatvād anāśaṅkyas tadabhyāsaḥ vairāgyaṃ punar anupāttatvād āśaṅkyeta tasmāt tad eva prapayatā na canirmokṣaḥ caḥ paṭhitaḥ yady evaṃ kasmān na sūtra eva vairāgyagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam pūrvatra paṭhitatvāt tatra kim arthaṃ paṭhitam iti cet vairāgyaprasaṅgāt pūrvavairāgyaviśeṣa evottaraṃ vairāgyam iti prasaṅgād uttaram duktam pūrvasya ca vairāgyasya samprajñātaviṣaye pi viniyogād aviśiṣṭya parasya sādhanatvād anyaviṣayatvāc ca nirbījena eva sambandha iti na sūtre vairāgyagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam sāmarthyaprāptaṃ tu bhāṣyakāro darśayati abhyāsavairāgyābhyām tannirodha iti hi pratipāditam sālambano hy abhyāso viruddhatvān nirālambanasya samādheḥ sādhanatvāya na kalpata iti nirvastuko api virāmapratyayo nirālambanasamādhyanurūpatvād ālambanīkriyate tasmāt tadabhyāsavairāgyopāyapūrvakaṃ cittaṃ nirālambanam abhāvaprāptam iva bhavati sa eṣa nirbījaḥ saṃskāraśeṣasvabhāvaḥ samādhir asamprajñāta iti sa khalv ayaṃ dvividhaḥ saḥ nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ upāyapratyayo bhavapratyayaś ca upāyena pratīyate prāpyata ity upāyapratyayo yogināṃ bhavati yady api videhā api yogina eva tathāpi yamādiyogasādhanānuṣṭhāyino bhipretāḥ teṣāṃ śraddhāvīryādy upāyalabhyaḥ samādhiḥ videhaprakṛtilayānāṃ tu janmanā eva labhyaḥ te hi tanutarapratibandhāvaśeṣāḥ sa tu pratibandhāvaśeṣas teṣāṃ sakṛdāsāditapunarjanmanāṃ samādhivyāghātāya na paryāpnoti sa tu janmapratilambhamātranimittam tvāt jñānavairāgyādyanuṣṭhānakāryatvād videhaprakṛtilayatvasya tad anuṣṭhānas ity arthasūtram īdṛśāṃ hi tadanusṭhānamāhātmyam yad uta sāmarthyādivaikalyād amhīṣsitaphalānavāptāv api mahanīyataraṃ videhaprakṛtilayatvaṃ prāpyate videhā nāma devāḥ puryaṣṭakaśarīropabandhāḥ te svasamskāramātropbhogena vairāgyābhyāsāhitaḥ samskāraśeṣas tanmātropabhogena cittena kaivalyam ihānubhavanta iti sattvaguṇavinirbhogāt tathājātīyaka svasaṃskāraparipākaṃ kṣpayanti prakṛtilayāḥ sādhikāre aparyavasitā dhi kāre yāvad dhi na kṛtā guṇapuruṣāntarakhyātiḥ tāvad aparisamāptādhikāram eva cittaṃ tasmin prakṛtlayāpanne kaivalyam ivānubhavantīti pūrvavat yāvan na punar āvartate dhikāravaśāt vidyākartavyatāvaśāt tāvad anubhavanti kaivalyam iva yeṣām upāyapratyayo yogināṃ teṣāṃ śraddhāvīryasmṛtismādhiprajñāpūrvakaḥ samādhiḥ śraddhā nāmāpavargaprāptau tat sādhanaśravaṇe ca katakaphalasaṃparka iva salilasya cetasaḥ samprasādaḥ saṃprasattiḥ sa hi jananīva kalyāṇī yoginaṃ pāti rakṣaty aśubhebhyaḥ tasya hi vivekārthinaḥ samyagdarśanārthino vīryam utsāha upajāyate yogasādhanānuṣṭhānaṃ prati sañjātavīryasyāgamajñānādiviṣayā dṛḍhatarā smiṛtir upatiṣṭhate vivekārthina iti sarvatrānuṣajyate dṛḍhasmṛtyupasthāne ca cittam anākulaṃ samāḍhīyate samāhitacittasya prajñāyā buddheḥ viviktatā sarvārthaprakāśanasāmarthyam ta thā t viśinaṣṭi yena yathābhūtam ātmādhi vastu jānātīti tad abhyāsāt etad uktaṃ bhavati ātmadarśanavirāmapratyayābhyāsād iti tad viṣayāc ca vairāgyā khyād viṣayā t parasmād vairāgyād iti asamprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ iti te api śraddhādisādhanā nava nupa yogino bhavanti tad darśayati tad yathā mṛdupāyo madhyopāyo dhimātropāya iti teṣām ekekas tridhā bhidyate tatra mṛdupāya iti sādhanānuṣṭhānaṃ prati mandopakramo madhyopakramaḥ tīvra tīvrasaṃvegoakrama iti evam itaratrāpīti nātra tirobhūtam t tatrādhimātropāyānāṃ tīvrasaṃvegānām āsannaḥ samādhilābhaḥ samādhiphalaṃ ca teṣām api mṛdu madhyatīvropāyakramatayā viśiṣyamāṇatvāt tato api viśeṣaḥ sādhanānuṣṭhānasaṃskārasya tadviśeṣād apy uttarasya samādhilābhaḥ pratyāsīd aitarām etad asya sūtrasya prayojanam yogasādhanānuṣṭhānaṃ prati yoginaḥ katham upabṛṃhitotsāhā bhaveyur iti yathā loke drutataraṃ sīmāntaṃ pari prati dhāvatām etat phalaṃ bhavatīti tadvat atha vā mandamandetaropakramāṇām api yoginām abhimataphalāvāptiprakāśanād anavasannacetasaḥ pravarterann iti itarathā tīvratarāyāsajanitabhītayo vasīdeyur iti kim etasmād eva āsannataro bhavati atha tasya asya lābhe bhavaty anyo api kaścid upāyo na vā iti upāyāntaram astīty āha īśvarapraṇidhānād vā īśvaraśabdārthm uttaratra vyākhyāsyati praṇidhānam iha vyācaṣṭe bhaktiviśeṣād āvarjita iti anugrahaṃ praty abhimukhībhāvam āpāditaḥ taṃ bhaktyatiśayayoginaṃ yoginam abhidhyānamātreṇa parama īśvaratvād eva nirāyāsatayā satyasaṃkalpatvāt anugṛhṇāti tadanugrahād api pratyāsannataraḥ samādhilābhaḥ phalaṃ ceti atha pradhānapuruṣavyatiriktaḥ ko yam īśvara iti sāṃkhyaśāstre prasiddhyabhāvād īśvarasadbhāve ca upapattim avaśyam anavagata īśvaraviśeṣo vā pṛcchati tatra tāvat pratijānīte kleśakarmavipakāśayair aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaviśeṣa īśvaraḥ kleśā iti avidyā ādayaḥ kleśayantīti kleśāḥ tat pūrvānuṣṭhitāni kuśalākuśalāni karmāṇi kuśalāni cākuśalāni ca kuśalakuśalāni cety ekaśeṣaḥ kuśalākuśalānīti yāvat tatphalaṃ vipākaḥ jātyāyurbhogalakṣaṇaḥ ta eva kleśādaya nirvāṇāc cherata iti kleśakarmavipakā āśayāḥ yadi vā kleśādīnāṃ rāśayaḥ kleśakarmavipakāśayāḥ te manasi vartamānā manovṛttiprabhavatvāt puruṣe vyapadiśyante kasmāt sa hi tat phalasya bhokteti yathā rājani jayaparājayau yuddheṣu vartamānāv apadiśyete tat phalaṃ rājasaṃbandha iti yo hy anena bhogenāparāmṛṣṭa iti ucyate na kālavivakṣā upalakṣaṇarthatvaṃ na parāmṛśyate nāpi parāmṛkṣyate nāpi parāmṛṣṭa iti kleśakarmavipakāśayāsaṃbandhī ndhayogī ty arthaḥ sūtrārthaviśuddhiṃ kurvann āha kaivalyaṃ prāptas tarhīti kleśādy aparāmarśasya kādācitkatayā api saṃbhavāt santi bahavaḥ kevalinaḥ kiṃ tadī te pī śvarā iti parāmarśasyāpi saṃbhavān na ta ekāntena kleśādibhir aparāmṛṣṭāḥ parāmarśāparāmarśau hi staḥ teṣām īśvaratvaparāmṛṣṭa eva na hy anavadhṛtaḥ śabdārtho lakṣaṇatvenopādeyaḥ aparāmṛṣṭa iti tasmād ya ekāntenāparāmṛṣṭa ity ucyate te hi trīṇi bandhanāni prākṛtavaikṛtadākṣiṇāni samyagdarśanena hitvā kaivalyaṃ prāptāḥ īśvarasya tu tatsaṃbandhaḥ kleśādisambandho na bhūto yathā muktasya pūrvā bandhakoṭer muktvopapatter eva jñāyate bandhapūrvikā hi kuktiḥ nāpi bhāvī yathā prakṛtilīnasya tasya hy anārabdhasaṃsārasya uttarā bandhakoṭiḥ sambhāvyate pravṛttasaṃsārasya cāprakṛtilīnacittasya sā samā adhikāratvāt pūrvottarabandhakoṭī sambhavataḥ tad idaṃ sarvam atrāparāmṛṣṭa iti kālāvivakṣāpradarśanārtham sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvaraḥ tatra puruṣaviśeṣa īśvara ity uktatvāt īśvarasya puruṣasyānaiśvaryadharmatvāt cittasya caiśvaryadharmatvāt niratiśayaiśvaryasya ca prakṛṣṭacittasambandhāpekṣatvāt prāptam evottarārtham anuvadati yo śau prakṛṣṭasattvopādānād īśvarasya śāśvatika utkarṣa iti nityaniratiśayasarvajñānāiśvaryaśaktisampattir utkarṣaḥ tatra pratijñāviśuddhyarthaṃ praśnapūrvam upakramate sa kiṃ sanimitta āhosvin nirnimitta iti nimittaśabdaḥ kāraṇaparyāyaḥ sa kiṃ sakāraṇa āhosmin niṣkāraṇa iti kiñcātaḥ yadi tāvat sakāraṇas tadā sadā eva īśvara ity ayuktam anityatvāt atha niṣkāraṇaḥ tathā ca utkarṣasya kāryatvād asattvaprasaṅgaḥ na hi niṣkāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ dṛśyate loke atrocyate na niṣkāraṇaḥ śāstranimittatvāt śāstraṃ jñānam śāstrasya hetutvāt yataḥ satvaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ nityaṃ dravyasvabhāvasādhyasādhanavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭāspadam yady evaṃ jñānasyānyato dhigamapūrvatvāt prāg anutkarṣaḥ prāpta ity ata āha śāstraṃ punaḥ kiṃ nimittam iti yadi svābhāvikaṃ jñānaṃ mattonmattajñānavad anutkarṣahetutvam atha punaḥ sanimittakaṃ nimittāt prāg anutkarṣa iti manyate na tāvan nirnimittam yataḥ prakṛṣṭasattvanimittaṃ prakṛṣṭasattvāśrayam iti yāvat ata eva svabhāvajñānadoṣābhāvaḥ kiñ ca svābhāvikajñānatve api na mattādijñānavad apakarṣahetutvam nityamuktakleśādisattvāśrayatvāt tatra yathā eva jñānasaṃskārasmṛtiprabandhānām anyonyanimittanaimittikabhāvena bījāṅkurvad anādisaṃbandhaḥ tathā eva śāstraprakarṣayor īśvaracetasi nityapravṛttaprabandharūpeṇa pravartamānayor anādyantaḥ saṃbandhaḥ tatrotkarṣo jñanasya kāryam eva jjānam api tasya kāraṇam eva anyeṣāṃ vyākhyānam nimittaśabdaḥ pramāṇavācī tasya śāstraṃ nimittaṃ pramāṇam tena hi tadutkarṣaḥ pramīyate śāstraṃ punaḥ kiṃpramāṇakam īśvaranirmalasattvapramāṇam viśuddhasattvapraṇītatvād dhi śāstrasya prāmāṇyam yathā manvādīnām tathā ca śrutiḥ yakiṃcinmanur abhyavadat tad bheṣajam iti yathā ca loke guruṇā bhihitam iti etayoḥ śāstrotkarṣayoḥ pramāṇaprameyatayā nirādyantaḥ sambandhaḥ nanu ca naiva īśvarasattve ā vartamānena śāstreṇacitta tadutkarṣaḥ pramīyate na eṣa doṣaḥ tat prabhavatvāt tatra vartamānam varta māna ta eva tat prabhavam api śāstraṃ tasmin sarvajñatvād eva loke api yato yat prabhavati vartate tat tasmin yathā tantvādiṣu paṭādi tat prabhavatvam anumānāgamābhyām avagamyate śāstrapramāṇakaḥ utkarṣaḥ īśvarapramāṇakaṃ śāstram iti bhinnāśrayatvāc chāstrotkarṣayor netaretarāśrayatvam nanu ca śāstrād īśvaraprāmāṇyaṃ tat prāmāṇyāc ca śāstraprāmāṇyam iti syād anyonyāśrayatvam usyate īśvaraprāmāṇyasyānumānena siddhatvād adoṣaḥ etasmād etad bhavati kasmāt īśvaraprakṛṣṭasattvāśrayayor niratiśayajñānotkarṣayoḥ kāryakāraṇarūpe prabandhanityayayā nityatvād etad bhavati sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvara iti ity atrāha tac ca tasyaiśvaryaṃ sāmyātiśayavimuktam iti vakṣyamāṇapramāṇaphalam etatsūtrapiṇḍārtho vā atiśayavimuktatāṃ vyācaṣṭe na tāvad aiśvaryāntareṇā tadatiśayyate kutaḥ yad evaiśvaryāntaraṃ tadatiśayānaṃ manyase tad eva ta aiśvaryaṃ mayā bhihitam yatraivaiśvaryāntarātiśayi bhavaty aiśvaryaṃ sa eva īśvara iti yāvat na ca tatsamānam aiśvaryam asti samāndadharmaprakarṣāsaṃbhavāt na hy ekasmin rājye dvayoḥ sabhavo rājñoḥ ekasya vā dve rājye tathā pratipādayati tad dvayos tulyatvaṃ prasaktam na hy ekasyānyataratra prākāmyam abādhitvā anyatarasmin pravṛttir upapadyate dvayoś ca yugapad ekārthayor ekasya prākāmyeṇa pravṛttir eva nāsti prakāmite vastuni samānaprakarṣasyārthasya viruddhatvāt yena ca samānaprakarṣatā tasya tena eva sa bādhyate te ca tac ca na vācā bādhanam itarasya rūpātiśayā āvṛttyatiśayāś ca viruddhyante sāmānyāni tv atiśayaiḥ saha vartanta iti vakṣyāmaḥ tasmād yasya sāmyātiśayaviproṣitam aiśvaryaṃ sa īśvara iti pradhānapuruṣavyatiriktaḥ pūruṣaviśeṣa īśvaraḥ siddhaḥ yathāpratijñātasya īśvarasya siddhau pramāṇam upanyasyate tatra niratiśayaṃ sarvajñabījam tatra tasmin yathāpratijñātalakṣaṇa īśvare niratiśayaṃ bhavitum arhati kiṃ tad iti yad idam avyabhicāri pratyakṣānumānajñānam atītaviṣayaṃ anāgataviṣayaṃ vartamānakāla pratyutpanna viṣaya m atītādisamuccayaviṣayam atīndriyaviṣayaṃ ca atīndriyayor atītānāgatayoḥ saṃbhavād atīndriya grahaṇa m ity ucyate tac cātīndriyagrahaṇaṃ trividham sūkṣmaviṣayaṃ vyavahitaviṣayaṃ viprakṛṣṭaviṣayañ ca alpaṃ bahv iti yathāprasiddham etad vivardhamānaṃ sātiśayatvena sarvajñabījaṃ yathā dhūmavijñānam agnivijñānasya katham yatra prakarṣakāṣṭhāṃ pratipadyate jñānasya jñātrāśrayatvāt yatreti jñātā ucyate yasmin jñātarīti sa sarvajñaḥ siddhaḥ tathā śaktir api sātiśayatvena vivardhamānā yatra kāṣṭhāṃ prāpnoti sa sarvaśaktiḥ tena jagannirmāṇasthāpanopasaṃhārādikartṛtvasiddhiḥ tathaiśvaryasyāpi vardhamānasya yatra kāṣṭhāprāptiḥ sa parama īśvaraḥ tataś cāśaktyādiviparyayadoṣābhāvasiddhiḥ athāpi syāt ajñānasyāpi vivardhamānasya svabhāvasiddhasya kāṣṭhāprāptasya tasminn īśvare siddhir iti na jñānavirodhāt na hi jñānājñānayor viruddhayor ekasminn abhisaṃyogo sti na hi jñāne prakarṣavati tatrājñānaṃ saṃbhavati yatra hi jyotir vivardhate tatra tamo pakṛṣyata eva viparyayo pīti cet tac ca na sati jyotiṣi tamaso nupalambhāt vidyamānaṃ hi tamo jyotiṣā tiraskriyate na kadācid vidyamānaṃ jyotis tamasā abhibhūyate yad api jaladharoparodhāt prāvṛṣi sveradarśanam tad api dṛṣṭavyavadhānamātram na punaḥ prakāśa eva torodhīyate tamovat tasmānnityā
