na yatra jñānavivṛddhis tatrājñānasya bhāvaḥ samitarīva tamasaḥ nityātyantatirohitarajas tamo guṇasattvopādānāt kiñ ca nājñānasyāvastuviṣayatvād vivṛddhiḥ saṃbhavati jñānasya jñeyavastuviṣayatvād abhivṛddhyupapattiḥ ajñānasya hi vastuviṣayatve jñānatvaprāptiḥ yaś cāpi sthāvarādhiśv ajñānaprakarṣa iti nāsau prakarṣaḥ atyantajñānābhāvāpekṣayā hi sa ucyate ajñānasya prakarṣe hi saty ajñānasahasrasya na jñānena ekena bādhaḥ syāt tathā dā hi pratyajñānaṃ jñānentpannenānekena bādhanaṃ syāt tasmānnityā nājñānasya prakarṣaḥ sverūpeṇa yasya hi sātiśayatvaṃ tasya kāṣṭhāprāptir dṛśyate yathā phalādiparimāṇānām ākāśaparyantatā tathā sarvajñabījam api parāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ prāptum arhati samastaṃ vyastaṃ ca sarvaṃ vastu jātam ekasya pratyakṣaṃ jñeyatvāt ghaṭādivat jñānaviṣayatvena puruṣārthatvāt ghaṭādivad eva utpattimatī ca pṛthivī sāvayavatvāt ghaṭādivat prāṇikarmatatsādhanavibhāgavideka gadhaika niṣpāditaṃ jagat tadupabhogyasthānādiracanāviśeṣavattvāt prāsādādivat anekaprāṇyupabhogavijñānavad ekanirvartitā pṛthivī anekaprāṇavadupabhogyatvāt brīhiyavādivat anekaprayojanārthinā ekena nirmitā pṛthivī gṛhādivad eva sarvaprāṇyāśrayo girinadīsamudāyaḥ tannivāsaparibhoga yogyavijñānavad ekakuśalotpāditaḥ prakṛtahetunidarśanābhyām eva anekaprāṇabhāk prakāśādisāmarthyajñānavatā ekena nirvartitaḥ savitā prakāśātmakatvāt pradīpādivat niyatakālam ādityodayāstamayādisañcaraṇam etat prayojanajñānavad ekaprayuktaṃ pratiniyatakālatvāt kṛṣyādivat budhimad eka īśvaraprayuktā sūryagrahacandranakṣatrādipravṛttiḥ pravṛtter duḥkhātmakatve sati niyatasamayatvāt dharmaśiṣyabhṛtyādipravṛttivat candramaso vṛddhikṣayau tithyādikālajñānavataikenaprayuktau kālaparicchedakatvāt ghaṭikā harā divat kalaparicchedajñānavataikena nirvartataś candramāḥ vṛddhikṣayayuktatvāt ghaṭikādivad eva buddhimad ekasvāmikaṃ jagat anyonyaviruddhasaṃhatānekaprāṇināyakādhiṣṭhitabahu maṇḍalatvāt itthaṃjātīyakaikarājyavat sarvam etat sādhanasādhyavyāpārāvasthaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kasyacid ekasyāvāntaravirodhānugrahavattayā ekaprayojanatvāt sāṃgrāmavastuvat saṃhatatvāt kulālādivastuvat sā eva pratijñā yugapac ca sarvaṃ pratyakṣam eka ta syānekatve tva saty anyonyasaṃbandhāt prasiddhasambandhānekārthavat agnihotrādisādhanasādhanīye kasyacit pratyakṣe sādhyasādhanarūpatvāt bhujitṛptivat sarvāḥ śaktayaḥ kasyacit pratyakṣāḥ vastutvāt ghaṭādivat a vā ntaraprativbandhābhāve sarvaṃ vastu jātaṃ nairantaryeṇa kasyacit pratyakṣaṃ śabdādimattvena sambandhāt drāghīyasīm iva śaṣkulīṃ bhakṣayataḥ śabda ādayaḥ svatantratayā kenacid ekena sarvaṃ pratyakṣaya upalabhyate jñeyatvenābhimatatvāt nāṭyavastuvat apratibandhena kasyacit pratyakṣopalabhyaṃ sarvam aneka sattve tve saty anyonyasaṃbandhāt nāṭyasaṃbandfinartakādivat saṃsārarahitaḥ sarvajñaḥ ajñānābhāvāt muktātmavat kleśādirahita īśvaraḥ apratibandhajñānatvāt siddhayogivat etena kleśādipratibandhājñānarahitatvena cakṣur ādīndriyagrāmanirapekṣasarvaviṣayajñānatvaṃ siddham sarvārthagrahaṇasamarthasya parama īśvaracittasya sarvavyāpino yugaptsarvaviṣyayogitvāt evaṃ sati samastavastugrahaṇābhāve kāraṇābhā vānu vopapatiḥ nāpi mūrtimatpratibandho apy ākāśavad eva sarvaviṣayayogino api cittasya viṣayānāvasthānād āvir bhāvatiro bhāvasmṛtisaṃkalpānavasthitatvopapattiḥ viṣayākāratayā vṛttilābhād arkaprabhāvat na hi kleśādyāvaraṇāvaddhannaṃ cittasattvam tasyādharmādiyogāt sarvagatasya sarvārthasyāpi sattvasya adharmādipratibandhakaniruddhasvakīyapravṛttimārgatvād indriyādidvārāpekṣitvam upapadyate yathā apavarakādyāvaraṇāvṛtaḥ pradīpas tadāvaraṇagatacchidradvāreṇa bahiḥ prakāśayati sa eva tu pradīpaḥ prabhinnāpakarakāvaraṇaḥ sannanapekṣya tat tacchidramārgaṃ samantataḥ prakāśayati tathā eva īśvarasattvam kleśādyāvaraṇayogābhāvād asati viṣayaviśeṣanirodhikāraṇe yugapad aśeṣārthagrahaṇam tatac ca svātilaṅghanānatilaṅghanādidoṣābhāvaḥ sarvasya viṣayatvāt sarvam eka īśvaraṃ jagat paripālakāpekṣasthānādyādyanekavastu viśeṣatvāt prasiddhaivaṃbhūtaikarājyavat tathā niyatasthitihetvanekopakaraṇatvāt anyonyābhibhavanīyaprabhūtataradurgayuktānekadeśatvāt abhaṅguravyavasthaśarīrabhedavattvāc ca pratītaivaṃvidhaikarājyavat anekakartṛbhoktṛkriyāsādhanaphalasaṃbandhaviśeṣajñānavad upadiṣṭāni varṇāśramādyanuṣṭhānāni phalārthibhiḥ pratyavāyabhīubhis taiś cānuṣṭhīyamānatvāt bhaiṣajyarasāyanādyanuṣṭhānavat tathā tadupadeśāḥ parārthatvāt upadeśatvāt vidvacchradveyatvāt upadeśād ṛte manuṣyānavagamyārthatvāc ca bhaiṣajyādyupadeśacat śarīrendriyāṇi sarvatatprayojanavid ekanimittakāraṇābhinirvartitāni niyamakriyāsthitihetusādhanatvāt prāsādagṛhadāruyantrādivat niyataprayojanaracanāvattvāc ca tadvad eva tathendriyāṇi karaṇatvāt vādīvṛkṣādānādivat tathā sarvaṃ kāryaniyatopādānatvāt bhoktrarthatvāt bhogasādhanatvāc ca ghaṭādivat utpattimattve apy ete hetavaḥ evaṃ madhyamaparimāṇatvāt anekavināśahetusaṃbandhayogyatvāt bhokādhiṣṭhānatvāt kriyāphalasādhanatad rūpādimattvāc ca ādhīyamānāpacīyamānāpūryamāṇāpanīyamānadahyamānābhidyamānānekadeśatvāt vinaśvarī pṛthivī śarīrādivann aśvarāṇi pṛthivyādibhūtāni anyonyanāśakaśaktimattvāt śastrapuruṣādivat tathā eva virodhāt puruṣaviparītatvāc ca utpttivināśadharmakam ākāśaṃ sākṣād upakaraṇatvāt ghaṭādivat bāhyendriyagrāhyaguṇāśrayatvāc ca tasmānnityā niratiśayaśaktijñānāiśvaryaḥ parama īśvaraḥ siddhaḥ atrocyate īśvaraśabdārthaḥ sarvajño na bhavati prameyatvavastutvaśabdābhidheyatvātmatvasādhanāpekṣopalabdhṛtvādibhyaḥ asmadādivat īśvaraśabdo api niratiśayajñānayuktābhidhāyī na bhavati śabdatvāt ghaṭādiśabdavat sarvajñasarva īśvaraśūnyaṃ jagat anekaprāṇivyapāśrayatvāt anyonyaviruddhanekanāyakarājyavat bhūtabhaviṣyatkālayor apīdānīm iva sarvajñasyānupalabdhāraḥ sarvaprāṇinaḥ prāṇitvāt asmadādivat vādyantarapaikalpitaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraś ca nāsti anupalabhyamānatvāt śaśaviṣāṇavat tathā asarvajño nīśvaraś cāśarīratvāt muktātmavat saśarīraś ced dharmādyapekṣaśarīratvaṃ tathā ca saṃsāritvam asmadādivad eva aśarīratvam eva iti cej jagatkartṛtvānugrāhakatvādyanupapattiḥ muktātmanidarśanena viśiṣṭaparibhoga yogyajagad racanā viśeṣopapattiḥ svabhāvād eva kaṇṭakatīkṣṇatvakumudakamalasaṅkocavikocādivat niśākaradivākaratārakādigamanāgamanādy api svābhāvikaṃ lohāyaskāntamaṇivat atrābhidhīyate svābhāvikī tāvan na bhavati pṛthivyadiracanā dṛṣṭānto na eva tatsādhanasya vidyate kaṇṭkādīnāṃ ca taikṣṇyaṃ na svābhāvikam abhyupeyate agnyādīnām iva ūṣṇyādi svabhāvo vastu dharmatvād dhetoḥ pṛthivyādiracaneti cet prāsādādiracanāyā vastudharmatvāt syād anaikāntikatvam atha svābhāvikatvād iti cet asiddhatvam jagadracanāyā dharmādharmaphalopabhogārthaprayuktatvābhyupagamāt kartṛdharmādharmāstitvam upariṣṭāt sādhayiṣyate tasmāt pṛthivyādiracanā svābhāvikī na bhavati prāṇyupabhogārthatvāt prāsādādiracanāvat candrādipravṛttir na svābhāvikī pravṛttitvāt asmadādipravṛttivat asmadādipravṛttir na svābhāvikīṭicet nāgnyuṣṇatvavan nityatvaprasaṅgāt na hy agnyuṣṇatvaṃ svābhāvikaṃ san niyataṃ nimittam ātmalābhāya kāṅkṣati dharmisattāvyatirekeṇa kriyāphalaracanā ādīnāṃ tu viśiṣṭanimittākāṅkṣṇam ātmapratilambhāyeti na svābhāvikatvam niyatanimittakāṅkṣṇam api prāsādādiracanānāṃ svabhāva iti cet astu tathāvishasvabhāvatvam tathā api pṛthivyādiracanāyā niyatanimittakāṅkṣṇasvabhāvatvaṃ prāsādādivad eva tataś ca nāmni vipratipattir na doṣāya kārkāntarāpekṣatvād iti pratijñā pratirūpakāriṇī ca bhavadbhir uktani anumānāni lokānumāgamavirodhāt apramāṇāni anumānavirodhaṃ tāvat sātiśayatvādibhyo brūmaḥ āgamavirodhañ ca yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvavit eko vaśītyevamādibhyaḥ samācakṣmahe samastalokavirodhaṃ cāpi sarva evā nārogopālaṃ saṃvyavaharamāṇāḥ satataṃ śivanārāyaṇādināmnā praṇihitacetasaḥ pratiṣedhasv api saṃbhinnabuddhiṣu akarṇīkṛtatatpratiṣedhaviṣayapallavāḥ parama īśvaraṃ praṇatam ūrdhānaḥ kusumānjaliprabhṛtibhir arcayanti phalaṃ cāpi tata eva prārthayante atha ced brūyāt sarvajñābhāvapratipādibhir asmadanumānair itarapratijñānāṃ vridha ity atrocyate na etāny anumānāni katham prathamaṃ tāvat pratijñāiva duṣṭā yadi tāvad īśvaraśabdārthaḥ sarvajño na bhavatīti yuṣmadabhipreta īśvara ucyeta tathā ca siddhasādhyatā syāt athāsmadabhipretaḥ tathāpi yuṣmākam asiddhaviśeṣyatā bhavet atha īśvaratvasyāsarvajñatvam ucyate tathāpi siddhaṃ sādhyate tathā eābhyupagamavirodho api katham aiśvaryasarvajñabījatvayor vivardhamānatvāt kāṣṭhāprāptiḥ parimāṇavad evābhyupagamanīyā tathā kāṣṭhāprāptaiśvaryasarvajñatvavācināv apīśvarasarvajñaśavdāv eṣitavyau kāṣṭhāprāptiś ca niravadhikatvam yathā parimāṇādīnām ātmākāśādyanantaparimāṇāntatvam tathā cānumānābhyupagamasvavacanavirodhāḥ syuḥ kiñcānyat kāṣṭhāprāpta īśvaratvasya śabdārthasya parityāge śabdārthavādaḥ prāpnoti na hi śabdaḥ parityaktābhidheyaikadeśa uccaritaḥ atha parimāṇāder api niravadhikaniṣṭhatvaṃ neṣyate siddhāntavirodhaḥ ātmākāśādīnāṃ hi sarvagatatvābhāve madhyamaparimāṇatvānityatvādidoṣaprasaṅgāś ca athāpy ātmanaḥ sarvatra kāryadarśanāt sarvagatatvam tatrāpi śakunyādyātmanāṃ manuṣyagocarākāśādigatatvaṃ kena vāryate athānumānavirodhān nāvadhāryata iti cet ātmādīnām api prameyatvavastutvadibhyaḥ pṛthivyādivad ity anumānavirodhodbhāvanā śakyate kartum vaktum na ca tāvatā trānumānavirodhitvam anumānābhāvaprasaṅgāt tathā anumānābhāva eva iṣyata iti cet pratyakṣe apy anāśvāsaḥ syāt atha niścīyamānabuddhyutpatteḥ pratyakṣapramāṇatvam anumānasyāpi tarhi niścitabuddhisamudhbhavād astu prāmāṇyam atha dṛṣṭasambandhadhūmadiviṣayam evānumānam iti cet tatrāpy anumānābhāva evānagniḥ dhūmavān predeśaḥ pratyakṣānupalbhyamānāgnisambandhe sati pradeśatvāt agniśūnyopalabhyamānapradeśavad iti atha pramāṇāntarasaṃvādadṛṣṭasambandhaviṣaye numānasyānumānatvam ucyate pratyakṣam api pramāṇāntarasaṃvādāt brahma om iti brahma ityādayaḥ smṛtayaś ca oṃ tat sat iti oṃ viśvaṃ viṣṇuḥ ityādayaḥ oṃ śabdasya kṛdantaṃ yanmāntam ityavayayatvād vibhaktinivṛttiḥ kim asya saṅketakṛtaṃ vācyavācakatvaṃ atha pradīpaprakāśavad asthitam iti kiṃ cātaḥ yadi tena bhagavatā anyair vā saṃvyavahārārtham asya nāmedam astv iti saṃketitam tato asya prāg oṃśabdāvācyatvād oṃśabdena vā praṇidhātāraḥ prāṇyadhiṣatānyena vā nāmāntareṇādhītavantas tathā idānīm apy astu kim oṃkāraviśeṣavacanenāthāpi pradīpaprakāśavad avasthitaṃ tathāpi prathamaśravaṇo pīśvara upalabhyeta yathā prakāśena savitā kiṃ ca saṅketo apy anarthakaḥ sthitasambandhanatvāt athāpūrvaṃ saṅketyeta pūrvoktadosaprasaṅga iti manyate atrocyate sthito asya vācyasya vācakena sambandho yadi nityaḥ śabdo yadi vā anityaḥ saṅketas tu tam eva sthitaṃ sambandham avajvalayati nanu ca uktaṃ sthitaś cet prathamaśravaṇe api taṃ pratīyur iti ucyate na hi pratyāyyaprattyāyakasambandhaḥ śabdārthayoḥ sthito api sann indriyeṇa gṛhyate yathendriyārthayoḥ apratyakṣe hi vācyavācakaśaktī tataś ca yena udyate śabdād artho numeya iti tad asat sambandhāgrahaṇāt paraprayogavyaṅgyatvāc ca sambandhasya na hy anumānaṃ paraprayogam apekṣate atha brūyād anumitāt sambandhād arthānumānam iti sa vaktavyaḥ katham anumitah śabdārthasambandhaḥ iti sa cet brūyāt kāryadarśanād arthaṃ hi pratītya paścād anuminoti tatsaṃbandham yathā cakṣuṣā rūpam upalabhya cakṣursambandham iti sa prati vaktavyaḥ siddhā tarhi vinā numānena śabdād eva pratipattir iti yo hi grāṣṭrapākena eva kṛtārthaḥ kiṃ tasya kilośipākena athāsakṛt prayogadarśanād gṛhyate sambandhaḥ yathā agnidhūmayor iti cet na tu brūmaḥ na hi sahasreṣv api prayogeṣu pratyakṣeṇa śabdārthayoḥ sambandho gṛhyate yathā agnidhūmayor ādāv api sambandho gṛhyate vākye apy ayam eva tasmād avasthitam eva vācyasya īśvarasya vācakena praṇavena sambandham avadyotayati saṅketo yathā sthitaṃ pitāputrasambandham saṅketopayāpekṣatvāt prathamaśrutān nārthaḥ pratīyate yathā cakṣusa ālokābhāve nanu ca śabdānityatvapakṣe katham anitye sambandhani nityaḥ sambandha iti na hy anityayor ajju ghaṭayoḥ sambandho nityah syāt ucyate yathā pramāṇaprameyayor indriyaviṣayayoś ca kriyākārakāṇāṃ sambandhaḥ sthita evānityeṣv api sambandhiṣu tadvad atrāpi sthita evāvyabhicāreṇa sambandhaḥ sargādiṣv api vācyavācakaśaktyapekṣaḥ saṅketaḥ yathā eva rūpacakṣuṣor grāhyagrāhakaśaktyapeksayā eva sargādau sargas tathehāpi vācyavācakaśaktyapekṣayaiva saṅketaḥ kriyate sampratipattinityatayā vṛddhaparamparayaiva gamyagamakabhāvena śabdārthayoḥ sampratipattinityā nānyathety āgamino vedavādinaḥ pratijānate sampratipattiś ca śabdārthasambandhasya hetus tadeṣām tad etad yuktaṃ bhavati yady āgamipakṣaḥ syād athānyapakṣaḥ sarvathā sthita eva sambandhaḥ pitāputrayor iva saṅketenābhivyasyata iti vācyavācakayor asthitasambandhatve tu praṇavarūpeṇābhimukhībhavatīśvara iti nāvakalpate na hi pācyapācakasambandhe na ca sthite pācakāgnyupādānaṃ pākārthaṃ kalpate sthite tu vācyavācakasambandhe bhavavadārādhanasādhanasya praṇavasyopādānabhavakalpata iti tatpratipādanārthaṃ sarvaṃ bhāṣyam evam avagatavācyavācakasambandhasya yoginaḥ parama īśvaraprasādanaṃ kathaṃ kriyata iti tadartham āha tajjapastadarthabhāvanam tasya īśvaravācakasya praṇavasyārdhacaturmātrasya trimātrasya vā japaḥ manasā upāṃcu vā āvartanaṃ japaḥ tadarthasya ca īśvarasya praṇavena vācakena samarpitasya buddho samāropitasya bhāvanam abhidhyānaṃ tadarthabhāvanam kartavyam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ tad evam ubhyaṃ kurvato yoginaḥ cittam ekāgraṃ sampadyate ekāgrasampattiṃ ca tadārādhanaphalaṃ darśayati tathā ca uktam svādhyāyād yogamā tiṣṭhet sīta svādhyāyāt praṇavajapād īśvaraṃ pratyavanatadittaḥ san yogam āsīta tadartham īśvaraṃ dhyāyet rasyayat tadarthadhyānāc cāpracalitamanāḥ svādhyāyaṃ praṇavam āmanet manasā bhijapet manaso bhijapaḥ praśasyate dhyānasyāsannataratvāt mā viṣayapravaṇacitto bhūt iti evaṃ svādhyāyayogasampattyā tadvirodhinā pratyayāntareṇānabhighātaḥ svādhyāyayogasampattiḥ tayā ca praṇavajapaparama īśvaradhyānasampattyā para ātmā parameṣṭhī prakāśate yogina iti kiñcāsya bhavati pūrvasūtre cittam ekāgraṃ sampadyata ity uktam ekaṃ phalaṃ tadapekṣayā kiñceti cakāraḥ kiñcānyad apy asti phalam āhosvic cittaikāgratvam eva iti tatrāha tataḥ pratyakcetanādhigamo apy antarāyābhāvaś ca tataḥ tasmād īśvarapraṇidhanāt pratyakcetanādhigamaḥ pratyak svabuddhiṃ detayata iti pratyakcetana ātmā tasyādhigamo yathāvat svarūpasaṃvedanam nanu cādhigata eva pratyātmaṃ puruṣo haṃ sukhī duḥkhī cāham iti evaṃ prasiddhaṃ tataḥ kiṃ viśeṣaṇocyate iti satyam evam kiṃ tv aviśiṣṭo sau pratyayaś sittasya vṛttyā kiñ ca sukhī duḥkhī cāham iti sukhaduḥkhisāmānādhikaraṇyād ihāhaṃ pratyayasya cittavṛttiviṣayatvād avidyapratyaya eva prasiddhiḥ katham tadhy adhihama ity āha yathāiva īśvaraḥ puruṣaḥ śuddhiḥ kleśādimalavarjitas tata eva prasannaḥ svaśśhas tata eva kevalo nistriguṇas tata eva nirupasargas tāpatrayavarjitaḥ prakṛṣṭasattvapratisaṃvedī ca tathā yam api madīyaḥ puruṣaḥ śuddhaḥ prasannaḥ kevalo nirupasargo buddheḥ pratisaṃvedīty avagacchati yathā tathā iti ca dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikanirdeśād īśvarakṣetrajñayor bheda ukto bhavati buddham uktopapatteś ca pradhānasya pārārthyopapatteḥ kṣetrajñānāṃ cāta eva parasparabhedaḥ kiñ cāsya bhavati ye tāvad antarāyā vyādhiprabhṛtayo vakṣyamāṇās te api cāsya īśvarapraṇidhānān na bhavanti tatra ke te ntarāyāḥ kiyanto vā ity āha vyādhis tyānetyādi saṃkhyayā tāvan navāntarāyāḥ svarūpeṇa ca vyādhyādayaḥ vyādhir dhātur asakaraṇavaiṣamyam dhātavo vātapittaśleṣmāṇas teṣāṃ viṣamabhāvo vaiṣamyaṃ tac ca vātapitaśleṣmabhūyiṣṭhadravyopayogādibhyo jāyate svayoyāgame hi dhātūnāṃ vṛddhim ācakṣate rasa upayuktāharasya pariṇāmaviśeṣaḥ sa ca saptadhā rasakāryatvād rasa ity ucyate rasalohitamedomāṃsāsthimajjāśuklākhyaḥ tasya vaiṣamyaṃ vṛddhikṣayau karaṇavaiṣamyamandhabadhiratvādi styānam akarmaṇyatā cittasya stimitam saṃśayaḥ sthāṇur vā puruṣo vā iti viruddhobhayakoṭismṛk pratyayaḥ pramādaḥ samādhisādhanānām abhāvanam aśīlam ālasyaṃ kāyasya cittasya ca gurutvād apravartanam aviratiś cittasya viṣayasamprayogasvabhāvo viṣayasamprayoganimitto vā garddhaḥ abhikāṅkṣā tṛṣṇā bhtāntidarśanaṃ viparyayajñānaṃ yogasādhaneṣu tanmārge vā viparītavṛttiḥ alabdhibhūmikatvaṃ samādhibhūmer alābhaḥ bhūmayo vitarkādayaś cittasya dharmaviśeṣā uktā vakṣyamāṇāś ca anavaritāyām api samādhibhūmau tataḥ katham api pracalitasya cittasya punar atrāvasthitatvam eva syāt tadalābhas tv anavasthitatvam ucyate tad ete navāntarāyāḥ antaraṃ vivaraṃ vicchedaṃ kurvanta āyāntīty antarāyāḥ vikṣepāḥ pratipakṣāḥ yogaprāpter upasargāḥ ete ca saha cittavṛttibhir bhavanti cittaṃ vikṣapanti viṣayeṣv iti cittavikṣepāḥ kṣiptaṃ te kṣipanti sahaite vṛttibhiḥ paścatayībhir anyonyaprayojakabhāvena bhavanti atheṣām abhāve vyādhiprabhṛtīnām abhāve sahāyavalābhāvān na bhavanti pūrvoktāḥ pramāṇādayaś cittavṛttayaḥ tad bhāvabhāvitvāt tulyapratyanīkā vṛttivikṣepā ity uktaṃ bhavati duḥkhaṃ yenābhihatāḥ prāṇinas tadapaghātāya prayatante ceṣṭante tac ca trividham ādhyātmikam adhi ātmanīty adhyātmam tatra bhavam ādhyātmikam tac ca śarīraṃ mānasaṃ ca śārīraṃ dhātuvaiṣamyādinimittam mānasam iṣṭavighātādihetukam ādhibhautikam adhi bhūteṣv ity adhibhūtam tatra bhavam ādhibhautikam tac ca paśumṛgādyupanipatitam ādhidaivikam ity adhi deveṣv ity adhidevam tatra bhavam ādhidaivikam adhyātmadibhyaṣ ṭhak ity upasaṃkhyānāt ṭhak anuśatikāditvād ubhayapada Vṛddhiḥ tac cāpi vātavarṣādinimittam tad ekam eva sannimittabhedena rajorūpaṃ bhidyate daurmanasyam icchāvighātāc cetasaḥ kṣobhaḥ ākulī bhāvaḥ saścalanam yad aṅgāny ejayati kampayati tadaṅgam ejayatvam na tac ca prāṇāyāmādy athābhyāsaprabhavaś cāsāvānandamahodanvattaraṅgāyamāṇaḥ api tathā samudbhavaḥ yad bāhyaṃ vāyum ācāmati bāhyavāyor ākarṣaṇabāhulakaṃ lyam niṣkramaṇam andatā ca śvāsaḥ tadviparītavyāpāraḥ praśvāsaḥ yat kauṣṭhyaṃ vāyuṃ nissārayati ete vikṣepasahabhuvaḥ vikṣepaiḥ sahaite vikṣiptacittasya eva bhavantīti vikṣepasahabhuvaḥ samāhitacittasyaite na bhavantīti yāvat yāvad yāvac cetaḥ samādhīiyate tāvat tāvan na bhavantīti tābhyām evābhyāsavairāgyābhyām upaśamayitavyāḥ nānyaṃ pratipakṣam apekṣante abhyāsavairāgye muktvā na hi parameśvarapraṇidhāyinyaḥ bhyaḥ prabhāvo bhavatīti gamyate antarāyābhāvaś cety ukyā prāktanād apīśvarapraṇidhānād antarāyā nirudhyante abhyāsavairāgyābhyām tannirodha ity uktam tatra vairāgyaviṣayaḥ pratipāditaḥ idānīm abhyāsasya viṣayam upasaṃharann āha tatpratisedhārtham ekatattvābhyāsa iti teṣāṃ vikṣepāṇāṃ pratiṣedhāya tat pratiṣedhārtham ekaṃ tattvam ekatattvam tad ca ekaṃ tattvaṃ vastutvānn abhyasituṃ śakyam na hy ātmādivastūnāṃ śilanaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate svamāhābhāgyāvasthitāni hi tāni na cittamātrāṇi vastūnāṃ tu cittatantratāṃ pratiṣedhayiṣyati na ca ekacittatantraṃ vastu ityādinā tasmād etad āśaṅkamāno bhāṣyakāra āha ekatattvālambanaṃ cittam abhyased iti sūtre apy ekatattvābhyāsa iti samāsād ayam artha upātta eva nanu na ekaṃ cittam avasthitam asti yasya ekatattvāvalambanaḥ pratyaya āpadyeta pratyayā eva cittam te ca pratyayaṃ niyatāḥ kṣaṇapraṇāśinac ca pratyātmasaṃvedyaṃ ca pratyayānām anavasthitatvam nāpi pratyayavyatirekeṇāvasthitaṃ pratyayi samānasantatipatitattvāt sād ṛṛśyanibandhanaḥ yathā sa eva pradīpaḥ ta eva keśā iti tad apy āha pratyahaṃ prati pratyayaṃ pratyayī bhinnaḥ pratyayebhyo yuantaparasparabhinnebhyo nanyatvāt eka ekapratyayasvarūpasadvartamānāhaṃ pratyayaviṣayaḥ pratyayī bhūtabhaviṣyatkālāhaṃpratyayaviṣayāt pratyayino bhinnaḥ bhinnapratyayaviṣayatvāt ghaṭat gha paṭa iva yadi vā bhinnakālatvāt vinaṣṭabhaviṣyadghaṭā Bhyāṃ vartamāno ghaṭaḥ iva ahaṃpratyayā sarve bhinnālambanāḥ pratyayatvāt ghaṭapaṭādiviṣayapratyayavad iti atrābhidhīyate svaśāstravirodho api syād evaṃ bruvata ity āha kṣaṇikaṃ ca yasya cittaṃ tasya sarvam eva cittam ekāgram vikṣepābhāvād eva nāsyeva vikṣiptam iti sarvadittaikāgratvād vikṣepaprāptabhāvād vikṣepapratiṣedhāya śāstropadeśo narthakaḥ syāt asti ca cittaparikarmārthaṃ maitryādyupadeśaḥ sa ca virudhyeta itthaṃdharmaṃ cittam abhyupagacchatah nanu ca tavāpi vrttivṛttimator abhedād anupapanno vikṣepa iti tat pratiṣedhopadeśānarthakyam na eṣa doṣaḥ vṛttivṛttimattvābhyupagamāt yadi vṛttaya eva parasparabhinnāḥ vṛttimato tyantabhinnā jāyeran pratyarthaniyatāś ca tata eṣa doṣaḥ syāt na ca evam abhyupeyate kathaṃ tarhi vṛttimad rūpeṇa ekam anekārthaṃ ca tadvṛttnāṃ visayabhedād avasthitaṃ ca sadasator viparyayānabhyupagamād ity evam ātmapakṣe samañjasatāṃ darśayati yadi punar idaṃ cittaṃ vṛttibhedenānekadhā mmilavayāvad dhi prasṛtaṃ sāṃkhyayogavādina iva tavāpi sarvataḥ sarvebhyaḥ viṣayebhyaY pratyāhṛtya pratyanīyaikasminn ātmādyarthe samādhīyeta sthāpyeta tadā bhavaty ekāgraṃ puruṣaprayāsamāvyatvārham ity arthaḥ tato yuktas tat parikarmaṇe śāstropadeśaḥ ato na pratyakṣam ato smāt kāraṇāt tat parikarmaviṣayaśāstropadeśāt sāṃkhyayogavādivat kṣaṇikavādino api ekam anekārtham avasthitaṃ ca cittaṃ na pratyarthaniyataṃ vā paścād abhyupagamanīyam anyathā śāstravirodhaḥ syāt yo api sadṛśapratyayapravāhaṃ cittam ekāgraṃ manyate sadṛśaḥ samānaḥ pratyayapravāho yasya ekasyāṃ santatau tac citam ekāgram tadviparītam asamānapratyayapravāhaṃ vikṣiptam tathā caikāgratā vikṣepapratiṣedhena upapadyate tadarthopadeśaś ceti kutaḥ śāstravirodha iti itara āha na pravāhacittasya ekasya dharmiṇo nabhyupagamāt na hi pravāhacitaṃ nāmaikam atītavartamānabhaviṣyat pratyayānāṃ dharmiṇam abhyupagacchati yadi hy abhyupagacchet parityaktaḥ svapakṣaḥ kasmāt pravāhacittayākṣaṇikatvāt tad evaikaṃ nāsti yasyaikāgratā dharmaḥ pratyayān eva hy anyonyasaṃhatān pipīlikāpaṅktikalpānasāvabhyupagacchati athaivaṃ manyate yady apy ekaṃ nāsti tathāpi sarveṣām eva pratyayānāṃ sadṛśapravāhāṇām ekāgratā dharmaḥ pradīpārciṣām iva prakāśa iti tatrāha nāyugapatkālotpattivināśānāṃ samāhāraḥ sambhavati dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhyavikalatvāt na hi bahvīnām aiciṣām ekaḥ prakāśaḥ pratyarciṣam asya bhedāt na cāpi prakāśasyārciṣāṃ ca eko dharmo nā mā sti athāpi manyate pravāha aṃśasya eva pratyayasya kasyacid ekāgratā dharmaḥ yathaikasyāṃ pipīlikāsantatāv ekā api pipīlikā lohiteti tac ca na pūrvadoṣānuṣakteḥ sarvaḥ pratyayaḥ pravāhāṃśaḥ sadṛśavāhī visadṛśavāhī vā pūrvavat pratyarthaniyatatvād ekāgra eveti vikṣiptacittānava liptiḥ tasmād ekam anekārtham avasthitaṃ ca cittam abhyupagantavyam yadi śāstreṇacittaparikarmopadekṣyate kiṃ ca yadi cittenaikenānanvitāḥ karaṇena svabhāvabhinnāḥ pratyayā jāyeraṃs tadā brūhi katham anyapratyayadṛṣṭasyānyaḥ pratyayaḥ smartā bhaved devadattadṛṣṭasyeva yajñadattaḥ anyapratyayopacitasya vā karmāśayasyānyaḥ pratyaya upabhoktā na hi bhaviṣyat putrā racitakarmāśayaphalaṃ svargādi praty upabhuñjīta atha brūyāt viśiṣṭabhaviṣyat putravijñānārthaṃ vinaśyatpravṛttivijñānam ālayavijñānasaṃskāraṃ kañcanādhatte iti na etad evam ālayapravṛttivijñānayor atyantabhedād avastutvāc ca yady ālayavijñānān na tat pravṛttivijñānaṃ tadā tad eva tad iti nāmamātrabhedaḥ tathā ca saṃskārādhānayuktatvāt smṛtyanupak lptiḥ athāpy anyat evam apy anyatpravṛttivijñānam ālayavijñāne saṃskāraṃ nādadhīta abhinnatvāt yathā santaty antarālayavijñāne kiṃ ca yady api saṃskāram ādhattām tathāpi pravṛttivijñānāpāditasaṃskāram ālayavijñānam deśakālāntarākṣamam tasyāpi kṣaṇikatvābhyupagamād vinaśyac ca tāvaty eva nottaravijñānopkārāya paryāpnoti deśakālāntaravyavahitaṃ ced upakurvītqa tadā bhinnasantānāntarajanmanāpy upakartavyam atha kālāntarāvasthāyi tadā kṣaṇikatvahāniḥ kṣaṇāntaraṃ ced avatiṣṭheta dīrghakālāvasthāyitve kasya syād akṣamā athāpi pravṛttivijñānasaṃskāraviśiṣṭasyāntarālabhāvina ātmasadṛśasya bhavisyata ālayabijñānasya saṃskāram ādhāya pūrvam ālayavijñānaṃ vanaṅkṣyatīti tac ca na saṃskārāntarābhāvāt asti ced anavasthāprasaṅgaḥ atha nāsty ādhāraḥ tatra kiṃ pravṛttivijñānasyālayavijñānakalpanayā saṃskārādhānāya yathā ālayavijñānam utpitsiṣyamāṇasya tatkālam asataḥ ālayavijñānasya saṃskāram ādhatte tathā pravṛttivijñānam api utpitsiṣyamāṇasya tatkālam asataḥ pravṛttivijñānasya eva saṃskāram ādhattām anapekṣyālayavijñānam na ca vinaśyat anyasya bhāvinas tatkālam avidyamānasya saṃskāram ādhatte ity asya dṛṣṭānto dṛśyate nāpi bhāviny eva saṃskāraṃ kurvīta pūrveṇa bhaviṣyatsaṃskriyate bhaviṣyati ceti viruddham tatkālaṃ ced asadbhaviṣyatsaṃskriyate kiṃ tulyātulyasamtatikalpanenāsaṃbandhāviśeṣāt sarvaṃ sarveṇa saṃskriyeta nāpi bhaviṣyadvinaśyator yugapadutpattivinācāv akṣaṇikatvaprasaṅgāt atha tulāntayor iva natyunnatī yugapatpūrvavinācottarasamutpattī syātām na vastunor iti cet nābhyupagamavirodhāt na hi vaināśikenotpattivināśakriyā vytatirekeṇa kārkam anyad iṣyate abhyupagame ca siddhāntavirodhaḥ kiṃ ca kriyākārakayor yāvat kriyā utpatti kārakeṇāvasthātavyaṃ tataś ca kṣaṇikatvahāniḥ ā na vasthāne ca kriyārthaṃ tataḥ tasya upādānam anrthakam kiṃ cānyat kriyāyā eva kārakatve kārakasyāpi kriyātve kriyākārakaśabdao paryāyau syātām tataś cāṅkuro jāyate devadatto jāyata ity aṅkuradevadattoyoḥ paryāyatvaṃ syāt tayor janikriyāmātratvāt athānyajanikriyā devadattaviśiṣṭā anyā cāṅkuraviśiṣṭeti cet abhyupetaṃ tarhi viśeṣeṇa kārakaṃ na h svarūpeṇ akiṃcid viśiṣṭaṃ syāt athocyeta svarūpeṇa evotpattikriyā utpattikriyāntarād viśiṣṭā yathā svalakṣaṇāni rūpādīnīti tac ca na bhāvābhāvayor ekatvaprasaṅgāt ihāṅkuro jāyate naśyaty aṅkura iti ca ya eva jāyate sa eva nācyati tatra aṅkurajananam aṅkuravināśanam iti jananaṃ vināśa ity uktaṃ bhavati aṅkuro hi kriyā eva kārakam iti vocyeta citaḥ athāpi syāt anyā anyasya evāṅkurajananakriyāyā aṅkuravināśakriyā iti tathā apy aṅkurajananasya nityatvaprasaṅgaḥ vināśasyānyatvād eva athāpi nāśajananavad vastu śabalam iti tathā apy abhāvasya śabalatvaṃ prasajyeta katham kriyāvyatiriktasya kārakasyābhāve api nāśa eva jananavināśavān jananam eva jananavināśavad iti na hy abhāvasya śabalatvādiviśeṣo nirviśetṣavād bhāvābhāvayoś cāvirodhāt pratyakṣānumānānupapattiḥ yad apy ucyate tulāntayor nāmonnāāv iti tatra yuktā tulāntayor ekakālayor vidyamānatvād anyatarasya vastvantaragauravanimittā ānatirantarasya connatiḥ iha punar bhavadbhaviṣyatkālayor vijñānayor nāśotpattī tulānāmāhetuvat tṛtīyasya nmittāntarasyābhāvād ekakālaṃ na upapadyete vinaśyad eva vijñānam ātmasadṛśaṃ janayati vināśenākṣaṇatvāt atha mṛtpiṇḍo yathā ghaṭam utpādayan vinaśyati tadvad iti cet tac ca na mṛdavaytavānām eva ghaṭā kāreṇa pariṇatatvāt ekā eva hi mṛtpiṇḍaghaṭādi bahudharmayominī yac cāpi bījeṣu dravyāntaravāsiteṣu vāsakadravyānuvidhāyitvaṃ vāsyadravyasya iti tad apy akāraṇam vāsyavāsakayor avasthitatvāt avasthitāny eva hi bījeṣv aṅkura ādīni vāsyante bījavāsanena tad anyatvāt vāsakadravyasyāpy avayavānanupraviṣṭāḥ sūkṣmā vidyanta eva tasmād vidyamānāny evāṅkurādīni bījavāsanayā vāsyanta iti yuktam asatāṃ śaviṣāṇādīnām utpattyabhāvāt asatāṃ ced utpattiḥ syād vāsyavāsakayor Vinaṣṭatvādf avidyamānatvāviśeṣe vāsakadravyānanuvidhāyi na utpadyeta anyadf vā hastādi yadi vā atyantāsad eva śaśaviṣāṇādyutpadyeta ato viśiṣṭaṃ hi trayāṇām asattvaṃ vāsite bīje tasmād avasthitaṃ kārakaṃ bhūtabhaviṣyatkālānekavṛttiyogi cābhyupagantavyam anyathā pratyayamātraṃ kṣaṇikaṃ cittam iti samarthayamānasya samādhīyamānam api samarthyamānam api gomayapāyasīynanyāyam ākṣipati yathā eva bahūbhir api go vikāratvādihetubhiḥ samīhamāne kṛtāṭopenāpi gomayaṃ pāyasīkartuṃ na śakyam tathā kṣaṇikena cittena smaraṇādi samarthayitum kiṃ ca svātmānubhavāpahnavaḥ cittasyānyatve pratyayamātratve nānyadṛṣṭam anusmaratīti svātmanānubvhūtam apahnuvīta kiṃ tv abadrākṣīr ity ukto dṛṣṭavān api nāham adrākṣam iti bruvīta anyena hi tat pakṣe tat dṛṣṭaṃ dṛśyate tad apahneve cānubhūtasya pratipattiḥ katham yad aham adrākṣaṃ tat aham eva spṛśāmi yad aham asprākṣaṃ tat aham eva smarāmi iti saiṣa pratyayasmaraṇayor ekakartṛtve sati ghaṭanām upaḍhaukate pratipattiḥ anyathā matsadṛśo yad adrākṣīt tat sadṛśo haṃ taṃ smṛśāmīti smarāmīti ca syāt sarvasya puruṣasyāham iti pratyayaḥ smṛtipratyayayor kasmin sati teṣāṃ ca pratyayānām ekasmin kartari pratyayiny abhnne ca upasthitaḥ pratyakṣaś ca nanv ekapratyayaviṣaya evānyaḥ smṛter ekatve api kartur ahaṃ pratyemi smarāmy aham iti ca na bhavitavyaṃ pratyatā smarteti śabdabhedād bheda eva tatrāha na pratyakṣatvāt tad eva darśayati svānubhavagrāhyaś cāyam abhedāt mā aham iti pratyayaḥ atha pratyetā smarteti śabdabhedāt pratyayabhedāc cāhampratyayasya bhinnaviṣayatvam anumāyiṣyata iti ced ata āha na hi pratyakṣāsya māhātmyaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ cakṣuṣo rūpa i Vanumānād abhibhūyate bādhyate kiṃ ca pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam ayam ahaṃ pratyayo na tat smṛtipratyayānām ekasmin kartari sāmānyena vartamānaḥ sa cet pratyakṣapramāṇabhūto numānenābhibhūyeta tadānīm anumānasyāpi pramāṇatvaṃ hīyeta tanmūlatvād anumānasya tad etad āha pramāṇāntaraṃ ca anumānavirodhena ca prativādi pādita pramāṇapratijñā doṣo vyākhyātaḥ atītānāgatapratyayasaṃskārādhārād ananyaḥ idānīntanapratyayasaṃskārḍhāraḥ ekasantānasaṃbandhitve sati bodhātmakatvāt ātmasvarūpād yathā bhūtabhaviṣyatpratyayasaṃskāṛśrayaḥ vartamānapratyayasaṃskārāśrayād anyaḥ ekasantānasaṃbandhen sati bodhātmakatvāt ātmana iva svarūpāt vartamānāhaṃ pratyayī mhūtyabhaviṣyatpratyayibhyām abhinnaḥ ekasantānayoge sati pratyayitvāt yathā svarūpāt vartamānāhaṃpratyayī bhūtabhaviṣyatpratyayibhyām abhinnaḥ ekasantānayoge sati pratyayitvāt yathā svarūpāt bhūtabhaviṣyatpratyayibhyām anyo vartamānaḥ pratyayaḥ ekasantānasaṃbandhe sati bodhātmakatvāt ātmarāgasvarūpādibhya iva bhūtabhaviṣyatpratyayebhyo nānyo vartamānaḥ pratyayī ekasantānasaṃbandhitve sati bodhātmakatvāt ātmano yathā svarūpāt bhinnasantatiṣu parasparasmṛtipratisandhānādyanupalambhād ekasantāneṣu ca smṛtyādidarśanād eva siddham ekakartṛtvam tathā sarvapramāṇebhyo garīyasā pratyakṣeṇa pramāṇena tatra na kiṃcidanumānenasādhyam na hi kaścit karatalalāñchanadidṛkṣayā darpaṇamā datte tathā api vaināśikoparacitānumānāpaśadam asahamānāḥ kecit pratyanumānāni peśalāni darśayanti tathā ca āha tasmād ekam anekārtham avasthitaṃ ca cittam yasyedaṃ śāstreṇacitta parikarma nirdiśyata iti śāstropadeśasambandhitvaṃ cittasyāvasthitatve hetum upadiśati na hi vaiśīyamāṇasya ghaṭasya prakṣālanaparivartanādisaṃskāraḥ kriyate kathaṃ cittaparikarma nirdiśyate tathekatattvābhyāsa iti ca uktam kiṃ ca tad ekaṃ tattvam yadiviṣayo bhyāsa iti tata āha maitrīkaruṇāmuditopekṣāṇāṃ sukhaduḥkhapuṇyāpuṇyaviṣayāṇāṃ bhāvanātac cittaprasādanam iti maitrī mitraviṣayā bhāvanā tādṛśīṃ sukhiteṣu sukham anumodayantīmasūyādivaijitām tathā duḥkhiteṣu karuṇāṃ kṛpām anujānatīṃ duḥkham puṇyātmakeṣu muditāṃ puṇyaśīlatām anujānatīm apuṇyaśīleṣu copekṣām apuṇyaśīlavyāpāreṣūdāsīnatāṃ ca bhāvayed ity anuṣajyate sarvatraivam asya bhāvayataḥ śukla iti viśuddhiḥ prāṇyupaghātādivarjanāc chkulo dharmaḥ tataḥ sa dharma iva jātaś cittaṃ prasādayati tena prasannaṃ cittam ekāgraṃ sthitipadam labhate ekāgratayā samādhīyata ity arthaḥ tad uktam prasannacetaso hy āśu buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate iti tatropekṣāyā ākriyārūpatvād dharmāhetutve sati kim artham iha upādānam ucyate upekṣānupādāne cāpuṇyaśīleṣv api cittaṃ vyāpāraṃ yāyāt tataś ca tacvyāpāropadhānakāluṣyān maitryādibhāvanāyā na yogyaṃ bhavati apuṇyaśīlanimittanaimittikākāravyāpārād adharmo vā mā saṃjaniṣṭā iti cittasthitir eva upekṣā iti tasyā upādānam cittasthitiś ceha samīhitā tasmād itthaṃ samāhitacittasya maitrīkaruṇādy ekatattvālambanaṃ cittaṃ śīlayataḥ prāg abhihitā antarāyā na janiṣyante pracchardanavidhāraṇābhyāṃ vā prāṇasya vāśabdo maitryādibhāvanopāayāntaravikalpārthaḥ maitryādibhāvanādy upāyānām anyatamena yena kenacit cittasthitiḥ sampādanīyeti prakaraṇārthaḥ anekopāyapradarśanaṃ kasyacit kvacit sukaratābhiprāyeṇa pracchardanavidhāraṇābhyāṃ vyastābhyāṃ samastābhyāṃ vā pracchardanam kauṣṭhyasya vāyor ātamitor udvamanaṃ nāsikābhyām na sukhena vidhāraṇaṃ prāṇāyāma ātamitor eva yady api pracchardanenāpi prāṇaḥ āyamyate tathāpi bahirvṛttir na nirudhyata iti vidhāraṇaṃ prāṇāyāma iti viśeṣyate viṣayavatī vā pravṛttir utpannā sthitinibandhanī cittasya iti vākyaśeṣaḥ viṣayā gandhādayo yasyā yogapravṛtter gandhādisaṃvedanalakṣaṇāyā ālambanībhūtāḥ sa viṣayavatīty ucyate pravṛttir nāma yogino yogam abhyasyataḥ abhimukhī bhāvaṃ pratipadyamānasya yogasya yaḥ prathamo bhimukhībhāvaḥ pratyayakraṇo yogānuṣṭhānaṃ pratyutsāha janano nirmadhyamānasyāgner iva dhūmasamudbhavaḥ sāpravṛttiḥ sā ca tādṛśī pravṛttir utpannā pratyayakaraṇāt praharṣayantī yoginaś cittaṃ sthitau nivadhnāti nāsikāgre cittaṃ dhārayato gandhasaṃvit prahlādanakarasurabhigandhasaṃvedanaṃ nirantaratayā sammatasaṃyogam iva ācakṣāṇā jāyate sā gandhapravṛttiḥ tathā jihvādiṣu dhārayata iti sambadhyate tā etāḥ pravṛttayaḥ sthitau cittaṃ nibadhnanti saṃśayaṃ vidhamanti samādhiprajñāyāś ca dvārībhavanti etena raśmacandrādityagrahapradīpādiṣu cittaṃ dhārayato hṛdayapuṇḍarīke vā dhārayato vaiṣamyād raśmicandrādyākārā pravṛttir utpannā viṣayavatīty eva veditavyā yady api śāstrānumānācāryebhyo vagatam arthatattvaṃ tathābhutam evāvyabhicārisvarūpam eva teṣām anyathābhūtāpratipādakatvāt tathā Pi yāvad ekadeśo api svakaraṇasaṃvedyo na bhavati pratyakṣo na bhavati śāstrādu upadiṣṭsyārthasya ekadeśo api tāvat sarvaṃ parokṣam ivāpavargādiṣu sūkṣmeṣv artheṣu na dṛḍhāṃ buddhim utpādayati tasmāc chāstrānumānācāryopoddhalanārtham avaśyaṃ kaścid viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣīkartavyaḥ tatra śāstrādyupadiṣṭārthaikadeśapratyakṣatve sati sarvaṃ sūkṣmaviṣayam api ā apavargāc chraddhīyate etad artham evedaṃ citaparikarma yad etat maitrīkaruṇā ityādinā paramāṇuparamamahattvānto asya vaśīkāraḥ ity evam antena prakaraṇena yamaniyamāsanaviśiṣṭasya cittaparikarmopadiśyate tad etad uktaṃ bhavati etat prakaraṇopadiṣṭānām upāyānām anyatamānuṣṭhānāt pratyakṣīkṛtaikadeśatayā vidhūta pidhmāya saṃśayaṃ tu ā apavargāt dṛḍhāvasthitaśraddhānādi praśāntavahir vṛtti upasthitavaśīkārasaṃjñāvairāgyaṃ tasya tasya tṛtīyapādopadiṣṭapariṇāmatrayāder arthasya pratyakṣikaraṇāya samarthaṃ syāt jñānavibhūtyādiprāpyartham iti tataś ca evam arthaṃ cittaparikarmopadiśyata iti prakaraṇārthaḥ tayā ca bhāṣyakāraḥ pradarśitavān etad artham evedaṃ cittaparikarma ity evamādinā viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī pravṛttir utpannā manasaḥ sthitinibandhanīti prakṛtam abhisaṃbadhyate jyotir yasyāṃ vidyate pravṛttau sā jyotiṣmatī sā ca śokaṃ vyapagamayatīti viśokā nāma sā ca katham anupajāyata ity āha hṛdayapuṇḍarīke dhārayato buddhisaṃvid bhavati svarūpasavedanam buddhisattvam hi kiṃrūpam ity āha buddhisattvaṃ hi prabhāsvaraṃ prabhāsanaśīlam ākāśakalpaṃ vyāpi yatra yasmin budddhisattve sthitivaiṣamyād iti buddhisattvātmatāsāmyānāpatter iti hṛdayapuṇḍarīka eva dhārayataḥ pravṛttijyotiṣmatī sūryendumaṇiprabhārūpakāreṇa vikalpate tathā cāsmitāyām ahaṅkāre samāpnnaṃ syāt buddhisattvam svarūpeṇa sāmyāpatter nistaraṅgamahodadhikalpaṃ śāntam anantam asmitāmātraṃ bhavati yatredam uktaṃ yatrāsmitāsamāpatta taṃ etaṃ prakṛtam asmitātmānam ahaṅkāram aṇuṃ sūkṣmam ātmānam anuvidya prāpyāsmīty evaṃ tāvat saṃjātīta iti yad ṛṛśamālambanasvarūpam tāvan mātraṃ sañjānīte ahaṅkārasvarūpreṇa eva tadānurūpyād avacchidyate sphuṭikamaṇir ivopadhānarūpreṇa evaṃ dvayī viśokā pravṛttir viṣayavatī cāsmitāmātrā ca tara gandhasaṃvidādir āsmitāmātrāntā sarvā viśokā eva jyotṣmatī punar gandhasaṃvidādipravṛttipañcatayād anyatra viṣyavatī tv asmitāmātrāt prāg eva ity evaṃ viṣayavibhāgaḥ yayā viśokayā jyotiṣmatyā yoginaś cittaṃ sthitipadam labhate vītarāgaviṣayaṃ vā cittaṃ vīto rāgo yasmāt pratyayāt sa vītarāgaḥ rāgaśūnya ity arthaḥ sa eṣa viṣaya ālambanaṃ yasya cittasya tadvītarāgaviṣayam vītarāgaś ca pratyayaḥ prasiddho loke rāgiṇo api hi puruṣasya rāgakāraṇe api viṣaye yaḥ strīāu mātrādiṣu sa eva pratyayaḥ tam eva pratyaye vitarāgaḥ gaṃ ālambanatvenābhyasyet na tu tasya yo viṣayaḥ ālambanam viṣayāṇāṃ khalatvāt tat vītarāgapratyayālambanoparaktaṃ cittaṃ tadvad eva vītarāgaṃ prasannataraṃ sthitipadam labhate rāgādgikhalīkṛtaṃ hi kṛtakhalīnam iva turaṅgamānaṃ pracalati svapnanidrā jñānālambanamṃ vā svapnajñānālambanaṃ vā nidrājñānālambanaṃ vā cittaṃ tadākāram eva bhavati evaṃ svabhāvaṃ hi cittaṃ yadālambate tadākāraṃ bhavati svapne ca śabdādiviṣayaśūnyaṃ jñānam jñānasyāpi svabhāvo vabhāsakatā tatrāpi jñānasvaprūpam eva ālambate na tu smaryamāṇaviṣayasvarūpam smaryamāṇenāpi viṣayeṇa khalīkāro dṛśyate nidrā jñānaṃ tu viśeṣāgrahaṇātmakam abhāvapratyayālambanaṃ śāntam anantam anubhūyamānācalanadharmakam tataś ca tadālambanaṃ saccittaṃ sthitipadam labhata iti yuktam yathābhimatadhyānād vā yad evābhimatam iti cittasthityapekṣayā cittasthiteḥ prakṛtatvāt na tu sukhādyapekṣayā pratiṣidhatvāc ca na tv eva viṣayān prāpya dhārayeta kathaṃ cana iti tatra labdhasthitikaṃ karmaṇyaṃ sat anyatra śāstrīyeṣu api sthitipadam labhate paramāṇuparamamahattvānto asya vaśīkāraḥ antaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate sūkṣme niviśamānasya parimāṇe niviśamānasya yoginā saṃkṣipyamāṇasya abhuāsakāle tv alpam alpataraṃ ca krameṇālocayat paramāṇvantaṃ saṃkṣipyate sa ca paramāṇuc cittasya saṃkṣepakoṭiḥ tena tadantaṃ t sthitipadam ittham ubhayakoṭim anudhāvataś cittasya saṃkṣepaṃ vistāraṃ cānubhavato yaḥ tadvirodhinā pratyayāntareṇāpratighātaḥ sa paro vaśīkāraḥ pūrvo api pare eva tathāapy asyāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ tadvaśīkārāt paripūrṇam anavakhaṇḍitaṃ labdhasthitikaṃ na punar abhyāsakṛtaṃ parikarmāpekṣata iti pūrve tu kiyad api parikarmāntaram apekṣante tatra saṃkṣiptā viśālā vikaraṇī ceti trayī dhāraṇā tatrobhayakoṭismarśinī vikaraṇī paramamahatvāntaspṛgviśālā paramāṇvantaspṛk saṃkṣiptā sā ca trayy apīha sūtropāttā atha labdhasthitikasya cetasaḥ atha uktānām anyatamenopāyena labdhasthitikasya kiṃ svarūpā kiṃviṣayā vā samāpattir iti tannididarśayedaṃ sūtraṃ pravavṛte kṣīṇavṛtter abhijāyasyeva maṇer grahītṛgrahaṇagrāhyeṣu tatsthatadañjanatā samāpattiḥ nanu ca samāpatter viṣayaṃ vakṣyati tṛtīyapāde parārthāt svārthasaṃyamāt puruṣajñānam ity ādinā samāpattisvarūpam ca saṃyamasvarūpam tatkāryanirvartanena eva setsyati tataś cānarthakam idaṃ sūtram na eṣa doṣaḥ pūrvoktopāyavaśikāraṇārthavattvapradarśanārthatvāt evaṃ hy eṣa cittavaśīkāro rthāan yena grahītr ādyarthasamāpannaṃ cittaṃ tadābhāsaṃ bhavatīti kiñ ca vitarkādyanugamāt saṃprajñātaḥ ity uktam vitarkādisvarūpaṃ ceha darśayitavyam anuktāyāṃ samāpattau vitarkādisvarūpam āha na śakyaṃ darśayituṃ samāpattir dharmā di vitarkādaya iti kṣīṇavṛtter iti pratyastamitabāhyapramāṇādipratyayasya ity arthaḥ nanu sarva eva pratyayāḥ pratyastamitāḥ sarvapratyastamaye hi avasitādhikāraṃ na sthūlasūkṣmādikam ālambate abhijātasya iva maṇer iti dṛṣṭānt upādānam yathā sphaṭika epāśrayabhedāt tat tad rūpoparakta upāśrayākāreṇa nirbhāsate tathā grāhyālambanoparaktaṃ cittaṃ grāhyasamāpannaṃ grāhyasvarūpākāreṇa nirbhāsate tathā bhūtasūkṣmoparaktaṃ tanmātroparaktaṃ bhūtasūkṣmasamāpannaṃ bhūtasūkṣmasvarūpāvabhāsam avabhāsate tathā sthūlālambanoparaktaṃ sthūlarūpasamāpannaṃ sthūlarūpābhāsaṃ bhavati tathā viśvabhedoparaktaṃ viśvabhedasamāpannaṃ viśvarūpābhāsaṃ bhavati tathā grhaṇeṣv apīndriyeśv api draṣṭavyam grahaṇālambanoparaktaṃ grahaṇasamāpannaṃ grahaṇasvarūpākāreṇa nirbhāsate tathā grahītṛpuruṣasamāpannaṃ buddhibodhakasvarūpam ity arthaḥ gṛhītṛsvarūpākāreṇa nirbhāsate tathā muktapuruṣāla banoparaktam iti sa eva buddhr boddhā yadā viṣayavṛttīnāṃ na boddhā bhavati tadā sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātimātrāvasthā yadā udāsīno muktapuruṣa ity ucyate tadā hi sarvakleśādimuktaṃ cittaṃ sā eva hi puruṣasya muktatā yā kleśādivimuktiś cittasya ata eva sūtre grahītṛgrahaṇam eva kṛtam grahītā puruṣaviśeṣa eva muktapuruṣa ihābhipreta iti yadā yathā hi puruṣagrahaṇam eva kuryāt parasyāṃ vaśikārasaṃjñāyāṃ jātāyāṃ na punaḥ saṃsārayogo bhavati tathā ca uktam śaty eva cittasattvasambandhe kleśādisambandhābhāvāt sa tu sadaiva muktaḥ sadaiveśvaraḥ iti tasmāt muktapuruṣāla banoparaktaṃ muktapuruṣasamāpannaṃ muktasvarūpākāreṇa nirbhāsata iti yo hi manyate nivṛttasattvasambandhena eva muktena puruṣeṇ asamāpannaṃ tadākāram eva nirbhāsata iti tad ayuktam cittasya svātmapralayaprasaṅgāt nirariśayasūkṣmaś c apuruṣas tatsamasūkṣmaṃ pradhānaṃ tatkāryakryakāryaṃ nimittaṃ sattvaṃ tac cittaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ vā samāpadyamānaṃ na sthitena svena rūpeṇa samāpattum utsahate na hi ghaṭo mṛdavasthām aparityaktasvarūpaḥ samāpadyate nanu ca kāryeṇāpi yogisattvena mahadahaṅkārau saṃvedyāv ucyete mahati tāvadvipratipattiḥ saṃvedyate na vā iti yadā hisaṃvedyatā grahītṛmuktasvarūpavat saṃbandhaviśeṣa upapadyate mahadahaṅkārayor api vyaktau hi tau tataḥ saṃbandhaviśeṣo yujyate saṃbandhaviśeṣāc ca yathā svapuruṣo grahītṛ svarūpaś ca muktaś ca cittavṛttiviśeṣasaṃbandhāt gṛhyate tadvat na tu sarvātmanā eva mahadahaḥkārayor api grahaṇaṃ mahattvāt tayor api tāv api yadi sarvātmanā gṛhyeyātām cittasattvamātrātmānau jāyeyātām tathā ca sati tadviṣayagrahaṇam eva na syāt pradhānaprurṣayos tutatsaṃbandhasya cātyantam avyaktasvarūpatvān na svarūpagrahaṇam nanu ca īśvarasyāsarvajñatā yataḥ pradhānapuruṣatatsaṃbandhā na pratyakṣā iti ucyate pradhānapuruṣasaṃbandhebhyo anyat sarvaṃ pratyakṣam ity atra tāvat avipratipattiḥ niravadhikapratyakṣajñānābhyupagamāt yatra tv anumānagośaraḥ yad tu asmākam agocaraḥ tat sa eva īśvaro jñātum arhati jñeyaṃ ced asti tat sarvam asau yathā vā tathā vā jānātīti niścayaḥ ajñātṛkasya jñeyatvānupapatteḥ kiñ ca yadi prakṛtipuruṣau svarupeṇa jñeyatvam ā nā padyeyātāṃ tadā buddhivadbhogyatāprasaṅgaḥ tataś ca parārtho api syāt paraścānyaḥ kalpyaḥ syāt nanu puruṣāṇām anyonyabhogyatā iti na paro bhoktā kalpyaḥ na etad evam samatvāt puruṣāṇāṃ viṣayaviṣayitvānupapatteḥ na hi pradīpāv anyonyam uparut rutaḥ kiñ ca bhogyatve sukhādirūpatāprasaṅgaś ca puruṣasya tathā ca sati pradhānasya nirhetukatvaprasaṅgaś cety evam ādayo bhūyaṃso doṣāḥ nanu ca parārthāt svārthasaṃyamāt puruṣajñānam iti puruṣapratyaykṣatāṃ vakṣyati satyaṃ yuktam uktam ata evocyate puruṣo na svarūpeṇa viṣayibhavatīti yena evaṃ tatra uktam na ca puruṣapratyayena buddhisattvātmanā puruṣo dṛśyate puruṣa eva taṃ pratyayaṃ svālaṃbanaṃ paśyatīti tathā hy uktam vijñātāramare kena vijānīyāt itīti nanu puruṣālambanoparaktaṃ cittaṃ puruṣasya viṣayaḥ tathā ca sati pratyakṣa eva puruṣaḥ yathā ghaṭālabmbanoparaktte pratyaye puruṣeṇopalabhyamāne ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣa ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ ghaṭavat purusasya cittenāvyāpyatvāt ghaṭādis tu bāhyaś cittena vyāpyate na puruṣaḥ ānantyāt paricchinnaṃ hi cittaṃ viṣayīkurvan na puruṣaṃ viṣayiṇamanantaṃ vyāptum utsahate yadi puruṣaṃ vyāpnoti pradhānam api vyāpnuyāt tasmād yathā darpaṇe mukhaṃ chāyārūpeṇa gṛhyate tathā puruṣacchāyākāreṇa pariṇataḥ pratyayo gṛhyate puruṣeṇa tathā ca vyāsaḥ yathā darśatalaprakhye paśyaty ātmānam ātmani iti na tu muktānyapuruṣākāreṇa pariṇatau dvāram asti yadi tadākāreṇa pariṇameta muktasyāpi tatsvam eva iti dṛśyam syāt na hi cittasya pariṇāmā anyatvaṃ nāmāsti svākāreṇa hi pariṇataṃ puruṣo na tu cittaṃ na paśyati svapuruṣe svatvāt sati saṃbandhe pariṇatidvāram asti kathaṃ tarhi svapuruṣād anyasya svatvāsaṃbandhino grahaṇam ucyate yathā paradarpaṇadvāreṇa paramukhadarśanaṃ tathā darpaṇasthānīyaparasatvākārapariṇataṃ svasattvaṃ puruṣaḥ paśyan param api puruṣaṃ jānāti tasyāyam ātmā mamāyam ity anyatvan tv anumānād eva pratipadyate svakīyād anyadīyasattvagataviśeṣaloggena sattvānāṃ ca triguṇatvād avaśyaṃ viśeṣāḥ santi puruṣāṇāṃ tu nirviśeṣatvāt svarūpeṇa bhedo duravabodha eva tasmād evam abhijātamaṇikalpasya cetaso grahītṛgrahaṇakrāhyeṣu puruṣendriyabhūteṣu tatsthatadañjanatā teṣu grahītrādiṣu tiṣṭhatīti tatsthaṃ tatsthatāviśiṣṭā yāṃ grahītrādyañjanatā tad eva āha teṣu sthitasya tadākārāpattiḥ samāpattir ity ucyate samyag āpattiḥ samāpattiḥ sā ca tādṛśī pratyastamitabahirvṛtter eva bhavati yady api vyutthitacittasyāpi samāpattir asti tathā api sā na samīcīnatarā rajas tamobhyāṃ cittasattvasyātyantābhibhūtatvād iti saiṣā samāpattiś catuṣṭayī tatra prathamāṃ samāpattiṃ vyācaṣṭe śabdārthajñānavikalpaiḥ saṅkīrṇā savitarkā samāpattiḥ śabdaś cārthaś ca jñānaṃ ca śabdārthajñānāni teṣāṃ vikalpāḥ śabdārthajñānavikalpaḥ vyātavyālambanaviṣayair vikalpaiḥ saṃkīrṇā vimmiśrā itaretarapratyayānubuddhā sā saṃkīrṇasamāpattiḥ nanu ca śabdārthapratyayā itaretaravyāvṛttasvarūpāḥ yogī ca ekaṃ vastu dhyeyatvenālambate śabdam arthaṃ pratyayaṃ vā tatra kaḥ śabdārthajñānavikalpasaṅkaraḥ evam evaitat tathā api ayam eva saṃvyavahāro loke yad utāvibhāgena grahaṇam tadyathā gaur iti śabdo gaur ity artho gaur iti jñānam ity avibhāgena loke grahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭam evaṃ hi lokaḥ trayam api gaur ity eva vyapadiśyati tathā anyataragrahaṇe avaśiṣṭayor api smṛtiḥ nanu ca tathābhutam etadvastu na evaṃ śabdārthasaṅketagrahaṇottarakālabhāvitvāt nanu saṅgetād api prāk sāmānyaśabdaṃ yaṃ kañcid adhyavasyaty eva na viviktānām api grahaṇadarśanāt vivicyamānāś cānye śabdadharmā gakārādivarṇodāttasvaritatadrutam adhyavilambitaśrotragrahaṇādayaḥ te nārthajñānayoḥ tathānye rthadharmāḥ sasnālāṅgūlakakudakhuraviṣāṇadarśanādayaḥ tathā ca anye pratyayadharmāḥ puruṣagrāhyātmakatvāvabhāsātmakatvasaṃskārādhāyitvādayaḥ na te śabdārthayoḥ na tena paramārthato nyonyadharmasaṅkaragandho apy asti tena viviktaḥ pandhās teṣām tatra yatra kvacana samāpannasya yo hy evārthaḥ samādhiprajñām upārūḍhaḥ sa cec chabdārthajñānavikalpānuviddhaḥ śabdārthasaṅketakṛto ya itaretarasmṛtyanuvyādhas tadviśiṣṭaś ced artha upāvartate sā saṅkīrṇā samāpattiḥ savitarkety ucyate anekajanmāntaraśabdārthasaṅketajñānasaṃskāraviśiṣṭatvād yogino api prathamatarā samāpattir lokapratyaya aviśiṣṭā eṣa tu viśeṣo yat labdhasthitipadatvād yogicittasya samānapratyayapravāhate idānīṃ nirvitarkā samāpattir ucyate yadā punaḥ śabdasaṅketasmṛtipariśuddhau śabdasaṅketo syāyaṃ vācakaḥ ayam asya vācya iti samayapratipattiḥ tajjanitasmṛtiḥ śabdasaṅketasmṛtiḥ tasyāḥ pariśuddhir mithyātvād vinivṛttiḥ sā rajas tamasor nyag bhāvāt śrutijñānaṃ āgamikam anumānajñānaṃ laukikaṃ te ca sāmānyaviṣaya evānumānāgamajñāne tayor vikalpo hi viśeṣādhyāropaḥ tenādhyāsena śūnyāyāṃ yoginaḥ samādhiprajñāyāṃ vyāvṛttalaiṅgikasāṅketikajñānādhyāsāyāṃ svarūpamātreṇa mātragrahaṇaṃ digdeśakālānubhāvādibhyo api vyāvṛtta ity evam arthaṃ svair eva dharmair mahīyamānaḥ tatsvarūpamātratayā eva tasyārthasya svarūpamātratayā eva yoginaḥ prajñā avicchidyate na tasmād arthād bahirdeśakālādi kiṃcid ālovayatīty arthaḥ svam api grahaṇātmakaṃ rūpaṃ tat prajñā na ālocatati nirmalataratvāt grāhyamātrā eva sā vibhajyate sā ca tādṛśī nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ nirgato vitarko syāḥ nirvitarkaḥ vitarko dhyāropaḥ so syāṃ nāsti tat etat param utkṛṣṭaṃ śuddhaṃ pratyakṣaṃ aparaṃ pratyakṣaṃ sarvasādhāraṇaṃ purastād vṛttimadhye paṭhitam idaṃ yogina eva iti tacchutānumānayor bījam yady api pūrvoktam api śrutānumānayor bījam eva tathā api tatkārye śrutānumāne vyabhivarato api na punar nirvitarkasamādhijapratyakṣaprabhave vyabhivarata ity ata āha tataḥ śrutānumāne prabhavata iti na ca nanu śrutānumānajñānasahabhūtaṃ tad darśanam śrutānumānajñānābhyām asamāniviṣayam ity etat viśeṣaviṣayaṃ hi tad darśanaṃ sāmānyaviṣaye śrutānumānajñāne tasmād asaṅkīrṇaṃ pramāṇāntareṇa yogino nirvitakajaṃ darśanam iti tannirvitarkāyāḥ tad iti tasmād iti samāpatter asyāḥ sūtreṇa lakṣaṇaṃ dyotyate samṛtiparuśuddhau svarūpaśūnyevārthamātranirbhāsān nirvitarkā śabdasaṅketaśrutānumānajñānavikalpasmṛtipariśuddhau śabdasaṅketavikalpaḥ śrutajñānavikalpaḥ anumānajñānavikalpaś ca sa eva smṛtiḥ smaraṇena hy anyasyānyadharmo adhyāropyate na hi vastu svarūpeṇa vastvantare dhyāropayituṃ śakyam nanu ca kathaṃ śrutānumite pratyakṣe adhyāropyete nanu ca prasiddho dhyāropaḥ tathā cedaṃ mayā śrutam idaṃ mayā numitam idam iti ca paśyati nanu tad eva tat dṛśyamānam api yad anumitaṃ śrutaṃ ca na sāmānyaviśeṣabhedāt sāmānyaṃ śrutam anumitaṃ ca viśeṣas tu pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ tasmiṃś ca tatsāmānyādhyāsaḥ prasiddha eva grāhyoparaktā yoginaḥ prajñā evaṃ prajñārūpam grhaṇātmakaṃ tyaktvā padārthamātrasvabhāvā grāhyasvarūpāpanneva bhavati ivaśabdena grahaṇātmakatāṃ na jahatīti na hi sphaṭika upādhyāśrayatāyāṃ svāṃ svaccharūpatāṃ hāsyati kiñ ca grahaṇavyatiriktaṃ ca grāhyaṃ vastvantaram astīti ca uktaṃ bhavati sā nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ tathā ca vyākhgyātam tasyā hy ekabuddhyupakramo rthātmā upakramyate ekayā buddhyā yaḥ sa ekaśbuddhyupakramaḥ ekabuddhiparicchedya iti arthātmā bodhyātmety etat gavādir ghaṭādir vā viṣayaḥ na tu bodha eva gavādyākāro viṣayaḥ aṇupracayaviśeṣātmā aṇūnāṃ tanmātrayavānāṃ pracayaviśeṣa ātmā yasya sa gavādir ghaṭādir vā ālambanaṃ buddheḥ sa ca viṣayaḥ saṃsthānaviśeṣaḥ tathā saṃsthitāni hi tāni bhūtasūkṣmāṇi etad uktaṃ bhavati bhūtasūkṣmāṇāṃ sādhāraṇo dharma iti ātmabhūto na vyatiriktaḥ yathā sarpasya ābhogakuṇḍalanādi yeṣāṃ punar atyantavyatiriktam anyad eva kāraṇāt kāryaṃ teṣāṃ kāraṇatantratvaṃ kāryasya na prāpnoti aṃśu tantro hi tantuḥ tantutantraś ca paṭaḥ na cātyantāvyatve nyatantratvaṃ dṛṣṭam ansyasya yathā mṛtpiṇḍatantratā na paṭasya tantūnāṃ vā kiñ ca tadvināśānuvināśitvaṃ ca na śakyaṃ na hi kapālavināśam anuvinaśyati paṭaḥ athocyeta sambandhaḥ kāraṇam iti paṭasya hi tantavas tantūnāñ cāṃśava iti sambandhas tatra hetuḥ kāraṇaṃ tat tantratvatadanuvināśayor iti atrocyate caitrakṣetrādisambandhe api prasaṅgaḥ syāt caitrasyāpi kṣetrāditantratā tadanuvināśitvam ca sambandhaviśeṣāt prasajyeta athāpi syāt samavāyalakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ kāraṇam iti na tasyāpi saṃbandhatvāviśeṣād ahetutvaṃ yathānyasaṃbandhaḥ saṃbandhinor anyataratantratvādy ahetuḥ evaṃ samavāyalakṣaṇasyāpi saṃbandhatvād anyataratantratvādāv ahetutvam eva kiñcānyat saṃbandhasya ca saṃbandhinor evānyataratantratvādihetutve samavāyasyāpi samavāyāntaraṃ tasyāpy anya ity anavasthā prasajyeta yathā guṇādīnāṃ samavāyalakṣaṇāt saṃbandhāt dravyatantratvaṃ tathā samavāyasyāpi dravyavyatiriktatve dravyatantratvārthaṃ samavāyāntaraṃ kalpyeta tasyāpy anyat tasyāpy anyad ity anavasthā syāt prāg utpatter abhāvāt kāryasya kāraṇena saṃbandhānupapattiḥ aviśiṣṭaṃ cāsattvaṃ śaśaviṣāṇasya ghaṭasya ca tatra ghaṭena eva kāraṇasya saṃbnandho na śaśaviṣāṇādibhir iti hetur vāditavyaḥ prāk asannotpadyeta śaśaviṣāṇavat yas tu tantubhyo nyaḥ sa tantubhyo na utpadyate tantubhyo nyatvāt yathā tantubhyo ghaṭaḥ itara āha prāk sannapi na utpadyate satvāt visyamānaghaṭavad iti yo yasmād ananyaḥ so api tasmānnityā na utpadyate vidyamānatvāt svarūpavad iti apara āha yadi sannotpadyata iti sata ytpattyabhāva ucyeta siddhasādhyatā syāt athābhivyaktyabhāvaḥ tadā dṛṣṭāntābhāvaḥ yad apy ucyate yo yasmād ananya iti tatrāpi siddhasādhyatā dṛṣṭāntābhāvaś ca svarūpād eva hy bhivyajyate nāsaty abhivyaṅgyasvarūpe abhivyaktir abhivyañjakasahasreṇāpi śakyate kartum kiñcānyat sarvavyavahāralopaś ca katham yadā devadattasya gaur aśvo vā prātar vidyamānakarṇalāṅgūlaḥ punar aḍavīṃ gataḥ kenacil lūnakarṇo lūnalāṅgūlo vā syāt tadā pūrvāvayavavibhāgād vinaṣṭaḥ anyas tu navaḥ pralūnakarṇalāṅgūlo svāmikaḥ sañjāta iti yena kenacid upādīyeta tathā cāvayavavibhāgaḥ sarvatra sambhavatīti svasvāmisambandhādiniyamābhāvād aśeṣavyavahāralopaḥ syāt atha brūyāt pūrvopārjitāvayavair evāvayavī navaḥ pralūnakarṇalāṅgūla ārabdha iti na evam na hi mātāmitrādivyatirekeṇa idānīntana lūnakarṇalāṅgūlāvayavyantarapratyārambhiṇo dṛśyante kiṃ ca yasya ca kṣetre lūnakarṇalāṅgūlo jātas tasya evāsau syāt na pūrvāvayavikasya tatkṣetrajātatṛṇapalāśādivat yathā cānyakṣetragatāni bījāni salilaughenāne akṣetrem upanītāni cet tat tadbījaniṣpannasasyaṃ kṣetravān eva gṛhṇāti na tu pūrvabījavān taḥ na cāsyāsau pratibadhnāti vidvān api madīyabījapariniṣpannaṃ sasyam aham upādīyeti tathā lūnakarṇakāṅgūlam api kṣetravān eva gṛhṇīta na tatra pratibandha rūpa nīyam madīyāvayavair ārabdho yam avayavīti yeṣām apy ekasmin gṛhīte tasminn aśve lūnakarṇalaṅgūlake jāte svakṣetre ca dṛṣṭe sa evāśvadātā anyoyaṃ vitisanyoyaṃ mahattamādaśvānmayā datto mahattama iti hareta haratām iti cet satvavyavahāralopaprasaṅgaḥ śāstrakopaś ca tasmād ā nyo vayavebhyaḥ kāraṇebhya eko vayavī kāryam iti siddham yad apy ucyate śabdapratyayadharmādibhedād anya iti tad apy uktam dṛśyate hi śabdādibhede apy ananyatvam yathā hastaḥ karaḥ pāṇir iti śabdabheda ekasyapitṛtvaṃ putratvaṃ ca pratyayabheda ekasya eva baddhaḥ punar muktaḥ sthito gataś ceti kālabhedāt dāhakatvaṃ pācakatvam ity ādayo dharmabhedā iti dig deśādibhedās tv asiddhā eva tasmād āha ātmabhūta iti sa ca svaphalena vyaktenānumitaḥ phalena udakāharaṇādhāraṇasambhavanādinā yasya hi phalaṃ kāryaṃ vyaktam upalabhyate sa astīti niścayaḥ anumita iti vipratipannāpekṣayā sādhāraṇaśabdena śaktirūpeṇa vocyate sa tu pratyakṣa evāvyaktena daṇḍasūtrakūlālādikārakavyāpārābhivyaktena phalena kāryeṇa ghaṭākhyena prāg api mṛdādyavasthāyām astitvenānumitaḥ saiva daṇḍādikārakaiḥ svavyañjakair abhivyajyamānaḥ prādur bhavati dharmāntarodaye ca tirobhavati saiva bhūtasūkṣmāṇāṃ dharmo vayavīty ucyate etad uktaṃ bhavati aṇūnām apratyakṣatvān nāvirbhāvatirobhāvau yuktau tata s tāś ca tau tasmād ya āvirbhavati dharmāntarodaye virodhāttirobhavati ca āvir bhāve ca yo vyañjakādyapekṣate so vayavīty ucyate yaś ca evaṃ dharmaḥ so ṇubhyo nya iti kiñ cāmī apy anye hetavo vayavisadbhāve yo sāv ekaś ca mahāṃś ca āṇīyāṃś ca kriyādharmakaś cānityaś ca pratyekam ete hetavaḥ api ca eko ghaṭa iti ghaṭaśabdavācyasya ekatvena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt asti cedaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ yo sāv eka iti na hi bahūnām aṇūnām ekatvena sāmānādhikaraṇyam upakalpete tathā mahatvena na cāṇūnāṃ amahatāṃ mahatvena sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ yujyate tathā aṇīyastvena na hy aṇūnām aṇvantarāpekṣayā anīyastvaṃ ghaṭate sarva eva hi te ṇīyāṃsaḥ nāpi cāṇūnām aṇutvaṃ gṛhyate ṇubhyaḥ aṇutve vastvantarasyāṇīyastvam upapatsyate kiñ ca kriyādharmakaś ca kriyā dharmo yasya sa kriyādharmakaḥ phalavad vyāpāranirvṛttikaratvād ity uktaṃ bhavati na hy aṇūnāṃ phalavadvyāpāranirvṛttikaratvaṃ yuktam aśakyaprayojyatvād asmadādibhiḥ kiñ cānityatvāt na hy aṇūnām anityatvaṃ gṛhyate kiṃ ca dṛśyatvāt na hy aṇavo dṛśyante tathā spṛśyatvāc ca hānāc copādānāc ca dhāraṇāc cety evam ādayaḥ tenāvayavinā vyavahārāḥ kriyante nānubhir iti yasya punaḥ itthaṃ pramāṇasuprasiddhasattāko api avastu kaḥ avayavī sa pracayaviśeṣaḥ sūkṣmaṃ ca kāraṇam anupalabhyaṃ aṇvādi tasyāvayavyabhāvād atad rūpapratiṣṭhaṃ mithyājñānam iti prāyeṇa saevam eva visayajñānaṃ prāptaṃ mithyājñānam tataḥ sarvam eva jñānaṃ śabdādyākāreṇa sukhādyākāreṇa tadjñānākāreṇa ca upajāyate śabda ādayaś ca jñānākārakarāvayavitvābhimatā nābhyupagamyante sukhādayo api viṣayatvād avayavipakṣā eva tathā tajjānam eva jñānākārakaratvāt svarūpam api mithyeti prāptaṃ sarvam eva mithyājñānam tataś ca pratyakṣānumānayor apy ābhāsatvam eva tenābhupetaṃ tayor api śabdāddiviṣayatvāt yad api sarvajñajñānam anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmakatvādiviṣayaṃ tasyāpi viṣayābhāvāt tad api mithyājñānaṃ prāptam iti svatantrasya tīrthakarasya cāprāmāṇyaṃ tatra tīrthakaras sahadharmābhāvaś cābhyupagato bhavati śabdādivat pramāṇaviṣayatvāviśeṣāt tad etat pratipādayati samyagjñānam api kiṃ syād viṣayābhāvāt yad yad upalabhyate tat tad avayavitvenāghnātam iti jñānasya svākārasamarpakatvāviśeṣāt tac ca svākārasamarpakaṃ kiñcana nābhyupeyata iti sarvasyātmīkasya jñānasya tena mithyātvam āpāditam tathā ca samyagjñānam api kiṃ syāt yadapekṣayā mithyājñānam abhisandhīyate yadā ca avayavinaṃ sarvapramāṇasamyak sarvajñānasiddham apahṇute tadā na samyagjñānasya viṣayaḥ sampādayituṃ pāryate yadā ca na pārasyati tadā katham abhisandadhīta sarvaṃ mithyeti samyagjñānam apekṣya mithyā jñānaṃ mithyā bhāvam āsīdati āpekṣikatvāt samyaṅ mithyā jñānayoḥ yaś cāpi manate nirviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ samyag iti tasyāpi svarūpāgrahaṇāt tad astitvānupapattiḥ gṛhyate ced viṣayatvād avayavimithyātvaṃ tanmithyātvāc ca taj jñānamithyātvaṃ tathā taj jānam apīti satvamithyātvam uktaṃ pūrvam eva api ca nirviṣayajñānasamyaktve sarvajñānasya viṣayānabhyupagamān nirviṣayatvam iti samyaktvam eva prāpnuyāt tathāpi tu sarvajñānasamyaktvān mithyā jñānaṃ kiṃ syād iti vaktavyam athāpi brūyāt yat saviṣayam ivābhāti tan mithyājñānaṃ yad atyantanirviṣayaṃ tatsamyag iti tathāpi tasyāstitve pramāṇābhāva ity ukta eva doṣaḥ tasmād avayavī samyagjñānasya viṣayo vaśyāhyupagantavyaḥ ity āha tasmād asty avayavī yo mahatvād vyavahārāpannaḥ samāpatter nirvitarkāyā viṣayībhvatīti etayā eva savicārā nirvcārā ca sūkṣmaviṣayā vyākhyātā tatra bhūtasūkṣmeṣv abhivyaktadharmakeṣu tan mātreṣv eva deśakālanimittānubhavāv acchineṣu deśāvacchinnaśabdaḥ sarvaṃ hi vastu deśādibhir avacchidyamānaṃ viṣayiṇā jñātrā saṃbandhyamānaṃ vyavahārāya kalpate teṣv evaṃ bhūteṣv evaṃbhūtā eva deśādivikalpābhisaṃhitā eva yā samāpattiḥ sā savicārā ity ucyate tataś ca savicārāyāḥ savitarkāviśeṣatvaṃ siddham katham ihāpy adhyāsāviśeṣāt ayan tu viśeṣaḥ śabdasaṅketārthajñānadeśādisarvādhyāsāḥ savitarkāyām iha punas tanmātrasūkṣmadharmeṣu śabdasaṅketasyāprasiddhatvād viśiṣṭanāmasaṅketajñānānadhyāsaḥ deśādyadhyāsaś ca sūkṣmaviṣayatvañ vā iti savitarkāviśeṣatvasiddhiḥ tatrāpy ekabuddhinirgrāhyam evoditadharmaci viśiṣṭaṃ uktadeśādidharmaviśiṣṭam udbhūtadharmaviśiṣṭaṃ vā bhūtasūkṣmam ālambanībhūtaṃ na tu nirviṣayaṃ jñānam eva samādhiprajñāyām upatiṣṭhate yadā punaḥ sarvathā sarvaprakāreṇa sarvataḥ sarvatra śāntāś coditāś cāvyapadeśyāś ca ye dharmās te śāntoditāvyapadeśyadharmāḥ taiḥ anavacchinneṣu śānta iti yo vyāpāraṃ kṛtvā uparato dharmaḥ udita iti yo vyāpāram ārūḍhaḥ avyapadeśya iti na śānto nāpy uditaḥ nāpy udbhāvayad dṛśyamānanimittaḥ tadyathā suvarṇasyādṛśṭānekāśrutākāropajanaśaktayas tā avyapadeśyā dharmāḥ tair anavacchinneṣu bhūtasūkṣmeṣu sarvadharmānupātiṣu sarvan dharmān anupatanti sūkṣmāṇi sarvaviśeṣārambhakatvāt sarvātmakeṣu sarvebhyo viṣayebhyo nantatvāt tanmātrāṇām tatra yā samāpattiḥ sā nirvicāreti nirvitarkāyā yal lakṣaṇaṃ tat sarvam iha nivicārāyāṃ draṣṭavyam taddarśayati evaṃsvarūpaṃ hi tadbhūtasūkṣmamanenaiva svarūpeṇa deśakāla nimittānubhavādiviśeṣavirahitena sarvātmakena sarvadharmānupātinā ālambanībhūtameva samādhiprajñāmuparañjayati prajñā ca svarūpaśūnyevārthamātrā tadā bhavati tadā nirvicārā tasmin nirvitarkāviśeṣā nirvicārā tat svayam eva darśayati mahadvastuviṣayā mahataḥ vastu mahadvastv iti
