cāliṅgaparyavasānam pārthivasyāṇor gandhamātrasvarūpamātrateti pṛthivīsamīkṣayā sūkṣmo viṣayaḥ gandhamātrasvarūpamātrasyāpi liṅgamātraṃ mahattattvaṃ sūkṣmo viṣayaḥ tato liṅgamātrān mahato nirvṛttāni sahāhaṅkāreṇa tan mātrāṇi layaṃ gacchatīti liṅgaṃ layād vā pradhānāl liṅgāt pratyāgacchantīti liṅgaṃ tadviparītam aliṅgaṃ pradhānaṃ na layaṃ gacchati nāpy anyataḥ lutaś cit layād āgacchati liṅgamātrasyāliṅga sūkṣmo viṣayaḥ na cāliṅgāt paraṃ sūkṣmam asti sūkṣmaṃ nāma sthūlakāryāpekṣayā kāraṇaṃ tac cāliṅgāvasānam na cāliṅgāt pradhānā l liṅgā d anyat sūkṣmaṃ kāraṇam asti nanu puruṣa iti nanu tatra puruṣasyānāśaṅkā eva kāryakāraṇasūkṣmatayā prakramāt na eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣasyāpi kaiścit kāraṇatvasyābhyupagamāt tadā śaṅkayā eva hy etad ucyate nanu puruṣa iti satyam aliṅgātmaka tva m aliṅgasya saukṣmyam kutaḥ yataḥ kāraṇam alliṅgaṃ liṅgasya yady asyānvayikāraṇaṃ tattadapekṣayā sūkṣmam iti prakṛtam nanu puruṣo apy aliṅgātmaka eva bādhaṃ na tu liṅgāpekṣayā puruṣaḥ sūkṣmaḥ kutaḥ yat astu liṅgasyānvayikāraṇaṃ puruṣo na bhavati saty apy aliṅgātmakatve kāryasya caitanyenānanvitatvāt kiñ ca puruṣasyāpi bhogyatvaprasaṅgaḥ tathā ca pārārthyaṃ sukhaduḥkhamohātmakatvaṃ ca nirhetukatvaṃ ca pradhānasya puruṣasya tac ca sarvapramāṇa prāṇa viprakupitam ity ata āha hetas tu bhavatīti pradhānapravṛttau bhoktṛtvena nimittaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ ataḥ pradhānasya saukṣmyaṃ niratiśayaṃ vyākhgyātam tā eva sabījaḥ samādhiḥ catasraḥ samāpattayo bahirvastuviṣayā iti bahirvastuviṣayatvaṃ hetuḥ samījatve samādhir api sabījaḥ samprajñāto vitarkavicārānandāsmitārūpānugamāt samprajñātaḥ ity upavyākhyātaḥ sthūle rthe savitarko nirvitarkaḥ sūkṣme rthe savicāro nirvicāra iti copavyākhyātaḥ vitarkādilakṣaṇasūtreṇa nirvicāravaiśāradye dhyātmāprasādaḥ aśuddhyāvaraṇamalāpetasya aśuddhir eva āvaraṇaṃ tad eva malaṃ kleśādikaṃ tasmād apetasya prakāśātmano buddhisattvasya rajastamobhyām anabhibhūtaḥ svacchaḥ sthitipravāho vaiśāradyam yadā nirvicārasya samādher vaiśāradyam idaṃ jāyate tadā yogino bhavaty adhyātmaprasādaḥ ātmādijñānavivekaḥ asyaivavyākhyānam bhūtārthaviṣayaḥ kramānurodhī paripāṭikayā yāvatkleśakṣayam anuruddhyata iti kramānurodhī sphuṭaṃ viviktataraṃ śuddhatarātmakaḥ prajñālokaḥ prajñāivālokaḥ tayā yathāvastu jānāti tathā coktam prajñāprāsādam ārudhya na śocyaś śocato janān bhūmiṣṭhān iva śaulasthaḥ sarvān prājño nupaśyati iti ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā tasmin prajñāloke dhyātmaprasāde samāhitasya yā prajñā jāayate vivekajanmā tasyā vivekajanmanaḥ ṛtambharā iti saṃjñā bhavati anvarthā eva sā satyam eva vibharti na tatra viparyāsajñānagandho apy asti prakṣīṇasakalaviparyāsakalmaṣasya hi jāyate jāyamānā ca viṣayakatthaṅkam amanudati tathā coktam āgamenānumānena dhyānābhyāsarasena ca tridhā prakalpayan prajñāṃ labhate yogam uttamam iti yogāṅgaprajñāṃ tridhā vibhajate tatra eko bhāgaḥ śāstrācāropadiṣṭārthānusārī dvitīyas tasya eva yuktyā numānena vicāryāgamārthavirodhinirākaraṇapūrvakaṃ tat samyag upapādanaparaḥ tṛtīyas tu sadāgama anumānasamyag upapannārthālambanasya pratyayasyānuśīlanaṃ rasopayogī tad itthaṃ tridhā prakalpayan yogī yagaṃ labhate sā punaḥ ṛtambharā prajñā sāmānyapuruṣapratyayaviṣayād anyaviṣayety āha śrutānumānaprajñābhyām anyaviṣayā viśeṣaḥ viśeṣāṇām anantyān na saṅketayituṃ śakyate sāmānyena hi kṛtasaṅketaḥ śabdaḥ tataś cāgṛhītaviśeṣasaṅketo na viśeṣam abhidhātuṃ jñāpayituṃ vā śaknoti tathānumānaṃ sāmānyaviṣayam eva tad apy uktam eva sāmānyāvadhāraṇapradhānā vṛttih iti tathodāharaṇena ca pratipāditam yatra prāptis tatra gatiḥ yatrāprāptis tatra na bhavati gatiḥ ity anumānena sāmānyopasaṃhāraḥ sā mānyamātram anumānena upasaṃhriyate tasmāc chrutānumānaviññānaviṣayo na viśeṣaḥ kaścid asti yady evaṃ na lokapratyakṣeṇāpareṇa bhūtasūkṣmagataḥ puruṣagato vā viśeṣaḥ prajñāyeta nānyac ca pramāṇatrayavyatiriktaṃ pramāṇam asti yena tadviśeṣaṃ sañjānīmahe iti ced āha na cāsya sūkṣmavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭasya vastuno lokapratyakṣeṇa grahaṇam na cāsya viśeṣasyāpramāṇakasyābhāo stīti pramāṇāvagamyamānarūpo hi bhāvo sti rājavīthīm adhirohati tasmāt samādhiprajñānirgrāhya eva viśeṣo bhavati bhūtasūkṣmagataḥ puruṣagato vā nanu ca te sūkṣmagatā viśeṣāḥ pratyakṣeṇāvagamyante iti kim īśvaraññāpitam vastutvād avagamyanta iti cet āgamānumānābhyāṃ santīty avagamyanta eva na ca niyāmakaṃ kiṃcid asti pratyakṣeṇa eva nirgrāhyā iti na hi viśeṣā hastatalagatā api sarve gṛhyante na anyavastugataviśeṣāṇāṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatvasyānumeyatvāt katham evaṃ manyate bhūtasūkṣmādgatā viśeṣāḥ pratyakṣagrāhyāḥ kasya cit kāryavastuviśeṣatvāt gṛhyamāṇasvapāṇigataviśeṣavad iti tasmāc chrutānumānaprajñābhyām anyaviṣayā sā prajñā viśeṣārthatvād iti viśeṣārthā hi sā samādhiprajñāpratilambhe yoginaḥ prajñākṛtaḥ saṃskāro navo jāyate prajñā hi saṃskārārambhiṇīti siddham prajñābhinavbatvāt tatsaṃskāraḥ pratyagrataro jñyate iti viśeṣaḥ prajñānavatvaṃ tu tasyā sāmānya anyaviṣayatvāt taj jassaṃskāro nyasaṃskārapratibandhī ṛtumbharaprajñāprabhavasaṃskāro vyutthānasaṃskārāśayaṃ anyaṃ bādhate viśiṣṭyarthārthaviṣayaprabhavatvāt pratibandhnāti ā mokṣāc cheta iti saṃskārāśayaḥ vyutthānasaṃskārābhibhavāt vyutthānasaṃskārāśayasya samadhiprajñāsaṃskāreṇābhibhavāt tat prabhavāḥ vyutthānasaṃskāraprabhavāḥ pratyayā na bhavanti pratyayanirodhe vyutthānapratyayanirodhe samādhiḥ samprajñāta iva upatiṣṭhate tataḥ samādhijā prajñā tataḥ prajñākṛtaḥ saṃskārā iti evaṃ navaḥ saṃskārāśayo vardhate tataś ca prajñā tataś ca saṃskārā iti atrāha samādhiprajñābhavaḥ saṃskārāśayaś cittasyādhikārapravṛttihetuḥ pratyayaprabhavatāt vyutthānaprabhavasaṃskārāśayavad iti tathā cittasaṃskāratvāc ceti tad etad darśayati katham asau saṃskārāśayaḥ cittaṃ sādhikāraṃ saṃskāropetaṃ na kariṣyato iti na eṣa doṣaḥ tadviroshitvāt kathaṃ te saṃskārāḥ kleśakṣayahetutvāc cittam adhikāraviśiṣṭaṃ na kurvanti vyutthānapratyayaprabhavānāṃ hi saṃskārāṇām avidyādikleśahetutvāc cittasaṃskārābhimukhabhāvakāraṇatā tadvirodhipratyayaprabhavatvāt tu na samādhijapratyayajanmanāṃ saṃskārāṇām adhikārābhimukhyanimittatā kiñ ca cittañ ca te svakāryāt saṃskārābhimukhavṛttibhyo vasādayanti viramayanti khyātiparyavasānaṃ hi cittavicoṣtitam puruṣakhyātiś ca jātā saṃskāraś ca bhavatīti viruddham yo hi vigatatṛṣṇāsamuāyo nāsau pānīyaṃ pipāsati etāvad eva cittena puruṣasya karaṇīyam na hi kaścit kṛtaṃ karaṇīyaṃ cikīrṣati kiñ ca tasyāpi nirodhe sarvanirodhān nirbījas samādhir iti iti śabdaḥ parisamāptyarthaḥ tasyāpi samādhiprajñāprabhavasya saṃskārasyābhinavasya nirodhe apiśabdāt saṃskārakāraṇasya samādhiprajñāyā api nirodhe sarvanirodho bhavati uktam evopāyadvayaṃ paravairāgyavirāmapratyayābhyāsākhyaṃ tannirodhasya kiṃ punas tat sarvaṃ ṛtambharaprajñā janitasaṃskāraḥ samādhiprajñānirodhī yathā eva tāṃ samādhiprajñām ṛtambharāṃ niruṇāddhi tathaivātmanā sahātmasajātīyānāṃ svakāraṇaprajñkṛtānāṃ saṃskārāṇām api pratibandhī nirodhād bhavati kasmāt nirodhajaḥ saṃskāraḥ yasmāt samādhiprajñāyās tajjanmanaś ca saṃskārasya nirodhe nirodhakaḥ samādhiprajñājanitasaṃskārād anyo jāyate sa cāpi yataḥ samādhiprajñāṃ tajjanitasaṃskārāṃścātiraskṛtasya na janma pratipadyate tasmāt sa nirodhajaḥ saṃskāraḥ samādhijān saṃskāran bādhata iti kathaṃ punar asau nirodhajaḥ saṃskāro stīti gamyate vidyamane api sa bādhako bhavatīti āha nirodhasthitikālakramānubhaveneti nirodhasya sthitis tasyāḥ kālaḥ sa ca kālaḥ krameṇānubhūyate yataḥ pratabhyāsam abhivardhate tasmāt tena nirodhasthitikālakremānubhavena nirodhacittakṛtaṃ nirodhāvasthacittakṛtaṃ saṃskārāstitvam anumeyam vyutthānanirodhasamādhiprabhavaiḥ vyutthānasamādhiprabhavaiḥ nirodhasamādhiprabhavaś ca saha kaivalyabhāgīyaiḥ saṃskāraiś cittaṃ avasitādhikāratvāt svasyāṃ prakṛtau svakāraṇe smitāyām ahaṅkāre pravilīyate pratyastameti tasmāt te khyātinirodhajnmānaḥ saṃskārā yasmāt cittasyādhikāravirodhinaḥ na sthitihetavo bhavantīti yasmād avasitādhikāraṃ saha kaivalyabhāgīyaiḥ saṃskāraiś cittaṃ yaṃ puruṣaṃ prati caritaprayojanaṃ tasmāt nirvartate tasminvinivṛtte puruṣaḥ svarūpamātrapratiṣṭhaḥ kevalo mukta ity ucyate cittavṛttinivṛttir eva muktiḥ iti iti śrīgovindabhavgavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya paramahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrī śaṅkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śrīpātañjalayoga śāstra sūtrabhāṣyavivaraṇe prathamaḥ samādhipādaḥ athedānīṃ dvitīyaḥ sādhanapāda ārabhyate kaivalyasya sādhanaṃ samyagdarśanam yogasādhanāni ca yogadvāreṇa samyagdarśanasādhanāny eva tāni ca prādhānyenāsmin pāde pratipādyanta iti sādhanapāda ity ucyate tathā yogasādhanānuṣṭhānapravṛttasyānuṣaṅgikavibhūteḥ prādhānyena pratipādanād vibhūtipāda ity ucyate tṛtīyaḥ tathā sakalayogaiśvaryavibhūtibhyo viraktasya sarvopasaṃhāradvāreṇa kaivalyasya prādhānyena pradarśanāt kaivalyapāda ity ucyate caturthaḥ tathā samādhiḥ prādhānyenādāv upālbhyāta iti prathamaḥ samādhipāda ity ucyate tad etad āha uddiṣṭaḥ samāhitacittasya yoga iti karmaṇy acittasya ity arthaḥ maitrīkaruṇādibhāvanādyupā khyā yalabdhisthitipadasya yoginaḥ paravairāgyavirāmapratyayyasādhano nirbījaḥ samādhir uddiṣṭaḥ kathaṃ vyutthitacitto api yoga yuktaḥ syād iti vikṣiptacitto api kathaṃ nāma samādhiyogyo bhaved ity ata idam ārabhyate tapādisādhanam anukramyate tapas svādhyāya īśvarapraṇidhānāni kriyā yogaḥ nanu ca tapas svādhyāya īśvarapraṇidhānāni niyameṣu vadiṣyamāṇāni kim artham ihocyante nanu ca etad eva prayojanaṃ yad uktaṃ vyutthitacitto api yoga yuktaḥ syād iti na etad asti yatra niyamāḥ paṭhyante tatra evedaṃ prayojanaṃ sidhyati atha kleśatanūkaraṇārtham iti cet tasyāpi tatra evābhidhānāt yathā yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād aśuddhikṣaye iti aśuddhiś ca kleśādiḥ samdhibhāvanārthañ ca yogāṅgānuṣṭhānam āmnāyiṣyata eva yathā śamādhisiddhr īśvarapraṇidhānāt iti tasmād iha tapādisamāmnānam anarthakam na yogāṅgānuṣṭhānasya samyagdarśanopāyasya samyagdarśanapūrvatvapratipādanārthatvāt sarvāṇi ca yogāṅgāni samyagdarśanopāyatvāt samyagdarśanaprāk kālāni teṣāṃ ca niyamarkadeśa iha paṭhitaḥ sarvopāyaprākk ālatve nidarśanāya yady apy upāyatvād eva prāk kālatvam arthāt siddham tathā api spaṣṭatvam evaṃ sati syād iti nanu ca evam api prāk samyagdarśanād anantaraṃ paṭhitavyam ucyate na samyagdarśanasya eva sākṣātkleśādipratipakṣatvāt avidyā hi samastānarthamūlam sā ca sākṣāt pratyanīkabhūtasamyagdarśanena nirvartyate tapāades tadanantraṃ pāṭhe saty avidyāsamyagdarśanayor vyavadhānaṃ bhavet tato abhiśaṃkena kiṃ avidyāyās tapāadiḥ sākṣāt pratipakṣaḥ kiṃ vā samyagdarśanam eva iti kiñ ca viṣayaś ca prathamaṃ darśanīyaḥ samyagdarśanaśāstrasya sa ca kleśakarmavipākāśayābhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ yathā rogārtaḥ cikitsāśāstrasya viṣayaḥ tapādes tadanantaraṃ samāmnāne viṣayaviṣayiṇau vyavadhīyeyātāṃ tataś cāyaṃ viṣayo yañ ca viṣayīti na vivicyeta pādādau ca pāthe samyagdarśanopāyatvaṃ ca pratipāditaṃ bhavati prathamapādasambandhaś ca vyākhyātaḥ syāt samāhitacittasya yoga uddiṣṭaḥ vyutthitacitto api tapādisādhanaḥ kathaṃ yoga yuktaḥ syād iti kiñ ca samādhibhāvanakleśatanūkaraṇārthatvañ ca tapādīnāṃ darśayitavyam nanu parastād evaitad vakṣyati śamādhisiddhir iśvarapraṇidhānāt Y ṣ kāyendriyasiddhir aśuddhikṣayāt tapasaḥ Y ṣ ity evam pratyekasādhanānāṃ siddhiṃ ca vakṣyati na etad asti siddhānām iha tatra sādhanastutyartham anuvādāt atra hi tādarthyam ucyate tathā ca āha śamādhibhāvanārthaḥ kleśatanūkaraṇārthaś ca Y ṣ iti tatra hy anūdyante sādhanastutaye samprati sūtrākṣarāṇi vyākhyāyante tapaś ca svādhyāyaś ca īśvarapraṇidhānañ ca tapas svādhyāya īśvarapraṇidhānāni tāny eva kriyārūpo yogaḥ kriyāyogah tapādikriyā ca yogārthatvād yoga ity ucyate cittadharmo hi samādhir yogaḥ tadarthaś cāyaṃ kriyā yogaḥ tasmād anena kriyā yogena yogīti tapa iti kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādi śītoṣṇādidvandvasahatvam svādhyāyaḥ praṇavasya mokṣaśāstrāṇāṃ copanisatprabhṛtīnāṃ pavitrāṇāṃ japaḥ īśvarapraṇidhānaṃ kriyāṇāṃ paramagurāv īśvare samarpaṇam tāsāṃ vā phalasaṃnyāsaḥ parameśvare saṃnyasanam kathaṃ punaś cittasamādhānaṃ prati viprakṛṣṭasya kāyakleśādirūpasya tapaso yogatvam svādhyāya īśvarapraṇidhānayos tu yuktam antaraṅgatvād yogatvam iti tadartham āha nātapasvino yogaḥ sidhyatīti śarīrādipoṣaṇābhiratacittasya kāyendriyamanaḥkhed aparihārāyaṇasyātyantaśarīrādy ātmatvadarśinaḥ sukumārataraṃmanyasya na yogaḥ sidhyatīti tapasa upādānam kiñ cānādivāsanācitrā viṣayagrahaṇavāsanābhir anādikālabhir uparacitavicitrabhāvā tathā pratypasthitaviṣayajālā vartamānakālā viṣayā eva jālaṃ tena ca vartamānaviṣayākhyena jālena ānāyena jhaṣan iva cittaṃ acuddhiḥ pāśayati yā sā pratyupasthitaviṣayajalā satī yasmāt ṇaṇṭāṛeṇa tapasā vinā sambhedaṃ vināśam āpadyate asambhinnāśuddheś cittasya kutaḥ samādhiḥ iti tatsambhedanāya ca tapasa upādānam tac ca tapah cittaprasādanaṃ samādhyantaraṅgaṃ abādhamānam anenāsevyam iti yogā manyante cittaprasādārthatvāt tapasas tam eva ced bādheta tādarthyam eva hīyate sa hi kriyā yogaḥ kim artha iti tasya pārārthyapratipādanārtham āha samādhibhāvanārthaḥ kleśatanūkaraṇāyaś ca kathaṃ punar ubhayārthatvam ity āha sa hi āsevyamānaḥ samādhiṃ bhāvayati itara yogāṅgasahitaḥ samādhiṃ bhāvayati kleśāś ca tanū karoti vakṣyati ca yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād aśuddhikṣaye jñānadīptir ā vivekakhyāteḥ Y ṣ iti tad etad āha tanūkṛtān kleśān prasaṃkhyanena kleśatanūkaraṇāt sañjātasamyagdarśanaśīlanena dagdhabījakalpān bījānīva dagdhaprasavaśaktīn ata evāprasavadharmiṇaḥ avidyamānaḥ prasavo yeṣāṃ te aprasavāḥ aprasavāś ca te dharmiṇaś cety aprasavadharmiṇaḥ sarvabījādiṣu vā draṣṭavyam tānaprasavadharmiṇaḥ kariṣyati prasavaśaktirahitān kariṣyati teṣāṃ tanūkaraṇānujanmā punaḥ kleśair aparāmṛṣṭā satvapuruṣānyatāmātrakhyātiḥ samāptādhikārā prajñā pratiprasavāya kalpiṣyate saṃsārābhimukhatāyai punar na kalpiṣyate yady api śāstrācāryopadeśena yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād ṛte api satvapuruṣānyatāmātrakhyātir upajāyate tathā api na kleśādharmādīnatīvātiraskṛtya sā jāyateti punaḥ punaḥ kleśādibhiḥ parāmṛśyata ity etad darśayati punaḥ kleśair aparāmṛṣṭey anena ke te kleśāḥ svarūpeṇa kiyanto vā saṃkhyayā iti saṃkhyāsvarūpapratipādanārthaṃ sūtraṃ praṇīyate avidyā asmitā rāgadveśābhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ eṣām ekaikasya lakṣaṇaṃ sūtrair eva vyākhyāyiṣyata iti na vyākhyeyatve yatnaḥ kriyate vyākhyeyaṃ tv etāvad eva yathā pramāṇaviparyayavikalpādayaḥ parasparabhinnāḥ na tathā kleśānāṃ viparyayād bhedaḥ kintarhi viparyayasya evaite bhedā iti kasmāt viparyayabhāvabhāvitvād ity etad āha pañca viparyayā ity arthaḥ nanu ca yathā vṛttibhedavyākhyāne pramāṇavṛtteḥ pratykṣānumānāgamāḥ pramāṇāni iti tridhā bhedas tatra eva vyākhyātaḥ tathā kasmāt tatra evāsya viparyayasyāpi bhedaḥ pañcadhā nopavyākhyātaḥ cittavṛtter eva ca viparyaya ity uktam tathā codāhataṃśadviṣayeṇaikacandradarśanena dvicandradarśanaṃ bādhyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ kleśānām avṛttikatvāt na hi kleśāḥ pratyayamātrāḥ pratyayamātrā hi vṛttayaḥ kleśās tu cittasya malaṃ yathā cakṣuṣas timiram kleśamalaviyoge cittasya viparyayapratyayābhāvāt yadi hi pratyaya eva viparyayyaḥ tadā yathā kleśanirodhe api yoginaḥ smṛtipramāṇapratyayā bhavanti tathā viparyayo api bhavet na tu viparyayaḥ kṣīṇakleśānām tasmāc cakṣuṣa ivāyathārthagrahaṇanimittaṃ pratyayasya malaṃ viparyaya ity ucyate tat punaḥ pratyayavyatirekeṇa pratipattum ākhyātuṃ cāśakyam iti pratyayena evākhyāyate viparyayo vṛttiḥ iti tathā ca vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭākliṣṭaś ceti kleśena viśeṣitāḥ na ca vṛttibhr eva vṛttīnāṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ yuktam tathā kleśahetukā iti ca vyākhgyātam na ca vṛttaya eva vṛttihetukā iti yuktam tasmāc cāvṛttitvād vṛttibhedatvena na tatra kleśā vyākhyātāḥ tathā coktam cittamalaprasaṅgenabhidhāyiṣyante iti kleśānāṃ na vṛttitvaṃ malatvam eva ity abhiprāyeṇa abhedopacāreṇa tu pratyayena sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ yathā dhūmo malair agniṃ garbhādaśāntavṛttās tathā jñānam eteneti tathaivātrāpi pratyayaviparītatvam āha te spandamānā ityādinā spandamānāḥ pratyayadvāreṇodbhāsamānāḥ na hi svatas teṣāś calanam asti vastrādirāgavat guṇādhikāraṃ draḍhayanti guṇānām adhikāraṃ pravṛttiṃ saṃ kartavyatvaṃ sthirīkurvānti na hi teṣu parispandamāneṣu kartavyatā śūnyaṃ cittaṃ bhavati parīṇāmam avasthāpayanti punah punaḥ pariṇamayantīti yāvat kāryakaraṇasrota unnamayanti śarīrasya karaṇādīnāṃ cakṣur ādīnāṃ pravṛttisrota ucchrā va yayanti katham ity āha parasparānugrahatantrībhūtvā avidyā ādaya itaretaranimittanaimittikabhāveneti kiñ ca karmavipākāṃś cābhinirvartayanti karma trividhaṃ tadvipākāṃś ca jātyāyur bhogān iti avidyā kṣetram uttareṣāṃ prasupatatanuvicchinnodārāṇām katham asmitā ādayo viparyayā iti tat pradarśayate sūtreṇa eva avidyā kṣetraṃ prasavabhūmiḥ ātmalābhakṣetraṃ yathā pṛthivī tṛṇalatāgulm avīrudhāṃ svātmano natiriktānāṃ evam avidyāto viparyayād avyatiriktānāṃ asmitā ādīnāṃ caturṇām ekaikaśaḥ prasuptatanuvicchinnodāratayā caturvikalpānāṃ prasavabhūmir avidyā viparyayapratyayā hi tām āśritya ātmānaṃ pratilabhante tasmād acidyaivāsmitādicatuṣṭayarūpeṇa vipariṇamate tatra kā prasuptir iti asmitā ādīnāṃ prasuptir nāma dharma ucyate nāvidyāyāḥ kāraṇatvāt sarvāsmitādivikalpeṣv anugamāt sarvadā prabuddhā eva sā na prasuptā prasvapne vyavahārābhāvāt asmitā ādīnām anyatamasya prasuptāv anyatamasyāvasthānam avaśyam eva anyathā kleśāntarasya udbhava eva na syāt tasmād asmitā ādīnām eva caturṇāṃ prasuptādicaturvikalpatvam cetasi śaktimātrapratiṣṭhānam ity asya vyākhyānaṃ karoti bījabhāvopagama iti yathā bījaṃ sad evānaṅkurībhavad api bhūmigataṃ tiṣṭhati tathā cetasyāsmitādayaḥ śaktirūpeṇānabhivyaktasvarūpāṅkurā vyavatiṣṭhante tasya prabodha iti tasya kleśasyāsmitādeḥ prabodha udbhavaḥ ālambane viṣaye sammukhibhāvaḥ svavyañjakāñjanasya tatra etat syāt sarvadā eva kleśasya bījabhāvopagamaḥ prabodhaś ca niyamena syād iti tata āha prasaṃkhyānavataḥ samyagdarśanābhyāsavataḥ adagdhakleśabījasya yoginah saṃmukhībhūte apy ālambane nāsau bījabhāvopagamaḥ dagdhasya dagdhatvād eva kutaḥ punaḥ prabodhaḥ udbhavaḥ vidyamānasya hi bījasya kṣitijalādisaṃyoganimittaprāptāv aṅkurī bhāvo na dagdhabījaśakteḥ tathā kleśasyāpi yady evam eṣā pañcamī kasmād avasthā noktā dagdhaprasuptatanuvicchinnodārāṇam iti nāsādhāraṇatvāt na hi sarvadehināṃ sādhāraṇī pañcamī kleśāvasthā yogina eva hi sā tato nāmnāyate kathaṃ vā asādhāraṇīti tata āha tatra eva sā samyagdarśanābhyāsavaty eva dagdhā nānyatra kṣīṇakleśaḥ kuśalaś caram adeha iti samyagdarśana ucyate yogī tatra eva sā dagdhabījabhāvā pañcamī kleśāvasthā satāṃ kleśānāṃ tadānīṃ tagdhaṃ bījasāmarthyam yathā vidyamānānāṃ yavādibījānāṃ bharjitānāṃ bījasāmarthyaṃ dagdham viṣayasya sammukhī bhāve api na bhavaty eṣāṃ prabodhaḥ samyagdarśinaḥ saṃskāraśeṣāvasthatvadiṣor iva lakṣyavimuktasya uktā prasuptiḥ kiñ ca dagdhabījānāṃ ca kleśānām aprabodho yogina ukta iti tanutvaṃ idānīṃ ucyate pratipakṣabhāvanopahatāḥ pratipakṣasya śarīrādyavadyadarśanādeḥ bhāvanayopahatāh abalīkṛtā mandaprabhāvāḥ kleśās tanava ucyante tathā vicchidya vicchidyārthāntaropajanakālāntarāleṣu svātmānam apradarśayantaḥ tena tenātmanā yena rūpeṇa pūrvam upalabdhās tena eva ātmanā samudācaranti punar udbhavantīti vicchinnāḥ yadi vā vicchidya vicchidya vicchedakāle te vyaktenātmanā svarūpeṇa pūrvottarakālavat na samudācaranti tatrodāharaṇam kathaṃ rāgakāle krodhasyādarśanāt na hi rāgakāle krodhaḥ samudācarati kutaḥ rūpāriśayānāṃ vṛttyariśayānāṃ ca virodhāt sa hi rāgodayāttirobhūto nyenāvyaktenātmanā vartata iti vicchinnaḥ tathā rāgaś ca kvacid dṛśyamāno na viṣayāntare nāsti kutaḥ viṣayavirodhād atra pūrvatra rāgeṇa virodhād asamudācaraṇaṃ krodhasya atra tu viṣayāṇām anyonyavirodhāt na hi viṣaya ekasminn upajanayati rāgaṃ viṣayāntaram api tasya eva rāgasyotpādakam tad yathā na ekasyāṃ striyāṃ vcaitro rakta ity anyāsu viraktaḥ kin tu tatra rāgo labdhavṛttiḥ yasyāṃ raktaḥ anyatra bhaviṣyadvṛttiḥ anyāsu strīṣu sa hi bhaviṣyad rāgavyaktiviśeṣaḥ tadā prasuptas tanur vā iti nanu ca rāgaś kacit dṛśyamāna ityāddi bhāṣyaṃ kimarthaṃ nanu rāgasvabhāvākhyānaṃ ktthaṃ viṣayabhedāl labdhabhaviṣyadvṛttisvabhāvo rāga iti satyam tathāpi prakrāntānupayogaḥ prakrāntaṃ hi vicchedavyākhyānaṃ na ca etad vicchedavyākhyānam nāpi vakṣyamāṇodāravyākhyānnena sambandhaḥ tasya nirākāṅkṣatvāt evaṃ tarhi pūrvaśeṣa evāyaṃ katham evaṃ manyate prasuptatanūdāratvavtyatirekeṇa vicchittir nāma dharma eva nāsti katham yāvan na labdhavṛttis tāvat prasupta ity uktam pratipakṣabhāvanopahato mandapravṛttis tanur ity ucyate yaś cāpi labdhapravṛttiḥ sa udāra ity ākhyāyate vicchinno nāma sa bhavati yaḥ kvacid upalabdhaḥ punar upalabhyate yathā sarasvatīsrotaḥ na hi rāgodaye krodhaḥ kvacid api dṛśyate tasmānnityā na vicchittir nāma dharmo sti adarśanāt atrocyate yady adarśanād vicchedo nāsti tadā rāgasya kvacid dṛśyamānasyānyatrādarśanād abhāvo stu nanv astv evābhāvaḥ anyatrādarśanāt na hi kasmāt kvacit dṛśyamānatvād eva na hi viṣayāntarābhimukho na bhavatīti dharmiṇy api cetasi nāsti na hi cakṣuṣaḥ kadācid gajābhimukhaṃ na bhavatīti ghaṭābhimukhapravṛtaṃ sannāsti ghaṭābhimukhadarśanād eva tad etad āha kvacit dṛśyamāno na viṣayāntare nāstīty ādi tathā krodho api rāgeṇodbhūtenābhibhūtatvād vicchinnadarśano bhaviṣyati sarasvatīsrotovad eva sa hi viṣayāntare prasuptaḥ tanur vā tadābhimukhyenādṛśyamānaviśeṣatvāt kaḥ punaḥ prasuptivicchedayor viśeṣaḥ yāvatobhayatrādarśanam aviśiṣṭam ucyate pravṛttidarśanaprabandhasyāntarāvirodhinā anubaddhatvād adarśanaṃ vicchittir adagdhasya nanu ca evaṃ sati śa na hi tadā prasuptas tanur vā iti viruddhaṃ pravṛter adarśanaprabandho hi viṣayāntareṇa dṛśyate na viṣayāntābhimukhyasya vivakṣitatvāt viṣayāntarābhimukhyaṃ nāma yo rāgasya dharmaḥ sa hi tadā prasuptaḥ tanur vā na rāgaḥ sarvadā ātmanā eva rāgakāle sarvaviṣayeṣu na dṛśyate athavā vicchinodāharaṇāntarapratipādanārtham eva rāgaś ca kvacid ityādi bhāṣyam kathaṃ dviprakāro vicchedaḥ pradarśayuṣya ti te ekas tāvat pravṛttadarśanaprabandhasya virodhinā bhibhavāt sarvatrādarśanam yathā darśitaṃ rāgakāle lrodhasyādarśanād iti tathā yam anyo viṣayaviśeṣe dṛśyamānasya eva viṣayāntare prāptinimittasyādarśanam yathā caitrasya ekasyāṃ striyāṃ raktasyānyāsu satīṣv api rāgasyādarśanaṃ tatra labdhavṛttir anyatra na dṛśyata ity āha sa hi tadā prasuptas tanur vā na hi prasuptis tānavaṃ vā vivakṣyate yathā tathā vā bhavatu tatrādarśanaṃ vicchedatvena vivakṣitam viṣaye yo labdhavṛttiḥ sa udāraḥ nanu ca prasuptatanuvicchinnānāṃ kāryāsamarthānāṃ na kleśatā na hi prasuptas tanur vicchinno vā prasuptivicchittitanniyamāvasthāyāṃ kāryaṃ kartuṃ kṣamate na hy ajātaśśatrur upaghātāyālam vicchhinne vā pradeśe srotasi srātuṃ śakyam tasmād avidyā kṣetram uttareṣām ity etāvad evāstu kin tair akāryakṣamaiḥ prasuptatanuvicchinnair upadiṣṭaiḥ etad āśaṃkyāha sarve ca ete kleśaviṣayatvn nātikrāmantīti na hi śatruḥ prasupto janiṣyamāṇo vā nāpakariṣyati kas tarhi vicchinnaḥ prasuptas tanur udāro vā kleśaḥ na yuktam evaṃ bhedena vacanam ekam evodāharaṇam astu na codārāvasthāyā anyatra kāryaṃ kariṣyati satyam evam etat tathāpi parihāra ucyate kiṃ tu viśiṣṭānām evaiteṣāṃ apariktyuktakleśatvadhamakāraṇām eva vicchinnāditvam vicchinnādyavasthāyām api nāpagamadapakrtṛtvaśaktir ity adoṣaḥ tatkāle kāryākṣamatvam iti cet na pratipakṣavidhānārthatvād vacanasya na hi śatror adṛśyamānasya prasuptasya janiṣyamāṇasya vā na prativighātavyam śrūyate cendraḥ pratipakṣamayena diter garbham bhinad iti tatra kāraṇaṃ svayam eva prakaṭayati yathā eva pratipakṣabhāvanāto nivṛttis tathā eva svavyañjakāñjanena viṣayādinā abhivyakta iti yasmāt te punar abhivyaktāḥ punaś ca tirohitāḥ punar apy abhivyañjiṣyante ca tasmāt prasutādyavasthā api pratipakṣavidhānāya vaktavyā eva kleśatvānatikrāntatvāt idānīm upasaṃharati sarva evāmī kleśā avidyābhedāḥ kasmāt yasmāt sarveṣu asmitā ādiṣu avidyā eābhiplavate pratarati udbhūtā dṛśyate kiñca yad avidyayā vastvākāryate prakalpate tad anuśerate tadviṣayā upajāyante kleśāḥ rāgādayaḥ yathā stryādipiṇḍe heye api bhogyo yam ity avidyayā parikalpayātmābhimānaṃ kṛtvā rajyate dharmajñāne viparītaṃ prarikalpya dveṣṭi kathaṃ punas tad evānuśerate iti yasmāt viparyāsapratyayakāla evopalabhyante itaś cāvidyābhedāḥ yasmāt kṣīyamāṇām avidyām anu kṣīyanta iti avisyāpraṇāśānupraṇāśino hi kleśā asmitā ādayaḥ na hy asatyām avidyāyāṃ kaścid api kleśaḥ sambhavati tatrāvidyāsvarūpam āha ucyate kiṃ punar avidyāsvarūpākhyāne prayojanaṃ tat svayam eva bhāṣyakṛd ākhyāsyate avidyā mūlam asya kleśasantānasya ityādinā ajñāte ca kleśasantānamūlasvarūpe tan mūlonmūlanaṃ na śakyaṃ kartum iti tat svarūpam ākhyāyate anityāśuciduḥkhānātmasu nityaśucisukhyātmakhyātir avidyā katham anitye kārye nityakhyātiḥ nityam iti viparyayabuddhiḥ yathā dhruvā pṛthivī dhruvā sa candratārakā dyaiḥ amṛtā divaikasa iti nanu ca etasmān mantrāt pṛthivyādīnāṃ dhrutvaṃ pratīyate tatra katham eṣāṃ kāryatvam ucyate āpekṣikatvād adoṣaḥ manuṣyādyapekṣayā pṛthivyādayo dhruvāḥ kāryatvam anityatvaṃ casarvapramāṇasiddhaṃ śrutiṣu vacanāt dyair āsīn na pṛthivī nāntarikṣam ity ādiṣu siddham tathā aśucau paramabījabhatse paramodvegakare tyantaghṛṇāspade kārātmasadganīvāśucau kāye kathama pi sya bīmatsakatvam ity āha rathānādaśuciḥ garbhāśayasthānatvād aśuciḥ bījād aśuciḥ śklaśoṇitabījo hi kāyaḥ upaṣṭambhāt vātapittaśleṣmopaṣṭambhāt teṣāṃ cāśucitvaṃ prasiddham niṣyandāt prasvedamūtrpurīpādimalājasnaniṣyandāt nidhānād api maraṇāt mṛtasaṃbandhināṃ daśāhādyāśaucasmaraṇam nanu ca svabhāvato yady āśuciḥ kāyas tasya śaucavidhānama anarthakaṃ prāapnotīty ata āha kāyamodheyaśaucatvād iti śāstrata ādhātavyam eva śaucam asmin na svato stīti yāvat yad vā karaṇāni buddhisattvādīni sattvātmakatayā śucīnyādheyānyasminn iti tacchucitvād asyāpi śaucam buddhisattvādyādheyaviprayoge cātyantāśucitvadarśanāt tasmāt piṇḍatā hy aśuciṃ viduḥ piṇḍitagrahaṇaṃ viparyastadhiyāṃ śucitvagrahaṇakhyāpanārtham aśucau śucikhyātir dṛśyate viparītacetasām nanv eva śaśāākalekhā kamanīyā iyaṃ kanyā amṛtāvayavanirmitā iva candraṃ bhitvā iva nismṛtā jñāyate nīlotpalapatrākṣī bhāvagarbhābhyāṃ locanābhyāṃ jīvalokaṃ samāśvāsayantīti kasya kenābhisaṃbandho bhavatīti kva śarīrādi yāthātmyaṃ kva bhavaty evam aśucau kvacid vi śuciviparyāsa iti etenāpuṇye puṇyapratyayaḥ yathā saṃsāramocakānāṃ tathā evānarthe cārthapratyayo vyākhyātaḥ yathā taskarāṇām tathā duḥkhe sukhyakhyātiṃ vakṣyai pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhair guṇavṛttivirodhāc ca duḥkham eva sarvaṃ vivekinaḥ iti tatra sarvasmin saṃsāre duḥkhe sukhakhyātir avidyā tathā anātmany ātmakhyātir bāhyopakaraṇeu cetanācetateṣu gavādughaṭādiṣu bhogādhiṣṭhāne vā śarīre puruṣopakaraṇe vā manasy anātmany ātmakhyātir iti atrocyate kasya punar manasy anātmanu ātmakhyātir iti nanu manasa eva khyātiḥ kiṃ codyate yāvatā avidyā viparyayaś cittavṛttir iti hy uktam cittam eva prāptacaitanyopagrahaṇarūpatvād ātmānaṃ cetanam abhimanyate ahaṃ draṣṭṛ śrotṛ vā aham idaṃ mameti cāviśeṣeṇa tathaitad atra etasminn arthe uktaṃ vyaktam avyaktaṃ vā pradhānādikaṃ śarīrendriyādi viṣayaviśeṣaparyantaṃ kiṃcit vyaktaṃ ānubhāvikaṃ kiṃcid ānumānikam āgamikaṃ avyaktaṃ vā sattvam ātmatvenābhipratītaḥ pratipannaḥ tasya sampadam anunandati tasya vyaktāvyaktātmakasyātmatvenāvagatasya sampadaṃ samṛddhiṃ vibhūtim anu nandati anu hṛṣyati ātmasampadaṃ manvānaḥ sampanno ham anayā sampadā mamaiṣā sampad iti manyamānaḥ tasya vyāpadaṃ tasya kṣayaṃ anu śocati mamaiṣā vyāpadāham eva iti sa sarva evābhimānā apratibuddhiṃ ajña iti eṣā catuṣpadī bhavaty avidyā nanu cāpuṇye puṇyakhyātiḥ puṇye apuṇyakhyātiḥ ity ābhyāṃ saha ṣaṭpadītvam na catuṣv eva pādeṣu yathāsaṃbhavam antar bhāvāt avidyā mūlaṃ prabhavabījam asya kleśasantānasya abhiniveśāntakleśānām anavaratapravartanasya kiṃ ca karmāśayasya ca trividhasya jāñtyāyur bhogalakṣaṇavipākatrayasahitasya sakalasya saṃsārasya ity arthaḥ tasyāś cāvidyāyāḥ amitrāgoṣpadavad vastu satatvaṃ vastvantaratvaṃ vijñeyam kim artham idam ucyate yāvatā viparītakhyātir iti vastu satatvam uktam eva ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā iti nañ samāso yaṃ tatpuruṣaḥ sa ca uttarapadārthapradhāno vā syāt yathā rājapuruṣa iti yad vā pūrvapadārthapradhānaḥ ardhapiṣpalīti tatra yadi pūrvapadārthapradhānas tadānīṃ vidyāyāḥ pramāṇasyābhāva vādi iti yatraiva vidyāprasaṅgo vṛttisāmānyāt tatraiva smṛtya vṛttyantarādau pratītir ity karamāśayaḥ sati mūle tadvipākaḥ iti vakṣyate tasmāt te kleśā hātavyāḥ hānārthañ ca te pradarśitāḥ tadavahānau copāyaṃ vakṣyati dhyāna heyās tadvṛttayaḥ iti tatra na jñāyate kiṃviṣayo dhyānaprayogaḥ kiṃ dagdhabījakarmakleśaviṣayan kiṃ sarvaviṣayaḥ iti tādviṣayavibhajanārtham idaṃ sūtrem ārabhyate te pratiprasavaheyāḥ sūkṣmā iti te pañca kleśāḥ dagdhabījakalpāḥ yoginaś caritādhikāre cetasi pralīne dṛṣṭādṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ kleśā avidyā ādayo mūlaṃ janmakāraṇaṃ yasya karmāśayasya sa kleśamūlaḥ karmāśaya iti ākarmaphalapradānād antaḥkaraṇe śeta iti karamāśayaḥ śuklakṛṣṇātmakaḥ dṛṣṭaṃ cādṛṣṭaṃ ca dṛṣṭādṛṣṭe janmanī tayor vedanīyam anubhavanīyaṃ phalaṃ yasya sa dṛṣṭādṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ karamāśayaḥ yo dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakarmānubhavitavyaphalaḥ karamāśayaḥ sa kleśamūla iti sūtrārthaḥ yasya puṇyāuṇyarūpasya karmāśayasya yasmin janmani niṣpattis tasya tasmnn eva janmani vedanīyaṃ phalaṃ sa dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ yasya tu janmāntare vedanīyaṃ phalaṃ so dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ karmāśaya iti bhāṣyam idānīṃ vyākhyāyate tatra puṇyāpuṇyakarmāśayo lobhakrodhamohaprabhava iti kleśamūlatvaṃ tasya ācaṣṭe puṇyakarmāśayo lobhaprabhavo yathā svarge vā atra vā śubhaṃ phalam anubhaiṣyāmīti svargakāpaputrakāmayādādiḥ krodhaprabhavo yathā viśvāmitrasyāmbāyāś ca mohaprabhavo yathā draupadyāḥ kumbhakarṇasya ca apuṇyakarmāśayo api lobhavrabhavo yathā carmaṇī dvīpaniṃ hanti kuñjaraṃ hanti dantayoḥ karṇasya śāstrajñānalobhād aniṛtavacane krodhaprabhavo yathā brahmahatyā bhārate bhāve apy aśvatthāmnaś ca mohaprabhavo yathā saṃsāramocakādīnāṃ nahuṣasya ca asmitāvidyāyor lobhakrodhamohaiḥ tīvrataramohānuṣṭhānajane karmāśayena tiryaktvena pariṇata iti krodhādīnāṃ tu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭajanmavedanīyatvenodāharaṇāni vyākhyātāni pūrvam eva etena ca mandamandataralobhādikleśānuṣṭhānajanmānau puṇyapāpakarmāśayāvadrṣṭajanmavedanīyau vyākhyātau lokavad eva tatrapi tāvad ucyate tatra nārakāṇāṃ nāsti yair narakaprāptyartham eva karmānuṣṭhitaṃ adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ karamāśayaḥ kleśābhāvād eva na hi vītarāgo jāto dṛśyate kleśānāṃ karmārambha iva karmaphalārambheapi hetutvāt kṣīṇakleśasyāpi jñānaprāpteḥ prāg ārabdho dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ sambhavati karamāśayaḥ pravṛttiphalatvān muktaśaravad iti kiñ ca sati mūle tadvipāko jātyāyurbhogāḥ mūlaṃ hi karmaṇāṃ kleśaḥ asmin sati mūle kleśesu satsv ity arthaḥ tasya lobhakrodhaprabhavasya puṇyāpuṇyakarmāśayasya vipākaḥ phalaniṣpattiḥ atadvipākaḥ kiṃ punas tat phalam ity āha jātyāyurbhogāḥ bhāṣyaṃ satsu kleśeṣu karmāśayo vipākārambhī bhavati nocchinnakleśamūla iti mūlasyavyākhyānam tatra satsu kleśeṣu karmāśayo vipākārambhīty asya dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā tuṣāvanaddhāḥ śālitaṇḍulā adagdhabījabhā Vāḥ tuṣāvanaddhā api kadācid dagdhabījabhāvā na prarohasamarthā bhavanti dagdhabījabhāvā api vyapanītatuṣā na prarohāyālaṃ bhhavanti ubhayathā ca dārṣṭāntikapratipādanāṛthaṃ dṛṣṭāntavikalpaḥ katham tathā kleśāvvanaddhaḥ karṃāśayo vipākaprarohī bhavati kleśopabandhaḥ tuṣāvanaddhaśālitaṇḍulavat nāpanītakleśo na prasaṃkhyāna dagdhakleśabījabhāvo vā iti apanītatuṣālitaṇḍulavad apnītakleśo na vipākaprarohī yogāṅgānnuṣṭhānakleśakṣayapūrvasamyagdarśanānāṃ yoginām na tataś ca tādarthyacodanāḥ karmaṇāṃ bādhyeran atha prayāyeṇa janmārambhitvaṃ karmaṇām asaṃkhyeyatvāt kenacid eva phalam ārabdhaṃ nānyair iti tatra niyamānupapattiḥ kenārabdhaḥ kena vā neti tathā ca athāvināśa eva tathāpy avaśiṣṭasyārambhakālābhāvo mokṣābhāvaś ceti tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛttiśāstrārthavatvapratipādanārtham idaṃ vicāryate kim ekaṃ karma ekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇaṃ svargādiprāptinimitteṣu bahuṣu karmasu satsu atjaikaṃ karmānekaṃ janmākṣiptīti prathamā vicāraṇā viruddhapakṣadvayālambinī hi vicārāṇā ekā eva syāt dvitīyā vicāraṇā kim anekaṃ karmānekaṃ janma nirvartayati viruddhaphalam aviruddhaphalaṃ vā athānekaṃ karmaikaṃ janma nirvartayati viruddhaphalam aviruddhaphalaṃ vā kiñ cātaḥ na tāvad ekaṃ karmaikasya janmanḥ kāraṇam kasmāt bahuṣu karmasu satsv ekam eva karma janmaikaṃ nārabhata iti yady ekasya eva janmārabhitvaṃ tadā anādikālapracitasya saṃsārānāditvād ekaikena puruṣeṇāsaṃkhyeyam ekaikasmin janmani karma pracīyate viruddhaphalam aviruddhaphalaṃ ca tatrāvaśiṣṭasya pūrvajanmopacitakarmarācigatasya kasyacid eva bhaviṣyajjanmārmbhitvaṃ āhosvid idānīntanajanmakarmarāśigatasya kasyacid iti phalakramo na niyamyetteti anāśvāso lokasya kiṃ pūrvajanmakarmaṇā duṣṭenāduṣṭena vā phalam ārabdhavyam athedānīntanakarmaṇā duṣṭenāduṣṭena vā ity avisrambhāt na kaścid agnihotrādi kurvīta nāpi mokṣāya samīheta ity anāśvāsaḥ prasaktaḥ sa cāniṣṭaḥ idānīṃ prathamavicāraṇāyāṃ dvitīyaṃ pakṣaṃ nirākaroti na ca ekaṃ karmanekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam kasmāt ekaikasmiṃs tāvaj janmani anekaṃ karmānuṣṭhīyate tatra ekam eva cet karmānekasya janmavipākasya janmapariṇāmasya nimittaṃ bhavet tato avaśiṣṭasya ārabdhakāryād anyasya vipākakālābhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ sa cāpy aniṣṭaḥ phalakramāniyamś ceti pūrvadoṣo api na evaṃbhūtam aniṣṭam abhyupagantavyam yat tu brahmahatyādikarmaṇām ekaikasyānekajanmārambhitvaṃ tasya śāstragocaratvāt brahmahatyādi viṣayatvam evābhyupagamyate dvitīyavicāraṇāyām idānīṃ prathamaḥ pakṣo nirākriyate na cānekaṃ karmānekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam kasmād evaṃ nābhyupagamyate tad ucyate tad evānekaṃ janma yugamn na sambhavati ekasyānīśvarasya tataś ca krameṇa cācyamāne kim ekam anekaṃ janmārabhata iti tathā ca pūrvadoṣānuṣaṅgaḥ sarvatra prathamadoṣānuṣaṅgaḥ phalakramāniyamād anāśvāsa iti tasmāt evaṃ pakṣatrayānupapattāv idānīṃ siddhāntam upasaṃharati janma prāyaṇānrtare janmamaraṇayor antare madhye kṛtaḥ puṇyapāpakarmāśayaḥ prāyaṇābhivyaktaḥ yathā bījakṣetrasaṃskārasaṃyogo ṅkurabhāvābhivyaktikāraṇaṃ tathā prāyaṇam apy aviruddhānāṃ karmaṇām abhivyaktinimittam ekapradhadṛkena ekalolībhāvena samuccitaḥ ekībhūtaḥ ekam eva janma karoti tac ca janma tena eva prāyāṇbhivyaktātmanā karmaṇā labdhāyuṣkaṃ bhavati tasminn āyuṣi tyena eva karmaṇā bhogaḥ sampadyate yena janmāyuṣī kṛte yathā yena bījenāṅkuro nirvṛttas tena eva trivipāko abhidhīyate ayam aikabhāvikaḥ karmāśaya uktaḥ eka eva janmaprayojana ekabhavikaḥ dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyas tv ekavipākārambhī yathā putragrāmādikāmayāgaḥ dvivipākārambhī vā bhogāyur hetutvāt yathā āyurādikāmayāgaḥ trivipākārambhī vā nandīśvaranahuṣavat nanu ca nandīśvaranahuṣayor dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyatvaṃ trivipākārambhitvaṃ ca viruddham dṛṣṭaṃ hi janma nindīśvarasya manuṣyatvam yat punar nandīśvarasya devatvaṃ nahuṣasya cājagaratvaṃ tat dvayam apy adṛṣṭaṃ na hi manuṣyatva eva devatvaṃ saṃvedyaṃ nandīśvarasya nāpi devatva eva nahuṣasyājagaratvaṃ saṃvedyam iti kathaṃ trivipākārambhitvaṃ dṛṣṭajanmavedanītyatvaṃ ceti na eṣa doṣaḥ dṛśyamānajātiviśiṣṭam eva śarīraṃ tayor jātyantaratvena pariṇatam na ca yathā nyeṣāṃ dṛṣṭajātiviśiṣṭaśarīropamardena jātyantaropādānaniṣekādinimittāpekṣayā jātyantaraprāptiḥ tathā nandīśvaranahuṣayoḥ tasmāt trivipākārambhitvaṃ dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyatvaṃ cety udāhṛtam tatra trividhaḥ karmarāśir dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaś cādṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaś ca dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyas tv aniyatavipākaḥ kadācidbhogahetur ity ekavipākaḥ kadācid bhokāyurhetutvāt dvivipākaḥ kadācit jātyāturbhogahetutvāt trivipāko nandīśvaranahuṣayor iva adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyas tu dvividho niyatavipākaś cāniyatavipākaś ca niyatavipākas tu pradarśitaḥ tasmāj janmaprāyaṇāntare kṛta ity ādinā yas tv aniyatavipākaḥ sa trividho vakṣyate idānīṃ tu karmavipākajanito vāsanārāśir apara ākhyāyate kleśakarmavipakānubhavanirvartitābhiḥ kleśānubhavaś ca karmānubhavaś ca vipākānubhavaś ca kleśakarmavipakānubhavāḥ tair nirvartitābhiḥ vāsanābhiḥ saṃskāraiḥ anādikālasaṃmūrcchitam idaṃ cittaṃ citrīkṛtam iva paṭakuḍyādivat sarvato matsyajālaṃ granthibhir ivātataṃ vyāptam athaikaikasmin janmani anekabhavapūrvikā vāsanāḥ karmaṇi vipāke ca tad aṅgī bhāvena vyāpriyante na hi vāsanāyāḥ karmavipākānaṅgabhāve sati jātamātrasya pṛṣadaṃśdārakasya vṛṣayuvānaṃ prati sphuritaparikopasyāvaskandanaṃ jāghaṭīti na ca sakṛd anubhavavāsanāmātratayā tena śakyaṃ bhavitum yas tv ayaṃ karamāśayaḥ yas tv ayaṃ janmaprāyaṇāntare kṛto bhiruddhajanmadeanimittaḥ pradhānopsarjanībhāvena trivipākārambhī eṣa evaikabhavika uktaḥ na dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ nāpy aniyatavipaktir adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ nāpi ca vāsanāḥ tāsāṃ tāvat svarūpam ye saṃskārāḥ smṛtihetavas tā vāsanās tāś cānādikālīnāḥ saṃsārasya kleśakarmavipakānubhavarūpasyānāditvāt yas tv asāvānandamahodanvattaraṅgāyamāṇaḥ ekabhavikaḥ karamāśayaḥ pūrvoktas tasyāpavāda ucyate ukedeśasya kathaṃ sa niyatavipākaś cāniyatavipākaś ca ko sau niyatavipākaḥ yaḥ prāyaṇābhivyaktaḥ kāryam ārabhate sa eva ca ekabhavikaḥ yas tv viruddhajnamadeśakālanimittaḥ so dṛṣṭajanmavedanīyatvasāmānye saty apy aniyatavipākaḥ kasmāt niyatavipākena virodhāt na cāyam ekabhavikaḥ virodhād eva yat tv asya ekabhavikatvam uktaṃ yas tv asāv ekabhavikaḥ karmāśaya iti tad adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyatvasāmānyena nanu ca yady evaṃ janmaprāyaṇāntare kṛtaḥ puṇyapāpakarmāśayaḥ pracayavicitraḥ pradhānopasarjanabhāvenāvasthitaḥ prāyaṇābhivyakta ekapraghattena sammūrcchita ekajanma karotīty evamādiniyamo virudhyeta kutaḥ prāyaṇasya sarvapūrvakarmābhivyañjakatvāt āśayādhāropamardena cāśayāntarotpatteḥ mānuṣyakāśayādhāre pūrvaṃ daivatairyagyonāśayānāṃ samavasthānaṃ ekadeśaparityāgenābhibyanakti pradīpaḥ atrocyate na etad yuktaṃ karmānarthakyaprasaṅgāt bahuprakārāṇi hi karmāṇi parasparaviruddhāni kriyante yo hi svargārthaṃ karma kṛtavān sa eva paśukrāmādyarthaṃ karmānuṣṭhāya punar brahmahatyāṃ vā sthāvarādiprāptyarthaṃ vā balavatkarmānutiṣṭhetṭatra narakasthāvarādiprāptasya na hi paśugrāmādilābhasaṃbhavaḥ tataś ca tatkarmaṇām ānarthakyaṃ prasajyeta atha tatrāpi grāmādilābhasukhaṃ bhavatīti cet na hi gramakāma ity ukte grāmasukhatvam abhipretam na hi grāmasukhaṃ prāpto grāmaṃ prāptavān kiñ ca sarvaśāstraviprakopaś ca syāt adṛṣṭānāṃ ca svarganarakādīnāṃ sukhaduḥkhamātraprasaṅgaḥ tataḥ śeṣeṇa iti śṣasadbhāvajñāpanaśrutismiṛtayo bādhyeran tasmānnityā na sarvaṃ karma prāyaṇe bhivyajyate atyantaviruddhānāṃ karmaṇām ānarthakyaprāpteḥ karmaśāstrānarthakye ca mokṣaśāstre apy anāśvāsaprasaṅgaḥ abhivyañjakānām api kasyacid abhivyañjakatvaṃ kasyacinneti dṛśyate vyabhicāraḥ yathā cakṣuṣo rūpābhivyañjakatve api caitrolūkacakṣuṣor evābhivyaktiḥ tatra karmādyapekṣayā virodhād adoṣa iti cet ihāpi virodhād anabhivyaktiḥ sarvakarmaṇām na cāpi bījādhāre kṣetre upamardyamāne jalādinimittasaṃyoge saty api tad gatānāṃ bījānāṃ biruddhajātīyānām aṅkurādikāryārambhitvam evaṃ mānuṣyakālīnāśayādhāre apy upamardyamāne na viruddhajātīyadevatairyagyonāśayānāṃ sarveṣāṃ yugapadvṛttilābhaḥ na ca prāyaṇam eva karmaṇām abhivyañjakam prāyaṇabhedaḥ tasmān nityā na sarvakarmābhivyañjakatvaṃ prāyaṇasya anyathā viśeṣaṇānarthakyaprasaṅgāt na ca smaraṇādiviśeṣaṇena prakṛtasyānyathātvaṃ nāśo vā syāt tannāśānyathātvakaraṇe hi smaraṇasya prakṛtakrmasahakāritvaṃ na syāt svatantraṃ hi smaraṇaṃ syāt tathā cānuṣṭhitakarmanairarthakyaṃ bhavet kiṃ ca kalalādyavasthāsu bhṛtānāṃ mokṣaprasaṅgaḥ karmānārambhāt tāsāṃ phalatvavatt karmatvam apīti cet na karaṇāvyūhāt karaṇeṣu hi vyūhiteṣu karmaṇāṃ vṛttilābhaḥ phalatvaṃ ca na tadā tadvyūha upapadyate svapnavad iti cen na tatrāpi karmānabhyupagamāt śrutiś ca sa yat tatra kiṃcit paśyaty iti mokṣaprasaṅga eva garbhaprasṛtānām āpatita iti tasmānnityā na sarvakarmābhivyañjakatvaṃ prāyaṇānāṃ teṣāṃ ca cviśeṣopapatter ity ata idam ucyate tatrādṛṣṭajanmavedanīyasya nityatavipākasya evāyaṃ niyamo yo sau janmaprāyaṇāntare kṛta ity evamādibhāṣyeṇa trivipākārambhitvaniyama uktaḥ na tu adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyasyāniyatavipākasya kasmāt yas tv adṛṣṭajanmavedanīyaḥ aniyatavipākas tasya trayī gatiḥ katham kṛtasyāvipākasya vināśaḥ nāśakālam aprāptasya eva nāśaḥ yathā prāyaścittādinā pratiṣiddhasya kṛtasya nāśaḥ pradhānakarmaṇy āvāpagamanaṃ pradhānakarmaṇi niyatavedanīye āvāpāpattiḥ
