kleśakarmavipakātmakatvam yad vā pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhatvam atas te triparvāṇas tāpā anuplavante anuṣajyanti ta me d evaṃ avivekaṃ pratipattāram anādiduḥkhasrotasohyamānam ātmānaṃ ca duḥkhasrotasi magnaṃ tathā bhūtagrāmaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā yogī sarvaduḥkhakṣayakaraṃ samyagdarśanaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadyata iti nanu ca yogitvād eva samyagdarśanaṃ pratipannaḥ ucyate yogāṅgānuṣṭhānād eva yogitvaṃ ṛte api samyagdarśanāt tasmāt samyagdarśanasādhanatvaṃ yogasya darśayati yogaṃ yogaphalaṃ ca samvam eva duḥkhaṃ paśyan samyagdarśanaikaśaraṇaṃ pratipadyate tathā ca vakṣyati tadvairāgyād api doṣabījakṣaye kaivalyam iti itaś ca sarvaṃ duḥkhaṃ vivekinaḥ kutaś ca guṇvṛttivirodhāc cāpi nanu ca kimarthaṃ sūtre pṛthag bibhaktikriyā yāvatā pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraguṇavṛttivirodhair ity eva kartavyam na eṣa doṣaḥ sukhaduḥkhānubhavatadvāsanāḥ sarvajanaprasiddhā iti pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhair iti nirdiṣṭāḥ tatkāraṇavibhāgajñānaviśāradasya eva vivekaprakarṣavato guṇavṛttivirodhā vijñeyā iti pṛthakkaraṇam sarvaduḥkhahetutvasāmānyāt tv ekasūtravinyāsaḥ guṇāḥ sattvādayaḥ teṣāṃ vṛttayo guṇavṛttayaḥ tāsāṃ virodhād guṇavṛtivirodhāt te ca guṇā antaḥkaraṇādyākārasanniviṣṭāḥ teṣāṃ guṇapradhānabhāvenābhinnapariṇāmatvāc ca viruddhavṛttitvaṃ bhavati anyatamavṛttirudbhavantyā nyatamavṛttyābhibhūyate evaṃ trayāṇām api pratikṣaṇa pakṣa m anyonyavṛttitiraskāra itaretaravṛttyudbhāvitvaṃ ca na sukhaduḥkhamohātmakānāṃ guṇānām anytamavṛttilābho nyatamānanusaṃhitaḥ tata etat siddhaṃ bhavati yadā duḥkhātmakaṃ raja udbhavati tadā duḥkhatvād eva tadvṛtter na duḥkham iti vaktavyam sattvatamasor api rajo nugatir asty eva iti tayor api duḥkhatvam eva sattvatamaḥpravṛttinivṛttyor api rajovyāpārānujatvād duḥkhatvam eva sarvasya iti etad upavyācaṣṭe prakhyāpravṛttisthitiśīlābhir vṛttibhir guṇāḥ parasparānugrahatantrāḥ parasparairysshā api parasparopakāryopakārakabhāvena tailavartyagnivat śāntaṃ sāttvikam ghoraṃ rājasaṃ mūḍhaṃ tāmasaṃ pratyayaṃ triguṇam eva ārabhante i tare tarayor aṅgabhāvenānugatatvād yadā sāttvikaḥ śāntaḥ pratyaya udbhūyaḥ so nantaram evodbubhūṣatā tamo nusaṃhitena ghoreṇa rājasena pratyayena hanyate yadā ca rāsaso ghoraḥ pratyāya itaraguṇānugata udbhūto bhavati so nanntaram evodbubhūṣatā tāmasena pratyayena mūḍhena sattvānugatena sāttvikena vā tamo nugatena hanyate tathā tāmas O pītarapratyāyābhyāṃ paryāyeṇa tathā sāttvikena itarāv ity anoyonyodayābhibhavapravṛttayā guṇāḥ kasmāt yataḥ phalaṃ guṇavṛttaṃ guṇasvabhāvatvaṃ cittākāreṇa guṇāḥ sanniviṣṭā iti kṣiprapariṇāmaṃ cittam uktam kva tantre kasmāt punar guṇā virudhyanta iti anekātiśayānām ekatrāsambhavāt yathā apavarake tamaḥprakāśayor atiśayavatoḥ evam antaḥkaraṇākārasanniveśināṃ sukhaduḥkhamoharūpāṇāṃ prakāśapravṛttiniyamavṛttīnāṃ guṇānāṃ rūpeṇa ā sukhādinā vṛttyā vā jñānādilakṣaṇayā yugapad atiśayo na sambhavati sāmānyānāṃ tv avirodhād avyaktarūpāṇām ati Vayair vyaktaiḥ saha vṛtti yuktā tena rūpātiśayā vṛttyatiśayāś ca virudhyante sāmānyāni tv atiśayaiḥ saha vartante ity ucyate yadā sukharūpātiśayas tadā na duḥkharupātiśayo māṃharūpātiśayo vā tathā itarātiśaye netarātiśayaḥ tathā jñānavṛttyatiśaye na lobhapratyayavṛttyatiśayaḥ tathā anyatamavṛttyaticaye nānyatamavṛttyatiśayaḥ evam ete guṇā itaretaropāśrayopārjitasukhaduḥkhamohapratyayāḥ sattvena rajastamaupāśrayeṇopārjitaḥ sukhapratyayaḥ rajasāpi sattvatamaupāśrayeṇopārjito duḥkhapratyayaḥ tamasāpi sattvarajaupāśrayeṇopārjito mohapratyayaḥ tataḥ sarve sarvakāryā bhavanti yady evam ayaṃ pratyayaḥ sāttvikaḥ tāmaso yaṃ rājasaś cāyam iti viśeṣaḥ ka ity āha guṇapradhānabhāvakṛtas tv eṣāṃ viśeṣa iti pradhānopsarjanatayā saṃjñālābhālābhau yathā pāñcabhautikatve api pārthivaṃ taijasamāpyam iti yata evaṃ guṇavṛttivirodhaḥ tasmāt sarvam eva duḥkhaṃ vivekina iti guṇavṛttivirodhād ity etat paravairāgyārtham kathaṃ pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhair iti dṛṣṭānuśravika viṣayavitṛṣṇasya eva sarvasya duḥkhapratipādanārthaṃ pṛthagvibhaktikaṃ kṛtam na hi tatra duḥkhatvam apaśyato vairāgyam upakalpyata iti etat tu guṇavṛttivirodhāc ceti guṇānāṃ parasparavirodhivṛttitvena duḥkhapratipādanāt tebhyo vyaktāvyaktadharmakebhyaḥ paraṃ vairāgyam upakalpyata ity evam artham tathā ca atrāpi pradhānopasarjanabhāvena sarve sarvarūpā bhavantīti vyaktāvyaktadharmatvaṃ pratipāditam evaṃ ca kṛtvā sūtre api guṇavṛttivirodhāc ceti pṛthak paṭhitam pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhadharmatvāt tasyaitasya mahato guṇagauṇalakṣaṇasya duḥkhasamudāyasya prabhavabījam avidyā tasyāś ca samyagdarśanam abhāvahetuḥ pratipakṣatvāt bhūtārthāśrayatvād vidyāyā abhūtārthāśrayatvāc cāvidyāyā vidaivābhāvahetuḥ yathā sadviṣayeṇa ekacandradarśanenāsadviṣayasyānekacandradarśanasya bādhanam saha duḥkhanidānena kleśakarmavipakalakṣaṇena sarvaṃ duḥkham ity upapāditam anena duḥkhena yo duḥkhī vivekī sa etasya samyagdarśanaśāstrasya viṣayaḥ adhikṛto netaro duḥkhasya eva pratipattṛtvād ity etad dṛṣṭāntena pratipipādayiṣyann āha yathā cikitsāśāstraṃ caturvyūham rogo rogahetur ārogyaṃ bhaiṣajyam iti roherogahetumāṃs tannivivartayiṣui bhaiṣajyasya śāstrasyārogyasya prayojanasya viṣayaḥ evam idam api śāstraṃ caturvyūham eva yathā saṃsāraḥ saṃsarahetur mokṣo mokṣahetuḥ tatra duḥkhabahulaḥ saṃsāro heyaḥ pradyānapuruṣasaṃyogo heyahetuḥ saṃyogasyātyantikī nivṛttir hānam hānopāyaḥ samyagdarśanam ity ete catvāro vyuhāḥ yathā cikitsāśāstraṃ roge rogahetau ca ārogye ca tatprayojanake bhaiṣasye ca catuṣtaye svarūpapratipādanāya vyūhitaṃ tata eva ca rogādayo asya catvāro vyūhā iti caturvyūham tathā asya śāstrasya duḥkhabahulaḥ saṃsāraḥ heyaḥ avidyāhetukaś ca pradhānapuruṣasaṃyogo hetuḥ sanimittasya saṃsārasya hānaṃ samyagdarśanaśāstrasya prayojanaṃ tathā samyagdarśanaṃ ceti catvāra vyūhā asyāpīti caturvyūham śāstram eṣu vā rtheṣu caturdhā vyūho sya iti caturvyūham tatra hātuḥ svarūpam iti nanu draṣṭā dṛśimātraḥ iti hātṛ lakṣaṇasūtra etad viditavyam na eṣa doṣaḥ śāstrārambhaprayojanapratipipādayiṣuṇā kleśādikaḥ samasto duḥkhāvasānaḥ so asya śāstrasya viṣaya upapāditaḥ tasya vivekinaḥ śāstramataḥparam ārabhyante etac ca prathamasūtre pradarśitam ārambhyamāṇasya śāstrasya samyagdarśanam eva prayojanam tac ca saṃsāraduḥkhanirvarṇanānantaram avasaraprāptaṃ pratipādayitavyam ity etad ucyate tatra hātuḥ svarūpam iti hātā puruṣaḥ tasya svarūpam upādeyaṃ vā heyaṃ vā na bhavati kuta etad evam heyopādeyavyatikekeṇa vastvadarśanāt yathā loke sukhaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ copādeyaṃ duḥkhaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ ca heyam evam ayam api puruṣo vastutvād anyataradharmā bhavitum arhatīty abhiprāyaḥ kim ato yady evam ata etad bhavati hāne tv asyocchedavād aprasaṅga iti yady asau heyatvadharmā tata eṣa hātavyaḥ hāne tv asya kiṃ syāt ātmocchedavād aprasaṅgaḥ syāt ataḥ ko doṣaḥ syāt doṣaṃ kaivalyapāde pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ kiñ cānyat asya hātrantarasya kiñcānyatarasya abhāvād dhānānupapattitvam svayam eva ātmana ātmā hāteti cet na svātmani kriyāvirodhād bhedābhāvāc ca heyād ātmana ātmana hātā ced anyas tadā nanvasthāsaṅgaḥ yo yo hātā tasyāpi heyatvāt na ca yugapaddvyor hātroḥ saṃbhavo ati bhinnakālabhāvinos tu heyahātṛtvānupapattiḥ hātuś ca heyatvābhyupagame tasyānavasthitatvād dheyasambandhānupapattiḥ hātur anavasthitatve ca svayam eva heyatvapratipatter hātur hānāyodyamānarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ hānaphalānupapattiś ca na hi baddhasya svarūpanāśa eva phalam mokṣo hi tasya phalam nāpi mriyamāṇo api jñātakṣaṇāntaramaraṇaḥ svarūpavināśam icchati vināśasyāthaprāptatvād evam anavasthitaś ced dhātā na svarūpahānam icchet arthaprāpter hānasya yathā ca hātur nityatvaṃ tathā draṣṭṛ sūtre kaivalyapāde ca vyākhyāsyāmahe tasmānnityā na heyatvadharmā puruṣaḥ saṃsāras tu mahadādivyaktiḥ duḥkhabahulo heyaḥ tat tulyadharmakaḥ puruṣo na bhavatity arthaḥ tattulyadharmakatve tasyocchedavād aprasaṅga iti astu tarhy upādeyaḥ yathā sukhārthaṃ sukhakāraṇaṃdravyam na etad evam kasmāt upādāne tv asya hetuvādaprasaṅgāt tasya dravyādyupādānaphalena sambandhaḥ sa cedupādīyeta tannirhetukamasya upādānaṃ syāt anyasyopādātur abhāvāt na hi paṭaḥ paṭena eva upādīyate anyasya hy anyad upādeyam upādātrantarasambhave hi tadanavasthāprasaṅhaḥ so apy anyenopādīyate so api cānyeneti kiṃ ca pārārthyaprasaṅgaś ca anyasya hi hetor anyad upādīyate sattvādilakṣaṇasya pradhānasyopādāne puruṣo hetur abhyupeyate yathā ghaṭāya mṛtpiṇḍopādāne kilālo hatuḥ sa cet puruṣaḥ pradhānopādānahetuḥ pradhānavad upādīyeta tasyāpi sattvādidharmatvaṃ syāt upādeyatvān mṛt piṇḍavat tato asya pradhānasya nirhetukaṃ kāryārtham upādānaṃ prāpnoti atha īśvarārtham upādeyaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ vā parasparārtham iti cet bhogyatvācetanatvapariṇāmitvādidoṣasāmagrī prasajayeta tasmānnityā nāpi pradhānadharmakaḥ puruṣa ity upādāne ca hetuvādaprasaṅga ity ucyate tad uktam hetus tv apuruṣo bhavatīti tasya copādāne ahetuḥ pradhānavṛttirnirhetukī syāt na ca svayaṃ svārthaṃ śakyaṃ vijñātum prakāśādiṣu svārthatvād adarśanāt ubhayapratyākhyāne heyatvopādeyatvapratyākhyāne śāśvatavādaprasaṅgaḥ ātmanityatvavādaprasaṅgaḥ yady api pradhānasyopādeyasyāpi śāśvatatvaṃ tathāapi vikārātmanā tad aśāśvatam eva anekātmakatvam aśucitvam avidyātvaṃ parārthatvam ity evamādayo doṣāḥ pradhāne puruṣāṇām api tathātve saty anirmokṣaprasaṅgaḥ bandhomokṣayos taddhetvoś ca vidyāvidyayoḥ svarūpāvyatirekād bandhamuktayoś ca nirviśeṣatvaprasaṅgāt tasmād dheyopādeyatvapratyākhyānena śāśvatavāda ity etad eva samyagdarśanam yathā cikitsyavyatiriktarogādicatuṣṭayam antareṇa cikitsāśāstram ārogyaprayojanaṃ caturvyūham na saṃbhavati tathedam api hātṛ svarūpavyatiriktaheyādicatuṣṭayam antareṇa samyagdarśanaśāstraṃ hānaphalaṃ caturvyūham na sambhavatīti heyādicatuṣṭayapratipādanena tad etacchāstraṃ caturvyūham abhidhīyate katham heyaṃ duḥkham anāgatam duḥkham atītam atikrāntaṃ vartamānāj janmano tikrāntajanmalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkham tadupabhogenātivāhitam atinītaṃ na heyapakṣe vartate svayam eva hīnatvāt vartamānaṃ ca yajjanmalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhan svakṣaṇopabhogārūḍham svaṃ vartamānaṃ bhogaviśiṣṭaṃ kṣaṇamadhvānam upabhujyam ānātmakatvenārūḍhaṃ tat duḥkhaṃ na kṣṇāntare heyatām āpadyate svayam eva bhogena hīnaṃ na hānāya kṣaṇāntaram apekṣate tasmād yad evānāgataṃ prāyaṇānantarabhāvijanmaduḥkhalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ tad evākṣipātrakalpaṃ yoginaṃ kliśnātīti tad eva heyaṃ samyagdarśanena hānīyam ucyate bhaviṣyajjanmābhāvāyaiva yatitavyam na vartamānaduḥkhanirodhāya vartamānajanmayiyatiṣāyāṃ hi samyagdarśanam aśaktyaviniyogatvād anarthakaṃ syāt muktabāṇavat pravṛttaphalatvād vartamānaduḥkhasya bhaviṣyati punar apravṛttatvād bījanirodha upakalpata iti samyagdarśanārthavattvam svaviṣayo hi samyagdarśanasya sa iti tad etac śāstraṃ caturvyūham abhidhīyata ity uktam ekaś caturṣuvyūhaḥ pratipāditaḥ heyaṃ duḥkham anāgatam iti idānīṃ dvitīyovyūhaḥ tasya duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ hetuḥ pratinirdiśyate nanu nirdiṣṭam eva duḥkhakāraṇam iti tathaivopasaṃhṛtam ante tasyaitasya mahato suḥkhasamudāyasya prabhavabījam avidyeti satyam evam kin tu duḥkhasvarūpamātraṃ tatkāraṇasvarūpamātraṃ ca pūrvaṃ nirdiṣṭam na ca tatsvarūpamātre iti tatkāraṇaṃ nirdiśyate draṣṭṛdṛśyayoḥ saṃyogo heyahetuḥ draṣṭā buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī puruṣo vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇaḥ pratisaṃvedituṃ śīlam asya sa pratisaṃvedī kasya buddher iti dṛśyā buddhiḥ antaḥkaraṇaṃ pratyayarūpeṇa nanu ca cabdādayo api viṣayā dṛśyā eva ity ata āha sattvopārūḍhāḥ sarve dharmāḥ śabdādayo buddhisattvam upārūḍhā buddhipratyayākārā eva dṛśyā na svataḥ svataś ca dṛśyatve jñātājñātaviṣayatvaṃ puruṣasya syāt sadā jñātaviṣayatvaṃ ca puruṣasya nyānena sthāpyate tasmād buddhyupārūḍhā eva sarve dharmā dṛśyāḥ tad etad dṛśyam ayaskāntamaṇikalpam ayaso api kriyā arthena eva upakartā yaskāntamaṇir yathā tathā puruṣasya puruṣārthena dvividhena bhogāpavargalakṣaṇena upakartṛtvād ayakāntamaṇir iva svaṃ dṛśirūpasya cittatvarūpamātrasya svṃminaḥ kathaṃ svam ity ata āha karmaviṣayatvam āpannaṃ karmaiva viṣayaḥ karmaviṣayaḥ karmatvāpattir eva viṣayo dṛśirūpasya dṛśyatām āpanna ity etat katham bhūtaṃ satkarmaviṣayatām āpadyata iti tadviśeṣaṇārtham āha anyasvarūpeṇa pratilabdhātmakam iti anyasvarūpeṇ asvaparapuruṣarūpeṇādirūpeṇa ca pratilabdhātmakaṃ pratilabdhaviśeṣarūpaṃ pratilabdhapuruṣaśabdādiviśeṣasvabhāvaṃ puruṣasvarūpeṇa labdhātmakaṃ saddṛśyatvena karmatām āpannam apavargārthena svaṃ bhavati śabdādyākāreṇa labdhātmakaṃ saddṛśyatvena karmatām āpannaṃ bhogārthena svam bhavati nanu kathaṃ svatantrasya svatvam na hi kiñcit svatantraṃ svayaṃ vyāpriyamāṇam anyad apekṣate yad api svavyāpārānuniṣpādipuruṣārtharūpaṃ tad api svabhāvād eva na puruṣaniyogakārī tasmāt svatantrasya sataḥ svatvaṃ na yuktam ity ata āha svatantram api puruṣāṛthdvayakartṛtvena parārthatvāt paratantram tataś ca svam eva tayor drgdarśanaśaktyor iti draṣṭṛdṛśyayor ity upkramya dṛgfarśanaśaktyr ity upasaṃhāraḥ buddhipuruṣasaṃyogasya buddhyutpattyanantarabhāvitvād ādimattvam āśaṅkya tadanādimattvapradarśanārthaṃ kriyate dṛgdarśanaśaktyor anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ darmiṇāṃ nityatvāt nityasambandhopapattes tacchaktyor api draṣṭṛdṛśyatvalakṣaṇo nādiḥ saṃyogo rthakṛtaḥ puruṣārthaprayojavavaśa ity arthaḥ tathā ca saty anāditve api prayojananivṛttau saṃyoganivṛttir upapadyate karmiṇāṃ tu svarūpasaṃyogaḥ sattāmātreṇa na prayohjanakṛta iti nitya eva dharmamātrābhis tv anityābhir anityaḥ saṃyogaḥ sa tu buddhipuruṣasaṃyogo heyahetuḥ duḥkhasya kāraṇam ity arthaḥ tathā caoktaṃ tantre tatsaṃyogahetuvivarjanāt tayor buddhipuruṣayoḥ saṃyogas tasya hetur avidyā yadvivarjanāṭ kathaṃ vivarjanam vidyayā samyagdarśanena tatpratipakṣeṇa nirvartanāt tasmāt tatsaṃyogahetuvivarjanāt ātyantiko tyantāya prabhavati duḥkhapratīkāraḥ ko sau yatsamyagdarśitvam katham etad iti prasiddhaṃ dṛṣṭāntam āha tad yathā pādatalasya bhedyatā sukhamārataratvāt kaṇṭakasya bhoktṛtvaṃ karkaśasvabhāvatvāt tatsaṃyogo viśiṣṭo duḥkhahetur ity arthasiddham tatra kaṇṭakavyathāduḥkhasya parihāraḥ kaṇṭake padā pādenānadhiṣṭhānam etad dvayaṃ yo veda bhedyabhettṛdvayaṃ parihāradvayaṃ vā yo veda loke sa tatrānyataraṃ parihāram ārabhate sa tatra pratī Kāramāramamāṇo bhedajaṃ kaṇṭakabhedajanitaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāpnoti tathehāpi puruṣaḥ sattvadvāreṇa kaṇṭakasthānīyaṃ pradhānam tayor viśiṣṭaḥ saṃyogo vidyamātraviśeṣebhyo dṛśyebhyo nirapekṣatā samyagdarśanena prayojanābhāvaṃ buddhvā puruṣasyāvikriyatvāt kaṇṭakādhiṣṭhānavaccharīrārambhiṇo vā karmaṇo niyatavedanīyatvād avvaśyaṃ phaladāyitvaṃ buddhvā aprārthitopanatānāṃ śabda ādīnāṃ samyagdarśanavyavahitena sattvena bhogaḥ evaṃ parihāraṃ sañjānānaḥ kaṇṭakabhedaduḥkhaparihāram iva saṃsāraduḥkhaṃ nāpnoti kasmād etad evam iti tritvopalabdhisāmarthyāt pradhānapuruṣasaṃyogatritvopalabdhisāmarthyāt evaṃ hi vijñānasya sāmarthyaṃ dṛśyate pādatalakaṇṭakatatsaṃyogeṣv ajñānasya ca tritvānupalabdher duḥkhahetutvaṃ dṛśyata eva etam arthaṃ pracikhyāpayiṣann āhātrāpi tāpakasya rajasaḥ yady api pradhānaṃ kaṇṭakasthānīyaṃ tāpakaṃ tathāpi rajaso duḥkhātmakatvād rajodvāreṇa eva pradhānasya tāpakatvam ity ucyate tāpakasya rajasa iti tasya rahjasaḥ karmabhūtaṃ sattvam eva tapyam kasmāt cchidikriyāvattapikriyāyāḥ karmasthatvāt karmaṇi hi tapikriyā vartate na rajasastāpakasya viṣayiṇi puruṣe tapteś ca phalasya puruṣaviṣayatvāt na hi paraśuśdhettari svātmani vā vartate cchidir vā phalaṃ viṣaya eva chedye kāṣṭhādau evaṃ puruṣasya eva taptiḥ karmaṇi sattve vartamānā phalaṃ rajaś ca kāṣṭhādāv iva paraśuḥ sattva eva puruṣasya dṛśye vartate itaś ca puruṣe tapikriyā na vartate apariṇāmitvāt draṣṭu tapir api hi karmavikriyā yathā chedanasya phalaṃ chedyasya karmaṇo dvaidhī bhāvo vikriyā tadvat nāpariṇāmini niṣkriye kṣetrajñe apariṇāmitvaṃ ca sadā jñātaviṣayatvena sādhayiṣyati yady evaṃ puruṣaś cen na tapyate puruṣārthaṃ pradhānaṃ pravartata ity etad anupapannam vṛttisārūpyeṇa uktottaratvāt tad evvedam ucyate darśitaviṣayatvāt apariṇāmino vikriyatvād darśitaviṣayatvam tasmād dṛśikarmaṇi sattve tapye tadākārānurodhī tadākārānuvartī tadākārānurodhitvaṃ tad dṛśisannidhau bauddhasya pratyayasya dṛśirūpāvabhāsatā yathā lākṣārasasannidhau sphaṭihkasya lākṣākārāvabhāsatā tathā puruṣo api tapyata ity upacaryate dṛśyasvarūpam ucyate nanu ca draṣṭṛdṛśyayor ity uktaṃ pūrvasūtre tatra kramaprāptasannidhānaṃ dṛṣṭṛ svarūpam eva pūrvaṃ vaktavyam na eṣa doṣaḥ dṛśyasvarūpāvagamapūrvakatvād draṣṭṛsvarūpāvabodhasya dṛśyasya hi svātmavyatiriktadraṣṭrarthatvād vyatiriktadraṣṭṛsadbhāvasiddhiḥ ata eva prādhānyāt pūrvasūtre draṣṭuḥ pūrvanipātaḥ kṛtaḥ tal lakṣaṇe tv arthakramo vivakṣyate prakāśakriyāsthitiśīlaṃ bhūtendriyātmakaṃ bhogāpavargārthaṃ dṛśyam prakāśaś ca kriyā ca sthitiś ca prakāśakriyāsthitayaḥ prakāśasyābhyarhitatvāt pūrvanipātaḥ bahuṣu cāniyamāt sthitikriyāśabdayor aniyama iti kriyāśabdasya pūrvanipātaḥ tā eva śīlaṃ yasya tat prakāśakriyāsthitiśīlam prakāśanaṃ kriyā kathaṃ tacchīlaṃ sattvaṃ syāt rajo hi tacchīlaṃ sthitiśīlaṃ vā tamaḥ katham iti nanu ca svarūpam eva tatprakāśanaṃ sthitiś ca na svarūpamātre śīlaśabdāyogāt na hi mṛḍ aṅgaśīlo mārdaṅgikaḥ mṛḍaṅgavācanaśīlo hi sa ucyate na hi vyāpāraśūnye kvacid api śīlaśabdaḥ prayujyate nanu ca sthitiprakāśāv api sattvatamasoḥ svarūpam tad etena eva gamyate svarūpe śīlaśabdaḥ prasaṃkṣyata iti ucyate na svarūpe sarvatra śīlaśabdaprayoṅaḥ ihāpi rajasi duḥkhasvarūpe kriyā śīlam iti kriyayā samprayujya śīlaśabdavyapadeśaḥ sthitiprakāśāv api vyāpārarūpāvabhipretau athamataṃ kriyāpi rajasaḥ svarūpam eva iti na pradhānāvasthāyāṃ sāmyābhyupagamāt guṇānām yadi kriyā rajasaḥ svarūpam abhaviṣyat pradhānasyāpi kriyāvattvaṃ guṇasāmyāvasthāyām abhaviṣyat kāryāvasthāyāṃ hi kriyāvattvam abhyupagamyate na pradhānavelāyām tasmānnityā na svarūpābhiprāyeṇa śīlaśabdaprayogaḥ tatrākriyāśīlayor api sattvatamasor nityaṃ kriyā śīlena rajasā saṃyogād rajaḥ kriyayā eva kriyāvattvaṃ sthitiprakāśayor apīti tatkriyopacāreṇa prakāśaśīlaṃ sattvaṃ sthitiśīlaṃ tama iti vyapadiśyate sthitiprakāśayor ātmalābhasya rajaḥkriyāpūrvatvāc calator evābhivyaktes tācchīlyaṃ sattvatamasor ucyate tatra prakāśaśīlaṃ yat tat sattvam kriyā śīlaṃ pravṛttiśīlaṃ rajaḥ sthitiśīlaṃ varaṇaśīlaṃ niyamaśīlaṃ tama ity ete guṇāḥ parasparoparaktapravibhāgāḥ paraspareṇoparaktaḥ pravibhāgo bhedo yeṣāṃ guṇānāṃ te parasparoparaktapravibhāgāḥ yathā prakāśaśīlam iti sattvam ucyate traiva rajaḥkriyoparañjanāt sarvāvabhāsasamarthasyāpi sattvasya niyataprakāśatvaṃ tapauparaktatvena tathā rajasoapi pravṛttyabhivyaktiḥ sattvoparāgeṇa niyatapravṛttitvaṃ tu tamauparāgeṇa tathā tamaso api sthityabhivyaktiḥ sattvoparāgeṇa sthitiśīlatvaṃ rajauparāgeṇa sthitis tu svata eva rajaso api pravṛttiḥ svataḥ sattvasyāpi prakāśaḥ svata eva ittham evānyeṣv api kāryeṣu sattvādīnām itaretaroparāgo draṣṭavaḥ saṃyogaviyogadharmāṇaḥ saṃyogaś ca viyogaś ca saṃyogaviyogau tau dharmau yeṣāṃ te saṃyogaviyogadharmāṇa kasmiṃś cit kārya ārabhyamāṇe guṇapradhānabhāvenānyonyaṃ saṃyujyante tathā eva ārabdhakāryavirodhidharmāntarodaye parasparaṃ viyujyante itaretaropāśrayeṇopārjitamūrtayaḥ mahadādistambaparyantā mūrtaya itaretaropāśrayeṇopārjitā dharmarharmilakṣaṇā yais te itaretaropāśrayeṇopārjitamūrtayaḥ parasparato bhinnā api paramārthato nyonyato nye api asambhinnaśaktipravibhāgāḥ atyante vyāvṛttakāryārambhābhimukhyasāmarthyaprabhedāḥ etad uktaṃ bhavati ekasmin kārya ārabdhavye tyantavyatiṣaktaparasparaśaktayaḥ kāryārambhakāle pṛthaktvenānupalakṣyamāṇaśaktipravibhāgā iti tulyajātīyātulyajātīyaśaktibhedānupātinaḥ sāttvikānāṃ sattvaṃ tulyajātiñ rājasānāṃ rahastulyajātiḥ tāmasānāṃ tama iti ca parasparāpekṣayā tu bhinnajātīyatvam tulyajātīyātulyajātīyānāṃ śaktiprabhedam anupatituṃ śīlaṃ yeṣāṃ te tulyajātīyātulyajātīyaśaktiprabhedānupātinaḥ na hi sāttvike vā rājase tāmase vā prārabdhavyasya trayāṇāṃ śaktiprabhedānupātam antareṇa kāryārambhaḥ sambhavati yady evaṃ sarvaśaktiprabhedānupātitvād ekaikasya kāryārambhe tulyaṃ prādhānyam ity ata āha pradhānavelāyām upadarśitasannidhānāḥ sarve ekaikasmin prādhānyena svakāryārambhiṇi tatkāla itaraypr api sannidhānam upasarjanabhāvena upadarśitam iti pradhānavelāyām upadarśitasannidhānāḥ na hi sarveṣāṃ yugapat prādhānyam samapradhānatve hi pradhānam eva bhaveyuḥ na kāryārambhitvam athocyate kathaṃ punar ekasmin prādhānena kāryārambhiṇītarāstitvam avagamyata iti tad ucyate guṇatve copasarjanabhāve ca vyāpāramātreṇa pradhānopalakṣyamāṇena vyāpāramātreṇa pradhānāntarnītena na hi pradhānasyāntarnīto vyāpāraḥ itarayor upasarjanabhāvenāsannidhāne saṃbhaviṣyatīti pradhānavyāpāreṇānumitāstitvāḥ puruṣārthetikartavyatāprayuktasāmarthyāḥ puruṣārtho bhogāpavargau tasyetikartavyatā yathā yathā arthaniṣpattistathā tathā prayuktaṃ kāryārambhiṃ prati sāmarthyaṃ yeṣāṃ te puruṣārthetikartavyatāpratyuktasāmarthyāḥ sannidhimātropakārāṇiḥ vikārapratyayarūpasannidhimātreṇa puruṣāsyopakuruvantītyi sannidhimātropakāriṇaḥ ayaskāntamaṇikalpāḥ pratyayaṃ vṛttiṃ jñānam antareṇaikatamasya vṛttiṃ sthitilakṣaṇām samastām anuvarmānāḥ pradhānaśabdavācyā bhavanti naiva triguṇīvyatirekeṇānyat pradhānaṃ nāmāsti ta eva guṇāḥ sāmyāvasthāḥ pradhānaikaśabdābhidhānīyakaṃ pratipadyante vaiṣamyaṃ bhajanto vikāraśabdābhidheyā vṛttimanto bhavanti etad dṛśyam ity ucyate tad etad dṛśyaṃ bhūtenriyātmakaṃ bhūtātmakam indriyāmakaṃ ca kathaṃ tadātmakatvam ity āha bhūtabhāvena pṛṭhivyādinā sūkṣmasthūlena sūkṣmeṇa tanmātrarūpeṇa sthūlena viśeṣārūpreṇa dvividho hi bhūtabhāvas tanmātrarūpo viśeṣarūpaś ca vipariṇamate sthlasukṣmabhāvam āpadyate indriyabhāvenendriyarūpeṇa śrotrādinā sūkṣmasthūlena vipariṇamate sūkṣmeṇāhaṅkārarūpeṇa sthcūlena śrotrādirūpeṇa tat tu dṛśyaṃ nāprayojanam sarvatraiva pravṛtteḥ prayojanadarśanāt api tu prayojanamūrikṛtasyāṅgīkṛtya pravartate kiṃ punar dṛśyapravṛttiprayojanam ity āha bhāgāpavargārthaṃ hi dṛśyaṃ puruṣasyāgnyādipratipattivat kau oubas tau bhogāpavargāv ity āha tatreṣṭāniṣṭaguṇasvarūpāvadhāraṇam avibhāgāpannam iṣṭānāṃ agarucandanasparśanadilakṣaṇānāṃ aniṣṭānāṃ pratikūlātmakānāṃ kṛpāṇakaṇṭakādismarśanarūpāṇāṃ guṇānāṃ svarūpāvadhāraṇaṃ svarūpāvagamaḥ svarūpādhyavasānam tasya viśeṣaṇaṃ avibhāgāpannaṃ puruṣapratyaye nāyaṃ puruṣa idaṃ sattvam ity avibhāgatāṃ gatam prāptacaitanyopagraharūpatvād bauddhasya pratyaysya sa itthaṃ bhūtaḥ puruṣasya bhoga ity ākhyāyate tasmād bhogasvarūpād baduddhāt pratyayād vivicya tatsāmṣiṇo dṛśirūpasya svarūpāvadhāraṇaṃ bhoktṛsvarūpād avadhāryamāṇād uttarakālam apy apavṛttasya viśeṣābhāvād apvarga ity ucyate sarvadā svarūpapratiṣṭYho hi tadā sa iti vṛttisārūpyam itaratra viśeṣa iti dvayor bhogāpavargayor atiriktam anyat tṛtīyaṃ darśanaṃ nāsti yāvad avidyā tāvad iṣṭāniṣṭe sta iti bhoga eva puruṣasya tv aheyānupādeyasvarūpatvāt tadavadhāraṇe kuto bhoga iti bhogarūpasyāvidyālakṣaṇasya pratyayasya pratipakṣaḥ pratyayaḥ puruṣāvadhāraṇam yasmād etad ata etad darśanadvayavyatirekeṇa tṛtīyaṃ arśanāntaraṃ na kalpayituṃ śakyate tathā ca uktam ayaṃ tu khalv evaṃ samyagdarśī triṣu guṇeṣūktalakṣaṇeṣu kartuṣu sarvavyāpāranirvṛttikareṣv akartāri ca guṇadharmavilakṣaṇe puruṣe caturthe tatkriyāsākṣiṇi guṇakriyāsūpadraṣṭari sandhikriyāsākṣibhūtopadraṣṭṛvad upānīyamānān antaḥklaraṇalakṣaṇair guṇaiḥ prāpyamāṇān darśitaviṣayatvāt sarvabhāvān upapannān gauṇān eva bauddhapratyayākāreṇa pariniṣpnnān paśyan upalabhamāno nāhaṃ na mamety evaṃ na darśanam ito nyat sambhavati samyagdarśanam iti na śaṅkate nāsty evānyat samyagdarśanam iti manyate tāvatau bhogāpavargau buddhikṛtau buddhinirvartikau buddhāv eva vartamānau anyakṛtasyāpy anyatra vṛttir dṛṣṭā yathā rajakakṛto vastrarāga iti kathaṃ puruṣe apadiśyete iti tau buddhāv eva vartamānau puruṣe padiśyete iti kuta etat sa hi tat tat phalasya bhokteti smyaṅmithyāpratyayor upalabdheti dṛṣṭāntena vyākhgyātam artham nigamayati yathā vijayaḥ parājayo vā iti buddher evārthāparisamāptir bandha iti yāvat samāptau kartavyau bhogā apavargāv iti buddhir manyate tāvad bandhaḥ tadarthāvasāyo mokṣaḥ tasyā eva buddher arthāvasāyaḥ kartavyasamāptiḥ yadā ātmavilakṣaṇaṃ bandhamokṣāsambandhināṃ puruṣam īkṣite nāsya kartavyam astīti sa kartavyāvasāyo buddher mokṣa iti etena grahaṇadhāraṇavijñāna ūhāpohakriyā vacana yathānyāyāvadhāraṇābhiniveśāḥ puruṣe dhyāropitasadbhāvā iti jñeyāḥ pratyayatvāviśeṣāt buddhidharmāḥ buddhāv eva vartamānāḥ buddhikṛtāḥ puruṣe dhyāropitasadbhāvāḥ puruṣo gṛhṇāti puruṣo dhārayatīty evameva puruṣe adhyāropyante grahaṇaṃ śabda ādīnāṃ śrotrādibhir upādānam gṛhītānām avismaraṇaṃ dhāraṇam dhāritasya sāmānyaviśeṣāvadhāraṇaṃ vijñānam vijñātasya eva punas tad gataviśeṣāvabubhutsayohanmūhaḥ ūhitasya viruddhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ vyudasanam apohaḥ viṣayesu pravṛttiḥ kriyā vākyaviṣayo vṛttiviśeṣaś cittasya vacanam yo yo nyāyo yathānyāyaṃ yasya ca vastuno yathiavopapattis tathaivāvadhāraṇaṃ yathānyāyāvadhāraṇām tatra punaḥ punaḥ samyakpratyayāvicalanāya yaś cittasyābhiyogaḥ so abhiniveśaḥ ta ete grahaṇādayaḥ puruṣe dhyāropitasadbhāvāḥ sa hi tat phalasya bhokteti grahaṇādiphalasya upalabdheti dṛśyānāṃ guṇānāṃ yathāvyākhyātātmanāṃ svarūpabhedāvadhāraṇārthaṃ tattvāvasthābhedāvadhāraṇārtham idaṃ sūtram ārabhyate viśeṣāviśeṣaliṅgamātrāliṅgā guṇaparvāṇaḥ viśeṣāś cāviśeṣāś ca liṅgamātraṃ cāliṅgaś ca na liṅgati kutaś cinnāgacchati pradhānākhyo artha iti pacād yac sarvadhātubhya iti yaugikas sannabhidheyaliṅgaṃ bhajate yo vā liṅgaṃ na vidyate liṅgam avagamanaṃ paricchedaḥ pratyakṣeṇa pradhānākhyasyārthasyāsāv aliṅga iti bahuvrīhiḥ te ca viśeṣādayaḥ puruṣābhiprāyaṃ pālayanti bhogāpavargapradānena pūrayanti vā vikārān svān iti piparteḥ anyebhyo api dṛśyante iti kartari vanipratyayaḥ tathā ca sati yannāntam akartari tannapuṃsakam yat tu nāntuṃ kartari tatsarvaliṅgaṃ bhavati yathā berudṛśvā merudṛśvanīti tataś ca viśeṣādayaḥ parvāṇaḥ keṣāṃ te sambandhina iti guṇānāṃ parvāṇo guṇaparvāṇaḥ keṣāṃcid ayam eva pāṭho viśeṣāviśeṣaliṅgamātrāliṅkāni guṇaparvāṇīti tatrākāśavāyvagnijalabhūmayo bhūtāni śabdatanmātrārabdhamākāśam sparśatanmātreṇa śabdasparśalakṣaṇenārabdho vāyuḥ rūpatanmātreṇaśabdasparśarūpalakṣaṇenārabdho gniḥ rasatanmātreṇaśabdasparśarūparasacatuṣṭayalakṣaṇenāpāarabdhāḥ gandhatanmātreṇaśabdasparśarūparasagandhapañcatayalakṣaṇena bhūmirārabdhā nanu ca nityamākāśam prāgutpattervināśakālaṃ ca viśeṣābhāvāt yo yautpattimāṃstasya tasya pṛthivyāādeḥ prāgutpattervināśottarakālaṃ caviśeṣo dṛṣṭaḥ tathā ākāśaṃ yadyutpattimat syāt prāgutpattervināśottarakālaṃ ca bhvedviśeṣaḥ na ca so sti tasmādākācamanutpattikam athāvakāśadānābhāavo viśeṣa iti cenna mūrtimato nyasyābhāvāt tulyaṃnityatve api anityalakṣaṇābhāvācca nityamākāśam saragatatvādātmādivat na āgamavirodhāt tasmād vā etasmādātmana ākāśaḥ sambhūtaḥityāgamavirodhaḥ smṛtivirodhaś ca avakāśaṃ kurvati tadupacāra iticenna vāyvādiṣv apyupacāraprasaṅgāt ākāśād vāyuḥ sambhūtaityekavākyatvāt prāgutpatter viśeṣābhāvād anityo na bhavatīti ca bruvatā viśeṣābhāvānnityatvam ityuktaṃ bhavati tathā ca saty ātmādīnām apibandhamokṣopalabdhyādiviśeṣābhāvāt sato vaiśeṣikasya anityatvaprasaṅgaḥ tathā paramāṇvādīnāṃ cānityatvaṃ prasajyeta athāpyutpattimata eva prāgūrdhvaṃ ca viśeṣabhāvābhāvau vivakṣitāviticet na ākāśasyotpattyabhyupagamaprasaṅgāt athākāśotpattivādināviśeṣo vaktuṃ na śakyata iticet na puruṣārthasādhanāsādhanatvaviśeṣāt sarvagatatvāditicāsiddho hetuḥ asarvagatāni kākacigākāśamanāṃsy anityāni ca svārthābhāve parārthatvātghaṭādivat utpattimanti ca pradhānupuruṣābhyām anyatvāt ghaṭādivat evam ākāśaṃ utpattimad anityaṃ ca bāhyendriyaviṣayatvāt ghaṭādivat bhūtatvāc ca pṛthivīvat anityadravyasaṃyogotādyaguṇatvāt pṛthivyādivat vcikitsānivartyaprakopakaratvāt vāyuvat nabhaś ca prakopaś cikitsānirvartanīyaś cikitsakaprasiddhim upārūḍhaḥ etenānityasādharmyaṃ vyākhyātam etāni ca bhūtāni śabdasparśarūparasagandhatanmātrāṇām aviśeṣāṇāṃ viśeṣāḥ śāntaghoramūḍhādy anekaviśeṣavattvād viśeṣāḥ śāntādyavhāvāc cāviśeṣāḥ tan mātrāṇi tathā śrotratvakcakṣur jihvāghrāṇāni śabdādiviṣayabuddhyarthatvād buddhīndiryāṇi svaviṣayabuddhibhir evānumitāni vākpāṇipādapāyūpasthāni karmendriyāṇi vacanādikriyānirvartakāni tadanimitāny eva na vādādīni karmendriyāṇi siddhānīti cen na śrutiprasiddhatvāt indriyāṇi prakṛtya sarveṣāṃ vedānāṃ vāgekāyanam ityādiśruteḥ smṛtiṣu ca sarvatraiva vidhipratiṣedhaviṣayapravṛttinivṛttimatvāc ca śrotrādivad indryatvam na vākyacapalo na pāṇipādacapalaḥ ityāder vidhipratiṣedhaviṣayapravṛttinivṛttimattvasiddhiḥ tathā vāgāḍīnīndriyāṇi kauśalavattvāt cakṣurādivat sarvagātreṣu cendriyaśaktiḥ karaṇavṛttyāḥ sandarśanād iṣyata eva vāggudaprabhṛtīnāṃ sarpādīnāṃ mūkaṣaṇḍānāṃ ca mukham evopasthendriyam ekādaśaṃ manaḥ sarvārtham atītānāgatavartamānaviṣayārthaṃ buddhīndriyakarmendriyaviṣayārthaṃ ca etāny ekādaśendriyāṇy asmitā lakṣaṇasyāsmibhāvo smitā asmīti pratyayaḥ sa ca lakṣaṇaṃ yasya so smitalakṣaṇo smitāpratyayena hi lakṣyate liṅgyate ṣaṣṭham aviśeṣākhyaṃ tattvam ahaṅkāraḥ tasyāviśeṣasya viśeṣā etāni guṇānām aviśeṣākārasaṃsthitānāṃ sattvādīnām eṣa ṣodaśako viśeṣapariṇāmaḥ sattvabahulā pṛthivī grāhyatvāt tām asattve apy eṣāṃ guṇapradhānakṛto viśeṣaḥ karaṇāni prakāśatvāt sattvabahulāni manaḥṣaṣṭhāni tu buddhīndriyāṇi prakāśaprādhānyāt sattvabahulāni karnebdruyāṇi kriyāprādhānyād rajo bahulāni ṣaḍ aviśeṣāḥ tadyathā śabdamātraṃ sparśamātram iti dvilakṣaṇasyāpi pradhānena vyapadeśaḥ tathā rūpamātram iti trilakṣaṇasyāpi pradhānena vyapadeśaḥ tathottarayor api mātraśabdaḥ śāntaghorādiviśeṣavyāvartanārthaḥ ekadvitricatuḥpañcalakṣaṇabhedāḥ śabdatattvaikalakṣaṇaḥ śabdatanmātrabhedaḥ śabdasparśalakṣaṇaḥ sparśatanmātrabhedaḥ ity evam ekaikādhikyenottaratrāpi draṣṭavyam ṣaṣṭhaś cāviśeṣo smitamātraḥ śabdāditanmātrāpekṣayā ṣaṣṭha indriyāṇām ekādaśānām aviśeṣaḥ ete sattvamātrasyāstitvamātrasya liṅgamātrasya mūrtimātrasya pradhānasyāmūrtasya prathamā mūrtir iyaṃ yathā bījasyāṅkurībhāvaḥ ātmano vasturūpasya mahataḥ sarvaviśeṣāviśeṣebhyo mahattvāt ṣaḍ aviśeṣapariṇāmāḥ ṣaḍ aviśeṣā eva pariṇāmāḥ sattvādīnāṃ mahadrūpāvasthitānām amī aviśeṣapariṇāmāḥ yat tat paraṃ sūkṣmam aviśeṣebhyo liṅgamātraṃ mahattattvam tasminn ete sattāmātre mahattvānmahaty avasthāya kāraṇasvarūpe mahaty avasthāya vivṛddhikāṣṭhāṃ pṛthivyādiviśeṣāntatām anubhavanti pratisaṃsṛjyamānāś ca pratilīyamānāś cāviśeṣāḥ tasminn eva sattāmātre liṅgamātre mahaty ātmany avasthāyāvyaktaṃ prati yānti kiṃ viśiṣṭam nissattāsattvaṃ viśeṣāviśeṣadharmarahitam nissad asad iti avyaktādīṣadvikṛtam iti sat aviśeṣebhyaḥ sūkṣmataram iti cāsat sac cāsac ca sad asad iti mahattattvam ucyate tad dharmarahitam avyaktaṃ nissad asad iti eṣa teṣāṃ guṇānāṃ sattvādīnāṃ liṅgamātraḥ pariṇāmaḥ yasminn avasthāya vivṛddhikāṣṭhāṃ pratilayaṃ ca pratiyānty aviśeṣāḥ nissattasattaṃ cāvyaktaṃ ca yat sa teṣām eva guṇānām aliṅgapariṇāmaḥ paraś ca na sūkṣmo vasthāntarapariṇāmo sti guṇānām sūkṣmaviṣayatvaṃ cāliṅgaparyavasānam iti hi vyākhgyātam aliṅgatvād evāliṅgāvasthāyāṃ na puruṣārtho hetuḥ aliṅgāvasthānimittaṃ na puruṣārtho hetuḥ nāliṅgāvasthā puruṣārthaprayuktetyarthaḥ tad etat vyācaṣṭe nāliṅgāvasthāyām ādau puruṣārthatā kāraṇam kasmāt punas tadavasthā puruṣārthaprayuktā na bhavatīti tata āha yasmān nāsyāṃ puruṣārthatā kāraṇaṃ vidyate svayam api nasau puruṣārthatā mahadādivad asaṃvedyatvād īśvarāṇām api yataś caitad evaṃ tasmān nityā vyākhyāyate yo hi puruṣārthaprayuktaḥ so nityo dṛṣṭo yathā pṛthivyādiḥ na caiṣā pradhānāvasthā puruṣārthaprayukteti nityā vyākhyāyate trayāṇāṃ tv avasthāviśeṣāṇāṃ viśeṣāviśeṣaliṅgamātrāṇām ādau puruṣārthatā mahadādyavasthā puruṣārthaprayuktā sa cārthaḥ sa ca puruṣārtho hetur nimittaṃ kāraṇam ity anityā vyākhyāyante mahadādyastisno vasthāḥ guṇās tu sarvadharmānupātinaḥ sarvavikārānupātinaḥ yathā sarpaḥ prāṃśutvasarpaṇakuṇḍalatvādiviśeṣānupātī tathā viśeṣāditattvānupātino guṇāḥ piṇḍapratyayānupātinaś ca na pralīyante na upajāyante yathā sarpaḥ kuṇḍalāditve pralīyamāne na pralīyate tad upajane ca na upajāyate tathā eva guṇā api yathā ca ghaṭapiṭharādiṣu pralīyamāneṣu jāyamāneṣu ca mṛnna pralīyate nāpi jāyate guṇā vyaktibhir eva dharmair evātītānāgatavyayāgam avayībhistrilakṣaṇābhir guṇānvayībhir guṇopādānakāraṇābhir upajanāpāyadharmakā ivotpattipralayavanta iva pratyavabhāsante na svarūpeṇa vinaśyanti jāyante vā etasya evārthasya dṛṣṭāntam āha devadatto daridrāti kasmāt yenāsya mriyante gāva iti gavām eva maraṇāt tasya daridrāṇaṃ na svarūpahānād iti samaḥ samādhiḥ tulyaś caroco dṛṣṭāntena dārṣṭāntikasya devadattadaridrāṇavad eva guṇānugatābhir vyaktibhir mahadādibhir guṇavirmardabavaucitryakṛtābhir vivardhamānābhir guṇānām āḍhyatā tat pralaye ca teṣāṃ daridrāṇaṃ na svarūpeṇāpacaya upacayo vā iti tulyaḥ samādhir iti sarvasya pradhānakāryatve sati viśeṣā aviśeṣā vā kasmād anantaraṃ na upajāyanta iti tad āha liṅgasyāliṅgaṃ pratyāsannaṃ yathā mūlaṃ vṛkṣasya pratyāsannaṃ bīje saṃsṛṣṭaṃ mūlam eva prathamataraṃ vivicyte na vṛkṣasyottarāvasthā evaṃ tatra pradhāne tat liṅgaṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ saṃlīnaṃ prathamaṃ vīdyate āvirbhavati nottare viśeṣā viprakṛṣṭatvād eva tad eva āha kramānatipatteḥ kramānatikramāt na hi loke kasyacid utpadyamānasya kramātilaṅghanam asti tathā ṣaḍ aviśeṣāḥ pūrvoktā liṅgamātre pratyāsannatvāt saṃsṛṣṭatvād vivicyante kasmād ity āha pariṇāmakramaniyamāt tathā teṣv aviśeṣeṣu bhūtendriyāṇi tan mātreṣu bhūtāni saṃsṛṣṭāni vivicyante asmitāmātre indriyāṇi manassahitāni tathā ca ukta purastāt na viśeṣebhyaḥ prāg uktebhya ākāśādibhyaḥ paraṃ tattvāntaram asti na viśeṣāṇām anyas tattvāntarapariṇāma ity arthaḥ etad eva āha viśeṣāṇāṃ nāsti tattvāntaram iti tattvaṃ hi nāma sādhāraṇaṃ sarvaprāṇadhāriṇām ā mahāpralayasthāyi na evaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthivyādibhya utpadyamānam anyad asti dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmās tu bhavanty eva iti teṣāṃ tu viśeṣāṇāṃ dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāṃāvyākhyāyiṣyante tṛtīyapāde vyākhgyātam dṛśyam avadhṛtaṃ dṛśyam yad arthaṃ ca dṛśyate tasya idānīṃ draṣṭuḥ svarūpāvadhāraṇārtham idam ārabhyate draṣṭā dṛśimātraḥ śuddho api pratyayānupaśyaḥ draṣṭā dṛśyasya yathāvyākhyātarūpasya upalabdhā puruṣaḥ tasyedaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ dṛśimātraḥ śuddhe api pratyayānupaśyaś ceti punastād ākhyātam tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe vasthānam vṛttisārūpyam itaratra iti ca tad eva dvayam iha pratipādyate pratisaṃvedī buddheḥ puruṣa ity upapādayiṣyāma iti taccātropapādyate dṛśir darśanam upalabdhis tāvan mātro dṛśimātraḥ yata evaṃ tasmāc chuddhaḥ śuddho api sann asau bauddhasya pratyayasyānupaśyaḥ dṛśimātratvād eva tasmāt tam anupaśyan tatsvarūpo bhavati dṛśisannidhau vṛtter dṛśisvarūpāvabhāsatā draṣṭur vṛttisārūpyam dṛśimātrasya evāvikriyātmakasya sato asya bauddhapratyayānudarśanaṃ yasmāt tasmāc ca svarūpapratiṣṭhatā ca siddhā pratyayānupaśya iti etat tu tad astitvānumānam katham ghaṭādīnāṃ dṛśyānāṃ svarūpavyatiriktenānyena dṛśyatvadarśanāt tat prakāśakānāṃ ca ālokādīnāṃ vyatiriktadṛśyatvāt sarvārthāvabhāsakānām api pratyayānāṃ svarūpavyatiriktadṛśyatvaṃ dṛśyatvād avagamyate ghaṭāditadālokādivad iti yasmāc ca bauddham eva pratyayam anupaśyati taṃ ca paśyaty eva na kadācit svavisayaṃ pratyayaṃ na paśyati tasmād dṛśimātraḥ mātragrahaṇaṃ dharmāntaranirvartanārtham etena draṣṭur dṛśir ity etan nirvartitam iddhādisamānāśrayatvaṃ ca nirvartitaṃ dṛśer eva draṣṭṛtvāt tad etad ucyate dṛśimātra iti dṛkchaktir eva dṛg darśanaṃ tad eva śaktir dṛkśhaktiḥ nāpy anyo dṛkchaktimān asti sā eva śaktir dṛg iti tatra mātraśabdārthaṃ vyācaṣṭe viśeṣeṇāparāmṛṣṭety arthaḥ viśeṣeṇa kenacid icchādinā guṇair guṇadharmaiś cāparāmṛṣṭaḥ sa puruṣo buddheḥ pratiṣaṃvedituṃ śīlam asya iti pratisaṃvedī bauddhapratyayopalabdhisvabhāva ity arthaḥ puruṣo buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī dṛśimātraḥ śuddhaś ceti kathaṃ gamyata ity āha sa buddher na sarūpo nātyantaṃ virūpa iti na samānalakṣaṇo nāpy atyantavidharvety etat asarūpatayā dṛśimātratvaṃ śuddhatvaṃ ca āha nātyantavirūpa iti vṛttisārūpyatām āha kathaṃ punaḥ na sarūpatā iti ucyate na tāvat sarūpaḥ kasmāt ko hetuḥ buddhes tāvat svarūpam vaidharmyadarśanārtham āha jñātājñātaviṣayatvāt pariṇāminī buddhir iti kaḥ punar asau buddher iṣayo yo jñātaś cājñātaś ca yena bāhyākāreṇa pariṇatā buddhiḥ sa jñātaḥ yena ākāreṇa na pariṇatā so jñātaḥ yadi na pariṇametāpariṇamamānā ced viṣayaṃ vikhyāpayet sadā eva viṣayitvaṃ buddheḥ syāt tasmāt jñātājñātaviṣayatā pariṇāmitvaṃ khyāpayati pariṇāminī buddhiḥ jñātājñātaviṣayatvāt dīpacakṣurādi viṣaya vat tadvilakṣaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ sadā jñātaviṣayaḥ sarvadā hi jñāta eva puruṣasya svo viṣayaḥ tasmāt sadā jñātaviṣayatvaṃ puruṣasyāpariṇāmitvaṃ paridīpayati sadā jñāṣtaviṣayatvam asiddhaṃ puruṣasya ity āśaṅkyāha kasmāt ko hetuḥ na hīti hiśabdaḥ prasiddhāvadyotanārthaḥ buddhiś ca nāma buddhir iti bauddhapratyayaḥ puruṣasya viṣayaḥ syād agṛhītā gṛhītā ceti sarvadā ca gṛhīta eva bauddhaḥ pratyayaḥ tad avyabhicāreṇa eva puruṣasya vyatiriktatvasiddhiḥ tasmāt puruṣasya sadā jñātaviṣayatvam tataś cāpariṇāmitvaṃ iddham apariṇāmī puruṣa iti pratijñā sadā jñātaviṣayatvād iti hetuḥ vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto buddhyādiḥ nanu ca buddhyā vyavasitam arthaṃ puruṣaś cetayati buddheś ca sarvo viṣayo jñātaś cājñātaś ca puruṣasyāpi samānaḥ jñātājñātaviṣayatvaṃ buddhyā vyavasitārthopalambhitvāt tasmāt puruṣasyāpi pariṇāmitvaṃ jñātājñātaviṣayatvād buddhivad eva na eṣa doṣaḥ buddher eva puruṣaviṣayatvāt buddhir eva hi bāhyārthākārā puruṣasya viṣayo nārthaḥ kevalaḥ svarūpeṇa tasmānnityā na jñātājñātaviṣayaḥ puruṣaḥ buddhis tu sadā eva jñātā eva iti na pariṇāmitvaṃ puruṣasya nanu ca buddhyā vyavasitam arthaṃ puruṣaś cetayatīti kaścid āha tat katham ucyate na tair apy apariṇāmitvasyābhyupagamāt puruṣasya buddhyā vyavasitam artham ity etad uktaṃ bhavati buddhyākāraṃ cetayati buddhivyavasāyākārāpannam arthaṃ cetayatīti anyathā hi teṣāṃ pariṇāmitvaparārthatvasaṃhatyakāritvādayo buddhidharmāḥ sarva eva prasajeyuḥ athāpariṇāmitve darśanānupapattir iti cet na darśanasya eva puruṣasvarūpatāt yo hi puruṣapariṇāmitvam abhimanyate sa idam pra draṣṭavyaḥ kiṃ pariṇāmena kriyata iti sa ced abhidadhīta darśanam iti sa pratyabhidhānīyaḥ puruṣasya darśanam eva rūpaṃ ataḥ pariṇāmānarthakyam iti sa cet pratibrūyāt na puruṣasya upalabdhir bhogaḥ kasmāt tarhi vikriyā eva bhoga iti sa punar vaktavyaḥ tathāpi vikriyāvattvād anityatvam upanataṃ śarīrādivad eva athāpi pratibhāṣeta svātmani vikriyā nānityatvakāraṇaṃ syāt kiṃ tv avasthāntarabhāvikriyā hi kāraṇam anityatvasyeti sa punaḥ pratibhāṣitavyaḥ vikriyāvasthāyā evāvasthāntaratvāt pūrvam avikṛtasya vastunaḥ punar vikriyā avasthāntaram kiṃ ca viṣayābhyupagame ca vikriyā eva tāvatā niyamaḥ pāryate na kartum na cāpi svātmani vikriyamāṇānāṃ vajravaidūryādīnām anityatvaṃ nāsti na ca vikriyājanitasya eva darśanasya dṛśyaviṣayatvaṃ na nityasya darśanasya iti niyamahetur asti vikriyā eva upalabdhir na vikriyājaniteti cet na śarīrādīnāṃ vikriyāvatām upalabdhiprasaṅgāt tasmād dṛśimātra evāpariṇāmī ca sadā jñātaviṣayatvāt puruṣa iti siddhaṃ tasya ca ntyopalabdhisvarūpatve api dṛśyabauddhapratyayabhāvābhāvakṛto yaṃ vyapadeśaḥ paśyati darśayiṣyati dadarśeti ca savitrādipakāśanavyapadeśavat yathā prakāśayai savitā prakāśayiṣyati prācīkaśād iti ca prakāśyabhāvābhāvakṛto vyapadeśaḥ śuddhatvādayo hetavo vaidharmyeṇ abuddhyādayo dṛṣṭāntāḥ itaś cāsarūpaḥ sarvārthādhyavasāyitvād dhoraśāntādisamastārthāvasāyitvāt triguṇā buddhiḥ śrotrādivat guṇānāṃ tūpadraṣṭety upadraṣṭṛtvaṃ hetuḥ atriguṇaḥ purusa iti pratijñā vaidharmyeṇ abuddhyādir eva dṛṣṭānto triguṇatvāc cāsarūpaḥ astu tarhi virūpa eva tataś cātyantavirūpatvād bhogānupapattir iti atrocyate nātyantaṃ virūpaḥ kasmāt ko tra hetuḥ na hi śuddhasya buddhisvarūpavirūpasyāśuddhabauddhapratyayād atyantavairūpyasiddhaye hetur ity abhiprāyaḥ na buddhipratyayasākṣitvasya siddhatvāt yataḥ śuddho apy asau bauddhaṃ pratyayam anupaśyati tac ca bauddhapratyayānudarśanaṃ sādhitam anupaśyatīti viṣayakārapariṇāme sati bauddhaṃ pratyayaṃ paśyatīty arthaḥ tam anupaśyann api na tadātmā na triguṇaḥ tadātmaka iva śāntaghoramūḍhavyavasāyarūpa iva pratyavabhāsate tasmānnityā nātyantavirūpaḥ pravṛttisārūpyāt tatra yad uktaṃ buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī puruṣa ity upapādayiṣyāmaḥ iti tad upapāditam tathā ca tatsārūpyam ādarśitam tathā uktaṃ tantre apariṇāminī bhoktṛ śaktiḥ dṛkśhaktir yathāvyākhyātarūpā apratisaṅkramā ca pariṇāminy arthe bauddhe pratyaye pratisaṅkrānteva pratyayaviṣayatvāt tadvṛttim anupatantīvāsyā buddher vṛttim anupatantīva draṣṭṛtvād upalabhmānā bauddhaḥ pratyayo jāyamāna eva dṛkśhakteḥ karmatām āpadyate tam anupatanty upalabhamānā bhoktṛ śaktiḥ tasyāś ca prāptacaitanyopagraharūpāyāḥ prāptaṃ caitanyopagraharūpaṃ puruṣopagraharūpaṃ yayā buddhivṛttyā āsāditaṃ pāvakopagraharūpataptalohapiṇḍavad dṛśikarmatvād evānukāramātratayā buddhivṛttisārūpyamātratayā buddhivṛttyaviśiṣṭā jñavṛttir iti jña evopalabdhir eva vṛttir ity ākhyāyate tadartha eva dṛśyasyātmā tacchabdena draṣṭā dṛśimātraḥ śuddho yathādhigatātmā pratyāmnāyate tadarthaḥ asmai tadarthas tatprayojanaḥ dṛśikarmatvārtha ity arthaḥ bhogarūpeṇāpavargarūpeṇa ca ko sāv ity āha dṛśyasyātmā pradhānasyātmā svarūpam svarūpalābha iti nanu caturvyūhatvaṃ vyācikhyāsitaṃ kimartham etad aprakṛtam ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ ātyantikaduḥkhanivṛttiprayojanasya prakṛtatvāt kathaṃ dṛśyatādarthyalābhāvadhāraṇenātyantikī duḥkhaviratir uktā bhaved iti ucyate yadi dṛśyasvarūpapratilṃbhas tadartha eva tadā aśeṣatadarthaviratau punaḥ kṛtārthatvāt kāryābhāvād ātyantikadṛśyaviraktiḥ syāt tasya punaḥ pravṛttau prayojanābhāvāt na hi kṛtam eva punaḥ karaṇīyakam upāśnute atha tu svārtho api dṛśyasya ātmalāmho bhaviṣyad ataḥ svārthasya bhāvāt punaḥ punaḥ pravartiṣyata tataś ca na ātyantikī nivṛttiḥ tasmāt tādarthyam evovadhāryate dṛśyātmalābhasya svārthābhāvaś ca dṛśyasya bhogyatvāt odanādivat siddhaḥ acetanatvāt saṃhatyakāritvāc ca tadāha dṛśirūpasya puruṣasya karmaviṣayatām āpannaṃ dṛśyam iti itiśabdo hetvarthe tadartha eva dṛśyasyātmābhavati svarūpam bhavatītyarthaḥ puruṣārtha eva pradhānasyātmalābho dṛśikarmatāpatter odanādivat sūtraprayojanam ācaṣṭa idānīm tataś ca tādarthyasya niyatatvāt kāraṇāt puruṣarūpeṇa pratilabdhātmakaṃ prāptacaitanyopagraharūpaṃ sadbhogāpavargārthatāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ puruṣeṇa na dṛśyate bhogāpavargavyatirekeṇa kartavyābhāvāt sūtrasambandhaṃ karoti yaṃ puruṣaṃ prati caritārthaṃ dṛśyaṃ taṃ prati dṛśikarmatāṃ na āpatsyata iti svarūpahānam ataś ca svarūpahānād asya vināśaḥ prāptaḥ na tu vinaśyati sarvātmanā kasmāt ko hetuḥ pradhānānāṃ pratipuruṣaṃ bahutvāt kṛtārthaṃ prati naṣṭam eva iti manyate kṛtārthaṃ prati naṣṭam apy anaṣṭaṃ tad anyasādhāraṇatvāt kṛtārthaṃ yaṃ puruṣaṃ prati bhogāpavarhanirvartanena kṛtaprayojanaṃ tam ekaṃ puruṣaṃ prati punaḥ kāryakaraṇarūpeṇāpravartanād bhāvābhāvayor aviśeṣān naṣṭam api asya vyākhyānaṃ nāśaprāptam apīti anaṣṭaṃ tadanyapuruṣasādhāraṇatvāt yān praty akṛtārthaṃ tān praty anaṣṭam katham anaṣṭam ity āha kuśalapuruṣān prati nāśaprāptaṃ bhogāpavargapradānena kuśalapuruṣān prati kṛtaprayonajam akuśalapuruṣān prati akṛtārthaṃ bhogāpavargayoḥ kartavyayor akṛtatvāt teṣām akuśalānāṃ dṛśeḥ ta eva dṛśis tasyāḥ karmatāṃ dṛśyatām āpannaṃ labhata eva puruṣarūpeṇa puruṣanirvhāsatayā ātmarūpam iti ataś ca sādāraṇatvād ekam eva pradhānaṃ pṛthivyādivat kāryakaraṇānāṃ cābhinnatvāt puruṣāṇāṃ nānātvaṃ siddham sukhaduḥkhanānātvāc ca puruṣabhedasiddhiḥ ataś ca dṛgdarśanaśaktyor nityatvād anādiḥ saṃyogo vyākhyātaḥ tathā ca uktaṃ tantre dharmiṇām anādisaṃyogāt guṇānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ cānādisaṃyogād dharmamātrāṇāṃ mahadādikāryakāraṇāntānām api puruṣair anādiḥ saṃyogo dharmibhir dharmāṇām abhinnatvāt dṛśyam avadhṛtam draṣṭā cāvadhṛtaḥ draṣṭṛdṛśyayoḥ saṃyogo heyahetur iti ca uktam sa ca saṃyogo vadhārayitavyaḥ kīdṛśa iti tataś ca saṃyuogasvarūpāvadhāraṇārtham idaṃ sūtraṃ pravavṛte svasvāmiśaktyoḥ svarūpopalabdhihetuḥ saṃyogaḥ svasvāmiśaktyoḥ buddhipuruṣayoḥ svarūpopalbadher hetuḥ kāraṇam yasmin sati tayoḥ svarūpam upalabhyate vadanadarpaṇayor iva sa tayoḥ svarūpopalabdhihetuḥ saṃyogaḥ dṛṣṭṛdṛśyasvarūpakāryānumeya ity arthaḥ pramāṇaṃ cātra svasaṃyogapūrvikā buddhipuruṣayoḥ svarūpoplabdhiḥ viṣayaviṣayisvarūpopalabdhitvāt īkṣaṇadarpaṇasvarūpoplabdhivat yā kācit sukhaduḥkhopalabdhir vivādagocarāpannā sā sukhasuḥkhahetusaṃyogaoūrvikā sukhaduḥkhopalabdhitvāt candanakānṭakasukhaduḥkhopalabdhivat tad āha puruṣaḥ svāmī dṛśyena svena svayā buddhyā darśānaṛthaṃ bhogāpavargadarśanārthaṃ saṃyuktaḥ darśanaprayukta eva saṃyoga ity arthaḥ tasmāt saṃyogād darśanapratyuktā dṛśyasya upalabshiḥ aviśiṣṭā yā sa bhogaḥ yā tu draṣṭuḥ svarūpopalabdhir viviktā so pavargaḥ yasmād darśanakāryadvayaprayuktaḥ saṃyogas tasmād darśanakāryāvasānaḥ saṃyogaḥ tena puruṣasaṃyogavad darśanaṃ viyogasya kāraṇam ity uktam guṇapuruṣāntaradarśanaṃ pradhānapuruṣaviyogasya kāraṇam ity uktaṃ kāryasya darśanena paryavasitatvāt saṃsārisaṃsārahetuyāthātmyadarśanaṃ duḥkhaduḥkhisaṃyogahetunivartakaṃ duḥkhiduḥkhahetuyāthātmyaviṣayatvāt rogirogahetuyāthātmyadarśanavat avidyā draṣṭṛdṛśyayoḥ saṃyogakāraṇaṃ duḥkhanimittasaṃyogahetutvāt roggahetusaṃyoganimittamithyājñānavat draṣṭṛdṛśyasaṃyogo mithyājñānapūrvakaḥ duḥkhahetutvāt rogirogahetusaṃyogavat yasmād duḥkhiduḥkhahetuyāthātmyaviṣayaṃ darśanaṃ tasmāt tadanyathāviṣayasyādarśanasya pratidvandvam ity adarśanaṃ saṃyoganimittam ity uktaṃ tasya hetur avidyeti duḥkhanimittatvāc ca saṃyogasya yasmād adarśanam eva nivartayati darśanaṃ nānyatkāryaṃ karoti tasmān nātra darśanaṃ mokṣakāraṇam adarśanābhāvād evārthādarśanakāryasya duḥkhahetor bandhasyābhāvaḥ sa mokṣaḥ na punar bandhābhāvavyatirekeṇabhāvayitavyo mokṣaḥ tataś ca mokṣasya nityatvasiddhiḥ darśanasya bhāve draṣṭṛdṛśyaviṣayasya darśanasya bhāve tadviṣayasyādarśanasya nāśaḥ darśanādarśanayor ekatra virodhāt timioraravikiraṇajālayor iva ato darśanaṃ kaivalyakāraṇam uktam vivekakhyātir aviplavā hānopāyaḥ iti kiṃ cedam adarśanaṃ nāma nanu ca uktam avidyā eva sā cāmitrāgoṣpadavad iti vidyāviparyayeṇa vyākhyātā satyam evaṃ kin tu śāstragatā vikalpā darśayiṣyante svābhimatapakṣaniścīṣayā paraparikalpitavastukhaṇḍimānam āpādayatā hi nijābhimatanirūpitavas tu draḍhimānam atitarām ānīyate kiṃ cedam iti sarvair eva vikalpair vakṣyamāṇair abhisaṃbandhanīyam kiṃ guṇānām ahikāra iti sāmānyena paripṛṣṭasya viśeṣaparyanuyogaḥ adhikṛtir adhikāraḥ guṇānāṃ pravṛttiḥ nanu guṇānām adhikārasya katham adarśanāśaṅkā ucyate arthadvāreṇa bhavaty evādarśanam adhikāraḥ yāvad dhi guṇānāṃ pravṛttis tāvad bandhaḥ bandhakāraṇam avidyeti sthitisthairyam ānīyate śavdadvāreṇāpi darśanād anyad adarśanaṃ yadā bhavaty eva tadānīm āśaṅkā guṇādhikāro hi darśanād anya eva iti āhosvid dṛśisvarūpasya svābino darśitaviṣayasya sittasyānutpādaḥ iha tu pūrvapadārthapradhānatvam adarśanasya gṛgītvā śaṅkyate cittasyānutpādaḥ prāg utpatter darśanasyābhāvaḥ kim uktaṃ bhavaty anutpāda ity ata āha svasmin dṛśye tv arthadvāreṇa evāśaṅkā aprayojanavato hi prayojanam avaśyakṛtyam iti kim arthavattā guṇānāṃ bhogāpavargābhyāṃ yā guṇānām arthavattā tad adarśanam iti atra tv arthadvāreṇa evāśaṅkā prayojanavato hi prayojanam avaśyakṛtyam iti kaḥ punar eṣu pakṣeṣu doṣaḥ ucyate yady adhikāro guṇānām adarśanaṃ vidyānarthakyaṃ prāptam na hy asmin pakṣe vidyā pratyanīkabhūtā asārvabhaumī sā eva ca kālāvacchinnā yathā na caturdaśyāṃ na puṇye hanīti caturdaśyādi kālād anyaṃ kālaṃ na vayaśnuta iti sā apy asārvabhaumī tribhiḥ api jātideśakālaiḥ uparatasya tasya eva matsyabandhakasya samayāvacchinnā samayaḥ kartavyatāniyamaḥ katham devabrāhmaṇārthaṃ haniṣyāmi nānyathā iti śrāddhādisamayabhūmimanaśnānā vartata iti sā api na sārvabhaumī yathā ca kṣatriyasya yuddha eva hiṃsā nānyatra iti samayāvacchinnasya evodāharaṇam ye puner ete yamāḥ jātideśakālasamayair anavaddhinnā ahiṃsādayaḥ te sarvathā eva paripālanīyāḥ sarvabhūmiṣu jātyādiṣu sarvaviṣayeṣu sarvaprāṇiṣu sarvathā eāviditavyabhicārāḥ vinā vyabhicāreṇa te cetthaṃ viśiṣṭāḥ sārvabhaumā mahā vratam ity ucyante śaucasantoṣatapas svādhyāya īśvarapraṇidhānāni niyamāḥ tatra śaucaṃ mṛdādijanitam ādiśabdād udakaṃ ca medhyābhyvaharaṇāni ca ghṛtapayāadīni bhakṣaṇāni caśabdāt medhyadarśanaśreavaṇādīni ca bāhyam etac śaucam ābhyantaram ahunā ucyate cittamalānāṃ kāmakrodhādīnāṃ tat pratipakṣabhāvanāsalilaiḥ ākṣālanam santoṣaḥ sannihitasādhanāśvāsāt sannihitād āśvāsanimittāt adhiksādhanānupāditsā sannihitamātrād atṛptau satyām apy alaṃpratyayaḥ tapo dvandvasahanam dvandvaś ca jighatsāpipāse jighatsā attum icchā jighatsāpipāse alpīyaḥpānāśananimitte tapaḥ śītoṣṇe apratikriyamāṇe alpapratikriye vā tapaḥ sthānāsane tiṣṭhed ahani rātrāvāsīta iti smṛtiprasthānam kāṣṭhamaunākāṣṭhamaune kāṣṭhamaunaṃ hastaprayogādirahitam akāṣṭhamaunaṃ hastādiprayogayuktaṃ sambhāṣaṇādirahitam vratānicaiṣāṃ yogināṃ yathā yogaṃ yathāsambhavam homādiviruddhadharmaviruddhapratiṣedhārthaṃ yathā yogam ity āha kāni tāni kṛcchrādīni kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyādi tryahaṃ prātaḥ tryahaṃ sāyaṃ tryaham adyādayācitam upoṣaṇaṃ tryaham iti cāndrāyaṇaṃ yavamadhyapipīikāmadhyādi ekaikaṃ vadhayet grāsam ityādismṛtiḥ sāntapanam gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam ekarātropavāsaś ca kṛcchraḥ sāntapanaḥ amṛtaḥ etāny eva dravyāṇi trirabhyastāni mahāsāntapanam ādigrahaṇaṃ parākādipratyupādānārtham svādhyāyo mokṣaśāstrādhyayanam upniṣadādyadhyayanaṃ praṇavajapo vā pratyakcetanādhigamo apy antarāyābhāvaś ceti tatra yamaniyamānāṃ viruddhās tarkāḥ vitarkāḥ taiḥ bādhane sati pratipakṣān bhāvayet abhidhāsyamānena prakāreṇa apratibhāvyamānā hi vitarkā yoginaṃ hiṃsādiṣu praṇidhāpayeyuḥ yadā asya brāhmāṇasya vitarkā hiṃsādayo jāyeran tatrāhiṃsādivitarkā ye vā hiṃsā ādayas te vitarkāḥ kīdṛśā iti tatrāhiṃsāyā vitarkaḥ hiṃsā haniṣyābhyapakāriṇam iti tathā satyasyānṛtaṃ vadiṣyāmīti viruddhaḥ pratyayo vitarkaḥ tathaivāsteyasya vitarkaḥ dravyam asya svīkariṣyāmīti tathā brahmacaryasya vitarkaḥ dāreṣu cāsya gamiṣyāmīti tathā eāparigrahasya vitarkaḥ parigraheṣu cāsya svāmī bhaviṣyāmīti asya ity etat sarvatra hiṃsādiṣu anugamapratipādanārtham dravyam asya svīkariṣyāmīti paradravyasyātmasaṃbandhakaraṇam parigraheṣu cāsya svāmīti parasaṃbandhiṣv eva dreavyeṣu svayaṃ svāmīti yathā kumāranarapatisacivādīnām ittham unmārgahāriṇā vitarkajvareṇa dīptena bādhyamānas tatpratipakṣān bhāvayet kathaṃ bhāvayed iti ghoreṣu saṃsārāṅgāreṣu pacyamānena mayā cśaraṇam abhyupagataḥ sarvabhūtābhaytapradānena yogadharmaḥ sa khalv ahaṃ tyaktvā vitarkān hiṃsādīn punas tānādadānas tulyaḥ śvavṛtteneti śuna iva yasya saḥ śvavṛttaḥ śvavad vā vṛttaḥ śvavṛttaḥ tena tulya iti bhāvayet yathā śvā vāntāvalehī tathā tyaktasya punar ādānaṃ kurvan ity upaskāraḥ tena puruṣeṇa tulyo ham iti tathā katham ahaṃ bhaveyaṃ na yuktam etad iti bhāvayet ity evam ādi sūtrāntare api niyamasūtre api yojyam śauca ādīnāṃ pratyekaṃ vitarkā draṣṭavyāḥ śaucaṃ na kariṣyāmīty ādayaḥ bhāṣye tu yamānām eva pradarśanam teṣām avaśyakartavyatvāt akaraṇe ca doṣagauravāt atyādarārtham vitarkāṇāṃ svarūpam bhedaḥ prabhavahetuḥ phalaṃ ca sūtreṇa eva pradarśyate vitarkā hiṃsādaya iti svarūpam kṛtakāritānumoditā iti bhedaḥ lobhakrodhamohapūrvakā iti prabhavahetuḥ mṛdumadhyāhimātrā iti mandamadhyottamadoṣatvam duḥkhājñānānantaphalā iti pratipakṣabhāvanam phalaṃ vā tena eva vyākhyāyate tatra hiṃsā eva ekā udāhriyate sarveṣāṃ pradarśanāya sā kṛtā kāritā anumoditeti trividhā kṛtā svavyāpāreṇa kāritā prayojyavyāpāreṇa anumoditā pareṣāṃ vyāpāreṇa manasā naujñātā ekaikā punas tridhā katham lobhena māsacarmā sthi rthī mṛgaṃ hanasti krodhenāpakṛtam aneneti mohena dharmo me bhaviṣyatīti evam ete nava bhedāḥ ekaieka tvena sya punas tridhā bhedaḥ katham lobhakrodhamohāḥ punas tridhā mṛdumadhyādhimātrā iti ekaikaṃ punaḥ tridhā bhavati mṛdumṛdur madhyamṛdus tīvramṛdur iti tathā mṛdumadhyo madhyamdhyas tīvramadhya iti tathā mṛdutīvro madhyatīvras tīvratīvra iti evaṃ ekāśītibhedā hiṃsā bhavati sā ca punaḥ ekāśītibhedā api satī niyogavikalpasamuddayabhedāt asaṅkhyeyā yathā niyogabhedaḥ kaścinn ity uktaḥ sannanyaṃ niyuṅkte yathā rājñaḥ sa cāpi niyuktaḥ param sa cāpi param iti te ca sarve niyuktāḥ samuddayena vikalpena vā hiṃsanti tathā mūlaniyoktāpi niyojyaiṅḥ saṃhatya vikalpya ca hiṃsām anutiṣṭhatīti vadhyaghātakādiprāṇibhedasyāsaṅkhyeyatvād iti evam anṛtādiṣv api yojyam kṛtakāritānumoditādi yojyam te khalv amī vitarkā duḥkhājñānānantaphalāḥ duḥkhaṃ cājñānaṃ ca duḥkhājñāne te evānantaṃ phalaṃ yeṣāṃ te duḥkhājñānānantaphalāḥ duḥkham eṣām anantaṃ phalam ajñānaṃ ca eṣām anantaṃ phalam tasmād etān vitarkān manasā api na upekṣayed iti pratipakṣaṃ bhāvayet tatra hiṃsyasya triprakārā pīḍā pratipādyate tad bhedadvāreṇa phalabhedapradar Vanārtham tathā ca hiṃsako vadhyasya vīryam ākṣipati ghātakarūpāvalokanabhartsanādinā trastasya vīryam ākṣipya śastrādinipātanena duḥkhayati tato jīvitād api mocayati prāṇebhyo viyojayati tasya vīryākṣepād asya hiṃsituḥ cetanācetanaṃ paśu kṣetrādikaṃ upakaraṇaṃ kṣīṇavīryaṃ bhavati śastrādinipātanaduḥkhotpādāt hiṃsāviśeṣāt narakatiryakpretādiṣu duḥkham anubhavati tathā jīvitavyaparopaṇāt pratikṣaṇaṃ ca jīvitātyaye vartamāno janmamaraṇāntare vartmni pratikṣaṇaṃ maraṇam icchann api duḥkhavipākasya niyatavedanīyatvāt avaśyānubhavitavyatvāt kathaṃ cid evocchvas iti yadi ca kathaṃcit puṇyāvagamāt prabhūtapuṇyāvagatā alpīyasī vipākam aniṣṭaṃ bhāvayet na vitarkeṣu manaḥ praṇidadhīta pratipakṣabhāvanāheyā vitarkāḥ yadā ca sytut aprasavadharmiṇaḥ aprasavāś ca te dharmiṇaś cety aprasavadharmiṇaḥ yadā yogino manasi notpadyante nikṛttamūlāḥ santaḥ tadā tatkṛtaṃ yamaniyamasthairyakṛtam aiśvaryaṃ yoginaḥ siddhisūcakam ahiṃsādiphalasiddhijñāpakaṃ jāyata iti yogasiddhiphalam avasthitam eva anyad api yogāṅgastutaye aiśvaryam anuṣaṅgajātam ucyate katham ekaikasyāpy ahiṃsā ādīnāṃ sthiratvaliṅgam īdṛśaṃ yajñādidharmaphalair apy asamānaṃ pratyakṣata upalabhyate kim aṅga saṃhatānāṃ yogasiddhikaratvam iti tad etat pratidarśayati tad yathā ahiṃsāpratiṣṭhāyām ahiṃsāsthiratve avitarkaprādur bhāve tatsannidhau vairatyāgaḥ śāśvatikavicveṣiṇām api sarpanakulādīnāṃ tasyāhiṃsakasya sannidhau vairatyāgo bhavati satyapratiṣṭhāyāṃ satyasthair ye kriyāphalāśrayatvaṃ yajñādikriyāphalānām āgamanaṃ prāptir bhavati satyavādivākyād iti śeṣaḥ katham adhārmiko api dhārmito bhūyā ity ukte tadvacanād dhārmiko bhavati yathā dharme asya ramatāṃ mana iti devair uktaḥ kuṇḍadhārārādhī brāhmaṇo dhārmiko babhūva tathā svargaṃ prāpnuhīty uktaḥ svargaṃ prāpnoti yathā viśvāmitreṇa uktaḥ svargaṃ prāpnuhīti triśaṅkuḥ svargaṃ prāpa kiṃ bahunā amodhā asya vāk bhavati asteyapratiṣṭhāyāṃ asmṛhāyām tataḥ kim asya bhavati stnopasthānaṃ bhavati sarvadiksthāny asya upatiṣṭhante ratnāni ātmānaṃ darśayanti brahmacaryapratiṣṭhāyāṃ ābhyantaravṛttiḥ ābhyantarasya vāyor bahirnissāraṇaṃ prati vṛttir yasya sa ābhyantaravṛttiḥ tasmāt sa ābhyantaraḥ taṃ recaka ity ācakṣate tṛtīyas tu stambhavṛttiḥ tatrobhayābhāvaḥ ācamananiścāraṇayor uddhātaḥ tīvra iti tathā vāyūnāṃ dīrghatvam andatvāpatteḥ sūkṣmaṃ ca bhavati bāhyābhyantaraviṣayākṣepī caturthaḥ bāhyasya viṣayāḥ pādāṅguṣṭhādayaḥ bāhyo hi vāyur ācabhyamāno ntardeśān vyāpnoti ākṣipati ābhyantarasya viṣayā bhūmyādayaḥ sa ca bahirniścāryamāṇo bhūmyādīn deśakālasaṅkhyāparidṛṣṭān vyāpnoti ākṣipati sa bāhyābhyantaraviṣayāk ṛṛpī caturthaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ deśakālasaṅkhyābhir bāhyavastuviṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭa ākṣipto vyāptaḥ tathā ābhyantaraviṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭo deśakālasaṅkhyābhiḥ ākṣipto vyāptaḥ ubhayathā dīrghasūkṣmaḥ bāhyābhyantaraviṣayākṣepeṇobhayathā dīrghasūkṣmatvāpannaḥ kim ubhayabṛttisāmānyād aviśeṣatvam āśaṅkyāha tṛtīyas tadviṣayānālocitaḥ sakṛd ārabdha eva gatyabhāvo deśakālasaṅkhyābhiḥ paridṛṣṭo dīrghasūkṣmaḥ caturthas tu śvāsapraśvāsayoḥ ātamitoḥ viṣayāvadhāraṇāt samāptyarthaḥ yāsāṃ ca vaśyatānāṃ madhye pratyāhārasthairyāt paramā vaśyatā jāyate tā ucyante śabdādiṣv indriyajayaḥ avyasanaṃ punaḥ punar apra Vrttir anāsaktir vā iti kecid āhuḥ vyasanam iti nirbravīti saktir vyasanam katham vyasyati kṣipati enaṃ pratipattāraṃ śreyasaḥ sakāśād iti vyasanam aviruddhā pratipattir vā viruddhānāṃ vā śabda ādīnām apratipattir vaśyateti tasya eva vyākhyānaṃ nyāyyaḥ śāstrānujñātaḥ śabdādiṣu saṃyogaḥ svecchyā teṣv aviruddheṣu yadīcchati pravartate na vā ity evam anye manvate rāgadveṣābhāve sukhaduḥkhaśūnyaṃ heyopādeyatvavarjitaṃ śabdādijñānāṃ vaśyatety eke indriyavaśyatāsūpāyāntaram apekṣante jayārthaṃ asyāṃ punar na prayatnakṛtam upāyāntaram apekṣante yoginaḥ iti śrīgovindabhgavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya paramahāṃsaparvrājakācāryasya śrīśaṅkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śrīpātāñjalayoga śāstra sūtrabhāṣyavivaraṇe dvitīyaḥ sādhanapādaḥ uktāni pañca bahiraṅgāni sādhanāni samprajñātasya yogasya adhunā antaraṅgaṃ dhāraṇādhyānasamādhisamākhyaṃ sādhanatrayaṃ tasya evābhidhīyate bahiraṅgāntaraṅgatvabhedād eva hi bahiraṅgasādhanavyākhyānena eva pādaḥ parisamāpitaḥ saṃhatyakāritvāc ca sādhanatrayasya pṛthagvacanam
