samākhyālābhe kāraṇam avādiṣma dhāraṇā vaktavyā pratyāhārānantaraṃ kramopanītasannidhānā dhāraṇā abhidhānīyā deśabandhaś cittasya dhāraṇā deśabandhanaṃ deśabandhaḥ kasya cittasya svayam eva ca sarvaṃ vyācaṣṭe nābhicakre nābhideśaś cakram iva sarve vāyava avayavās tatra cakrībhūtā iti nābhicakram hṛdayaṃ puṇḍarīkākāram mūrdhajyotiṣi mūrdhanāḍīdvāraṃ prabhāsvaratvāj jyotir ity ākhyāyate nāsikāgre jihvāgre ity evam ādiṣu deśeṣu bāhyeṣu ca viṣayeṣu candrādityādiṣu cittaṃ badhyate tasya cittasya ity evam ādiṣv apracalitarūpeṇa yā vṛttiḥ sā dhāraṇety ucyate vṛttimātreṇeti tad deśapratyayamātreṇa vikṣepaśūnyatayā vartata iti tatra pratyayaikatānatā dhyānam tasmin deśe dhāraṇāvṛttiviṣaye nābhicakrādau dhyeyālambanasya dhyeyo deśādi tadālambanasya pratyayasya ekatānatā sadṛśapravāhaḥ tulyapratyayānāṃ pravāha ekākāraḥ pratyayasantānaḥ pratyayāntareṇa vijātīyena aparāmṛṣṭaḥ anākīrṇaḥ tat dhyānam dhāraṇā tu tasminn eva dhyeye tadavasthasya eva cittasya tadviṣayavikalptaiḥ pratyayāntaraiḥ parāmṛṣṭā api yathā sūrye dhāryamāṇasya tad gataparimaṇḍalatīvrataradīdhititvādipratyayeṣv api dhāraṇā eva vṛttimātreṇa tatra eva vartamānatvāc cittasya dhyānaṃ punaḥ na tu tathā bhinnajātīyapratyayāntarāparāmṛṣṭa ekapratyayapravāha eva hi dhyānam tad evārthamātranirbhāsaṃ svarūpaśūnyam iva samādhiḥ tad eva dhyānaṃ tulyapratyayapravāharūpaṃ svām ekapratyayasantānatām iva hitvā dhyeyākāranirbhāsaṃ dhyeyākāravad avabhāsate pratyayātmakena svena grahaṇātmanā svarūpeṇa śūnyam iva yathā sphaṭikadravyam upadhānāvabhāsaṃ svarūpaśūnyam iva yadā bhavati dhyeyasvabhāvāveśāt kāraṇāt cittasya tadā tad eva dheānaṃ samādhir ity ucyate nanu ca yogaḥ samādhir ity aṅgī pūrvam uktaḥ ihāṅgo yogasya samādhir ity ākhyāyate kaḥ punar atrāṅgāṅginor bheda iti ucyate yogaḥ samādhir iti cittasthitiviśeṣo vivakṣitaḥ iha tu pratyayasantānasya eva dhyeyasvabhāvāveśāt dhyeyākāratvam aṅgam iti viśeṣaḥ tad etad dhāraṇā dhyānasamādhitrayaṃ yad vyākhyānaṃ tat ekatra ekasmin deśe pariniṣpannaṃ sat sāṃyama ity ucyate tad āha ekaviṣayāṇi trīṇi sādhanāni saṃyama ity ucyate tad asya trayasya itthaṃ krameṇābhiniṣpannasya yatra yatra saṃyamaḥ śrūyate jetavyajayāya vā tatra tatra trayam etat praveditavyam ity evam artham etasya trayasyāsmin śāstre paribhāṣeyaṃ saṃyama iti vakṣyati ca pariṇāmatrayasaṃyamād atītānāgatajñānam sthūlasvarūpasūkṣmānvayārthavattvasaṃyamād bhūtajayaḥ iti ca tajjayāt prajñā lokaḥ tasya saṃyamasya jayāt sthiratvāpādanāt abhīpsitārthābhivyañjanasamarthaḥ pradīpālokadeśīyaḥ samādhiprajñāyā bhavaty ālokaḥ yathā yathā saṃyamaḥ sthirapado bhavati tathā tathā samāhiprajñā sthirapadī bhavati yena samādhiprajñā lokena vyavahitaviprakṛṣṭādivastunirbhāsanasamarthena yoginaḥ karatalakalitam ivābhimatam artham avalikayanti tasya bhūmiṣu viniyogaḥ tasya saṃyamasya bhūmiṣu bāhyādhyātmikeṣu dhyānālambanabhūtāsu vakṣyamāṇāsu pariṇāmatrayādiṣu viniyogaḥ prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ tadbhūmijayasākṣāt prayojanārthinā tasya saṃyamasya jitabhūmeḥ jitāyā bhūmeḥ yatra bhūmau yoginaḥ saṃyatāyāṃ saṃyamo labdhaḥ tasyā jitāyā bhūmeḥ anantarā yā bhūmis tatra saṃyamasya pūrvabhūmijayānantaraṃ viniyogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ tad yathā pṛthivyādīnāṃ sthūlasvarūpasūkṣmānvayārthavattvabhūmiṣu krameṇa jetavyāsu sthūāyāṃ bhūmau saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā tajjayānantaraṃ svarūpa evānantare saṃyamo viniyojanīyah nānantaraṃ svarūpam vyatilaṅghya sūkṣmādibhūmiṣu saṃvidadhīta kasmād evam na hy ajitādharabhūmir anantarāṃ bhūmiṃ vilaṅghya prāntabhūmiṣv uparitanīṣu bhūmiṣu saṃyamaṃ labhate yadi cānantarāṃ bhūmim ajitvā prāntabhūmiṣu saṃyamaṃ viniyuṅkṣeta tam eva saṃyamaṃ na labhate tataś ca tad alābha eva doṣaḥ tadalābhāc ca saṃyamābhāvāc ca kutas tatra saṃyamaviṣaye prāntabhūmāv ity arthaḥ prajñā lokaḥ nimittābhāvāt na hy asati tailavartijvalanābhisannipāte pradīpālokaḥ jitottarabhūmikasya jitottarātmādibhūmikasya yoginaḥ nādharabhūmiṣu paracittajñānādiṣu saṃyamo yuktaḥ kasmāt tadarthasya ātmādeḥ uttarabhūmer apakṛṣṭaparacittajñānādibhūmivaiparītyena anyathā evādhigatatvāt paracittajñānādibhiḥ saṃkīrṇaṃ asamādhigatavivekātmakatvāt tatra hi jitottarabhūmisaṃyamasya parakīyacittālambanatve saṃkīrṇacittākāratā yogicittasyāpi syād iti na yuktaḥ tatrātmāder arthasyānyathā eva viviktatayā adhigatatvāt anyeṣāṃ vyākhyānam arthasya paracittajñājādeḥ anyathā evādhigatatvāt ātmādyuttarabhūmisamādhigamanena eva adharaparacittajñānādibhūmer arthasyādhigatatvāt iti asmin pakṣe adharabhūmiṣu saṃyamo narthaka iti vaditavyam abhaviṣyat na na yukta iti na yukta ity etad asamīcīnam iva dṛśyate bhūmer asyā iyam anantarābhūmiḥ iyam anantaraṃ jayanīyā iti katham avabhotsyata ity āha tatra yoga evopādhyāyaḥ yogaḥ pūrvadhūmau saṃyamalābhaḥ tena eva ānantaryam avagamyate katham evaṃ hy uktam yogena yogo jñātavyaḥ pūrvasaṃyamalābhena yogenānantaro togaviṣayaḥ prajñānīyaḥ sa ca yogaḥ saṃyamaḥ tyogāt eva pūṛvasaṃyamalābhād eva pravartate vivicyate yathā eva januṣā andhakasya sopānapaṅktimārurukṣataḥ prathamasopānapratilabdhapadasparśapratyayena anantarasopānajñānam upaploṣyate tathā yogo yogāt pravartate yata evaṃ tasmāt sa itthaṃ jānan apramattas tu yogī yogena yuktaḥ san yogeṣu yogaiśvaryaphaleṣu ramate ciram iti trayam antaraṅgaṃ pūrvebhyaḥ dhāraṇādhyānasamādhitrayam antaraṅgaṃ pūrvebhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ sādhanebhyaḥ yamādibhyaḥ samprajñātasya yogasya tatrāntaraṅgagrahaṇaṃ pūrvasādhanāsampattāv apy atra trayo ādaraḥ karaṇīya ity evam artham vināpi hi yamādisādhanapañcatayasampadanena janmāntaravihitasaṃskārāveśavaśād eva videhaprakṛtilayānam iva dhāraṇāditrayasampattyā yoga upakalpyate dhāraṇāditrayeṇa vinā na yogaḥ saṃbhavati kasyacit tadvyāpāranairantaryasaṃvādātmakatvād dhāraṇādhitrayasya yagasya cittasampattirūpatvāt yadā tu jñānavairāgyasampattiḥ tadā na kiṃcid anyaddhāraṇādy apy apekṣyate tathā ca maṅkipiṅgalāprabhṛtīnām anuśrūyate vairāgyād eva samastasiddhiḥ tathā ca uktam sthānāsanavidhānānīti pūrvatra ślokadvayam tad api vbahiraṅgaṃ nirbījasya tad api etat antaraṅgam api sabījasya yogasya bahiraṅgaṃ bhavati nirbījasya yogasya kasmāt tad abhāve bhāvāt tasya sabījāntaraṅgasādhanatrayasyābhāve api puruṣasarvaviśeṣāpekṣayā nirbījayogasya bhāvāt bahiraṅgatvam kecid atisamīcīnadarśanā janmaniva saṃskārādparaktāḥ teṣāṃ paravairāgyavirāmapratyayasaṃśīlanādisamīkṣayā nirbījaḥ samādhir upajaniṣyata eva na hi teṣāṃ dhāraṇādisamīkṣaṇam tathā ca uktam uktaḥ samāhitacittasya yogaḥ vyutthitacitto api kathaṃ yoga yuktaḥ syād ity ata idam ārabhyate iti tathā bhavapratyayo videhaprakṛtilayānām iti atha nirodhacittakṣaṇeṣu nirodhayuktaṃ niarudhyamānaṃ cittaṃ yeṣu kṣaṇeṣu nirudhyate te nirodhacittakṣaṇāḥ teṣu nirodhakāle ity arthaḥ kṣaṇeṣv iti bahuvacanaṃ atītānāgatavartamānavṛttitvapradarśanārtham nirodhasya trikṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇo hi nirodhadharmam anvīyamānaṃ cittaṃ nirudhyate calaṃ guṇavṛttaṃ gauṇaṃ cittaṃ guṇavṛttaṃ calam ity avaśyaṃ bhāvī tasya bāhyavṛttibhyo nirudhyamānacittasya pariṇāmḥ na hy apariṇamamānasya cittasya puruṣavat kauṭasthye nirodha upakalpate tataś ca āha kīdṛśas tadā nirodhapariṇāma iti vyutthānanirodhasaṃskārayor abhibhavaprādur bhāvau nirodhakṣaṇacittānvayo nirodhapariṇāmaḥ vyutthānaṃ vividham utthānaṃ calanaṃ pratyayākāreṇa cittasya tadupajanitaḥ saṃskāraś cittasya dharmiṇo dharmaḥ na sa pratyayātmakaḥ tathā nirodhajanmā saṃskārah apratyayātmakaḥ cittasya eva dharmaḥ sa ca vyutthānasaṃskāro pratyayātmaka iti sa pratyayanirodhe na nirudhyate vyutthānapratyayanirodhe nābhibhūtaḥ pratyayanirodhāc ca nirodhajaḥ saṃskāraḥ sañjāyate tayoḥ vyutthānanirodhasaṃskārayoḥ dharmiṇi citte vartamānayoḥ abhibhavaprādurbhāvau bhavataḥ kiṃ tācāvirbhāvatirobhāvau aniyamena bhavataḥ na kathaṃ tarhi vyutthānasaṃskārā hīyante svakāryākṣamatvam upāśnuvate nirodhasaṃskārā ādhīyante tau cābhibhavaprādurbhāvau nirodhakṣaṇaṃ cittaṃ dharmitvena naveti sa tayor abhibhavaprādurbhāvayoś cittenānugamo nirodhapariṇāmaś cittasya tat etad abhihitaṃ bhavati ekasya cittasya pratikṣaṇam idaṃ saṃskārānyathātvaṃ vyutthānasaṃskārābhibhavena nirodhasaṃskāraprādurbhāvena saṃskārānyathātvam vyutthānasaṃskārāṇām api hīyamānatayā saty api sambandhe prādurbhavatā nirodhena eva balavattvāt nirodhapariṇāma iti samākhyātam tadā nirodhyamānaṃ bāhyebhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ saṃskāraśeṣaṃ cittam iti vyākhgyātam virāmapratyayābhyāsapūrvaḥ saṃskāraśeṣo nyaḥ iti kim etena āha nirodhāvasānatvāt pratyayābhāvāvasānatayā pariṇāmasya nirodhapariṇāma iti samprajñātāvasthāyāṃ santo api pratyayā na vivakṣitāḥ kiṃ tu pratikṣaṇasaṃskārānyathātvam eva vivakṣyate yathā niruddhabhūmini cetasi vidyamāno api samādhiḥ na vivakṣyate nirodhamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt tathā sabījāvasthāyām api saṃskārānyathātvamātram eva vivakṣitam na pratyayāḥ samādhir ekāgratā ceti tasya cittasya nirodhapariṇāmam anugacchataḥ praśāntavāhitā saṃskārāt nirodhasaṃskārapāṭavāpekṣā nirodhasaṃskārasya pāṭavaṃ draḍhimā draḍhimā tadapekṣā praśāntavāhitā prasannata cittasya bhavati sā praśāntavāhitā kiyantaṃ kālam ity āha taṃ saṃskāraṃ nirodhasaṃskāraṃ ārabhya yāvat vyutthānadharmiṇā vyutthaānaṃ dharmo byutthānajanitatvād yasya tena saṃskāreṇa nirodhadharmasaṃskāro nābhbhūyate tāvantaṃ kālam asya praśāntavāhitā nirodhasaṃskārasamudayād iti sarvārthataikāgratayoḥ kṣayodayau cittasya samādhipariṇāmaḥ sarvārthatā bhogāpavargārthayogyatāvicitratā cittadharmaḥ vakṣyati draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ cittaṃ sarvārtham iti ekāgratāpi cittasya dharmaḥ śāntoditapratyayoḥ sāmyaṃ samādhīyamānasya cittasya sarvārthatāyāḥ kṣayaḥ bhavati tirobhāva ity arthaḥ na hi kiṃcidvidyamānaṃ vinaṅkṣyati ekāgratāyā udayaḥ bhavati āvirbhāva ity arthaḥ nāvidyamānam utpadyate tayoh kṣayodayayoḥ dharmitvenānugataṃ cittam pūrvasūtrād anvayagrahaṇam ihāpi sannidhīyate sarvārthatāyāḥ kṣayam ekāgratāyāś codayaṃ niyamenānvīyamānaṃ cittaṃ samādhiprādhānyena pariṇamate yo asau cittena sarvārthataikāgratākṣayodayayor anugamah sa samādhipariṇāmaḥ samādheś ca prādhānayam ekāgratābhūmau vyākhyātam yas tv ekāgre cetasi sa bhūtam arthaṃ pradyotayati iti tad evāha tad idaṃ cittam apāyopajanau svātmabhūtau avyatiriktau tayor dharmayoḥ sarvārthataikāgratayoḥ anu bhavā gamāt samādhīyate sa cittasya samādhiprādhānyāt samādhipariṇāmaḥ tatra punaḥ samādhikālae śāntoditau tulyapratyayau cittasyaikāgratāpariṇāmaḥ samāhitacittasya niruddhabāhyavṛtteḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaḥ śāntaḥ tirobhūtaḥ uttaras tatsadṛśa uditaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ samādhicittaṃ samāhānaviśiṣṭaṃ samādhyavastham samādhicittamubhayoḥ śāntoditayoḥ pratyayoḥ anugatam punas tathā eva yathā pratyaya ādyaḥ śānta uttaras tatsadṛśa upajātaḥ sa ca śāntaḥ punar anya uditaḥ sa śāntaḥ punaś cānya uditaḥ ity evaṃ ā samādhibhreṣāt vyutthānasaṃskāreṇa yāvat samādhiḥ vibhraṃśate sa khalv ayaṃ dharmiṇaḥ cittasya pratikṣaṇaṃ sad ṛṛśaśāntoditapratyayayor anugamaḥ ekāgratāpariṇāmaḥ tatra yāvat bāhyavṛttinirodhād ārabhya cittasya saṃskārapariśeṣatā tāvat nirodhapariṇāmaḥ tathā bāhyapratyayanirodhāt prabhṛti ā prāk aśeṣapratyayanirodhāt aśeṣapratyayanirodhottarakālaṃ ca ekāgratodayābhāvāt tāvat samādhipariṇāmaḥ tathā samāhipariṇāmakāla eva śāntoditayos tulyayoḥ saṃbhavād ekāgratāpariṇāmaḥ pūrvapariṇā māna manāntarīyakatvam uttarottarapariṇāmasya iti krameṇa trayo api pariṇāmā vyākhyātāḥ kim anena pariṇāmānvākhyānena prayojanam ucyate calaṃ guṇavṛttaṃ gauṇaṃ ca samastaṃ pariṇāmadharmakam anavasthitam iti vairāgyabhāvanārtham tathā pariṇāmatrayasaṃyamād atītānāgatajñānārthaṃ ca etad anvākhyānam etena bhūtendriyeṣu dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmā vyākhyātāḥ etena pūrvoktena cittapariṇāmena kiṃciśiṣṭena dharmalakṣaṇāvasthārūpeṇa dharmarūpeṇa lakṣaṇarūpeṇāvasthā rūpeṇa ca bhūtendriyeṣu bhūteṣu pṛthivī prabhṛtiṣu sthūleṣu indriyeṣu śrotrādiṣu yeṣāṃ tattvāntarapariṇāmo nāsti dharmapariṇāmo lakṣaṇapariṇāmo vasthāpariṇāmaś ca ukto veditavyaḥ cittasyānavasthitatvena gamyamānena pariṇāmena bhūtendriyāṇāṃ pariṇāmasya pariṇāmasya prakāratrayayoginaḥ cittapariṇativat asuvijñānatvāt atideśaḥ kriyate nanu ca nirodhasamādhy ekāgratāp ariṇāmāś cittasyābhihitāḥ na tu dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmāḥ kutas tatrātideśa ity abhihitatvam eṣāṃ darśayati tatra vyutthānanirodhayoḥ dharmayoḥ abhibhavaprādur bhāvau dharmiṇi citte dharmapariṇāmaḥ etasmād dhi dharmabhedavacanāt dharmabhedam avādiṣma tayoś ca dharmapariṇāmayoh vyutthānanirodhayor abhibhavaprādurbhāvavacanāt lakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmāv api cāvādiṣma eva katham vartamānalakṣaṇād atītalakṣaṇam abhisampadyamāno dharmo abhibhūyate yaś cānāgatalakṣaṇāt vartamānalakṣaṇam abhisampadyamānaḥ sa prādur asti tad abhibhavaprādur bhāvavacanāc ca pratikṣaṇaṃ durbalarūpo vasthāpariṇāma ukto bhavatīty āha lakṣaṇapariṇāmī kūṭastha ity ucyate sa khalu nirodhaḥ anāgatalakṣaṇam adhvanaṃ hitvā dharmatvaṃ nirodhadharmatvaṃ anatikrāntaḥ asatkāryārambhāvāt asatkāryārambhe hi trikālatvam ekasya vastuno na upapadyate nāpi kālatrayaparicchedyasya trilakṣaṇasyābhāvāt ata ucyate dharmatvam anatikrāmann eva vartamānaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pratipannaḥ yatra yasmin vartamāne lakṣaṇe asya svarūpeṇābhivyaktiḥ eṣo asya nirodhasyānāgatādhvasamīkṣayā dvitīyo dhvā yadā tu vyutthānaṃ vartamānaṃ lakṣaṇam ārokṣyati tadā nirodho tītalakṣaṇam adhvānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ prāpsyatīti sa tṛtīyo dhvā bhaviṣyaty eva syād etat vartamānalakṣaṇapratipattau nirodhasya tryadhvaṃ nāstīty ata āha na cātītānāgatābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyāṃ viyuktaḥ kutaḥ yena sa evānāgato vartamāno tītaś ceti tathā vyutthānaṃ trilakṣaṇaṃ tribhir adhvabhiḥ atītānāgatavartamānaiḥ yuktaṃ vartamānalakṣaṇaṃ hitvā dharmatvam anatikrāntaṃ yathā vyākhgyātam nirodhe nirodhini dharme vartamānam adhvānam ahisampadyamāne atītalakṣaṇaṃ adhvvānaṃ pratipannam eṣo asya vyutthānasya vartamānaṃ prathamam adhvānam abhisamīkṣya dvitīyo dhvā dvitīye tu paryāye tṛtīyua evādhvā dvitīyo bhaviṣyati na cānāgatavartamānābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyāṃ viyuktam punar vyutthānaṃ nirodhasaṃskāreṇa upasampadyamānam anāgatalakṣaṇaṃ adhvānaṃ hitvā dharmatvam anatikrāntaṃ vartamānalakṣaṇaṃ pratipannam yatrāsya svarūpeṇābhivyaktau satyāṃ vyāpāraḥ svakāryāpādanasāmarthyam eṣo asya svarūpeṇābhivyaktaū satyāṃ vyāpāraḥ svakāryāpādanasāmarthyam eṣo asya anāgatābhisamīkṣyā dvitīyo dhvā na cātītānāgatābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyāṃ viyuktam yathā cittaṃ vyutthānanirodhadharmābhyāṃ na yujyate evaṃ punar nirodhaḥ evaṃ punaḥ vyutthānam iti eṣa lakṣaṇapariṇāmaś cittadharmayor vyutthānanirodhayoḥ tathā avasthāpariṇāmaḥ paridṛśyate katham nirodhakṣaṇeṣu nirodhe vartamāne nirodhasaṃskārā balavanto bhavanti saṃskārabalavattvena nirodhabalavattvam api durbalā vyutthānasaṃskārāḥ tata eva vyutthānadurbalatvam api tathā vyutthānalakṣaṇe vyutthānasaṃskārabalīyastvaṃ nirodhasaṃskāradurbalatvam ity evaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ dṛḍhadurvalāvatthābhyāṃ yujyamānānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ avasthāpariṇāmaḥ tatra kena rūpeṇa kasya pariṇāma iti darśayati dharmiṇo dharmaiḥ pariṇāmaḥ yathā cittasya dharmiṇo nirodhavyutthānādidharmaiḥ dharmāṇāṃ tryadhvanāṃ lakṣaṇaiḥ pariṇāmaḥ yathā nirodhādicittadharmāṇāṃ anāgatādilakṣaṇaiḥ lakṣaṇānām apy avasthābhiḥ pariṇāmaḥ yathā vartamānādilakṣaṇānāṃ dṛḍhadurbalatvādyavasthābhiḥ ity evaṃ dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmaiḥ aśūnyalakṣaṇam aśūnyarūpaṃ guṇāvṛttam avatiṣṭhete calaṃ guṇavṛttam etad eva tu guṇasvabhāvyaṃ pravṛttikāraṇaṃ sakalavyāpārakāraṇaṃ uktaṃ guṇānāṃ sattvādīnām iti etena cetasi prasiddhena dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmatriyena bhūtyendriyeṣu dharmadharmibhedāt trividhaḥ pariṇāmo veditavyaḥ paramārthatas tv eka eva pariṇāmaḥ katham dharmisvarūpamātro hi dharmaḥ na hi dharmiparihāreṇa dharmo nāma pṛthag asti nāpi dharmaparityāgena lakṣaṇaṃ nāma pṛthak bhāvyate nāpi lakṣaṇavyatirekeṇāvasthānāṃ pṛthaktvaṃ bhavati tena dharmivikriyā evaiṣā dharmadvārā dharmabhedadvāreṇa tridhā prapañcyate kathaṃ punar dharmivikriyā evaiṣā na punar atyāntāpūrvotpattivināśāv iti tata āha tatra dharmasya ghaṭādeḥ dharmiṇi mṛdākhye vartamānasyādhvasvatītānāgatavartamāneṣu bhāvānyathātvam eva pratyayānyathātvam atīto ghaṭaḥ vartate anāgataḥ iti ca dharmiṇivartamānasya eva sa eva dharmasyāvirbhāvatirobhāvānyathātvam na dravyānyathātvaṃ tad eva mṛd dravyaṃ dharmi rūpā antaraṃ ca udāharaṇaṃ paridarśayati yathā suvarṇabhājanasya bhitvā anyathā kuṇḍalādibhāvena kriyāmāṇasya bhāvānyathātvaṃ svastikakuṇḍalādisaṃsthānānyatvam na suvarṇadravyānyathātvam iti apara āhāsatkāryasamārambhābhimānī dharmābhyadhiko dharmavyatirikto dharmī dharmaś cāvidyamāno anyaś cānyaś ca samudāyiṣyate na punar eko dharmī dharmeṣu bhūtabhaviṣyadvartamāneṣu dharmāvyatirikto nvayīti yady anvayī dharmānabhyadhiko dharmāvyatiriktaḥ pūrvatattvāt pūrvapūrvadravyasvarūpāt anatikrāman pūrvāparāvasthābhedam atītādyavasthābhedam anugatitaḥ anugataḥ syāt tataś ca eṣa doṣaḥ prasajati sa dharmī tavābhimataḥ kauṭasthyenāpi parivartetāpariṇāmmitve varteta atrāhāyam adoṣaḥ kasmāt ekāntānabhyupagamāt ātyantakauṭasthyavināśayoḥ dharmiṇo nabhyupagamāt yady atyantaṃ kūṭastho dharmī syāt ātmavat tataś cāsmād dharmiṇo dharmāṇām abhedāt kauṭasthaṃ prasajyateti doṣaḥ syāt na tu dharmiṇāṃ guṇānām atyantakauṭastham abhyupagamyate pariṇāminityatvaṃ hi guṇānāṃ vadiṣyati atha vā dharmadharmiṇoḥ ekāntabhedānabhyupagamāt ekāntena hi dharmibhyo nvayibhyo dharmiṇāṃ ā bhedaṃ kauṭasthyaṃ prāpnuyāt atyantabhede vā dharmāṇāṃ atyantavināśaḥ syāt na tv atyantabhedābhedāv abhyupayiṣyete tasmāt na kauṭastgyadoṣa iti kathaṃ kauṭasthyābhāva ity āha tad etat vailokyaṃ vyakter apaiti na kūṭastham kasmāt nityatvapratiṣedhāt kāryatvād eva hi nityatvaṃ pratiṣiddham athātyntavinaṣṭam iti ced āhāpetam apy asti vināśapratiṣedhāt kāraṇasya nityatvāt tad abhedāc ca kāryasya atyantavināśaḥ pratiṣiddha eva tataś ca yad ucyate kaiś cit viruddhahetvābhāsodāharaṇam etad iti kathaṃ yathā asau vikāro vyakter apaiti nityatvapratiṣedhāt apetam apy asti vināśapratipadhot ity atra nityatvapratiṣedhāt ity ayaṃ hetuḥ apeto api vikāro stīty anena siddhāntena virudhyate katham vyaktir ātmalābhaḥ apāyaḥ pracyutiḥ yady ātmalābhāt pracyuto vikāro sti nityatvapratiṣedho na upapadyate yat tu vyakter apetasyāpi vikārasyāstitvaṃ tat khalu nityatvam iti nityatvapratiṣedho nāma vikārasyātmalābhāt pracyutiḥ yadātmalābhāt pracyuvate tad anityam yad asti na tāatmalābhāt pracyuvate astitvaṃ ca ātmalābhāt pracyutiś ceti viruddhāv etau dharmau saha na sambhavataḥ so yaṃ hetuḥ yaṃ siddhāntam āśritya pravartate tam eva vyāhantīti viruddho hatur iti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ vastūnāṃ vyaktāvyaktadharmakatvābhyupagamāt yathā hi ghaṭādividyamāno api san agāre na upalabhyate na ca tāvatā asau nāstīti śakyaṃ pratijñātum ālokopāyena hi vyajyate tathā idaṃ trailokyaṃ kāraṇe saṃsṛṣṭaṃ vidyamānam eva anabhivyaktātmakaguṇasvabhāvatayā puruṣārthanimittenāviṣkriyate tathā eva ca gatisaṃskārakṣaye sthitisaṃskārābhivyaktau kāraṇaṃ prati saṃsṛjyamānaṃ vyakter apaiti yathā dīpālokatirodhāne vidyamāno api ghaṭādih santam asāvaṣṭambhāt vyakter apasarati tathā atrāpi mahadādayo dharmāḥ tryadhvānaḥ saṃsargavisargadharmāṇaḥ na tu sattvādayo dharmiṇaḥ tatas trailokyaṃ mahadādistambaparyavasānaṃ sattvādīnāṃ dharmabhūtam na bhivyaktidharmakaṃ sat atyantaniruddhasūkṣmadharmasamudāyāt vyaktisthūladharmarūpeṇa na gṛhyata ity ucyate tad etat trailokyaṃ vyakter apaitīti na punaḥ darmisvarūpeṇāpāyaḥ tathā ca dharmirūpeṇa nityatvād ucyate tadapetam apy astīti tad evaṃ vyaktirūpaś ca śaktirūpaś ca eko dharmī vyaktirūpeṇa ca tasyānityatvaṃ śaktirūpeṇa ca nityatvam iti katham eṣa virodhaḥ syāt na hi devadattaś calanādivyāpāreṇa sarvadā gṛhyamāṇaś calanādivirāme viraṃsyati calanam eva hi tirodhīyate tasmād avyaktāvasthitaghaṭādivat vyaktir api svakīyadharmāntarasamīkṣayā dharmiṇī sā ca dharmirūpeṇanityā dharmarūpeṇānityā abhyupeyate evaṃ vikāreṣu dharmadharmibhedo anavasthita ity anavasthāapi iṣyata eva tatra vyakter apaitīty anena na virudhyate nityatvapratiṣedhāt ity ayaṃ hetuḥ nāpi apatem apy astīty anena virodhaḥ ubhayor bhinnaviṣayatvāt nāpi vināśapratiṣedhāt ity ayaṃ apetam apy astīty anena virudhyate yathā bāhyād apeto apy asti devadattam tad etad anirjñāya parābhiprāyaṃ virodhodāharaṇatvāpādānam andhadarpaṇīyavṛttāntam udbhāvayati yathā kila kaścid andhaḥ svāṃ adarśanaśaktiṃ anavadhārya svārtham ādarśam upājayati tadvad etad ābhāti api ca yady apy ekatraivavyaktau śaktau vā nityatvam anityatvaṃ ca adhyāropya tvaṃ pakṣasiṣādhayiṣayā bravīthāḥ evam api viruddhodāharaṇatvaṃ na sambhavati viparītā ta sādhanāt katham apeto apy astīti nityatvapratiṣedhāt ity ucyate nityatvapratiṣedhāt ity anityatvād ity uktaṃ bhavati apetasyāpy astitvaṃ nityatvam ucyate nityatvasya viparītam anityatvam na ca pakṣasyānityatvasyānityatvaṃ hetur bhavati yo viparītaṃ sādhayan nityatvaṃ virundhīta na hy aniṣṭam asādhayan viruddhatām iyāt athāpi nityatvapratiṣedho nāma ātmalābhāt pracyutir iti vika lpasya lpya vāvadyothāḥ evam api śabdabhdamātraṃ trāt nārthabhedaḥ ātmalābhāt pracyutiḥ anityatvaṃ ity eko rthaḥ athāpi nityatvopapattyabhāvād ity avalambethāḥ evam api nityatvapratiṣedhāt ity ayaṃ śabdaḥ ekasyāṃ śuktikāyāṃ nityatvopapattyabhāvād ity asyārthasya ā vācakaḥ athāpi vācaka ity āropya pratibhāṣeta evam api śaktivyaktidharmadharmibheda rūpeṇa de na nityatvam anityatvaṃ tyrūpaṃ cety ukyam eva samādhānam etena vyakteḥ apeto apy asti vināśapratiṣedhāt iti virodhodbhāvanaṃ praty ākhyātam evam avasthite vyakter apetasya pratyakṣeṇānupalbhyamānasya katham astitvam yāvatā nāsti snupalabhyamānatvāt nabhaḥkusumavat iti atrocyate anupalabdhir asiddho hetuḥ anumānāgamābhyām upalabdheḥ yad etat vyaktaṃ etat prāg utpatter apy asti yata utpadyate asaccennotpadyeta caśaviṣāṇavad eva kiṃ cāsataḥ sattve sataś cāsattve sarvatra na āśvāsyuḥ kiṃ cānupalabdheś ced asattvaṃ muktātmakāraṇādīnāṃ ca prāg upalambhād ūrdhvaṃ cāstitvaṃ kena lahyate tathā nasato vidyate bhāvo nābhāvo vidyate sataḥ BhG iti āgamaḥ pratyakṣānupalabdhiś ca nāsattvasya kāraṇam atha vyakter eva vikārp vidyamānaś cet kuto na upalabhyata iti āha sākṣāt kāraṇe saṃsargād asya saukṣmyam ato nupalabdhiḥ nāsatvāt idānīṃ bhūtendriyāṇāṃ lakṣaṇapariṇāma idam ucyate lakṣaṇapariṇāmo dharmo yathā mṛdo ghaṭādiḥ adhvasu atītādiṣu vartamāno tīto dharmaḥ kim uktaṃ bhavati atītalakṣaṇayuktaḥ na punar asattvam āpannaḥ itarābhyāṃ cānāgatavartamānābhyām aviyuktaḥ kāraṇasya mṛdo vartamānatvāt tatra saṃsṛṣṭasya ghaṭasya ā vidyamānatve pi nasyāpi yukto vartamānena lakṣaṇena ghaṭaḥ tathā bhaviṣyann api ghaṭo mṛda evānāgataḥ san bhaviṣyatīty anāgatalakṣaṇenāpy aviyuktaḥ tathā vartamānah vartamānalakṣaṇayuktaḥ atītānāgatābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyām aviyuktaḥ tathā anāgataḥ anāgatalakṣaṇayuktaḥ vartamānātītābhyāṃ lakṣāṇābhyāṃ aviyuktaḥ atītānāgatalakṣaṇayoḥ mṛdātmakatvāt ghaṭasya vyavahitenāpy atītalakṣaṇenāviyogaḥ katham ekalakṣaṇayukto dharmo lakṣaṇābhyām aparābhyām aviyukta ity aviyogasya dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā puruṣa ekasyāṃ striyāṃ rakto na śeṣasu virakto bhavati śeṣāsu tu bhūtabhaviṣyallakṣaṇayukto rāgaḥ sataś cāvināśād asataś cānutpatter iti hi pratipāditam atra lakṣaṇapariṇāme sarvasya dharmasya sarvalakṣaṇayogād adhvasaṃkaraḥ paurdoṣaś codyate katham yo hi bhaviṣyati sa vartate atītaś ca tenātīte vartamānabhaviṣyattvam vartamāne atītabhaviṣyattvam bhaviṣyati cātītavartamānatvam ity evam anyonyādhvasaṃkaraḥ tasya parihāraḥ ayam ucyate dharmiṇo mṛdākhyasya dharmāṇāṃ miṇḍaghaṭakapālānāṃ dharmatvaṃ dharmāntarāc cābhinnatvam aprasādhyam sati ca dharmatve tad bhede ca lakṣaṇabhedo api siddho vācyaḥ katham yathā piṇḍāvasthāyāṃ anāgatalakṣaṇayukto ghaṭo na vartamāno nāpi atītaḥ yady api mṛttvabhaviṣyattvasamīkṣayā atītavartamānābhyāṃ api avi yuktaḥ tathā vartamānalakṣaṇayukto nātīto nāpy anāgataḥ yady api dharmirūpeṇāpe ve kṣyamāṇaḥ atītānāgatalakṣaṇābhyāṃ hīyamānajāyamānābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyām api vi yuktaḥ tathā piṇḍakapālādiṣu yojanīyam tasmād āha na vartamānasamaya evāsya ekaṃ lakṣaṇo dharmasya kiṃ tarhi prakāreṇoktena trilakṣaṇatvam ato nādhvānaḥ saṃkīryante evaṃ hi na cittaṃ rāgadharmakam iti na citte vi rāga dharmiṇi rāgādīnāṃ dharmatve tadbhede ca siddhe advasaṃkaraḥ kasmāt krodhakāle rāgasyāsamudācārāt na hi krodhakāle rāgaḥ svakāla iva samudācarati krodhakāle hi rāgaḥ atīto nāgato vā tathā krodho api rāgakāle yadi hi vartamānasamaya evaikaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ abhaviṣyat kodhakāle nāsti kiṃ ca trayāṇāṃ lakṣaṇānāṃ yugapad ekasyāṃ lakṣaṇasya vṛttau virodhāt nāsti sambhavaḥ krameṇa lakṣaṇānāṃ krameṇa svavyañjakānjanasya ghaṭādisvavyañjakāñjanasyānyatam asya kaṣaṇasya bhavet sambhavaḥ uktaṃ ca rūpātiśayāḥ vṛttyatiśayāś ca virudhyante vartamānarūpavṛttyatiśayair yukte ghaṭe ca piṇḍādivyaktirūpātiśayā virodhāt na saṃbhavanti ata evātītānāgatarūpā dharmisāmānyānugatatvenāvirodhāt atiśayaiḥ saha vartante tasmāt adhvanām asaṃkaraḥ yathā rāgasya eva kvacit samudācāra iti na tadānīm anyatra ctriṣu abhāvo rāgasya kin tu kevalaṃ sāmānyena cittarūpeṇa samanvāgataḥ atīto nāgato api san ity asti tadā tasya rāgasya bhāvaḥ tathā lakṣaṇasya iti nanu ca piṇḍakapālayor atītānāgatatvāt ghaṭāvasthāyām abhāvāc ca tābhyāṃ mṛdākhyasya dharmiṇo api atītānāgatatvam iti dharmiṇi piṇḍakapālayor abhāva iti kṛtvā dharmāṇāṃ piṇḍakapālādīnām adhvatrayānupapattir iti pariśaṅkamānaḥ kathayati na dharmī tryadhvā mṛdākhyo hi dharmī piṇḍakpālātītānāgatatvena nātīto nāgato vā sarvadharmeṣu mṛdabhijñānānu pra vṛtteḥ kiṃ tarhi dharmāḥ piṇḍādayaḥ tryadhvānaḥ ghaṭakāle piṇḍakapālayor adarśanāt tasmād adhvatrayāyogo na dharmāṇāṃ pariśaṅkanīyaḥ te dharmā lakṣitāḥ piṇḍādayaḥ tryadhvatvenābhilakṣitāḥ tāṃ tām avasthāṃ dṛḍhadurbalatvādikāṃ prāpnuvanto nyatvena navo ghaṭaḥ purāṇaś cety anena pratinirdiśyante vasthāntarataḥ na dravyāntarataḥ mṛdatiriktāt yathā ekā rekhā śatasthāne śūnyadvayena tṛtīyasthāne śataṃ bhavati sā eva ca daśasthāne ekena śūnyena dvitīyasthāne daśa sā eva prathamasthāne ekā yathā vā ekatve api strī mātā cotyate duhitā ca sā eva anyāpekṣayā svasā ca tad evam avasthāntarād eva śabdapratyayādibhedāḥ na dharmadharmibhedena tasmāt yad ucyate paraiḥ śabdapratyayalakṣaṇadharmakālādibhedo hetuḥ kāryakāraṇabhede iti so nenānaikāntikīkṛtaḥ avasthāpariṇāme tṛtīye smin kauṭasthyaprasaṅgadoṣaḥ kaiścit uktaḥ kathaṃ kauṭasthyaprasaṅgaḥ adhvānaḥ vartamānādayaḥ svavyāpāreṇa vyavahi sthi tāḥ katham yadā dharmo ghaṭaḥ piṇḍāvasthāyāṃ svavyāpāraṃ na karoti tadā anāgataḥ yadā karoti tadā vartamānaḥ ayam yadā kṛtvā nivṛttaḥ tadā atītaḥ tatra sa eva dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ kariṣyamāṇaḥ nijavyāpāropārūḍhaḥ dharmitvātmabhūta evāvasthāpitaḥ na vyatiriktarūpaḥ tena dharmiṇāṃ guṇānāṃ nityatvāt nityatvāvyatirekāt dharmalakṣaṇāvasthanāṃ kauṭasthyaṃ prāpnoti iti doṣa ucyate nāsau doṣaḥ kasmāt guṇinityatve api guṇānāṃ vimardavaicitryāt udbhavābhibhavatvavicitratayā puruṣavad ekāntakūṭasthatā neṣyate guṇānām pariṇāmābhyupagamāt na cānavaratapariṇatīnām api parasparavimardātrirekeṇa dravyāntarabhāvāpattir iti na kauṭasthyam kathaṃ vimardavaicitryam ity āha yathā saṃsthānaṃ śarīrādikaṃ ādi mat kāraṇavat dharmamātraṃ kāraṇasyātmabhūtam avyatiriktaṃ vināśi tirobhāvadharmakaṃ dharmāntarasamudaye keṣāṃ saṃsthānam ity ā mā ha śabda ādīnām avināśinām evaṃ liṅgaṃ mahadākhyaṃ ādimat kāraṇavat dharmamātraṃ vināśi guṇānām avināśinām ātmabhūtam tasmin mahadādidharmamātre vikārasaṃjñā na guṇānāṃ vimardavicitratayā vināśitvaṃ guṇāsvarūpeṇa nityatvaṃ iti tatrdāharaṇam mṛta dharmī piṇḍākārā piṇḍākārāt ākārāntaraṃ ghaṭaṃ upasampadyamāno dharmataḥ pariṇamate ghaṭākāro nāgataṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hitvā vartamānalakṣaṇaṃ pratipadyata iti lakṣaṇataḥ pariṇamate tathā ghaṭo navapurāṇatāṃ pratikṣaṇam anubhavan avasthāpariṇāmaṃ pratipadyata iti dharmiṇo api mṛdādeḥ dharmāntaraṃ piṇḍādikaṃ avasthā dharmī piṇḍakapālādirūpāvasthām āsīd iti tata eka eva pariṇāmo bhedena upadarśita iti evaṃ adārthānareṣv api mṛdaḥ anyeṣv api śarīrendriyādiṣu yojyam ta ete dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmā dharmisvarūpam anatikrāntā ity eka eva dharmiṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ sarvān dharmalakṣaṇāvasthāpariṇāmān viśeṣān abhimpavate kutaḥ yena avasthitasya dravyasya pūrvadharmanivṛttau dharmāntarotpattiḥ pariṇām iti dharmī pariṇām eva iti śakyaṃ pratipattum kaḥ punar asau dharmī yasmin avasthite dharmāntaravirāme dharmāntarodayaḥ pariṇāma iti tatra śāntoditāvyapadeśyadharmānupātī dharmī śāntoditān avyapadeśyāṃś ca dharmānanupatituṃ śīlaṃ yasya so nvayī bhinneṣv abhinnātmā dharmīti vyapadiśyate dharmaḥ nāma yogyatāvacchinnā śaknoti raśaṇākuṇḍalādibhāvam āpattum iti yā suvarṇasya dharmiṇaḥ kuḍalatvādikā śāktiḥ sa eva dharmaḥ sa cāvyakto api san dharmiṇi phalaprasavabhedānumitasadbhāvaḥ yathā deśāntare kālāntare ca tāḍaṅkādikāṃ phalaṃ kankapiṇḍaḥ prasūyate tatphalaprasavabhedadarśānenānyānanyān api prakārānyaṃ prasavituṃ vibhavatīti tasmin dharmiṇi phalaprasavabhedānumitasadbhāvaḥ ekasya dharmiṇaḥ anyaś cānyaś ca dharma ity anena ekasya dharmiṇo dharmāsāṃkhyatvam āha tatra yo dṛṣṭaḥ sa vartamānaḥ svaṃ vyāpāram udakāharaṇādikaṃ anubhavan dharmāntarebhyaḥ śāntebhyaś cāvyapadeśyebhyaś ca bhidyate yadā tu sāmānyena dharmirūpeṇa samanvāgato bhavati atha tadā dharmisvarūpamātratvāt dharmisvarūpātmabhūtatvāt ko sau viśeṣataḥ kena vā bhidyate vyāpārādhirūḍharūpāṇām eva bhedo na kāraṇasamuanugamanirīkṣitātmanām ity arthaḥ ke punaḥ śāntā uditā avyapadeśyā vā te khalu dharmiṇo dharmāḥ śāntāḥ ye kṛtvā vyāpāram paratāḥ savyāpārā uditāḥṭe cānāgatalakṣaṇasya samanantarāḥ tathā vartamānasyānantarā atītāḥ kimartham atītasyānantarā na bhavanti sa santīty arthaḥ pūrvapaścibhābhāvāt yo yasya paścād bhavati sa tasya paścimo nantaraḥ itaraś ca tadapekṣayā pūrvaḥ tad iha paścibhābhāvāt eṣa svayam api pūrvo na bhavatīti pūrvapaścibhābhāvād atītasyānantarā na santi yathā anāgatavartamānayoḥ pūrvapaścimatā na evam atītasya tasmāt na nātī tasyāsti samanantaraḥ yas tv ayaṃ pāṭhaḥ tadanāgata eva samanantarībhavati vartamānasya iti na tasya prakṛtena sambandhaḥ tasmāt tadanāgata eva samanantaro bhavaty atītasya ity ayam eva pāṭhaḥ arthopapatteḥ kathaṃ yadā vyutthānasaṃskāro nirodhasaṃskāreṇa ādyo abhibhūyate tadā vartamānam adhvanaṃ hitvā vyutthānasaṃskāro tītam adhvānam upasampadya punar anāgataḥ san vartamānībhavatīty asamanantaro apy anāgata eva samanantarībhavaty atītasya ity ucyate atītānāgatayor lakṣaṇayor dharmāṇāṃ dharmisvarūpamātrāviśeṣāt athāvyapadeśyāḥ ke tadavyapadeśyābhipradarśanārtham āha sarvaṃ sarvātmakaṃ iti katham tatra uktam jalabhūmyoḥ pāriṇāmikaṃ rasādivaiśvarūpyaṃ sthāvareṣu dṛṣṭam yathā rasa eka eva ikṣuśṛṅkagerakādiṣu madhurakaṭukatvādi vaiśvarūpyaṃ pratipadyate tathā rūpasya śuklakṛṣṇatvādivicitrarūpatvam evaṃ gandhādiṣv api tathā sthāvarāṇāṃ jaṅgameṣu rasādivaiśvarūpyam sthāvarāṇām upayuktāṇāṃ jaṅgameṣu rasalohitādiviśvabhedaḥ tathā jaṅgamānāṃ sthāvareṣu upayuktānām vṛkṣāyurvedaprasiddhaṃ rasādivaiśvarūpyam evaṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ sthāvareṣu jaṅgamānāṃ jaṅgameṣu ity evaṃ jātyanucchedena sattvādyavināśena sarvaṃ sarvātmakam aṅguliśikhare lokatrayam apy asti tathā cāṅguṣṭhād asṛjat brahmā romakūpebhyaḥ ity ādiśrutismṛtiśataprasthānam yadi sarvaṃ sarvātmakam tadā sarvaṃ sarvatropalabhyeta sammativiprayogajanmā ca śoko mā pra ti vartiṣṭetyāder uttaraṃ pathati deśakālākāranimittāpabandhāt deśādīnām apabandhaḥ avabandhaḥ tasmāt na samānakālaṃātmanāṃ sarvavastūnāṃ abhivyaktiḥ kasya cit kvacid eva deśe kāle ca kena cidevākāreṇa tanubhṛtāṃ ca dharmādinimittābhisamīkṣayā kvacid evābhivyaktiḥ yathā rāhuprabhṛtīnām etena eva sammativiprayoganimittaśokādyupapattiḥ ata ekaikasmin atilaṅghitasaṃkhyāgocaratvāt dharmā na śakyā vyapadeṣṭum ya teṣu śāntoditāvyapadeśyeṣu abhivyaktānabhibyakteṣu dharmesu anupātī sāmānyaviśeṣātmā sattvādiśabdādirūpeṇa so nvayī dharmī yasya tu Vadinaḥ dharmamātram evedaṃ niranvayaṃ bāhyamādhyātmikaṃ ca yasya ca jñānamātram eva tasya dharmāṇāṃ kṣaṇapraṇāśitvād atītānāgatavartamānaparhārohiṇāṃ samānakālānāṃ ca bhoktṛbhogyatvādisaṃbandhānupapatteḥ bhogābhāvaḥ sambandhābhāvaṃ darśayati kasmāt anyena vijjānena kṛtasya karmaṇo anyat vijñānam akartṛ bhaviṣyat kathaṃ bhoktṛtvenādhikriyeta kartuś ca phalābhipravṛtteḥ phalena saṃbandho yujyate anyaḥ kartā phalena cānyaḥ sambadhyata iti virudhyate smṛtyabhāvaś ca kṛtakaraṇīyādiviṣayasmṛtyabhāvaś ca anyadṛṣṭasya smaraṇam anyasya nāstīti na hi caitradṛṣṭasya vasumitraḥ smarati vastu pratyabhijñānāc ca yasmāt tad evedam iti vastu pratyabhijānīmaḥ tasmāt sthito nvayī dharmī dharmānyathātvaṃ dharmair anyathātvaṃ abhyupagataḥ pratipannaḥ na tu svarūpeṇānyathātvam yathā rucakādibhedānugatam api kanakam eva iti pratyabhijānīmaḥ tasmāt nedaṃ dharmamātraṃ niranvayam iti idānīṃ pariṇāmabhede hetur ucyate siddhe hi bhede pariṇāmatrayasaṃyamaḥ prayoktur upakalpeta yataḥ kayācil liṅgadvārā atītādiṣu matir upajanayituṃ śakyate nānyathā iti kramānyatvaṃ pariṇāmānyatve hetuḥ ekasya dharmiṇaḥ cittādeḥ eka eva pariṇāma iti prasakteḥ dharmādīnāṃ dharmtabhedād iti pariṇāmabhedasiddhaye hetur eṣa ucyate kramānyatvam kramaḥ anatarabhāvaḥ tasyānyatvaṃ bhedaḥ trayo hi kramā anyonyavidharmāṇa upalakṣyante lakṣaṇāvasthākramābhyām anyo dharmakramaḥ dharmāvasthākramābhyām anyo lakṣaṇakramaḥ dharmalakṣaṇakramābhyām anyo vasthākramaḥ yac ca teṣām anyatvaṃ prasiddhamārgam adhirūḍhaṃ tat kramakāryāṇāṃ pariṇāmānām anumāpakaṃ anyatve hetuḥ tadyathā mṛt dharmī cūrṇamṛt iti cūrṇādibhir dharmair ayugapatkālajanmabhiḥ kramavartibhiḥ paiṇamate sarvatra mṛdgrahaṇeṇadharmiṇo mṛdākhyasya parasparalakṣyamāṇabhedacūrṇapiṇḍaghaṭakapālakaṇādidharmānugamaṃ pratipādayati cūrṇasyānantaraḥ piṇḍaḥ piṇḍasyānantaro ghaṭaḥ ghaṭasyānantarāṇi kapālāni kapālānāṃ kaṇā anantarā iti dharma eva cūrṇamṛt piṇḍamṛt ghaṭamṛt kapālabṛt kaṇamṛt iti kramaḥ dharmāntarasya kramaḥ na lakṣaṇaṃ nāpy avasthā yathā yo yasya dharmasya samanantaro dharmaḥ sa tasya kramaḥ katham piṇḍo ghaṭa upajāyata iti piṇḍarūpā mṛt ghaṭībhavatīty arthaḥ abhedopāaerṇa piṇḍo ghaṭa upajāyata ity ucyate na punaḥ piṇḍo dharmo dharmāntarātmatāṃ pratipadyate piṇḍadharmavimardanena tadvirodhī tadanantaraṃ ghaṭākhyo dharma upajāyate dharmapariṇāmaś ca dvividhaḥ tulyapariṇāmaś cātulyapariṇāmaś ca yathā piṇḍo ghaṭa upajāyata ity atulyapiṇḍasya ghaṭādhidharmair mṛdākhyo dharmī pariṇamate saḥ atulyadharmapariṇāmaḥ yāvac ca ghaṭasya janmanaḥ prabhṛti ā kapālāpatteḥ tāvat ghaṭarūpeṇa eva pariṇamate mṛd iti sa tulyadharmapariṇāmaḥ idānīṃ lakṣaṇapariṇāmakrama ucyate lakṣaṇapariṇāmakramaḥ ghaṭasyānāgatāt lakṣaṇāt vartamānabhāvaḥ tathā piṇḍasya virodhidharmodaye vartamānād atīta bhāva ḥ kramaḥ nātītasyāsti kramaḥ dharme hi vartamānalakṣaṇasya samanantaraṃ yal lakṣaṇaṃ sa lakṣaṇakramaḥ na cātītalakṣaṇasya samanantaraṃ lakṣaṇam asti kasmāt pūrvāparatāyāṃ hi satyāṃ samanantaratvam sā cātītasya nāsti tasmāt dvayor evānāgatavartamānayoḥ lakṣaṇayoḥ kramaḥ atītasya kramābhāvapratipādane prayojanam kṣaṇatatkramayoḥ saṃyamāt ity atra bhaviṣyati tathā avasthāpariṇāmakramaḥ ghaṭasyābhinavasya prānte avasānāvasthāyāṃ purāṇātā dṛśyate sā ca kṣaṇaparamparā nupātinā krameṇābhyūhyamānā pratikṣaṇam abhinavabhāvaparimardanena purāṇatā sañjaniṣyate sā ca prānteṣu parāṃ vyaktim āpāditā madhye tu sūkṣmatayā na vibhāvyate tena madhyāvasthāyāṃ sann api kramo na lakṣyate prāntakālābhivyaktiliṅgenānumāyiṣyate yena iyaṃ purāṇatā parāṃ vyaktim upaprāpitā so yaṃ krama iti na hi ghaṭe pariniṣpannmātre pratikṣanājanmā api purāṇatā gṛhyate tathā ca vadiṣyati kṣaṇapratiyāgī pariṇāmāparāntanirgrāhyaḥ kramaḥ iti tasmāt dharmalakṣaṇakramābhyām avasthākramasyānyatvāt dharmalakṣaṇapariṇāmābhyāṃ viśiṣṭo yaṃ tṛtīyaḥ pariṇāmaḥ ta ete kramā dharmadharmibhede sati pratilabdhasvarūpāḥ vivakṣite tu dharmadharmiṇor abhede tatra kramabhedo na labhyate dharmo api dharmī bhavaty anyadharmāpekṣayā guṇabhyo nyatra dharmadharmitvaṃ nāma na vyavasthitam mahadādīnām apy aviśeṣāpekṣayā dharmitvam aviśeṣāṇāṃ ca viśeṣāpekṣayā viśeṣāṇāṃ ca śāntoditāpekṣayeti yadā tu saṃskārasākṣātkaraṇāt daśasu mahāsargeṣu janmapariṇāmaṃ anupaśyato vivekajaṃ vairāgyanimittaṃ jñānaṃ prādur abhūt atha bhagavān āvaṭayaḥ tantradharaḥ tam uvāca daśasu mahāsargeṣu bhavyatvāt anabhibhūtabuddhisattvena tvayā narakatiryaggamanaduḥkham anupaśyatā devam anuṣyeṣu punaḥ punaḥ utpadyamānena sukhaduḥkhayoḥ kim upalabdham adhikam iti bhagavantam āvaṭyaṃ jaigīṣavya uvāca daśasu mahāsargeṣu bhavyatvāt anabhibhūtabuddhisattvena mayā narakatiryaggamanam anupaśyatā devam anuṣyeṣu punaḥ punaḥ utpadyamānena yat kiñcit anubhūtaṃ tat sarvaṃ duḥkham iti duḥkham eva pratyavaimi bhagavān avaṭya uvāca yad idam āyuṣmataḥ pradhānavaśitvam anuttamaṃ ca sanyoṣasukhaṃ kim idam api duḥkhapakṣe nikṣiptam iti bhagavān jaigīṣavya uvāca viṣayasukhāpekṣayaivedam anuttamaṃ santoṣasukhaṃ prdhānavaśitvasukhaṃ ca uktam kaivalyasukhāpekṣayā duḥkham eva buddhisattvasyāyaṃ dharmaḥ triguṇaḥ triguṇaś ca pratyayo heyapakṣe nyasta iti kim apekṣayā punar etat dvayaṃ sukhaṃ bhavatīty āha duḥkharūpas tṛṣṇātantuḥ tṛṣṇāsantānaduḥkhopaśamarūpaṃ tu prasannam anābādhaṃ sarvānukūlaṃ sukham idam uktaṃ sanyoṣasukhaṃ pradhānajayasukhaṃ ca pratyayasya paracittajñānam parapratyaye saṃyamāt parapratyayasya sākṣātkaraṇam tatsākṣātkaraṇe tatsaṃbandhinaḥ paracittasya jñānaṃ bhavati tatra parapratyayasākṣātkaraṇāt tadduḥkhe duḥkhitvaṃ tatsukhe skhitvaṃ ca prāpnotīty āśaṅkyāha na ca sālambanaṃ tasya aviṣayībhūtatvāt raktaṃ pratyayaṃ jānāti yogī parasyāmuṣmmin ālambane raktaḥ pratyaya iti na jānāti parapratyayasya yadālambanaṃ sukharūpaṃ duḥkharūpaṃ vā yena sukhī duḥkhī vā bhavet nanu ca ālambanam asañjānānaḥ katham amusmin rakta iti sañjānīta iti ucyate raktam amuṣminn iti sāmānyaṃ vijānāti na punaḥ sukhaviśeṣaṃ sukhinaḥ pratyayasyālambanībhūtam ālambate parapratyayamātraṃ tu yogicittasyālambanībhūtam kāyarūpasaṃyamāt tadgrāhyaśaktis tambhe cakṣuḥprakāśāsamprayoge antardhānam yogina ātmīyasya kāyasya rūpaṃ kāyarūpam tasmin rūpe saṃyamāt tasya rūpasya yā paracakṣurgrāhyā śaktiḥ tāṃ pratibadhnāti niruṇāddhi tataḥ pareṣāṃ cakuṣuḥprakāśo yogikāyarūpeṇa na samprayujyate tataś ca āntardhānam etena śabdādyantardhānam uktam yogiśabdasya yā grāhyaśaktiḥ tasyāṃ saṃyame sati yā śabdasya grāhyaśaktiḥ sā pratiṣṭamyate tena yogiśandaṃ na paraḥ śṛṇoti tathā sparśādiṣv api draṣṭavyam so pagamaṃ nirupakramaṃ ca karma tatsaṃyamād aparāntajñānam ariṣṭebhyo vā āyurvipākaṃ karma dvividhā katham tv aritaṃ nimittam ādāya phalapadaṃ sopakramam ucyate yat tu mandaprasaraṃ cireṇa phalaṃ dāsyati tat nirupakramam yathā ārdraṃ vastraṃ vitānitaṃ vistāritaṃ kṣepīyasā kṣipratareṇa kālena śuṣyet tathā sopakramaṃ karma kṣipramāyurvipākaṃ kṛtvā kṣīyate tad eva vastraṃ sampiṇḍitaṃ avitānitam vireṇa śuṣyed evaṃ nirupakramaṃ cireṇa āyuḥ karoti yathā vā agniḥ śuṣke kakṣe yuktavāte anukūlamātariśvani samantato niyuktaḥ kṣepīyasā kālena dahet tathā sopakramaṃ karma kṣepīyasā kālena āyurdhakṣyati sa evāgniḥ tṛṇarāśau krameṇa nyastaścireṇa ddaheta tathā nirupakramaṃ karma tad etat dvividham ekabhavikam āyuṣkaraṃ karma tatsaṃyamād aparāntajñānam aparāntasya prāyaṇasya ātmīyasya jñānam tathā parakīyadvividhakarmasaṃyamāt paraprāyāṇajñānam api bhavati prāyaṇajñāne ca prayojanaṃ puruṣakartavyatāṃ pratisamīhanam ariṣṭebhyo vā prāyaṇajñānam trividham ariṣṭam ādhyātmikam ādhibhautikam ādhidaivikaṃ ca tatra ādhyātmikasyodāharaṇam ghoṣaṃ svadehepihitakarṇo na śṛṇoti jyotir vā netre vaṣṭbdhe na paśyati tathā ādhibhautikaṃ yamapuruṣān paśyati pitṛnatītān āgatān aksamād vetti ādhidaivikam akasmād eva siddhādīn paśyati viparītaṃ vā sarvaṃ paśyati karoti ca tatrāriṣṭam iti laukikī vācoyuktiḥ evaṇ hy āha viparītadarśanaṃmamāsīd ariṣṭam iti maitryādiṣu balāni maitrī karuṇā muditeti tisro bhāvanāḥ tatra bhūteṣu sukhiteṣu maitīṃ bhāvayitvā maitrī balaṃ labhate duḥkhiteṣu karuṇāṃ bhāvayitvā karuṇābalaṃ labhate puṇyaśīlesu muditāṃ bhāvayitvā muditā balaṃ labhate bhāvanātaḥ maitryādibhāvanātaḥ samādhir yaḥ saṃjāyate sa saṃyamaḥ maitryādibhāvanāsrthair yannimittaḥ tataḥ saṃyamāt maitryādigatāt yogino balānyavandhyavīryāṇi jāyante pāpaśīleṣu tu asya upekṣā na tu bhāvanā tataś ca bhāvanāyā abhāvāt tasyām upekṣāyāṃ nāsti samādhir ity ato na balam upekṣātaḥ tatra saṃyamābhāvād iti balesu hastibalādīni etair maitryādinimittair balair balavān yogī hastyādīna baleṣu saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā hastyādibalo bhavati pravṛttyālokanyāsāt sūkṣmavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭajñānam yā asau jyotiṣmatī pravṛttir uktā tasyāṃ prakāśaḥ ālokaḥ taṃ prakāśaṃ yogī sūkṣme vā vyavahite vā viprakṛṣṭe vā arthe vinyasya sthāpayitvā tam adhigaddhati bhuvanajñānaṃ sūrye saṃyamāt sūrye saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā samastaṃ bhuvanaprastāraṃ pratyakṣīkurvīta bhāṣyaṃ tu gatārthaṃ sarvapurāṇaprasiddhatvāt candre tārāvyūhajñānam sūrye saṃyamanād bhuvanaprastāraṃ viditvā tadanantaraṃ candre saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā tārāṇāṃ vyūhaṃ vijānīyāt sūryasaṃyamād bhuvanaprastāramātraṃ prajñātam evaṃ prastīrṇāḥ lokā nadyaḥ samudrā girayaś ceti na tu tārā itthaṃ vyūhitā anena sambaddhā iti candrasaṃyamāt tu tārāvyūhaprakārāvagatir iti dhruve tad gatijñānam tataś ca samanantaraṃ dhruve saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā tārāṇāṃ gatiṃ vijānīyāt anena prakāreṇa sañcakaramāṇā anena viśiṣṭā ity asmin kāle anena graheṇāyaṃ graho virudhyate ittahastamayaḥ ittham udayaḥ tad dvāreṇa prāṇabhṛtāṃ śubham aśubhaṃ cetyādi vijānīyāt evam anyeṣu cordhvaṃ vimāneṣu saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā tāni vimānānītthaṃ prakārāṇyevaṃ gatānīty evam ādi sarvaṃ vijānīyāt nābhicakre kāyavyūhajñānam nābhicakre saṃyamaṃ kṛtvā kāyavyūhaṃ vijānīyāt vātapitaśloṣmāṇas trayo doṣāḥ etāvatpramāṇā etat pratiṣṭhā ityādi jñeyam tathā dhātavaḥ sapta bāhyābhyantarabhāvenāvasthitāḥ rasaḥ tvak bāhyā sarveṣām tato hyantaraṃ lohitaṃ tato māṃsaṃ tato sthi tato medaḥ tato majjā tataḥ śuklaṃ sarvābhyantaram ity evaṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvam eṣāṃ bāhyam ity eṣa vinyāsaḥ tathā nāḍīnāṃ ca vyūhaṃ vijānīyāt kaṇṭhakrūpe kṣutpipāsānivṛttiḥ jihvāyā adhastāt tantuḥ unnāmikāyāṃ jihvāyāṃ dṛśyate tantor adhattāt kanṭhaḥ tato dhastāt kūpaḥ tatra saṃyamāt kṣutpipāse na pratibādhete karmanḍyāṃ sthairyam kūpasyādhastād urasi kurmānāma nāḍī tasyāṃ kṛtasaṃyamaḥ sthirapadaṃ labhate cittasthairyaṃ labhate yathā sarpo godhā vā dhāraṇād urasā atyantaṃ sthirībhavati mūrdhajyotiṣi siddhadarśanam śiraḥ kapāle nyaś cchidraṃ prabhāsvaratvāt jyotiḥ ity ucyate tatra saṃyamāt siddhānāṃ dyāvāpṛthivyor antarālacāriṇāṃ darśanaṃ bhavati prātibhād vā sarvam ātmani saṃyamaṃ kurvataḥ īśvaraṃ vā atyarthaṃ praṇīdadhānasya yoginaḥ prātibhaṃ tārakaṃ svayam utthitaṃ mānasaṃ jñānam tat vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇasya vivekajasya jñānasya pūrvarūpam yathā udaye prabhā auṣasī kiṃcid unmīlantī lohitāyamānā bhāsakarasya ujjigamiṣataḥ pūrvarūpam tasmād vā sarvaṃ vijānanti yoginaḥ prātibhasya jñānasyotpādād iti bh hṛdaye cittasaṃvit yad idam asmin brahmapure śarīre daharam bh alpaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ puṇḍarīkākāro māṃsapiṇḍo dhomukhaḥ veśmavadane kanāḍīsuṣirayogād veśma tatra vijñānaṃ cittaṃ tasmin urassarovilagnāle prāṇaveśmani puṇḍarūke saṃyamāc citte sattve saṃvit bhavati sattvapuruṣayor atyantāsaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyayāviśeṣo bhogaḥ parārthāt svārthasaṃyamāt puruṣajñānam sattvaṃ cittaṃ puruṣo bhoktā tayoḥ atyantāsaṅkīrnayoḥ atyantavilakṣaṇayor atīva pṛthagbhūtayoḥ vṛttisārūpyaṃ pratyayāviśeṣaḥ sa bhogaḥ puruṣasya parārthāt sattvāt puruṣapratyayena saṅkīrṇābhāsāt vivicya svārthe citimātrasvarūpe saṃyamāt puruṣajñānaṃ bhavait kīdṛśaṃ tat parārthaṃ cittasattvam yato vivicya svārthe puruṣe saṃyamaḥ kriyata iti buddhisattvam prakhyāśīlaṃ samānaṃ sattvaṃ vastukāryaṃ puruṣāṛthakartavyatayā samavashānam upanibandhanaṃ yoyos te samānasattvopanibandhane rajastamasī vaśīkṛtya nyag bhāvam āpādya sattvapuruṣānyatāpratyayena yoginaḥ pariṇatam tasmāc ca sattvāt pariṇāminaḥ triguṇād anityād aśuddhāt parārthād acetanāt atyantavidharmā viśuddho nyaḥ apariṇāmī svārtho nityaḥ cinmātrarūpaḥ puruṣaḥ tayor atyantāsaṅkīrṇayoḥ pratyayāviśeṣo bhogaḥ puruṣasya darśitaviṣayatvāt sa bhogapratyayaḥ nāppariṇāmitve sati darśitaviṣayatvād anyo bhogaḥ sambhavati sattvasya parāthatvāt abiśiṣṭo bhogapratyayo dṛśyaḥ puruṣeṇ na yas tu tasmāt gauṇapratyayāt pratyayinaś ca viśiṣṭaś citamātrarūpo nyaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ pratyayaḥ svārthaḥ puruṣa eva pariṇāmāṇupapatteḥ pratyayaḥ tatra sayamāt puruṣaviṣayā prajñā jāyate nanu ca yadi puruṣaḥ pratyayasya viṣayīkriyate tena cet puruṣo gṛhyate parārthaḥ puruṣaḥ prāpnoti na eṣa doṣaḥ na ca puruṣapratyayena puruṣaviṣayeṇa pratyayena buddhisattvātmanā buddhisattvadharmeṇa puruṣo dṛśyate buddher acetanatvāt puruṣa eva taṃ pratyayaṃ svālambanaṃ puruṣābhāsaṃ paśyati puruṣābhāsatvem eva pratyayasya puruṣālambanatvam na pratyayasya puruṣālambanatvam yathā mukhasannidhau darpiṇo mukhākāreṇa pariṇamate tathā cittaṃ puruṣākāreṇa pariṇataṃ puruṣābhāsaṃ puruṣeṇa gṛhyate tathā coktam vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti na kasyacit puruṣaḥ karmatāṃ pratipadyata ity arthaḥ nanu cakṣurādarśatalapratihataṃ pratinivṛtya yathā mukhasya grāhakaṃ padaṃ puruṣoapi cittasattvapratihataḥ pratinivṛtya svātmānaṃ gṛhṇīyāt na pariṇāmānupapatteḥ puruṣasya na hy apariṇāminaś cittaṃ prati pravṛttiḥ pratinivṛttir vā sādhimānam upāśnuvīta na cāpi cakṣuḥ pratinivṛtya mukhaṃ grāhayati mukhasya darpaṇamaṇḍalādhikaraṇatvenānubhūyamānatvāt na hi svamukhaṃ darpaṇādhikaraṇastham kiṃ ca ādarśānuvidhānāc ca yathā khaḍge dīrghaṃ mukhaṃ dṛśyate na svamukhaṃ dīrgham pratihatena ced upalabhyate cakṣuṣā nijāmukhaṃ tatra ādarśānuvidhānam ayuktam tataḥ prātibhaśrāvāṇavedanādarśāsvādavārtā jāyante tataḥ svārthe samādhānāt pratibhāt ātmasaṃyamajanitāt mānasāt jñānāt sūkṣmavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭātītānāgatajñānam sampadyate śrāvaṇāt divytaśabdānāṃ śravaṇam vedanāt sparśajñānnāt siddhādīnāṃ sparśaṃ jānāti ādarśāt cākṣuṣāt jñānāt divyaṃ rūpam avagacchati āsvādāt rasanendriyajñānāt divyarasasaṃvedanaṃ bhavati vṛttau bhavaṃ vārtaṃ lokasaṃvyavahārajñānaṃ tasmād eṣa saṃvyavahāratattvarūpaṃ yathāvad adhigacchati te samādhāv upasargā vyutthāne siddhayaḥ te prātibhādayaḥ puruṣe samāhitacittasya u sya samu utpadyamānā upasargāḥ puruṣadarśanapratyanīkatvāt vyutthitacittasyotpadyamānāḥ siddhayaḥ yady api puruṣe saṃyamād utpadyante tathāpi na viraktasya samāhitascittasya jāyate bandhakāraṇaśaithilyāt pracārasaṃvedanāc ca cittasya paraśarīrāveśaḥ lolībhūtasya ghaṇṭābhighātulyasya dedīpyamānāṅgārarāśidyuticañcalasyamanas O pratiṣṭhasya śarīre karmāśayād bandhaḥ pratiṣṭhety arthaḥ śarīramātrasaṃkocāvasthānam tasya bandhasya karma kāraṇam kāraṇaśaithilyaṃ karmāśayaśithilatvaṃ samādhibalād bhavati pracārasaṃvedanaṃ ca cittasya samādhijanmeiva karmabandhakṣayāt svacittapracārasaṃvedanāc ca asminnimitte hṛṣyati muhyati lubhyati cānena kāraṇena ity evamādisvacittasañcaraṇasattavavedanāc ca yogī cittaṃ svaśarīrān niṣkṛṣya śarīrāntareṣu nikṣipati cittam asya utpatat indriyāṇi anūtpatanti tasmād indriyavṛttilābhāt paraśarīreṣu prāṇādivṛttaya utpadyante yathā madhukararājaṃ makṣikā utpatantam anūtpatanti niviśamānam anu niviśante tathendriyāṇī paraśarīrāveśe cittam anu vidhīyante udānajayāt jalapaṅkakaṇṭakādiṣv asaṅga utkrāntiś ca samastendriyavṛttiḥ jīvanaṃ sarveṣām ekādaśānām indriyāṇām ekena saṃmūrcchtena vyāpareṇa yena śarīraṃ dhriyate tajjīvanam tasya jīvanasya puruṣārthakartavyatāniyamāt pañcatayī kriyā prāṇāpānavyānodānasamānabhedena prastīryate tatra prāṇo mukhanāsikāgatir āhṛdayavṛttiḥ samaṃ nayanāt samānaḥ ānābhivṛttiḥ ānārbhadeśaṃ vartate mūtrapurīṣādīnām apanayanādpānaḥ sa ca nābhiprabhṛti āpādat alaṃ vartate ūrdhvaṃ śarīrasya nayanād udānaḥ sa ca pādatalād ārabhya āmastakavṛttiḥ samastaśarīravyāpī vyāna iti eteṣāṃ pradhānaḥ pradhānaḥ prāṇaḥ tajjayāc ca sarveṣām apānādīnāṃ tu jayo bhavati teṣāṃ tu jayopāyo vistareṇa hairaṇyagarbhe vyākhyātaḥ iha tu manojayānujitatvāt teṣāṃ jayopāyo na pṛthag abhihitaḥ prāṇāyamajayāt tu jīyanta eva na pṛthag eṣāṃ jayopāyapratipādanam ādṛtyam iti phalamātram udānajiter ucyate udānajayāt jalapaṅkakaṇṭakādiṣu ādinā kṛpāṇadhārādiṣv asaṅgaḥ kiṃ cotkrāntiś ca prāyaṇakāle bhavati tāṃ prāyaṇakāle bhavantīm utkrāntim udānajayāt vaśīkṛtya svatantratayā pratipadyate samānajayāt jvalanam jitasamānaḥ tejasa upadhyamānaṃ kṛtvā samānavāybāśrayatvāt udānatejasoḥ tadupadhmānakarmakārakas tāvad yogī jāṭharaṃ jvalayati śrotrākāśayoḥ saṃbandhasaṃyamād divyaṃ śrotram kaḥ punar asau saṃbandho yatra saṃyama ityāha sarvaśrotrāṇām ākācaṃ pratiṣṭhā śabdānāṃ ca ākāśakuṇatvād ākāśam eva pratiṣṭhā grāhyaṃ śabdaṃ prati śratrasya vyavadhānābhāvaḥ śrotrākāśayoḥ sambandhaḥ tathā ca uktam tulyadeśaśravaṇānām śrūyate neneti śravaṇam tulyadeśāni śravaṇāni yeṣāṃ te tulyadeśāśravaṇāḥ teṣām ekaśrutitvaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhavati tad ekasminn avakāśadāyini nirāvaraṇātmake vastuni sati yujyate taccaitad ākāśasya sattve liṅgam tathā anāvaraṇātmakaṃ ca uktam kutaḥ tathā mūrtasyānyatrākāśāt ākāśavilakṣaṇāsya ghaṭādeḥ āvaraṇadarśanāt ato yasya maṇivajrādimadhyeṣv apy āvaraṇaṃ nāsti tadākāśam ata eva vibhutvam api prakhyātam ākāśasya śrotrasya liṅgam āha śabdagrahaṇānumitaṃ tu śrotram yasmāt badhirābadhirayor ekaḥ śabdaṃ gṛhṇāti aparo na gṛhṇāti yannimittam abadhirasya śabdagrahaṇam itarasya cāgrahaṇaṃ tacchrotram tasmācchrotram eva śabdaviṣayam badhireṇāśravaṇāt śrotrākāśayoḥ saṃbandhe kṛtasaṃyamasya toginaḥ civyaṃ śrotraṃ pravartate kāyākāśayoḥ sambandhasaṃyamasya laghutūlasamāpatteś ca ākāśagamanam yatra kāyāaḥ tatra ākāśam tasyāvakāśadānāt kāyasya avinābhāvalakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ tenākāśena tatra kāyākāśayoḥ itaretarāvinābhāvaprāpti lakṣaṇasambandhe kṛtasaṃyamo yogī jitvā tatsambandhaṃ tato laghuṣu tūlādiṣu ā paramāṇubhyaḥ samāpatteḥ jitasambandhaḥ tūlādivat lāghavaṃ pratipadyate jitakāyākāśasambandhaḥ samāpannaḥ tūlāditulyalāghavaśīanārthaṃ jale pādābhyāṃ viharati tataḥ ūrdhvam ūrṇānābhitantumatre viharati tatra sañjātakokilatantusamānalāghavaḥ punaḥ raśmiṣu viharati tato mātariśvani tato yathā iṣṭam ākāśe gatir asya bhavati bahir akalpitā vṛttir mahā videhā tataḥ prakāśāvaraṇakṣayaḥ śarīrāt bahiḥ deśāntare viṣayaviśeṣe svayam eva samāhibalāt upajāyate yā manaso vṛttiḥ sā mahā videhā nāma dhāraṇā sā yadi śarīrapratiṣṭhasya eva manasp vṛttimātreṇa bahiḥ viṣaye bhavati tadānīṃ kalpitā ucyate śarīrasthamnassaṅkalpapūrvakatvāt yā tu samādhibalanimittāt śarīre bandhakāraṇaśaithilyāt śarīranirapekṣā bahir bhūtasya eva manaso bahir vṛttiḥ sā khalu akalpitā ity ucyate yathā eva kalpitāyāṃ śarīrāvadhika eva bahirvṛttilābhaḥ evaṃ nākālpetāyāṃ śarīrādhiṣṭhānāvadhisamīkṣā sā cobhayy api videhā eva bahir upakalpitatvāt tatra yā iyam akalpitā mahāvideheti samākhyāyate tatra kalpitayā sādhayanty akalpitāṃ mahāvidehām kalpanāsaṃśīlanasāvyatvād akalpitāyāḥ kalpitayā ca saṃsādhayanti yayā mahāvidehayā paraśarīrāṇy āviśanti yoginaḥ tataś ca dhāraṇātaḥ mahāvidehātaḥ prakāśātmano buddhisattvasya yadāvaraṇaṃ kleśakarmavipakatrayaṃ rajastamomūlaṃ tasya ca kṣayo bhavati sthūlasvarūpasūkṣmānvayārthavattvasaṃyamāt bhūtajayaḥ sthūlaṃ ca svarūpam ca sūkṣmaṃ cānvayaś cārthavattvaṃ cety evam ekaikaṃ bhūtaṃ pañcātmakam tatra pārtivāḥ śabda ādayaḥ śabdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ viśeṣāḥ pañcalakṣaṇatanmātrārabdhatvāt pṛthivyāḥ saha ākārādibhiḥ pṛthivyās tāvad ākārādayaḥ ākāro gauravaṃ raukṣyaṃ ceraṇaṃ sthairyam eva ca sthitir bhedaḥ kṣamā kāṣṇryaṃ kāṭhinyaṃ sarvabhogyatā iti tathā snehaprabhāsaukṣmyamārdavagauravarakṣāpavitratvasandhānādaya audakā guṇāḥ tathā taijasāḥ ūrdhvabhāktvapāvanatā dagdhṛtvapācakatvalāghavabhāsvaratvādayaḥ tathā vāyavīyāḥ tiryag yānapavitratvākṣepabalanodanatva ādayaḥ tathā nābhasāḥ sarvagatyavyūhaviṣṭambhāḥ tad etaiḥ ākārādibhiḥ saha śabdādayo viśeṣāḥ sthūlaśabdena saṃvyavahārārthṃ śāstre paribhāṣitāḥ evamāpyāścatvāro rasādayo viśeṣāḥ saukṣmyādibhiḥ saha evaṃ taijasā rūpādayas trayo ūrdhvabhāktvādibhiḥ saha sthūlā ucyante tathā vāyavīyāḥ śabdasparśatiryakpātāayaḥ sthūlā viśeṣāḥ evam ākāśasya sarvagatatvādayaḥ sthūlā viśeṣāḥ tat etat bhūtānāṃ prathamaṃ sthūlaṃ rūpaṃ uktam dbitīyam adhunā svarūpam ucyate tac ca sāmānyaṃ prthiveṣu bhinneṣv abhinnam anugataṃ mūrtir eva bhūmīti tathā rasādiṣv āpyeṣv anugataṃ sāmānyaṃ sneha eva jalam iti tathaivāgnayeṣu rūpādiṣv anugataṃ sāmānyaṃ bahnir uṣṇatvam eva tathā sparśatiryakpātādiṣv anugataṃ sāmānyaṃ praṇāmitvam eva vāyuḥ tathā śabdādi ṛṛv anugatam sāmānyaṃ sarvatogatir eva ākāśaḥ ity etat svarūpaśabdena uktaṃ dvitīyaṃ rūpam tasya sāmānyasya rūpasya śabdādayo viśeṣāḥ tathā ca uktam ekajātisamanvitānāṃ sattvādiguṇasamanugatānām eṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ pṛthivyādīn sāmānyānāṃ śabdādidharmamātraṃ vyāvartate sāmānyaviśeṣasamudāyo dravyam kasmāt dviṣṭho hi samūhaḥ dvābhyāṃ prakārābhyāṃ sthito dviṣṭhaḥ pratyastamitabhedāvayavaḥ vyāvṛttapratyayaśūnya ity arthaḥ yathā śarīraṃ vṛkṣo yūṭhaṃ vanam iti upāttabhedāvayavānugataḥ āgṛhītabhedāvayavānugataḥ samūhaḥ uhayaśabdenopādīyate ubhaye devam anuṣyā iti tadyathā samūhasya devā eko bhāgaḥ manuṣyā eko bhāgaḥ tābhyām eva bhāgābhyām āgṛhīta yathāsvabhedānugatābhyām abhidhīyate samūhaḥ ubhaye iti tayoḥ bhedābhedo vivakṣitaḥ āmnāṇāṃ vanam iti āmnāṇām iti bhedena vivakṣā vanam ity abhedena tābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ bhedābhedābhyām āmnāṇāṃ vanam iti ṣaṣṭhī prathamā taddvayor vivakṣita ekaḥ samūha iti sa punar dvividhaḥ samūhaḥ yutasiddhāvayavo yutasiddhāvayavaś ca yutasiddhāvayavaḥ pṛthaksiddhāvayavaḥ samūho vanaṃ saṅgha iti ayutasiddhāvayavaḥ apṛhaksiddhāvayavaḥ saṅghātaḥ śarīraṃ vṛkṣaḥ paramāṇur iti paramāṇūnām api sāvayavatvaṃ sattvādikāryatvāt mūrtatvāc ca ghaṭādivad eva ayutasiddhāvayavabhedānugataḥ samūho dravyam iti patañjaliḥ etatsvarūpam ity uktaṃ sāmānyaviśeṣātmakam atha kim eṣāṃ sūkṣmaṃ rūpam iti tanmātraṃ bhūtakāraṇam anekaparamāṇūpārabdhatvāt tasya tanmātrasya eko vayavaḥ paramāṇuḥ so api sāmānyaviśeṣātmā ayutasiddhāvayavabhedānugataḥ samudāya iti evaṃ sarvayanmātrāṇi tataś ca tanmātrāṇiviśeṣavinirmuktāni tadavayavāś ca paramāṇava iti etat bhūtānāṃ tṛtīyaṃ sūkṣmākhyaṃ rūpam saṃyamasya viṣaya iti tanmātrārabdhatvāc ca sāvayavam ākāśam anityaṃ ca na ca śabdavyatirekeṇa ākāśaṃ nāma dravyam upaladhuṃ śakyam dharmadharmiṇor abhedāt nanu ca keśādīnāṃ kṛṣṇmā apy apaiti śuklimā samupajāyate tathā cāpāyopajanadharmāṇaḥ kṛṣṇimādayaḥ te guṇāḥ yat tu na kṛṣṇimānam anu vinaśyati śuklimānamanveti tat dravyam evam ākāśādīnām api guṇāvyatirekeṇa sadbhāvaḥ śabdapratyayādibhedāt iti na dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt te eva kṛṣṇāḥ śuklāś ca kleśāḥ kṛṣṇaśuklatvādidharmaiḥ pariṇamante sarvaṃ hi sarvātmakam ity uktam na khalu kvacid api kūṭasthe vyapanayanena dravyasvarūpam yad api darśanasparśanābhyāṃ yad upalabhyate tat deavyam iti tad apy ayutasiddharūpasparśasamudāyatvād ubhābhyāṃ daranasparśanābhyāṃ gṛhyata ity adoṣaḥ nanu ca na rūpaṃ sparśanena gṛhyate nāpi darśanena saprśaḥ yad ubhYbhyāṃ gṛhyate yat paśyāmi tad eva sparśāmīti tad dravyam yat tu cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate sparśanena eva ca gṛhyate sa guṇa iti na māṣatilayavādibhinnajātivimiśrarāśāv anaikantikatvāt gṛhyate ca darśanasparśanābhyāṃ rāśiḥ kiṃ ca darśanasparśane guṇasya eva grāhake bāhyendriyatvāt śrotravat na hi jātir api guṇavyatiriktā vidyate bhedenāgrāhaṇāt kiṃ ca ghaṭādāv api parasparādhyāsena darśanasparśanābhyāṃ rūpasparśayor eva grahaṇam yathedaṃ rūpaṃ durgandhi surabhirandhi ceti tasmād ākāśam api tanmātrārabdhaṃ śabdavyatirekeṇāśakyaṃ pratipattum iti sāvayavam anityaṃ ca atha bhūtānāṃ caturthaṃ rūpam khyātiriyāsthitiśīlā guṇāḥ kāryasvarūpānupātinaḥ kāryadharmānuyāyinaḥ anvayaśabdena uktāḥ anugamāt tad etadbhūtānāṃ caturthaṃ rūpaṃ saṃyamasya guṇānvayāhkyo viṣayaḥ atha eṣāṃ pañcamaṃ rūpam arthavattvam asya vyākyānaṃ bhogāpavarkārthatā sā ca guṇeṣv anvayinī tatra yā guṇeṣv anuvṛttā bhogāpavargāyatā tad idaṃ bhūtānāṃ pañcamaṃ rūpaṃ saṃyamasyārthavattvākhyo viṣayaḥ guṇās tan mātreṣu bhūteṣu bhūtavikāreṣu cānvayinaḥ evaṃ tanmātraṃ sūkṣmarūpaṃ bhūtabhūtavikāreṣv anugatam bhūtasvarūpam ca sthūleṣi bhūtavikāreṣv anugatam iti sarvam arthavat guṇānāṃ bhogāpavargārthatvāt teṣāṃ ca sarvānvayitvāt tadarthavattvena sarvaṃ bhūtavikārādikam arthavat teṣv idānīṃ bhūteṣu mañcasu pañcarūpeṣu sthūlāddippañcarūpeṣu yathākramaṃ saṃyamāt pūrvaṃ sthūlena saṃyamaṃ kṛtvāatajjayasālṣātkaraṇānantaraṃ svarūpasaṃyamaṃ kurvīta punaḥ sūkṣme punaś cānvaye punaś cārthavattve ity evaṃ yathākramam saṃyamāt tasya tasya sthūlādikasya darśanaṃ jayaśś ca yathāvat prādurbhavati tatra bhūtasvarūpāṇijitvā yogī bhūtajayī bhavati tajjayāt vatsānusāriṇya iva gāvaḥ yathā prakṛtibhūtā gāvaḥ asya saṃkalpānuvidhāyinyo bhūtaprakṛtayo bhavanti svaṃ saṃyamaphalam idānīm āha tato ṇiprādurbhāvaḥ kāyasampat tad dharmānabhighātaś ca tatrāṇimā ko bhavatīty āhāṇuḥ iti sūkṣmād api sūkṣmataro bahvatīddhātaḥ tenāṇimnā sarvam anupraviśati vajram api tathā sarvasyādṛśyo bhavati laghimā laghuḥ laghubhyaḥ tūlādibhyo api laghutaraḥ bhavati tena nirālambanaḥ sarvato gantuṃ paryāpnoti mahimā mahān bhavati ākāśam api vyāpnoti prāptiḥ ihastha evāṅgulyaguṇāpi spṛśati candramasam prākāmyaṃ pracurakāmo yatheṣṭakāmo bhavatīddhānābhighātaḥ bhūmāv unmajjati ca yathākāmatvāt yathā udake vaśitvam sarvalokavaśitvam asya vyākhyānaṃ bhūtabhautikavaśī bhavati avaśyaś cānyeṣām īśitvam teṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavavyūhāpy ayānām utpattisthitipralayānām īṣṭe yatrakāmāvasāyitvam yasmin kāmas tatreva tadavasānaṃ tadantaṃ gacchati satyasaṃkalpād hetoḥ yathā saṃkalpaḥ tathā bhūtaprakṛtīnām avasthānaṃ bhavati śakto api sa yogī na padārthaviparyāsaṃ karoti nāgniṃ śītīkaroti kasmāt anyasya yatrakāmāvasāyinaḥ pūrvasiddhasya parama īśvarasya tathā teṣu padārtheṣu viparyāsena saṃkalpāt na hi padārthaviparyāsaṃ cikīrṣamāṇasya pūrva shiddhaṃ prati vinā dveṣeṇa tadviparyāso bhavati tad aśuddhyabhāvād eva na padārthaviparyāsaṃ karoti kaliāṇatarācaraṇo hi sa iti etāny aṣṭāv aṇimādyaiśvaryāṇi bhūtajayād bhavanti kāyasampadvakṣyamāṇā tddharmānabhighātaḥ teṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ dharmaiḥ na yogino bhighāto bhavati pṛthivī svena dharmeṇa mūrtyā na viruṇaddhi yoginaḥ śarīrādikriyām katham śilām apy anupraviśati nāpaḥ snigdhā yoginaṃ kledayanti varṣasahasram apy udake tiṣṭhantam nāgnir uṣṇe dahati na vāyuḥ praṇāmī vahati anāvaraṇātmake api prakaṭarūpe api bhavaty āvṛtaḥ prakaṭo na bhavati siddhānām apy adṛśyo bhavati rūpalāvaṇyabalavajrasaṃhananatvāni kāyasampat rūpavān darśanīyaḥ lāvaṇyavān kāntimān atiśayabalo vajrasaṃhananaś ca bhavati grahaṇasvarūpāsmitānvayārthavattvasaṃyamād indriyajayaḥ sarvam etad gatasūtreṇa tuyavyākhyānam asmitāmātraṃ tu viśeṣo bhūtānām iva tan mātrāṇi sāmānyaviśeṣātmā śabdādir viṣayaḥ teṣv indriyāṇāṃ yā vṛttiḥ viṣayaviśeṣāvalokanātmikā tat grahaṇam na ca tatsāmānyamātre śabdādisāmānyābhāsanamātre manasi grahaṇākāraḥ upapadyate katham anālocitaḥ svaviṣayaviśeṣa indriyavasīyeta na kathaṃ cid anuvyavasīyeta taimirikātaimirikayor anuvyavasāyānanuvyavasāyāhyām tasmānnityā nendriyeṇānālocite viṣaye manasā anuvyavasāyaḥ tatrāsyāṃ viśeṣātmikāyāṃ vṛttau prathamaṃ saṃyamaḥ kartavyaḥ atha svarūpam punaḥ indriyāṇāṃ dvitīyaṃ rūpam prakāśātmanoḥ sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ viṣayaviśeṣālocanam indriyāṇāṃ viśeṣaḥ yathā pradīpasya ghaṭādiviśeṣākārāloko viśeṣaḥ prakāśamātraṃ sāmānyam ataḥ sāmānyaviśeṣātmakam ayutasiddhāvayavabhedānugataṃ dravyam indriyaṃ pradīpavat yathā sāmānyamūrtidharmaḥ sthūrādiṣv anupravartate tathendriyaṃ prakāśātmakaṃ dravyaviśeṣātmikāyāṃ grahaṇavṛttāv anupravartate tad etasmin dvitīye indriyāṇāṃ svarūpe saṃyamaḥ kriyeta teṣāṃ indriyāṇāṃ tṛtīyaṃ rūpam asmitā lakṣaṇo haṅkāraḥ tasya ahaṅkārasya sāmānyasyendriyāṇi ayutasiddhāvayavabhedānugatāni grahaṇarūpānvayīni viśeṣāḥ tatrāsmitāyāṃ saṃyamaḥ karaṇīyaḥ caturthaṃ rūpaṃ vyavasāyātmakāḥ prakāśakriyāsthitiśīlā guṇāḥ yeṣām incriyāṇi sāhaṅkārāṇi pariṇāmaḥ tatra guṇānugame saṃyamaḥ kartavyaḥ pañcamaṃ rūpaṃ guṇeṣu yad anugataṃ puruṣārthavattvam ataḥ sarveṣām arthavattvam anugamaś ca pūrvavat evaṃ eṣu pañcasv indriyarūpeṣu yathākramam kramānatikrameṇasaṃyamaḥ tatra pratyekaṃ pañcasu jayaṃ ṛtvā pañcasvarūpajayaṃ labhate tasmāt pañcasvarūpajayād indriy ādi jayo vakṣyamāṇaphalāya prādurbhavati yoginaḥ yat tu tataḥ paramāvaśyatendriyāṇām iti tadviṣayagrahaṇavṛtter vaśitvamātraṃ viṣayāpratipattirūpam tato manojavatvaṃ vikaraṇabhāvaḥ pradhānajayaś ca tata itndriyajayāt kāyasyānuttamaḥ na vidyate smād uttama ity anuttamaḥ gatilābho manojavatvam videhānāṃ śarīranirapekṣāṇāṃ indriyāṇāṃ abhipretadeśāpekṣo bhipretakālāpekṣo bhipretaśabdādiviṣayāpekṣaśa ca vṛttilābho vikaraṇabhāvaḥ sarvaprakṛtivikāravaśitvaṃ aṣṭānāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tadvikārāṇāṃ ca vaśitvaṃ pradhānajaya ity etās tisraḥ siddhayo madhupratīkāḥ iti ucyante tāś ca pañcasvarūpajayād adhigamyante sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātimātrasya sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvaṃ sarvajñātṛtvaṃ ca sarvaprakāreṇa sarvasādhanena nirdhūtarajastamomalasya sattvasya pare vaiśāradye svaddhe sthitipravāhe pare vartamānasya parasyāṃ vaśīkārasaṃjñāyāṃ jñānaprasādamātre niratiśaye vartamānasya sattvapuruṣānyathā khyātimātrarūpapratiṣṭhasya sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvam sarvasya vastujātasyeṣṭe sarvātmanā sakalaprakṛtivikārātmanā guṇādhyavasāyātmakāḥ buddhyādikāraṇabhāvapariṇatādhyavasāyātmakāḥ śāntoditāvayapadeśyadharmānuprasarmṇaḥ svāminaṃ k ṛṛstrajñaṃ dṛśimātraṃ aśeṣaguṇāḥ dṛśyatvena bhogyatvenāvasthitāḥ labhyante ity arthaḥ sarvajñātṛtvaṃ sarvātmakānāṃ śāntoditāvyapadeśyadharmatvena avasthitānāṃ guṇānāṃ akramopārūḍham ekakālabhāvi vivekajaṃ jñānam ity arthaḥ ity eṣā sarvavaśitvasarvajñātṛtvalakṣaṇā viśokā nāma siddhiḥ yāṃ prāpya yogī sarvajñaḥ kṣīṇakleśabandhano viharati vaśī tadvairāgyād api doṣabījakṣaye kaivalyam yadā asya evaṃ bhavati sarvajñasya sarvabhāvānadhitiṣṭhataḥ kleśakarmakṣaye vivekī sattvasya pratyayaḥ kīdṛśa puruṣaś ca sattvavidharmā apariṇāmī śuddho nyaḥ sattvāt ity anena prakāreṇa tataḥ api sarvajñasarvabhāvādhyakṣatvāt virajyamānasya yāni kleśabījāni avidyāvāsanārūpāṇi dagdhaśālibījakalpāni prasavāsamarthāni tān caritārthena pralīyamānena saha āśrayeṇa manasā pratyastaṃ gaddhanti teṣu pralīneṣu puruṣaḥ punar idaṃ tāpatrayaṃ ādhyātmikādilakṣaṇaṃ na bhuṅkte tad eṣāṃ guṇānāṃ manasi kleśakarmavipakasvarūpeṇābhivyaktānāṃ caritārthānāṃ pratiprasave pralaye puruṣasyātyantiko guṇaviyogaḥ kaivalyam tadā svarūpapratiṣṭhā citiśaktir eva puruṣaḥ tatra tadvartāgyād apītyapiśabdād aprāptayogaiśvaryasyāpi samyagdarśanāt kaivalyam iti sthānyupamantraṇe saṅgasmayākaraṇaṃ punar aniṣṭaprasaṅgāt sthānaṃ svargādikaṃ yeṣān te sthānino devā indrādayaḥ taiḥ upamantraṇaṃ bho bho ihoṣyatām ityādi tasmin satyātmano hīnatvaṃ smarataḥ prāpnutaḥ saṅgasmayau arthād iti tau ca na kartavyau saṅgasmayakaraṇe niṣṭaṃ prasajyeta catvāraḥ khalv amī yoginaḥ prāthamakalpiko madhubhūmikaḥ prajñājyotiḥ atikrāntabhāvanīyaś ca tān krameṇa vyācaṣṭe tatrābhyāsī abhyāsanaśīlaḥ pravṛttajyotiḥ jyotiṣmatyādīnām anyatamā pravṛttiḥ pravṛttā yasya sa pravṛttajyotiḥ prathamaḥ ṛtambharaprajño dvitīyaḥ bhūtendriyajayī tṛtīyaḥ sa tu sarveṣu bhāviteṣu bhāvanīyeṣu sākṣāt kṛteṣu jiteṣu ca kṛtarakṣābandhaḥ upāttasya hi rakṣā vidhānīyā bhāvanīyeṣu sākṣātkaraṇīyeṣu kartavyatāsādhanavāṃś ca kartavyatāyāḥ sādhanāni kartavyatāsādhanāni abhyāsavairāgyādīni yasya saḥ kartavyatāsādhanavān yas tv atikrāntabhāvanīyaś caturthaḥ tasya cittapratisarga eva cittapralaya eva eko rthaḥ pariśiṣṭaḥ saptavidhā tasya prāntabhūmim prajñā tatra madhumatīṃ bhūmiṃ dvitīyām ṛtaṃbharaprajñābhūmiṃ sākṣātkurvato brāhmāṇasya sthānino devāḥ sattvaviśuddhimanupaśyantaḥ sthānair upamantrayante bhoḥ ityādi prasiddhārthaṃ bhāṣyam kṣaṇatatkramayoḥ saṃyamād vivekajaṃ jñānaṃ kṣaṇaṃ kramaṃ ca svayam eva vistareṇācaṣṭe tatrāpakarṣaparyantaṃ yataḥ param apakarṣo na śakyate kartuṃ tad dravyaṃ paramāṇuḥ evaṃ lokabudhivikalpitād ahorātralakṣaṇād apakṛṣyamāṇāt kālād alpīyaḥ parijighṛkṣayā yataḥ param apakraṣṭuṃ na śakyate saḥ apakarṣaparyantaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ vastubhūtaḥ yad vā yāvatā samayena vicalitaḥ paramāṇuḥ pūrvaṃ deśaṃ jahyād uttaram abhisaṃpadyeta sa kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ sarvathā yu asti sūkṣma kṣaṇa ity arthaḥ tasya pravāhavicchedabhāvinaḥ tasya kṣaṇasya pravāhaḥ prabandhaḥ avidhedo nairantaryaṃ tathā bhavituṃ śīlaṃ yasya kṣaṇasya pravāhāvicchedabhāvinaḥ kṣaṇasya yat ānantaryaṃ saḥ kṣaṇasya kramaḥ tayoś ca kṣaṇatatkramayor nāsti vastusamāhāraḥ kṣaṇakramasyāvastutvāt kṣaṇasya ca ekatvāt nāsti tayoḥ samāhāraḥ samūhaḥ nanu cāsati kṣaṇatatkramasamāhāre kathaṃ māsasaṃvatsarādāḥ pravarterann iti tadartham āha buddhisamāhārāt buddhiparikalpitāt kṣaṇatatkramayoḥ samāhārādād ityādideśāntarasaṃbandhāvabandhabuddhisamudbhāvitāt muhūrtāhorātrādayaḥ tataś ca buddhisthita eṣa bhedaḥ yo hi prasannasamānapratyayavāhinasaḥ ekāgrabhūmipratiṣṭhicittasattvaḥ tasya saty api kālānubhave kṣaṇayugasahasrayos tulyatā na evaṃ vyutthitacittasya tathā svapne api ghaṭikāmātreṇa buddhiparikalpitaṃ yojanasahasram anekaṃ saṃvatsareṇa eva gantavyaṃ gaddhati tasmād buddhivaicitryanimrmita eva kālasamāhāraḥ yasya tu kriyāvyatiriktaḥ kālaḥ nityo vibhuḥ tasya cirakṣipratvādy api kriyāmātre paryavasitatvāt pṛthakkālāstitvena liṅgaṃ ghaṭate niyataparimāṇā hi kriyānavagatapariṇāmāyāḥ kriyāyā lakṣaṇam yathāgodohanaṃ svapiti odanapākam adhīte iti sa eva ca kālaḥ na hi nityasya vibhoḥ tasya kūṭasthasyāsambandhatvāt vastvantaraparicchedakatvaṃ prasthādivad upapadyate kriyāvān kālaḥ paricchedakaḥ prasthādivad iti cet tasyāpi kriyāvattvāt kriyāvataś ca pariddhedanīyatvād anyena kriyāvatā paricchedakena kālena bhavitavyam tasyāpy anyenety anavathāprasaṅgaḥ kriyāvattvāc cānityatvam api atha svavyāpāreṇa eva kālaḥ paricchedanīyakaṃ yāyād iti cet anye api svavyāpāreṇa eva paricchedyā iti kālapṛthaktvakalpāa nirarthikā tathā ca kriyā evāstu kālaḥ athāpi sadbhāvamātreṇa kālaḥ paricchedaka iti sarveṣām api sadbhāvāviśeṣād evaṃ prasaktam kriyākālapakṣe apy eṣa vikalpaḥ prāpta iti cet na kriyāyāḥ sarvaprasiddhatvāt paricchedakatvasya ca ā godohamās te ityādiṣu siddhatvāt kriyā eva pricchedikā labhyate nāparaḥ kālaḥ pariddhedaka iti ciraṃ kṣipram iti ca prayatnamandimapāṭavakṛtaḥ pratyayo na vyatiriktakālanibandhana ity āha sa khalv ayaṃ kālaḥ saṃvatsarādirūpo vastuśūnyo buddhinirmāṇaḥ buddhyā nirmāpiṣyate śabdadharmānupātī truṭinimeṣāhorātrādiśabdavikalpānupravartī laukikānāṃ vyutthitadarśanānāṃ vastusvarūpa ivābhāsate kṣaṇas tu vasturūpaḥ vāstavikaḥ taddravyānyathātveenānumīyamānaḥ kramāvalambī kramaś ca kṣaṇānantaryātmā kṣaṇapravāhāviddhedabuddhinimittaḥ taṃ kṣaṇaṃ kālavidaḥ kāla ity ācakṣate yoginaḥ na ca dvau kṣaṇau saha bhavataḥ yayoḥ samāhāraḥ kalpyeta ekasmin dharmiṇi sahajanmanoḥ kṣaṇayor asaṃbhavāt jāyamāno hi caitra ekasmin kṣaṇe jāyate na tatra dvau kaṇau saha bhavataḥ kramaś ca na dvayoḥ kasmāt dvayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ sahabhuvorāsambhavāt pūrvasmād uttarasya bhāvino yad ānantaryaṃ kṣaṇasya sa kramaḥ yathā piṇḍād uttarabhāvino ghaṭasya yad ānantaryaṃ sa kramaḥ na hi cakrāntarasthasya mṛt piṇḍasya cakrāntarasthamṛtpiṇḍajanito ghaṭaḥ krame vartate tasmād vartamāna ekaikaḥ kṣaṇaḥ na pūrvottarāv atītānāgatau staḥ pūrvottarayor dharmisvarūpamātratvāt dharmī ca vartamānakṣaṇārūḍha eva tasmānnityā nāsti tatsamāhāraḥ kṣaṇatatkramasamāhāraḥ ye tu bhūtabhāvinaḥ atītabhaviṣyantaḥ kṣaṇāḥ te dharmiṇaḥ pariṇāmāstitayā dharmipariṇāmāpekṣayā vyākhyeyāḥ tena ekena kṣaṇena kṛtsno lokaḥ pariṇāmam anubhavati tatkṣaṇopārūḍhāḥ vartamānakṣaṇopārūḍhāḥ khalv amī sarve dharmāḥ sarvapadārthāḥ yad uktam atītakṣaṇasya nāsti krama iti tasyatat prayojanaṃ tatkramakramapratiṣedhaḥ kṣaṇakramakrame hi sati kṣaṇakramasya vastutvaṃ prasajyeta vastuno hi etayoḥ kṣaṇa tat kramayoḥ saṃyamāt tayoḥ sākṣātkaraṇam tataś ca vivekajaṃ jñānam kṣaṇatatkramāṅkitā eva hi sarve padārthā iti tān aśeṣān vivicya vijānāti tasya vivekajasya jñānasya kīdṛśaṃ jñetam iti tasya viṣayaviśeṣaḥ upakṣipyate jātilakṣaṇadeśair anyatānavaddhedāt tuyayos tataḥ pratipattiḥ tulyayor deśalakṣaṇasārūpye jātibhedaḥ padārthānām anyatāyāḥ anyatvāvaddhedasya hetuḥ yathā gaur iyaṃ baḍabeyam iti yatra jātibhedo nāsty ekā eva jātiḥ tatra tulyajātitve lakṣaṇaṃ liṅgam anyatvāvaddhedakaram kālākṣī gauḥ svastimatī gaur iti yatra na jātibhedo nāpi lakṣaṇabhedas tatra deśabhedo nyatvāvacchedahetuḥ yathā dvayor āmalakayor jātilakṣaṇasārūpye deśabhedo nyatvakaraḥ idaṃ pūrvam āmalakam idam uttaram iti yadā tu pūrvam āmalakam anyavyagrasya samākulitacittasya jñātūr uttaradeśa upāvartate pūrvadeśe cottaraṃ tadā tulyadeśatve pūrvam etad uttaram etad iti tulyayoḥ pravibhāgānupapattiḥ asandigdhena tattvajñānena bhavitavyaṃ jñeyasya vidyamānatvād ekarūpasya ity ata idam uktaṃ tataḥ pratipattir vivekajñānād iti kṣaṇatatkramasaṃyamāpāditavivekajanmano jñānāt pratipattir iti tatkatham pūrvāmalakasaha la kṣaṇo deśaḥ pūrvāmalakasahacaro deśaḥ uttarāmalakasaha la kṣaṇāt uttarāmalakasahacarāt deśāt bhinnaḥ te ca āmalake pūrvottara la kṣaṇasahacarite svadeśa la kṣaṇānubhavabhinne svadeśacihnabhūte yaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tad anubhavabhinne svadeśa la kṣaṇānubhācihnite anyadeśa la kṣaṇānubhavas tayor anyatve hetur iti anena dṛṣṭāntena paramāṇor atulyajātilakṣaṇabheda deśa sya pūrvaparamāṇudeśasaha la kṣaṇasākṣātkaraṇāt pūrvaparamāṇudaśena sahabhūtasya la kṣaṇasya sākṣātkaraṇāt uttaraparamāṇos tad deśāpavṛttau pūrvadeśagatāv api uttarasya tad deśānubhavabhinnaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇabhedāt tayor īśvarasya yogino nya thā tvapratyayaḥ bhedāvacchedo bhavati atrāpare varṇayanti ye antyā viśeṣāḥ paramāṇu gatā nityāḥ te eva anyatāpratyayaṃ kurvantīti kiṃ tatkṣaṇatatkramasaṃyamena yathā ghaṭādigatā viśeṣā anyatāpratyayaṃ kurvanti tathā paramāṇu gatā ye viśeṣāḥ ta eva tadbhāvapratyayaṃ svasadbhāvapratyayaṃ ca kurvīran āśrayabhedapratyayam api kurvanti atrocyate deśalakṣaṇabhedo mūrtivyavadhijātibhedaśa cānyatve hetuḥ ukta eva sthūleṣu na tu nanu paramāṇuṣu pratikṣaṇapariṇāmitvāt avasthiteṣu hi viśeṣeṣv antyeṣu syād anyathā vadhāraṇam na cānavaratapariṇāmeṣu ghaṭate yadā pūrvaḥ paramāṇur uttaraparamāṇurūpeṇa pariṇamate pūrvaparamāṇurūpeṇa cottaraḥ tatrāvasthitāntyaviśeṣābhāvād vivekapratipattir anupapannā tatrāvaśyaṃ kṣaṇatatkramasaṃyamajanitavivekañānād eva saṃpratipattiḥ anityāś ca paramāṇava iti hy uktam tasmāt kṣaṇabhedas tu yogibuddhigamya eva tathā cānityatvasya paramāṇunām ācāryāntaramatapratipādanadvāreṇa prasiddhiṃ darśayati ata uktam mūrtivyavadhijātibhedābhāvāt nāsti mūla jāti pṛthaktvam iti vārṣagaṇyaḥ yathā pratikṣetrajñaṃ pradhānabahutvaṃ nyāyaviruddhaṃ mūrtivyavadhijātibhedābhāvāt pradhānānāṃ pṛthatvam ekapuruṣārthadṛśyavat anupapannam evaṃ paramāṇunām api mūlatve pṛthaktvaṃ na upakalpate tataś ca ekaṃ mūlam iti prāptam na paramāṇubhedo hi nityo uktaḥ paramāṇunām ca mūrtatvāt rūpādimattvāc cānityatvaṃ ghaṭādivad eva iti tāra Kaṃ sarvaviṣayaṃ sarvathāviṣayam akramaṃ ceti vivekajaṃ jñānam kāṣṭhāprāptaṃ jñānaṃ devarṣigandharvādīnām tārakam iti vivekajam idam ucyate svapratibhottham anaupadeśikam ity arthaḥ nānyena upadeṣṭaṃ śakyaṃ nāpy upadeśena yathāvat grahītuṃ śakyate yasmāt tat sarvavastuviṣayam nāsya kiṃcid aiṣayībhūtam sarvathāviṣayaṃ ca sarvam atītānāgatapratyutpannaṃ sarvaprayāyaiḥ sarvaviśeṣaṇaiḥ sarvathā sarveṇa prakāreṇa jānāti akramam ekakṣaṇopārūḍham ekasmin kṣaṇe sarvaṃ sarvathā gṛhṇāti nāsadādivat krameṇa tat etad vivekajaṃ jñānaṃ paripūrṇam asya evāṃśo yogapradīpaḥ sa eva jñānāṃśo yogaś ca pradīpaś ca yogasya vā pradīpo yogapradīpaḥ madhumatīṃ bhūmim upādāya ārabhya yāvad asya vivekajasya jñānasya parisamāptiḥ tāvat vivekajajñānaprisamāptiparyantāni jñānāni monojavattvādiyuktāni asya evāṃśaḥ yagaje jñānāaiśvaryasyā eva tadvairāgyānantaraṃ kaivalyam iti prāptamata āha prāptavivekajñānasya aprāptavivekajñānasya vā bāhyadarśananivṛttau kaivalyam katham iti sattvapuruṣayoḥ śuddhisāmye kaivalyam iti yadā nirdhūmatarajas tamomalaṃ puruṣānyatāpratyayamātram anyatāmātrapratyayavaibhavayuktaṃ dagdhakleśabījaṃ vinivṛttāvidyāpratyayavāsanārūpaṃ buddhisattvam bhavati tadā puruṣasya śuddhisārūpyam ivāpannam yady api triguṇaṃ puruṣavilakṣaṇaṃ puruṣaś ca tadvilakṣaṇaḥ tathāpi puruṣānyatāpratyayapariṇāmitvāt śuddhisārūpyam ivāpannam ity ucyate etasyām avasyāyāṃ kaivalyaṃ bhavatīśvarasyānīśvarasya vā vivekajñānabhāginaḥ itarasya vā yasmād ubhayor avidyānivṛttir eva kāraṇaṃ tasmāt na hi dagdhakleśabījasya jñāne kācid apekṣā yataḥ samyagdarśī sarvaṃ triguṇam iti manyate triguṇaś capratyayo heya iti madhumatyādijñāne tasya na kadācid apy apekṣā yat tu yogajñānam aiśvaryaṃ ca uktaṃ tat samyagdarśanārthānukrāntasattvaśuddhipadamārgeṇa prakrāntam ānuṣaṅgikam paramārthatas tu jñānād adarśanaṃ vinivartate tasmin vinivṛtte na santy uktakleśāḥ asmitā ādayaḥ teṣām avidyākṣetratvāt kleśābhāvāc ca karmavipākābhāavaḥ kleśamūlaḥ karamāśayaḥ sati mūle tadvipākaḥ iti hi pratipāditam tasmāt samyagdarśanārtham evedaṃ śāstram na jñānāiśvaryavibhūtiprayojanam caritādhikārāś ca etasyām avasthāyāṃ guṇāḥ na puruṣasya punar dṛśyatvenātiṣṭhante tat puruṣasya kaivalyam tadā puruṣaḥ svarūpamātrajyotiḥ ity amalaḥ kevalībhavatīti itiśabdaḥ samāptyarthaḥ iti śrīgovandabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya paramahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrī śaṅkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau pātañjalayogasūtravbhāṣyavivaraṇe vibhūtipādas tṛtīyaḥ prathame pāde samādhiḥ prādhānyena nirdiṣṭaḥ dvitīye tatsādhanāni vyākhyātāni tṛtīye tu samyagdarśanārtha yogāṅgānuṣṭhānānuṣaṅgajñānāiśvaryānukramaṇaṃ kṛtam tac ca sarvaṃ duḥkhasya iti jaigīṣavyakhyānena pratipāditam duḥkhahānaṃ ca ātyantikaguṇoparama ity uktam tathā eva tadvairāgyād api doṣabījakṣaye kaivalyam prāptavivekajñānasya aprāptavivekajñānasya vā sattvapuruṣayoḥ śuddhisāmye kaivalyam ity anantaram uktam tac ca kaivalyaṃ pratipakṣanirvartanena pratipādanīyam itīdaṃ kaivalyapādānukramaṇaṃ kriyate tathā anekajanmāntaroparjitavāsanoddhedaprakārāś ca kaivalyārtham eva pradarśanīyāḥ tathā kaivalyopayogisamādhisiddhistutyarthaṃ pūrvatrānuktaṃ siddhyantaraṃ prakriyate talyajātīyānām anyatamanindanenānyatamastutir bhavati tatra dhyānajamanāśayam karmaśuklākṛṣṇaṃ yoginas trividham itareṣām iti vakṣyamāṇena stutyarthatā āviṣkariṣyate janmauṣadhimantratapassamādhijāḥ siddhayaḥ dehāntaritā yathā yogādinā dehāntareṣu svargādiṣu janmasiddhiḥ oṣadhibhir asurabhavaneṣu rasāyanena somāmalakādibhakṣaṇena pūrvadehānapanayena eva mantraiḥ upajpyamānaiḥ ākāśagamanādi tapasā saṃkalpasiddhiḥ kāmarūpī yatra kāmagamana ity evamādiḥ samādhijāḥ siddhayaḥ pūrvam eva vyākhyātāḥ tatra siddhiḥ kāyakaraṇānām utkarṣaḥ janmasiddhau tu patitapūrvopārjitakāryakaraṇasya śarīrāntaram upādāyiṣyata iti nāsti tatra saṃśayaḥ apatitaśarīrasya tu jātyantarapariṇāme kiṃ tad eva kāryakaraṇam upādānam utānyad apīti tatra kāyendriyāṇām anyajātipariṇatānāṃ jātyantarapariṇāmaḥ prakṛtyāpūrāt pūrvapariṇāmāpāye samavasthitānām eva pūrvakāryakaraṇānām uttarapariṇāmopajanaḥ apūrvāvayavānupraveśena bhavati kasmāt alpaparimāṇasyopādānaya mahāparimāṇakāryānupapatteḥ na hi daśapalāt tapanīyapiṇḍādaśītipalā patrī janiṣyate kāyendriyaprakṛtayaḥ svaṃ svaṃ vikāraṃ kāyam indriyaṃ vā anugṛhnanty āpūrṇadharmādinimittam ādigrahaṇād adharmam api nimittam apekṣamāṇāḥ dharmādinimittam apekṣamāṇāḥ svaṃ svaṃ vikāram anugṛhṇāntīty uktam tatrakioṃ dharmādinimittaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ prayojanaṃ kim vā neti tad āha nimittam aprayojakaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ varaṇabhedas tu tataḥ kṣetrikavat na hi dharmādinimittaṃ prayojakaṃ prakṛtīnām kasmāt na hi kāryeṇa dharmādinā nimittena kāraṇaṃ kāryakaraṇapratirūpaṃ pravartyate kathaṃ tarhi varaṇabhedas tu tataḥ dharmādinimittāt bhavati kṣetrikavat yathā kṣetrikaḥ kedārād apāṃ pūrṇāt kedārāntaraṃ piplāvayiṣuḥ nāpaḥ pāṇinā apakarṣati āvaraṇaṃ tu tāsāṃ bhinatti tasmit bhinne svayam evāpaḥ kedārāntaram āplāvayanti tathā dharmaḥ prakṛtīnām āvaraṇam adharmaṃ bhinatti dharmam adharmo api bhinatty āvaraṇam tasmin bhinne svayam eva prakṛtayaḥ svaṃ svaṃ vikāram āplāvayanti pūrayanti yathā vā sa eva kṣetrikas tasmin eva kedāre na prabhavaty audakān bhaumān vā rasān dhānyamūlāny anupraveśāyitum kiṃ tu mudgatindukagavī śrukaśyāmākādīn tasmāt dhānyamūlāt apakarṣati apakṛṣṭeṣu teṣu svayam eva rasā dhānyamūlāny anuviśanti tathā dharmo nivṛttimātre kāraṇam adharmasya adharmo api dharmasya śuddhyaśuddhyor atyantavirodhāt na tu prakṛtipravṛttau dharmo hetur bhavatīti yadā tu yogī bahūn kāyān nirmīte tadā kim ekamanaskās te bhavanti athānekamanaskā iti samādhisiddhau kaścid anukto viśeṣa ucyate nirmāṇacittānyasmitāmātrāt so haṅkāraṃ cittakāraṇam upādāya nirmāṇacittāni nirmitāni cittāni aprakṛtānīśvaracittāni navāni karoti yogī cittagrahaṇam udāharaṇamātram indriyāṇy apy asmitāmātrād eva tataḥ te sacittāḥ sakaraṇāś ca bhavantiu cittendriyābhāve ca mṛtadeśīyaḥ kāyo nirarthakaḥ syāt ekacittatve tu guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ pravṛttibhedaś ca na upakalpate tatra vibhutvād ekakṣetrajñatve api bahukāyārambhitvam upapadyate guṇāpradhānānekapravṛttibhedārthaṃ tu karaṇabheda eṣitavyaḥ kecit tu kṣetrajñā apy anye pratikāyabhedaṃ bhavantīti manvate kecid atra codaytanti akṛtābhyāgamam anye tu tadanurūpopārjitakarmāṇaḥ kṣetrajñā bhavantīti parihāram āhuḥ yady evaṃ bahūnāṃ cittānām ekacittābhiprāyapurassarāpravṛttir iti tatra ucyate pravṛttibhede prayojakaṃ cittam ekam ankeṣām pravṛttibhede saty api savacittānāṃ prayojakaṃ cittam ekaṃ phalādhikṛtadeśīyaṃ śarīrāntare nirmimīte tac ca yogibuddhim anuvartate anyāni ca nirmāṇacittāni bhinnānekapravṛttīni tannāyakacittānuvartīni bhavanti tataś ca teṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ apekṣā ity evamādipravṛttibhedaḥ upapadyate rāhaprakṛtipravṛttibhedavat evam ekacittābhiprāyapuraḥsarā ca pravṛttir avakalpate tatra dhyānajamanāśayam pañcavidhaṃ nirmāṇacittaṃ janmaiṣadhimantratapas samādhisāmarthyanirmitam tatra teṣu yad eva dhyānajaṃ cittaṃ tad evānāśayaṃ kleśakarmāśayāpavarjitam tasya eva nāsty āśayaḥ rāgādipravṛttiḥ ato na puṇyapāpābhisaṃbandhaḥ kṣīṇakleśatvād yoginaḥ kleśamūlo hi karamāśayaḥ ity uktam tadabhāvāc ca karmāśayānupapattiḥ apareṣāṃ tu janmādisiddhānāṃ karamāśayaḥ akṣīṇakleśatvād vidyate eva kuta etad yogina eva na karamāśayaḥ itareṣāṃ tv astīti yataḥ karmāśuklākṛṣṇaṃ yoginas trividham itareṣām siddhāsiddhasāmānyaviṣayam idaṃ sūtram nanu ca pūrvasūtram api sāmānyaviṣayam eva na samādhisiddhistutyarthatvāt sāmānyaviṣayatve tu samādhisiddhistutir anupapannā syāt siddhiparisaṃkhyānena tu viśeṣaviṣayatve tulyajātīyajanmādisiddhicatuṣṭayasāvadyatvasaṃkīrtanāt samādhisiddheḥ stutir upapadyate kiṃ ca janmādisiddhisādhanānāṃ kaivalyārthatāpratiṣedhaś cārthād iti viśiṣṭaviṣayam eva pūrvasūtram idaṃ tu sāmānyaviṣayam eva pūrvasūtrahetutvenopādānāt catuṣpadī khalu ayaṃ karmajātiḥ kṛṣṇā durātmanāṃ śāstramārgātivartiduṣṭacetasām aśuddhatarā yā tu bahissādhanasādhyā jāyāputrapaśuyājakādiniṣpādyā sā śuklakṛṣṇā kā sau yatra para pīḍā nugrahadvāreṇa karmāśayapracayaḥ sā kleśabāhulakaniṣpādanyatvāt kṛṣṇā ca śuklā ca nanu jyotiṣṭomādikarmaśāstrasamadhigatatvān na kṛṣṇaṃ śuklam eva tu tat atrocyate na kāmyair anaikāntikatvāt tāny eva cārthānarthobhayakāraṇāni atha tat phalasya svargāder abhimatatvād arthatvam eva iti cen na paradārābhimarśanasyāpi vāñchitatvād arthatvaprasaṅgāt atha paradārābhisaraṇādāv abhyugradoṣasampātāt pratiṣiddhatvāc ca rāgāginiyogapravṛtteś cāsamānam iti cen na tatrāpi samānatvāt kāmātmatāniṣedhād aniṣṭayogaś ca janmamaraṇayor abhyugradoṣabhūtayor avaśyaṃ bhāvitvād iṣṭāniṣṭadvayahetutvam eva sa cāniṣṭayogaḥ parapīḍāder ity avasīyate tat pratiṣedhopapatteḥ avaśyaṃ hi janmamaraṇadvayena vinā svargādiphalam upabhoktuṃ na śakyam tac ced asti tasya duḥkharūpatvādāyātaṃ tarhi jyotiṣṭomādīnām ubhayātmakatvam atha karmāntaram eva pratiṣiddhaṃ janmamaraṇārambhakāraṇam iti cen na tadbhāvabhāvitvāt tasmin hi sati janmamaraṇabhāvāt atha tu bhavatpakṣe nityam eva kurvīta na janmamaraṇe pravarteyātām kurvata eva te bhavato nākurvataḥ tasmānnityā nimittatvam avagamyate kiṃ ca yena janmamaraṇam ārapsyate svargādau tat karma yadi janmāntaragataṃ tatrānirmokṣaprasaṅgaḥ kāmyapratiṣiddhākriyāyām api pūrvajanmakṛtaphalasya avaśyaprāpaṇīyatvāt atha prāktanajanmakarmakṣayārthāni nityānīti cet tan na niyamānupapatteḥ aniṣṭaphalānyevārabdhakāryāṇi pūrvakarmāṇi na tv iṣṭaphalānīti na nityantuṃ śakyate adṛṣṭaphaleṣu hi satsu nityāny eva kurvato api mokṣānupapattir janmārambhitvaṃ ca tata iṣṭānām apy ubhayahetutvaṃ siddham bāhyasādhanānāṃ karmaṇāṃ pīḍānugraharūpatvāt na vai khalv api nityena pūrvakṛtakarmaṇām iṣṭānāṃ jyotiṣṭomādīnāṃ nivṛttir upakalpate virodhābhāvāt avirodhaś cobhaeṣāṃ śuddhirūpatvāt tantrasiddheś ca athāpi brūyāde dane kajanmārabdhāni karmāṇi janmai kai kamārabhante nānārabdhakāryam avaśiṣyata iti tathā api pūrvajnmakarmaṇaidānīntanajanmaphaladānena kṣayaṅgatatvād adhunātanajanmaniṣpāditānām abhinavānām eva kāmyānāṃ svargaphalajanmamaraṇaduḥkhārambhitvam iti śuklakṛṣṇarūpāpattiḥ tataś ca janmamaraṇaduḥkhasya svargābhidhānāyāḥ prīteś ca darśanāt tatkāraṇasya dvirūpatvam anumāsyāmahe tathā ca siddhe pratiṣiddhabhūtahiṃsācaraṇaṃ kratvartham apy agnīṣomīyādau pravartmānaṃ ṛṣṇarūpam ity anumāsyāmahe kratvarthāpi satī hiṃsā aniṣṭabhūtā eva tārthatāṃ pratipadyate yad uktam abiśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovad iti cottaram iti tatra śirovad ity evaṃ jātīyakadṛṣṭāntāsiddhatvam aviśeṣeṇa yac chāstram iti tu homasvarūpasya virodhād bādhyabādhakatvam upapadyate hiṃsāyās tu virodhābhāvād ubhayor hetutvaṃ bhojanasyeva sukhaśarīrasthitidvayahetutvam yathā ca tīrthasnānasya hlādādṛṣṭārthatvaṃ tathā hiṃsāapy aniṣṭaphalatvam aparityajantī mahāphalaṃ kratuṃ na eva nābhinirvartayati atha bāhyasādhanasādhyam api nityaṃ kevalaṃ kāmasaṃyogābhāvāc chuklam eva iti ced evam ucyate na doṣavattvena nityakāmyānām aviśeṣāt yathā kāminaḥ kāmyānīti kāmasaṃyogena kāmyānāṃ doṣavattvam evaṃ kāmādihetu bhūtāvidyādoṣavattvam aviśiṣṭam iti nityānām apy ubhayātmakatvam eva avidyāvattvaṃ ca nityeṣu pravṛttasya prāyaścittanimittotpatter avaśyaṃ bhāvitvāt api cāviduṣa eva sarvaṃ karma viduṣaḥ karmānutpatteḥ vidvān hi puruṣaḥ svarūpāvasthānavyatirekeṇa phalaṃ nābhimanyate svarūpamātrāvasthānaṃ ca samastavyāpāravirāmeṇa pravartate na ca evaṃ viduṣaḥ kriyā uṣṭhānaṃ ghaṭate na hi sthalapathenābhipratiṣṭhāsmāno jalamārgābhiprasthānasādhanaṃ nāvādikam anutiṣṭhati nanu na ca nityakāmyayor evaṃ satyaviśeṣaḥ syāt atrocyate kāmitaphala tanmātraṃ ni karmamātranivṛttiprayojanatvān nityānām adoṣaḥ yo hi kāmyādvinivṛttas tasya bahulaṃ karmaṇāṃ kāmarahitena śuddhena kartrā kṛtatvād atiśuddhaphalatvaṃ śuklatvabahutvāc ca saṃskārārthatvam api ca kāmanivṛttir eva mahat phalam kiṃ ca nityaṃ kurvataḥ kim arthaṃ karomi kiṃ vā asya phalaṃ ke vāsyānuṣṭhāne doṣāḥ iti samyagdarśanarūpaḥ parāmarśo jāyata iti nityasyāsti viśeṣaḥ śuklajṛṣṇātmakatvaṃ tv aviśiṣṭam ubhayeṣām api karmaṇām
