bāhyasādhanasādhanīyatvena parapīḍopapatteḥ iti tasmād ucyate śuklā karmajātiḥ tapas svādhyāyānavatām sā hi kevale manasyāyattatvād abahissādhanā bāhyasādhānānapekṣā na parān pīḍayitvā bhavati aśuklākṛṣṇā saṃnyāsināṃ kṣīṇakleśānāṃ caram adehānām eṣām ārabdhaikaśarīrāṇām aśuklā saṃnyāsāt akṛṣṇā cānupāānāt akaraṇāt nāpi śuklakṛṣṇavimiśrā bāhyasaṃnyāsānupādānābhyāṃ hetubhyām tathā ca uktam aniṣṭam iṣṭaṃ miśraṃ ca trividhaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam bhavaty tyatyāgināṃ yogināṃ pretya na tu saṃnyāsināṃ kvacit iti itareṣāṃ tu bhūtānāṃ janmauṣadhimantratapassiddhānām anyeṣāṃ ca trividhaṃ śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ miśraṃ ca pūrvam iva yathā dvitīye pāde kleśamūlaḥ ityādau kaivalyasya prastutatvāt tasya ca prativandhahetavaḥ kleśāḥ karmāṇi vāsānāś ca vyākhyātavyāḥ kleśānāṃ tu vyāpāraḥ pratipakṣaḥ nivṛttiś ca teṣāṃ vistareṇa vyākhyātāḥ evaṃ karmaṇām api vāsanānāṃ tulyavyāpārāvasthānapratipakṣanivṛttayo nirvarṇanīyā ity ata uttarāṇi sūtrāṇy ārabhyante yatastannivṛtau kaivalyam upapadyate nānyathā tatas tadvipākānuguṇānām evābhivyaktir vāsanānām tataḥ tasmāt trividhāt uktalakṣaṇāt kṛṣṇaśuklavimiśrarūpāt karmaṇaḥ pravipacyamānād hetu bhūtāt tadvipakānuguṇānāṃ tasya eva karmaṇo vipākaḥ phalaṃ tadanuguṇānāṃ tadanurūpāṇāṃ tādṛśīnām eva vāsanānām abhivyaktiḥ etad uktaṃ bhavati devatiryaṅmanuṣyavipākahetuṣu karmasu madhye yajjātīyasya karmaṇ O yādṛśo vipākaḥ tasya vipākasyānuguṇā vāsanāḥ tat karmavipākam anuśarete anūtpadyante tāsām evābhivyaktiḥ tatsadṛśena karmavipākena saṃskṛtatvāt yathā mātṛ sadṛśīṃ pravilokya vatso nudhāvati nānyāsām atadanuguṇānām abhivyaktiḥ na hi daivaṃ karma vipacyamānaṃ phalābhimukhībhāvam āpadyamānaṃ nārakatiryaṅ manuṣavāsanā abhivyaktinimittaṃ saṃ bhavati nimittanaimittakayoḥ pratiniyatānuguṇatvāt kiṃ tu daivānuguṇā evāsyābhivyajyante nārakatiryaṅmānuṣeṣv evaṃ samānaścarcaḥ samādhiḥ nārake karmaṇi vipacyamāne tatkarmānuguṇā vāsanāḥ prādurbhavanti tathā tairyagyonakarmaṇi vipacyamāne tadvipākānurūpā vāsanā vyajyante tathā mānuṣe api samāno nyāyaḥ na hi svavipākasadṛśīr anupādāya vāsanās tasya tasya karmaṇo vipākaḥ saṃbhavati nāpi vāsanānām ātmaniṣpādakavipākārambhikarmatulyarūpāṇi karmāntarāṇi vipākābhimukhāny antareṇābhivyaktiḥ evaṃ karmaṇāṃ vāsanānāṃ ca parasparahetuhetamadbhāvo nācibhūtaḥ tatra vāsanānām anekajātikāladeśavyavadhānena davīyasīnām ānantaryaṃ vipacyamānena karmaṇā saha nāsti yathā davīyasāṃ mitrasvajanādinām yathā eva ca nedīyasī vāsanā paṭīyasī na tathā daviyasī paṭīyamānam āsīdati tasmānnityā nāsti davīyasīnām ānantaryaṃ vāsanānām tadabhāve cāyaṃ doṣaḥ prāpnoti yathākalpaśātāntaritaḥ vṛṣadaṃśavipākaḥ bhaviṣyataḥ vṛṣadaṃśavipākābhisyānantarātīto daivavipākaḥ tatra nedīyasī daivavāsanā viruddhatvāt vṛṣadaṃśavipākābhivyaktihetutāṃ na pratipadyate kalpaśatavyavahitānām api vṛṣadaṃśavāasnānāṃ viprakarṣād anupādāne vṛṣadaṃśavipākahetoḥ karmaṇo vipāko nāvakalpeta tataś ca karmaṇāṃ vāsanānāṃ ca ānarthakyaṃ prasajyeteti atrocyate jātideśakālavyavahitānām apy ānantaryaṃ smṛtisaṃskārayor ekarūpatvāt vṛṣadaṃśavipākādayaḥ svakarmavyañjakāñjanāḥ vyañjakena svena karmaṇā vyajyamānāḥ yadi jātiśatena vā duradeśatayā vā kalpasamasreṇa vā vyavahitāḥ nanu ca jātivyavadhānena eva kālaviprakarṣa uktaḥ kiṃ kālagrahaṇena ucyate bhūyaṃsi janmāni divase ekasminn api kṣudrajantuprabhṛtīnāṃ keṣāṃcid bhavanti na tatrātītakālaviprakarṣa iti kālagrahaṇam teṣu vṛṣadaṃśavipākādayaḥ pūrvam api svavyañjakanirvartitāḥ santaḥ punaś ca svavyañjakāñjanodayāḥ drāg ity eva kṣipram eva vṛṣadaṃśavipākābhisaṃskṛtā vāsanā upādāyābhibyajyante kasmāt evam yato vyavahitānām apyāsāṃ sadṛśaṃ karmābhivyañjakaṃ nimittībhūtam iti na hi balīvardavipākābhivyaktikāraṇaṃ karma vṛṣadaṃśavāsanābhivyaktinimittaṃ bhavati visadṛśatvāt anurūpaṃ hi nimittam abhivyañjakam āmlādikṣaṇadarśane jihvā sravati tasmāt ānantaryam eva vāsanānām yatas tāsāṃ vyañjakaṃ tulyam tathā ca sati na ca āsanānāṃ nedīyas tā davīyas tā vā samānacittāśrayatvāt kutaś cāyam apy aparo hetur ānantaryasya smṛtisaṃskārayor ekarūpatvād iti pūrvaṃ tulyajātīyaṃ karmābhivyañjakaṃ vāsanānantaryahetur uktaḥ idānīm ayam anya ucyate yathā anubhavās tathā saṃskārāḥ yādṛśāḥ pratyayāḥ tathā vāsanāḥ te ca saṃskārā vāsanārūpāḥ yathāvasanāḥ smṛtaya iti tathā ca uktam grāhyoparaktaḥ pratyayo grāhyagrahaṇobhayākāranirbhāsaḥ ityādi jātideśakālavyavahitebhyaḥ saṃskārebhyaḥ smṛtayaḥ smṛtibhyaś ca punaḥ saṃskāro ity evam ete smṛtisaṃskārāḥ karmāśayavṛttilābhavaśābeśād abhivyajyante karmāśayasyāpi vṛttilābho deśādinimittāpekṣayeti pratipāditam ataś ca vyavahitānām api nimittanaimittikabhāvānucchedād ānantaryam eva yādṛśaḥ saṃskāras tādṛśī smṛtiḥ pratiniyatavyañjakatvāc ca tayor na viprakarṣaḥ kāraṇam yataḥ kalpaśatavyavahitād api saṃskārād eva tulyajātīyā smṛtir iti ānantaryam eva siddham odānīṃ vāsanānām anāditvena vipākanirvartakatvam abhidarśayati saṃskārasya cānāditvam ekaikasya cāsaṅkhyayonigamanaṃ vairāgyapratipattyarthaṃ pratipādayati tāsām anāditvaṃ cāśiṣo nityatvāt tāsāṃ vāsanānām āśiṣo nityatvād anāditvam yeyamātmāśīḥ maraṇaṃ mā nu bhūt iti evam āśīr vā bhūyasam iti sarvasya dṛśyate sāna svābhāvikī svarasapravṛttā api nirūḍhā api kasmāt jātamātrasyānannubhūtajananamaraṇadharmasya dveṣānusmṛtinimitto duḥkhānusmṛtihetuko vā maraṇatrāsaḥ kathaṃ bhavvet na hi kathañcana duḥkhasmaraṇādinimittopādānaṃ svābhāvikasya upapadyate na ca svābhāvikaṃ vastu nimittam upādatte na hi jvalanasyoṣṇatvam svābhāvikaṃ sadātmīyakārye nimittam īkṣeta na cānanubhūte viṣaye smṛtir iṣṭe niṣṭe vā kasyacid upaploṣyate anubhūtapriyānanusmaraṇe na ca tadviṣyavāñdhā tathā anubhūtāpriyānanusmaraṇe na tadviṣayo dveṣastrāsaś ca loke paridṛśyate tathā ca yo yo jātas tasya tasyeha janmany ananubhūtajanmamaraṇasya janmānantaram evātmāśīr abhidṛśyate tasmāt tadāśīr ityatvāt pūrvajanmamaraṇānubhavo numīyate tataḥ pūrvas tato api pūrva iti smṛtisaṃskārāṇāṃ tatkāraṇānāṃ ca janmamaraṇānubhavānām anāditvam anumimīmahe tathā eva ekaikasya prāṇabhṛto nekayonigamanasiddhiḥ evam etā vāsanā duravahānā avihānīyāḥ kuta evam yasmād anādivāsanānuviddhaṃ cittam idaṃ nimittavaśāt karmanimittavaśāt kāścid eva ca āsanāḥ pravipacyamānakarmatulyajātīyakriyā vipākābhi nna niṣpāditāḥ pratilabhya puruṣasya bhogāyopāvartate yāvad avasitādhikāram iti tad etac cittaṃ ghaṭaprāsādapradīpakalpaṃ saṃkocavikāsi hastimaśakādiśarīraparimāṇākaraṃ yathā dīpo ghaṭaprāsādādiṣu tad evam apare pratipannaḥ tatra ca yuktam āha tathā ceti tathā ca saṃkocavikāsitve cāntrābhāvaḥ maraṇād uttarakālam janmanaś ca prāg etasminantarāle bhavatīty antarābhāvaḥ saṃsaraṇaṃ sañcaraṇṃ yena sañcarati tad api śarīram ātivāhikaṃ cittasyāvibhutve yuktam iti bruvanti vṛttir evāsya vibhunaś cittasya saṅkocavikāsinīty ācāryāḥ ācāryagrahaṇam upapattimattvāt pūjārtham cittasya sthitir gatiś ca pariṇāmitvād vibhutve pīndriyāṇāṃ ca upapadyate yogināṃ ca vikaranabhāvaḥ sarvajñātvaṃ vibhutve ghaṭate na copabhogaśūnyasyātivāhikaśarīrasya kalpanāyām asti pramāṇam caśaviṣāṇavad anupalabhyamānatāt na ha vai saśarīrasya sataḥ priyāpriyayor apahatir astīti śruteḥ tathā atha yo haitānanantānupāste iti śrutiḥ karaṇavyāpitvaṃ khyāpayati tac ca saṃkocavikāsitvaṃ vṛtteḥ dharmādinimittāpekṣam nimittaṃ ca dvidhā bāhyam ādhyātmikam ca śarīrādisādhanāpekṣaṃ bāhyaṃ stutyabhivādanādi karma kiṃ punar ādhyātmikam āha kevalacittamātrādhīnaṃ śraddhādi tathā ca uktam ye vaite maitryādayo dhyāyināṃ vihārāḥ vittavyāpārāḥ veṣṭāni te bāhyasādhananiranugrahāḥ bāhyasādhananirapekṣāḥ kevalacittamātranirvṛttāḥ prakṛṣṭaṃ dharmam abhinirvartayanti tayoḥ bāhyādhyātmikayor nimittayoḥ mānasam ādhyātmikaṃ maitryādicittābhiniṣpannaṃ nimittaṃ balīyaḥ katham iti jñānavairāgye kenātiśyyete na kenāpīty arthaḥ yatas tṛtīyapādānukrāntavibhūtijātaṃ jñānavairāgyasādhyam daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ cittabalavyatirekeṇa kaḥ kartuṃ śaknoti kaś ca pibet samudram agastyavat iti ato mānasabalam eva balam na śārīram tasmāt mānasaṃ paramaṃ vadantīti śruteḥ tathā ca bhagavān ābhāṣe śreyān dravyamayādyajñāj jñāna yajñaḥ parantapa sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate Bh ṅ iti kathaṃ punas tāsāṃ vāsanānāṃ nivṛttiḥ anādirūḍhatvāt na nivṛttir āsāṃ ghaṭām āḍhaikate na ca tannivṛttim antareṇa kaivalyopapattir ity ata ucyate hetuphalakāśrayālambanaih saṃgṛhītatvād eṣām abhāve tadabhāvaḥ hetuś ca phalaṃ ca āśrayaś ca ālambanaṃ ca hetuphalāśrayālambanāni taiḥ saṃgṛhītatvād upagrathitatvād eṣāṃ hetvādīnām abhāve tad abhāve vāsanānām abhāvaḥ tasmād upapadyate vāsanānāṃ nivṛttiḥ ko sau hetuḥ ity āha dharmas tāvad avidhāvinamitacetasām tato dharmāt sukham sukhānuśayī rāgaḥ evam avidyāta eva niṣdiddhācaranat adharmaḥ tato duḥkham duḥkhānuśayī dveṣaḥ tataḥ sukhopārjane duḥkhaparihāre ca pūrvavad eva prayatnaḥ tena prayatnena vācā kāyena parispandamānaḥ param anugṛhṇāty upahanti ca punaś ca tataḥ parānugrahaparapīḍanābhyāṃ dharmādharmau tābhyāṃ sukhaduḥkhe tābhyāṃ ca rāgadveṣau pūrvavad eva tataḥ prayatnaḥ ity evam anavarataprārabdhaparibhramaṇaṃ pravṛttim idaṃ ṣaḍaraṃ saṃsāracakram asya ca pratikṣaṇam āvartamānasyāvidyā netrī rathacakasya turaṅgayuvatir iva sā mūlaṃ sarvakleśānām iti yad etad avidhānetṛkaṃ ṣaḍaraṃ cakram eṣa hetuḥ vāsanānām etac cakrāvṛttikṛtā hi tāḥ avidyāyās tv abhāve viśīrṇanābhibandhanam iva cakraṃ dharmādihetu cakram api viśīryate tad viśareṇa ca cakrāvṛttikṛtajanmanāṃ vāsanānām akāryakṣamatvam phalaṃ tu yam artham āśritya yasya pratytpannatā tat tasya phalam tad api vāsanānāṃ saṃgrāhakam tadabhāve vāsanābhivyaktyabhāvāt sukhādiphalasya vāsanādhāyitvāt na hy apūrvopajanaḥ nātyantam asad utpadyate manaḥ sādhikāraṃ kartavyatāvat na puruṣārthaśūnyam kṛtapuruṣārthasvarūpajñānaṃ vinivṛttāvidyākam iti sādhikāram āśrayo vāsanānām tad āśritya hi hetucakraparibhramaṇam na hy avasitādhikāre karaṇīyapuruṣārthaśūnye manasi nirāśrāyā vāsanāḥ sthātum utsahante yad abhimukhībhūtaṃ vastu yāṃ vāsanāṃ vyankti tasyās tadālambanam evaṃ hetuphalāśrayālambanir etaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ sarvā vāsāaḥ teṣāṃ hetvādīnām abhāve tatsaṃśrāyāṇām api vāsanānām abhāvaḥ chatrābhāve chāyānivṛttivat eṣāṃ cābhāvopāyo dvitīyapāde vyākhyātaḥ tasmāt na ca āsanā samyagdarśane sati kaivalyaprativandhinī bhavaty evāvidyānvṛttau kaivalyam iti nanu ca eṣām abhāve tad abhāva ity uktam tathā ca asiddhāntahānniḥ katham evaṃ hi siddhāntaḥ nāsty asataḥ sambhavaḥ utpattiḥ na cāsti sato vināśa iti atha punaḥ santi vāsanās tadā dravyatvena vastusatyaḥ sambhavantyaḥ kathaṃ nivartiṣyante na eva nirvartiṣyanta ity arthaḥ tatra katham uktam eṣām abhāve tadabhāva iti kathaṃ vā kaivalyam anuvṛttāsu hetukṛtajamasu vāsanāsv ity ata uttaraṃ paṭhati atītānāgataṃ svarūpato sty adhvabhrdād dharmāṇām evaṃ vaitat atha vā siddhāntapakṣeṇa eva neyaṃ bhāṣyam katham eṣām abhāve tadabhāvaḥ iti hetvādīnāṃ vāsanānāṃ ca nātyantābhāva ucyate kasmāt nāsty asataḥ sambhavo na cāsti sato vināceti dravyatvena vastutayā sambhavantyaḥ kathaṃ nirvartiṣyante vāsanāḥ śabdavikalpitatve vāsanā nātyantaṃ nivariṣyante santy evātītasvarūpeṇety arthaḥ bhaviṣyadvyaktikaṃ bhaviṣyati vyaktiḥ yasya tat bhaviṣyadvyaktikam yathā piṇḍāvasthāyāṃ ghaṭarūpam pravṛttetikartavyatāsādhanaṃ tat anāgatam bhūtavyaktikam atītaṃ bhūtā atikrāntā vyaktir upalabdhiviṣayatvāpattir yasya yathā prabhagno ghaṭaḥ tad atītam ity ucyate avyaṅgyam abhaviṣyat yasya vyañjane sādhanam upādeyam anatītavyaktikam abhūtam kiṃ tarhi vyāpāripārūḍhaṃ tat vartamānam yathā ghaṭaḥ svakriyāyāḥ trayaṃ ca etat atītānāgatavartamānalakṣaṇakaṃ vartamāne dharmiṇivartamānaṃ dharmarūpaṃ vastu samastalokaviniścitarūpasyāvyabhicāriṇo jñānasya pramāṇabhūtasya jñeyam iti saṅgirāmahe kasmāt niścitajñānotpattiviṣayatvāt yadi ca etad vastu svarūpato nābhaviṣyat nedaṃ nirviṣayaṃ jñānam udapatsyata yathā śaśaviṣāṇādi niścitajñānotpattikāraṇaṃ na bhavati na ca tatheha niścitavastujñānotpattiviṣayatvāt atha vā nāvastuviṣayam atīte bhaviṣyati ca ghaṭādau jñānam śabdavikalpitatve sati niścitarūpeṇa utpadyamānatvāt vartamānaghaṭādiviṣayajñānavat avyabhicārāc ca liṅgānumeyatvāc ca dhūmenāgnyādijñānavat liṅgadarśanānantarotpatter vā yad vā atītam anāgataṃ ca vastu sat svarūpeṇa liṅgadarśanānantarabuddhiviṣayatvāt prasiddhānumeyavat tasmād atītānāgataṃ svarūpato sti kiṃ ca bhogabhāgīyasya bhogahitasya yāgādeḥ apavargabhāgīyasya vā apavargahitasya samādhyādeḥ karmaṇaḥ phalam utpatsu yasya nāsti tasya vādinaḥ tat nirupākhyaṃ prāpnoti śaśaviṣāṇavat na hi śaśaviṣāṇaṃ bhaviṣyatīty upākhyāyate na tatheha kiṃ tarhi yāhena svargo bhaviṣyati samādhyādinā mokṣo bhaviṣyatīti ca kuśalaiḥ atikṭhor matibhir upākhyāyate tasmāt nirupākhyatvāt tad uddeśena phaloddeśena nirupākhyatvāt tena phalena nimittena kuśalānujñānam idaṃ kuru bhaviṣyati cānenādaḥ iti svayam apratipadyamānāḥ kuśalāḥ katham anujāni īyuḥ upadiśeyur vā kiṃ ca dṛṣṭamātrapratipattau kuśalākucalāviśeṣaś ca prāpnoti kuśalānāṃ vā mithyāpratipattiḥ akuśalāḥ samīcīnadarśanāḥ iti kiṃ cābhāvajñānāt kuśalā api phalāya nābhisamīheran abhāvāviśeṣāc ca kāraṇaniyamo nākalpiṣyata na sarvato vā sarvam udapatsyata nāpi kāraṇam upādāsyata upādāne vā tailārthī saikatam apy upādāsyata kiṃ kilair anekāyāsaniṣpādyaiḥ atyantāsad apūrvaṃ cedam ajaniṣyata na ca etad dṛṣṭam tasmāt tadbhokabhāgīyam apavargabhāgīyaṃ vā karma nimittam kāraṇaṃ vidyamānasya eva tasya phalasya vartamānīkaraṇe samarthaṃ nāpūrvopajane siddhaṃ hi svena ātmanā nimittaṃ sthālī kṣīradharmātañjanādi dadhyādikasya naimittakasya karkaśatarabhāvādyabhivyaktidvāreṇa viśeṣānugrahaṃ kurute nāpūrvam eva dadhi utpādayati tatheha bhogabhāgīyādikarma kiṃ ca dharmī cānekadharmasvabhāvo nekadharmātmā yathā kanakapiṇḍaḥ śāntoditāvyapadeśyarucakakuṇḍalādidharmātmakaḥ tasya dharmiṇaḥ adhvabhedenātītādilakṣaṇabhedena dharmāḥ pratyavasthitāḥ yathā vartamānaṃ vastu vyaktiviśeṣāpannaṃ kuṇḍalādivyaktiprāptaṃ dravyataḥ kāryarūpataḥ asti vyāpārādhirūḍhatayā na evam atītam anāgataṃ ca kiṃ tarhi svena eva vyaṅyena svarūpeṇabhaviṣyatā anāatam asti svena cānubhūtavyaktikena atikrāntopalabdhikenātītam asti vartamānasya eva tv adhvanaḥ svarūpato vyaktir iti na sā vyaktiḥ bhavaty atītānāgatayor adhvanoḥ ekasya cādhvanaḥ samaye kāle dvāv adhvānau dharmisamanvāgātau virodhāt na bhavata eva iti tathā ca ukto dhvasaṃkaraparihāraḥ yasya punar atītam anāgataṃ ca lakṣaṇaṃ svarūpeṇa nāsti tasya dharmāṇām adhvabhedo na prāpnoti katham na hi tasya ghaṭo bhaviṣyann atīto vā vidyate na hi kapālāni piṇḍo vāghaṭaḥ ataś ca vartamāna eva ghaṭo tīto nāgata iti cocyeta piṇḍakapālayor aghaṭatvāt mṛdi ca ghaṭasyābhāvād bhaviṣyati ghaṭo tīto ghaṭa iti ca piṇḍakapāle nirucyeyātām tathā ca vivakṣato gaur apy aśva syād aśvo api gaur iti athocyeta ghaṭasya pragabhāvapradhvaṃsābhāvāv atītānāgatatvenābhidhīyete iti tato apy eṣa vastuvācinā śabdena ghaṭo tīto nāgata iti cābhāvasyābhidhānaṃ yujyate sa tya tvavādinām nāpi niyama upapadyate ghaṭena eva vyapadiśyate ghaṭo tīto ghaṭo bhaviṣyatīti ca na punaḥ kulālādibhir apadiśyate kulālādayo tītā bhaviṣyanti vā iti atha ghaṭasya eva tatrānpalabhyamānatvād iti cet na hastiśārtulādīnām api tatrānupalambhe vyapadeśaprasaṅgāt athopalabdhapūrvasya eva vyapadeśa iti cet na ghaṭakriyādiṣv api prasaṅgāt atha ghaṭasya tena kriyādyabhāva iti cet nābhāvasya sambandhaviśeṣānupapatteḥ na hi samavāyalakṣaṇaḥ prāptilakṣaṇo vā sambandho bhāvābhāvayor avakalpate yenāsau ghaṭasyābhāvo na punaḥ kriyā ādīnām anyatarasambandhe cābhāvasya vastutvaprasaṅgaḥ atha vastv eva iti cet siddhas tarhi bhaviṣyann atītaś ca padārthaḥ atha upacārāt siddhakapālāvasthā avayavā bhaviṣyati ghaṭo bhūto ghaṭa iti ca āpadiśyeran sambandhāt tadyathā annaṃ prāṇā ity atrāpi yathā kulālacakradaṇḍasūtrādiṣu ghaṭi nāsti tathā piṇḍakapāleṣv apīti tadabhāvāviśeṣe ca kapāleṣu ghaṭo tīta iti vyapadeśo na kulālādiṣv iti niyamānupapattiḥ na cāpi vidyamānānāṃ sādhanānāṃ ghaṭādiniṣpādinām apy avidyamānair utpādyair ghaṭādibhiḥ sambandha upapadyate na cāsati sambandhe ghaṭotpādanābhiprāyeṇa kārakapravṛttiḥ athāyutasiddhaḥ samavāyalakṣaṇaḥ sambandho janyānāṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca na pratiṣidhyata iti cet na yutasiddhāyutasiddhatvasya samānakālabhāvināṃ vastūnāṃ darśanāt nābhāvābhāvayoḥ kvacid api yutasiddhatvam ayutasiddhatvaṃ vā dṛśyate tasmāj janyajanakānām api sambandhābhyupagamād vidyamānatvam eva iti utpatteprāg ūrdhvaṃ ca vidyate kāryam vastvantarasambandhāt prasiddhaṅhaṭādivat upalapsyamānatvād upalabdhatvāc ca apavarakasthaghaṭādivat uddiśya kartrā prāpyatvāt deśāntaravat tathā kartṛvyāpāraprāpyatvāc ceti kiṃ ca na oaukikā atītānāgataśabdābhyāṃ gaganakamalinīvad avidyamānam arthaṃ pratiyanti pratipādayanti canirmokṣaḥ tasmād adītam anāgataṃ ca svarūpato vidyata eva nābhūtvā bhāvas trayāṇām adhvanām kiṃ tarhi vidyamānānām evābhivyaktiḥ tasmād vyaktirūpeṇa vāsanānām atyantavinivṛttiḥ guṇarūpeṇa tu satīnām api kāryāsamarthatvān na kaivalyābhāvadoṣaḥ nāpi siddhāntavirodhaḥ atītānāgatavartamānadharmāḥ kena punā rūpeṇa santīti tatpratipādanārtham āha te vyaktasūkṣmā guṇātmānaḥ te khalv amī tryadhvānaḥ atītānāgatavartamānādhvatrayopārūḍhāḥ dharmāḥ vartamānāḥ vartamānalakṣaṇopārūḍhāḥ vyaktātmānaḥ likapratyayaviṣayībhūtasvabhāvāḥ atītānāgatāḥ sūkṣmātmānaḥ lokapratyayaviṣayabhāvam aprāptāḥ ṣaḍaviśeṣasvarūpāḥ asmitādisvabhāvāḥ tataś ca vyaktātmānaḥ ṣoḍaśavikārāḥ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇāḥ sarvam idam ādhyātmikaṃ kāryakāraṇarūpaṃ vyaktātmakaṃ yac ca sūkṣmam aviśeṣalakṣaṇam asmitādi yac canirmokṣaḥ liṅgamātraṃ sūkṣmatvāviśeṣāt sarvam idaṃ jagat guṇānāṃ sattvarajastamasāṃ prakhyāpravṛttisthitiśīlānāṃ sanniveśaviśeṣamātram iti paramārthato guṇātmānaḥ guṇasvabhāvāḥ tathā ca śāstrānuśāsanam guṇānāṃ paramaṃ rūpaṃ svaṃ paramārtharūpam anpāyopajanātmakam ekaikasya tac ca na dṛṣṭipatham ṛcchati na dṛṣṭigocarībhavati yat tu dṛṣṭapathaṃ prāptaṃ guṇāparimardena viṣam abhāvakṛtasanniveśalakṣaṇaṃ tanmāyeva na tu māyā evāsāratvāt tu māyāvad iti sutucchakam atyalpam ekadeśamātrapariṇāmatvāt sāmyāvasthānāṃ guṇānām yadā sarve guṇāḥ pṛthivyādayaḥ tadā katham ekaḥ śabdaḥ śaṅkhādijanitaḥ ekam indriyaṃ śrotrādikam ity ekabuddhyālambanatvaṃ bhavet na khalu bhavitavyam triguṇatvena hi kāraṇena traya iti pratyaya syāt evam indriyṇāṃ ca pratyekaṃ tritvam tathā ca niyamo na prāpnoti na hi grāhyatvam ekasya eva śabdasya grāhakatvaṃ ca ekasya śrotrasya iti niyam upakalpate tathā sparśādiṣu tvagindriyādiṣu ca yojyam niyamaś ca dṛśyate kāraṇaṃ tatra vacanīyam ity āha pariṇāmaikatvād vastutattvam prakhyāpravṛttisthitiśīlānāṃ guṇānāṃ grahaṇātmakānāṃ sattvaprādhānyāt boddhātmanām asmitāsaṃsthānānāṃ karaṇabhāvenaikaḥ pariṇāmaḥ śrotrendriyam yathā viruddhānāṃ tailavartitejasāṃ pradīpaḥ tathā tvagādīndriyeṣu pruṣāṛthetikaraṇīye prayuktānām ekaikam indriyaṃ pariṇāma iti yojyam bhūtāntareṣv api yojyam śabdasparśarūparasānāṃ snehasmānajātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ rasatanmātrāvayavaḥ jalaparamāṇuḥ teṣāṃ paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇāmo jalam śabdasparśarūpāṇām uṣṇatvasamānajātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāmo rūpatnamātrāvayavaḥ tejaḥ paramāṇuḥ teṣāṃ paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇāmo bahniḥ salilendhano dāruśakaladīpanaś ca tathā śabdasparśayoḥ praṇāmitvasamānajātīyayoḥ sparśatanmātrāvayavaḥ vāyuparamāṇur ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ teṣāṃ paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇamāḥ vāyuḥ sapta marud gaṇāś ca tathā śabdatanmātrāvayavānām anāvṛttatvasamānajātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāma ākāśaḥ ity evam uktena mārgeṇa snehauṣṇyapraṇāmitvādyupādāya sāmānyam ekavikārārambhaḥ samāḍheyaḥ yojyaḥ tasmād bahūnām apy ekapariṇāmitvād ekaviṣayatvaṃ grāhyagrahaṇaniyamaś ca sarvam upapadyate nanu ca nāsty evāsāv ekapratyayaviṣayaḥ śabdādiḥ etat tu sarvaṃ vijñānaparijṛmbhitam eva vijñānabhāvabhāvitvāt kathaṃ tadbhāvabhāvitvam ity āha nāsti artho vijñānavisahacaraḥ pṛthag vijñānād upalabdhaḥ pṛthag bhāvī vā vijñānam arthavisahacaraṃ pṛthaktvena upalabdhaṃ pṛthag bhāvi vā asti tasmād artho vijñānavyatirekeṇa nāstīti pratijānīmahe pramāṇam apy atra bhavati vijñānavyatirekeṇa nāsti grāhyaṃ vastu vijñānavyatirekeṇānupalabhyamānatvāt vijñānasvarūpavat bāhyārthaśūnyāni jāgradvijñānāni vijñānatvāt svapnasamayavijñānavat vijñānaparikalpitā vā jāgradviṣayāḥ viṣayatvāṭ svapnaviṣayavat vijñānaṃ vā viṣayā vyatireki vijñānatvāt svapnavijñānavad iti yady evaṃ syāt kiṃ naś chinnaṃ syāt puruṣasya dṛśyaviyogāt kaivalyaṃ prastutaṃ na siddhaṃ syāt yathā upalabhyamānasya stambhāder abhāvaḥ evam upalabhyamānatvād vijñānasyāpy abhāvaḥ tad abhāve ca liṅgābhāvād upalabdhur apy abhāvaḥ prāpnuyād iti kasya kaivalyam kena dṛśyena viyogaḥ syāt kena samprayoge vā bandhaḥ pratijñāyeta bandhābhāve cābhyudayaniḥśreyasārthapravṛttiphalatā na prasajyeta kiṃ cānyat vijñānavyatirekeṇārtho nāstīti bruvatā vijñānam artha iti ca ekaḥ padārtho abhyupagato bhavati yathā agnir anala iti evaṃ ca sati vijñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakam arthaḥ grāhyo grāhakaś ceti nāmamātre vipratipattiḥ na punar ekasya grāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ pratyākhyāyate tathā ca sati puruṣasyāpi grāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ prāptaḥ tathā api vipramokṣānavak lptiḥ ity evamādayo bhūyāṃso doṣāḥ prāpnuvanti tasmāt amuyā diśā anena nyāyābhāsabalena ye vastu svarūpam apahṇuvate jñānaparikalpanāmātraṃ vastu svapnaviṣayopamam na tu paramārthato astīti te svayaṃ tathā ity abhyupagamya svamāhātmyena pratupasthitaṃ vastu katham apramāṇātmakena vikalpajñānabalena vastu svayam upagṛhyābhyupagamya tad evābhyupagataṃ apalapantaḥ idam ity abhyupetya idaṃ nāstīty apahnuvānāḥ śeaddheyavacanāḥ syuḥ na hi svānubhavapratyākhyāyinaḥ śraddhānīyavacanavistārā bhavitum arhanti tatra vijñānavyatirekeṇārtho nāstīti pratyakṣavirodhinī pratijñā saṃvedanīkārakaṃ vijñānaṃ pratīyāmaḥ pṛthubudhnādyākāram arthaṃ pratipadyemahi grāhakaṃ ca vijñānam avabhāsakaṃ avabhāsanīyaś cārthaḥ svalakṣaṇabhedenārthajñānayor upalabhyamānatvān nāvyatirekagandho api tataś ca vyatirekeṇānupalabhyamānatvād ity asiddho hetus tava na ca jñānasya eva pṛthubudhnādyākāratā jñānasya ekasyāvabhāsyāvabhāsakatvānupapatteḥ pradīpasyeva kevalasya bhinnayoḥ pradīpayoḥ prakāśyaprakāśakatvānupalmbhād ekasya ca svātmani prāptyasambhavāt evaṃ jñānasya svapnajñānam api upalabdhārthaviṣayatvāt na nirālaṃbanam pratijñāyāḥ pratyakṣavirodho lokavirodhaś ca sarvaṃ jñānaṃ sālambanaṃ jñānatvāt prativādiduṣṭavākyajñānavat svavākyaguṇajñānavac ca tataś ca jñānatvādīnāṃ nirālaṃ banatvahetūnām evamādibhir anaikāntikatā kutaś ca etad anyāyyaṃ vastu nāstīti vastu sāmye cittabhedāt tayor viviktaḥ panthāḥ bahucittālambanībhūtaṃ anekacittaviṣayībhūtaṃ ekaṃ vastu putrādikaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ samānam tat khalu naikacittatantraṃ bhavati ekacittatantratvābhāvād anekacittaparikalpitam api na bhavati kin tu svarūpapratiṣṭhaṃ cittanirapekṣaṃ svatantratayā vyavasthitam katham vastu sāmye vastunaḥ putrāder ekatve cittabhedāt ekasmin putrādiviṣaye viṣayiṇāṃ jñānānām anekatvāt kathaṃ cittabheda ity āha dharmāpekṣaṃ cittasya vastu sāmye api yathā putrata eva mātāpitroḥ sukhajñānaṃ bhavati tata eva putrādeḥ adharmāpekṣaṃ ahitānāṃ duḥkhajñānaṃ upajaniṣyate yadi kasyacic cittena parikalpitam abhaviṣyat na anyacittaparikalpitenānyeṣāṃ cittam upāraṃkṣyata na etad yuktaṃ atyantāsambaddhānām adarśanāt yadi cānyaparikalpitenāpy anyacittoparāgo bhaviṣyat tadā sarve api sarvaṃ samjñāsyanta na cedaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tasmāt na cittaparikalpitaṃ vastv iti vastujñānayoḥ grāhyagrahaṇabhedād bhinnayor viviktaḥ panthāḥ nānayoḥ saṅkaragandho apy asti sukhajñānālambanībhūtaṃ purtādivastu na tajjñānaparikalpitam tadviruddhānekacittoparañjakatvāt vādiprativādipratijñāguṇadoṣatadābhāsavat ca ādiprativādiprabhṛtīnām api vijñānamātratve sādhyasādhanādivyavahāravilopaḥ syāt atha svavijñānavyatirekeṇa teṣāṃ jñānarūpāṇām eva pṛthaktvam iti cet astu tad eva vastu jñānāntaraviṣayatvād arthāmtaram siddham saṃjñāmātre vipratipattiḥ viṣayiviṣayabhedas tu na sādhyaḥ tasmānnityā nānayoḥ saṃkaragandho pīti atha vastuni svarūpapratiṣṭhe api sukhādibhinnapratyayālambanatā na samīcīnarūpeti cet atrocyate vastu punas triguṇaṃ calaṃ guṇavṛttam iti dharmādinimittaṃ cāpekṣya vittaiḥ sukhaduḥkhādibhedarūpeṇābhisaṃbadhyate pariṇāmitvād anekaśaktitvāc ca dharmādinimittānurūpasya cotpadyamānasya pratyayasya tena tena nimittena ātmanā hetur bhavati sattvātmanā dharmādinimittāpekṣaṃ putrādivastu sukhahetur bhavati rajas ātmanā tv adharmanimittāpekṣaṃ duḥkhahetur bhavati tamas ātmanā tv avidyāpekṣaṃ tad eva vastu mohahetur bhavati sattāmātrātmanā samyagdarśanāpekṣaṃ tad eva mādhyasthyajñānahetur bhavati kecid āhuḥ eṣām eva bauddhānām anyatame bāhyam artham abhyupagacchanta āhuḥ jñānasahabhūr evārthaḥ yathā vijñānaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ dharmiśūnyaṃ utpadyate vinaśyati ca tathā shaiva jñānenārtho vijñāyate vinaśyati ca bhogyatvāt sukhādivat tadyathā sukhaduḥkhādirūpaṃ bhogyaṃ vijñānasahotpattivināśam asādhāraṇam evaṃ ghaṭādir artho api vijñānasamānasamayajanmavināśa eva bhogyatvād iti te api tathā eva vijñānavādivat sādhāraṇatvaṃ anekasukhādicittālambanatvaṃ bādhamānāḥ pūrvottarakṣaṇeṣu svakīyavijñānotpatteḥ paurastyeṣu kṣaṇeṣu pāścātyeṣu ca vastu nāstīti vastusvarūpam evāpahnuvate tasmāt na hi vastunaḥ svarūpam vijñānasahabhāvi tad evedam iti pratyabhijñānāt nācarajanmapralayaṃ tad evedam iti pratyabhijñāyate yathā vijñānam na hi tad evādo me vijñānam iti bhavati vastu punas tad evedam iti pratyabhijñāyate arthajñānayor evekasamayabhavitve apy eka pariśeṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ syāt nāpi sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñānam grāhyagrāhakayor yugapadutpattivināśavattvāt vyavasthite hi vastvantaradṛśye anyatatsadṛśavastudarśanena sādṛśyapratyayaḥ evaṃ tatsadṛśaṃ vā drakṣyāmīty uttarābhilāṣaḥ na hi tad aharniścitamaraṇasyāparedyur arthadarśanākāṃkṣā jāyate nāpi matsacṛśa īkṣiṣyata ity abhilaṣati na ca evaṃ dṛṣṭam sarmo hi svārtham īhate bhinnasantatiṣv adarśanāt tasmād idānīṃtano rthaḥ nedānīntanajñānasahabhūr eva iti grāhyatvāt atītārthavat atīto vā nātītajñānasahanāśajanmā grāhyatvāt idānīntanārthavat bhūtabhaviṣyajjñānagrāhyā arthā adhunā api santi grāhyatvāt adhunātanapratyayagrāhyavat idānīntanam api vastu pūrvottarakṣaṇeṣu tathā eva atha sukhaduḥkhajñānādibhir anekāntikam iti cet na atītānāgataṃ svarūpato stīti sādhitvāt evaṃ ca sati sukhādīnāṃ ca svarūpeṇa sadbhāvāt sukhādivad iti sādhyasamāno dṛṣṭāntaḥ atha vartamānarūpaviśeṣeṇātītānāgatalakṣaṇayor arthasya sukhādivad abhāva iti cet siddhasādhyatā na hi kumārabhāva eva vṛddhatvaṃ vidyate itaś ca cittatantratā vastuno nāvakalpate ekacittatantraṃ vā vastu bhaved anekacittatantraṃ vā ekacittatantratve brūmaḥ na ca ekacittatantraṃ vastu tadapramāṇakaṃ tadā kiṃ syāt na tāvad ekacittatantraṃ ekacittatantraṃ ced vastu syāt yadi cedam ucyate taccitte yaccittatantraṃ vastu tasmiṃś citte vyagre parāsakte niruddhe vā vinaṣṭe vā tena pramāṇacittenāparāmṛṣṭaṃ cānyasya cāviṣayībhūtaṃ ekacittatantratayā eva tadā tat vastu apramāṇakam agṛhītasvabhāvaṃ pramāṇacittanirodhād eva tadānīṃ kiṃ tat syāt na hi kiṃ cid api syāt cittapramāṇakaṃ tat tadabhāve na tena bhavitavyam nanu ca yathā tat pramāṇacittaṃ nirudhyate tathā eva tad api kṣaṇikatvān niruddham eva kiṃ tatrābhidhānīyaṃ syāt ucyate na vyavahāravilopān niyamānupapatteś ca agnir ayaṃ māsprākṣīḥ imaṃ gṛhāṇa adaḥ pradehīti vyavahāro vilupyeta ekacittasahakṣayatvād vastunaḥ tatsantatijamatyantasadṛśaṃ vyavahārapratipattaye bhaved iti cet atrāpi tatsantānād eva tatsamānenānyenānubhavanīyaṃ parapramāṇasya ca tadviṣayabhūtam iti ko niyacchet na hi niyamahetur asti api ca ekacittatantratvād vyavahāravelāyām anyatara na redaṃpratyayaviṣayālambano nānyata na rpratyayo yujyate na hi khalv api bahucitatantraṃ vastu tataś ca kṛhāṇedaṃ prayucchāda iti kathaṃ vyavaharemahi nāpy evaṃ darśanaśālinaḥ śiṣyācāryopadeśapradānādibhir anyonyaṃ vyavahareran tasmānnityā na ca ekacittatantraṃ vastu pramāṇacittavināśe tadvyagrabhāve vā anavadhṛtasvabhāvatvād vastunaḥ saṃbandhyamānaṃ vā vastu punaś cittena kuta utpadyeta na kutaś cid utpattir upapadyate tatsantānād iti hi pratyavocāma kiṃ cāsya vastunaḥ anupasthitāḥ ekasya pratyayasyāviṣayībhūtā ye bhāgās te cāsya na syuḥ eko hi vastu bhāgo viṣayībhūtaś cittatantro nānyaḥ iti nāsti pṛṣṭham iti udaram api abhimukhībhūtaṃ na syād eva athāpi kākatālīyanyāyena bhūyāṃsi cittāni yugapad utpadyeran tadviṣayaṃ ca vastu tatsamānakālam unmajjatīti tad etena eva pṛṣṭhodarābhāvandarśanena pratyākhyāyi nāpi kākatālīyavṛttāntenānādisamayādhīno vyavahārasāgara uttīryate sarve ca vijñānadarśanaślādhiṣu doṣā ihāpi samānā eva tasmāt āha svatantro rthaḥ sarvapuruṣasādhāraṇaḥ yasminn avasthite samastalokavyavahāra upakalpiṣyate svatantrāṇi ca cittāni pratipuruṣaṃ pravartante tayoś cārthacittayoḥ smbandhād upalabdhiḥ puruṣasya bhogaḥ tasmād bhoktā puruṣaḥ cittaṃ karaṇam artho viṣayaḥ karmabhūta ity eteṣāṃ bhoktṛ karaṇakarmaṇāṃ viviktaḥ panthāḥ kathaṃ cittatadviṣayayoḥ sambandhāt puruṣasya bhoga ity āha yad vā yasya cittavyatirekeṇa vastu nāsti cittatantram eva vā vastu tasya jñātājñātaviṣayatvam anupapannam ity āha taduparāga apekṣatvāc cittasya vastu jñātājñātam tena viṣayeṇa cittasya uparāgaḥ taṃ prati apekṣā yasya tat cittaṃ taduparāgāpekṣam tasya bhāvaḥ taduparāgāpekṣatvaṃ tasmāt taduparāgāpekṣatvāc cittasya vastu jñātājñātam yena vastunā cittam uparajyate tat jñātaṃ yena ca na uparajyate tat ajñātam sa coparāgaś cittapariṇāmāpekṣaḥ indriyamārgeṇa cittaṃ bāhyākāreṇa pariṇāmamānaṃ hi sambadhyate kiṃ punaś cittapariṇāmanimittam ity āhāyaskāntamaṇikalpā ayaskāntasamānaḥ viṣayāḥ ayassadharmakam ekaṃ cittam ayassardhamakatvaṃ ca viṣayasannidhāne vikriyata iti viṣayāṇām apy ayaskkāntamaṇikalpatvaṃ sannidhimātreṇa cittavikriyāpādanasāmarthyāt ato viṣayā ātmākāreṇa pariṇitaṃ cittam abhisaṃbadhyoparañjayanti yena ca viṣayeṇoparaktaṃ cittaṃ sa viṣayo jñātaḥ tato nyaḥ ṇye punaḥ anuparañjako kā viṣayaḥ yā ajñātaḥ tāḥ tasmāt vastuno jñātājñātasvarūpa viṣaya tvāt pariṇāmi cittam atha punaś cittatantra eva viṣayaś cittam eva vā viṣayaḥ tasya vādinaḥ sarvaviṣayajñatvam aviṣayajñatvaṃ vā bhavet ajñātasya cittasyābhāvāt na cedaṃ dṛśyate kiṃ tarhi jñātājñātaviṣayatvam eva cittasya pratipadyāmahe tac ca etat sthirāvasthānānāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ prāptyabhāvād anyathā ca saṃbandhānavakalpanāc cittapariṇāmāpekṣam eva iti pariṇāmitvam yasya tu svāmino bhoktuḥ tad eva jñātājñātaviṣayaṃ cittaṃ vṛttirūpeṇa viṣayaḥ na hi niruddhavṛttinaś cetaso viṣayatvam iti tasya puruṣasya sadā jñātāś citavṛttayaḥ tat prabhoḥ puruṣasyāpariṇāmitvāt tāsāṃ pratyakṣatvāt sadā jñātaviṣayatvam aprasādhyam yad vā pratyakṣagamyaś cittavṛttayaḥ upalabdhatvena śabdaliṅgān apekṣaṃ smaryamāṇatvāt pratyakṣopalabdhaghaṭavat niścitarūpatvāc ca tathā eva saṃśayāviṣayatvāc ca yadi hi sadaivāpratyakṣāś cittavṛttayaḥ tā bāhyaviṣayavat saṃśayitā api kadācit kāścana bhaveyuḥ na hi kāścana kadācanasaṃśayamārgasaṃpātinyo dṛṣṭāḥ api ca bhavati hi kadācijjñātaḥ sann artho jñāta iti rpratīyamānaḥ cittavṛttipratyakṣāgrāhyatve tat na upapadyate na ca phaladvāreṇānumātuṃ tatra śakyate phalasyānavadhāraṇāt tasmāt saṃśayasya cāviṣayatvāt pṛthak ca viṣayāc cittavṛttīnāṃ svarūpamātreṇa eva svaryamāṇatvāt sarvadā sarvāḥ pratyakṣāś cittavṛttayaḥ tathā pratipattur avabhāsakatvāt karaṇatvāt abhivyañjakatvāc ca pradīpādivat na tu cakṣurādibhir anaikāntikatvam tatrāpi pratyakṣagrāhyatvāt yathā pradīpādyālokaviśiṣṭā ghaṭādayo gṛhyante tathā śrotrādisvālokaviśiṣṭā eva śabdādayo gṛhyante na ca vivicyāgrahaṇād apratyakṣatvam iti śakyaṃ vaktum yathā pradīpayoḥ parasparavyatibhinnā raśmayaḥ na cāsyāyaṃ raśmir asya cāyam iti vivicyate na ca tāvatā teṣām apratyakṣatvam evaṃ ihāpi cakṣur ādīnāṃ tulyajātīyabāhyālokādivyatiṣaṅgād vivicyāgrahaṇam na ca tāvan mātreṇa teṣām apratyakṣatvam yo hi pratyakṣāvasīyamānacittavṛttyapalāpaṃ karoti nūnam asāv ātmānam apy apaloped iti sarvopalabdheś cittavṛttyadhīnatvāt rūpopalabdher ivāloka pratyāyakaṃ tattvam pratyayādhīnatvam tasmād āha sadā jñātāś cittavṛttayaḥ puruṣasya iti yac ca etat sadā jñātaviṣayatvam tat prabhoḥ puruṣasyāpariṇamitvāt nityopalabdhṛ svarūpaprayuktaṃ hi tad iti yadi cittavat prabhur api puruṣaḥ pariṇameta tatas tadviṣayāś cittavṛttayaḥ cittasya iva śabdādiviṣayāḥ jñātā ajñātā api syuḥ yat tu jñātājñātaṃ śabdādiviṣayajātaṃ tat pariṇāminaś cittasya pariṇāmāpekṣaṃ draṣṭavyam tathaivendriyāṇām api pariṇāmāpekṣam eva jñātājñātaviṣayatvaṃ dṛśyate na ca tathā cittavṛttīnām anyatamāsām api jñātatvam ajñātatvaṃ ca nityatas tajjñātā eva cittavṛttayaḥ tasmād yad vṛttirūpena sadā jñātatvaṃ manasaḥ tat prabhoḥ puruṣasyāpariṇāmitvam anumāpayati apariṇāmī puruṣa iti pratijñā sadā jñātaviṣayatvād iti hetuḥ vaidharmyeṇa cittam indriyāṇi ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ upalabdhuś ca viṣayiṇaḥ prakṛtatvāt sadā jñātaviṣayatvapratiṣedhāya muktātmavad iti dṛṣṭānto na upapadyate muktasyāviṣayitvāt syād āśaṅkā cittam eva svābhāsaṃ viṣayābhāsaṃ ca bhaviṣyatīti grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ceti svasaṃviditākārā eva hi vṛttayaḥ yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśayati ghaṭādīnātmānaṃ ca kiṃ puruṣeṇa cittavṛttyupalambhinā cittavyatiriktena kalpitena iti atrocyate na tat svābhāsaṃ dṛśyatvāt yathetarāṇīndriyāṇi śrotra ādīni viṣayāś ca śabda ādayaḥ na svābhāsānīndriyāṇi nāpi svābhāsāḥ śabda ādayaḥ dṛśyatvāt tathā manoapi pratyetavyam na svābhāsaṃ cittaṃ dṛśyatvād iti pratipattavyam nanu cāgnivad eva svābhāsatvaṃ viṣayābhāsatvaṃ ca bhavaut yathā eva ghaṭādayaḥ prakāśyāḥ svarūpopalambhanārtham āolkāntaram apekṣante na tathā pradīpaḥ yathā pradīpaḥ svābhāso viṣayābhāsaś ca tathā mano apy avabhāsakatvād evaṃ bhavatu kim ātmanā na hi pradīpapratipattaye pradīpāntaram ādadate laukikāḥ yadi ca upādīyeran anavasthā eva syāt evaṃ vijñānasyāpi vyatiriktena grāhyatve tasya cānyena grahaṇaṃ tasya cānyenety evaṃ prasajyeta kiṃ ca vijñānasyāvabhāsātmakatvāt grāhakasyāpy avabhāsarūparvāt na parasparopakāryopakārakabhāvaḥ tadyathā pradīpayor dvayoḥ tasmāt kalpito api vijñānasya grahītānarthaka iti bhavatu jñānaṃ svābhāsaṃ parābhāsaṃ ceti atrocyate tad etad dṛṣṭāntāpaśadāvaṣṭambhena sakalalokaprasiddhamārgopārohiṇā ātmano nirākaraṇam aśakyam kasmāt na cāgnisya dṛṣṭāntaḥ na hy agnir ātmasvarūpam aprakāśaṃ prakāśayati yadi cāgnir aprakāśaḥ san ātmanā eva ghaṭādivat prakāśayiṣyata tata upāpatsyata dṛṣṭāntaḥ na tv evam na hi kadācid agnir aprakāśaḥ prakāśaś cāyam sa ca prakāśyaprakāśakasaṃyohe dṛṣṭaḥ na ca svarūpamātre sti saṃyogaḥ dvayor hi saṃyogaḥ nāsati saṃyoge svarūpāvabhāsakatvam yad apy ucyate ghaṭādivat prakāśāntaraṃ nāgnir apekṣata iti tat prakāśyarūpābhāvāt na tu tasya ghaṭādivat prakāśyaṃ rūpam asti na tāvatā vyatiriktāgrāhyatvam cakṣuṣā tulyavyatiriktena gṛhyata eva prakāśyasya haṭāder avatamasatir askārāya prakāśa upādāyiṣyate na tv aprakāśyarūpatvāt agner ālokāntarānākāṅkṣaṇaṃ tu bhavataivābhihitaṃ dvayoḥ pradīpayor nāsti parasparopakāra iti yatra nāma bhede api dvayoḥ pradīpayor nāsti aprakāśyarūpatvād anyonyopakāraḥ kim utāsati bhede tra prakāśāntaram eva nāpekṣate iti na tu vyatiriktagrāhyatvaṃ vyabhicarati pradīpayor dṛśyatvād ghaṭādivat etena vyatiriktagrāhyatvaṃ jñānasya dṛśyatvāt pradīpādivat siddhaṃ bhavati pradīpādivac ca jñānasya prakāśasvarūpatvāt karaṇāntarānapekṣāpi siddhā tathā ca anavasthādoṣagandho na vidyate yad apy ucyate jñānasyāvabhāsātmakatvāt tad grāhakasyāpy avabhāsarūpatvāt na parasparopakāryopakārakabhāvaḥ pradīpayor iva dvayor iti nāsau doṣaḥ cakṣuḥpradīpavad ātmajñānayor jātyantaratvāt nanu cāhaṃpratyayena cittaṃ pratyayi gṛhyata iti viṣayaviṣayitvam ekasya eva na eṣa doṣaḥ triguṇatvāc cittasya yat tatra tamaḥpradhānaṃ cittaṃ tad anyayā sattvātmikayā vṛttyā samālambyate hasteneva śarīraṃ kaṇḍūyamānam tatrāpy upalabdhā viṣayī bhinna eva puruṣaḥ etena jātyantaragrāhyagrāhakatvena niravayavatvena puruṣaś ca svayam eva grāhyaḥ grāhakaś cety etat pratyavocāma kiṃ ca svābhāsaṃ cittam iti ucyamāne cāgrāhyam eva cittaṃ syād iti evaṃ śabda arthaḥ svābhāsam iti hy ukte anyena nāvabāsyate na gṛhyata ity arthaḥ na tu svayam ātmānaṃ gṛhṇātīty ucyate evamādiśabdaprayogeṣu śabdasya viparītārthatvam tadyathā svātmapratiṣṭham ākāśam apratiṣṭham iti śabda arthaḥ tathā svastho devadatta iti ṇīroga ityarthaḥ na tu svātmanisthita iti tatra dṛśyatvād iti hetor asiddhim ācakṣāṇasya pratyakṣavirodho lokavirodho vyavahāravilopaś cety āha svabuddhipracārapratisaṃvedanāt sattvānāṃ prāṇināṃ pravṛttir dṛśyate kruddho haṃ bhogī ham amutra me rāgo mutra me krodha iti svāṃ svāṃ buddhim evaṃ carantīṃ pratisaṃvedya dṛṣṭvā krodhalobhādiparihārāya vivekavatāṃ pravṛttur upalabhyate tathā prasannaṃ me cittaṃ kalupitaṃ mūḍham iti ca tat etat svabuddher agrahaṇe na yuktam iti na hi niśamya parispandinīṃ buddhir adṛyeti yuktaṃ vaktum abhyupagamya vādo yam yady api svābhāsaṃ viṣayābhāsaṃ ca mano bhavatu tatra dūṣaṇam eyasamaye cobhayānavadhāraṇam viṣayaparicchedakatve nānākṣanatvād ātmaparicchedo na yujyate atha punar ātmānam avadhārayati na tadā viṣayābhimukhaṃ svātmapariddhedakatve nānākṣaṇatvāt athobhayaparicchittir ekaieveti cen na niravayavatvāt paricchitteḥ na hi vinavayavāyāś cittavṛtteḥ pradīpavad anekābvabhāsakatvaṃ yuktam avayavabhedāt tu pradīpasyānekaprakāśakatvaṃ saṃbhavati na tu jñānasya sāvayavatvaṃ parair abhyupeyate kiṃ ca jñānam ekam ekasmin kṣaṇe ubhayam avadhārayatīti cābhyupagame kriyākārakabhedaprasaṅgaḥ yad ubhayāvadhāraṇaṃ sā kriyā yad avadhārayati tat kārakam na ca ekasmin kṣaṇe svaparobhayāvadhāraṇaṃ kṣaṇavādino yuktam kasmāt uktaṃ hi kṣaṇkatvasiddhye yad bhāvnam utpattiḥ sā eva kriyā tad eva ca kārakam ity abhupagamaḥ kriyākārakabhede ca ksanābhaṅgabhaṅgaḥ syāt kārakeṇa hi kriyā kṣaṇam avasthānīyam syānmatiḥ kasyāpi svarasanniruddhaṃ cittaṃ cittāntareṇa gṛhyate iti bhāvena vinaṣṭaṃ bhaṅgurataraṃ cittaṃ cittāntareṇa samanantareṇa saṃjāyamānena gṛhyata ity athāpi nityāvasthitapuruṣaparikalpinā nirarthikā eva atrocyate cittāntaradṛśye buddhibuddher atiprasaṅgaḥ smṛtisaṅkaraś ca yadi cittaṃ cittāntareṇa svarasaniruddhaṃ paurastyaṃ pāścātyena jāyamānena samanantareṇagṛhyeta buddhibuddhiḥ ghaṭaviṣayā buddhiḥ buddhir ucyate tadviṣayā tu buddhibuddhiḥ sā kena gṛhyate vyavasthitagrāhakābhāvāt sā apy anyayā grahītavyā sā apy anyayty atiprasaṅgaḥ na cāgṛhītāsu buddhibuddhiṣu saṃvyavahāro ghaṭate smṛtisaṃskārānupapatteḥ tatra ekajātīyānām eva ghaṭabuddhibuddhīnāṃ dāśatayī mālā syād anavasthitā na ghaṭabuddhiḥ parisamāptau ca ghaṭabuddhibuddhīnāṃ asatyāṃ kathaṃ ghaṭādibuddhir upatiṣṭheta ayaṃ cāparo doṣaḥ smṛtisaṃkaraś ceti buddhibuddhīnāṃ tatsaṃskārāṇāṃ caikarūpatvāt smṛtisaṃkaraḥ prāpnoti yāvanto buddhibuddhīnām anubhavās tāvatyaḥ smṛtayaḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ prāpnuvanti tatsaṅkarāt smṛtisaṅkarāt smṛtyanavadhāraṇaṃ iyam asyā buddheḥ smṛtir ity anavadhārayantaḥ kathaṃ vyavaharemahi tathā ca sarūpatvāt smṛtisaṃkaraḥ prāpnoti yāvanto buddhibuddhīnāṃ vidānāḥ svabuddhismṛtipūrvavyavahārāsambhavāt sarve sammohena saṅgacchemahi yadi cānavasthāparijihāsayā kvacit buddhyantare samavatiṣṭhemahi tam eva buddhipratisaṃvedinaṃ buddhipratisaṃvedanaliṅgena spaṣṭataram api puruṣam apalapacbhir vaināśikair ākulīkṛtaṃ jagad iti nanu ca ālayavijñānakalpanayā navasthādoṣaṃ pariharemahi tathā ca ātmakalpanām apalapemahīty evaṃ te bhoktṛsvarūpaṃ yatra kvacana kalpayanto na nyāyena saṅgaddhante tasyāpy alayavijñānasya grāhyatvād anavasthitatvāc cabhihitasakaladoṣānuṣaṅgaḥ kecit vaināśikaviśeṣāḥ sattvamātram api śabdāntareṇa sattvamātraṃ bhoktṛsvarūpaṃ parikalpyāsti sa sattvo ya etān pañca skandhān rūpavedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānalakṣaṇān nikṣipya parityajyānyāṃś ca skandhān pratisandhāti gṛhṇātīty uktvā tata eva bhūtānāgataskandhapratisandhātr ekasattvaprikalpanātaḥ trasyanti tathā teṣam anyā viruddhakalpanā skandhānāṃ mahānirvedāya virāgāyānutpādāya praśāntaye guror antike brahmacaryaṃ carāmīty uktvā punas tam evābhyāgataṃ sattvasya sattva sādhyasādhanasambandha m apahnuvate vijñānamātraṃ kṣaṇikaṃ śūnyaṃ ceti ātmānam apalapanti namabhisandadhīmahi tad evaṃ sāṅkhyayogādayas tu pravādāḥ svaśabdenapuruṣam eva svāminaṃ vittasya bhoktāram abhyupayantīti kathaṃ bhoktāraṃ svaśabdenaivābhyupayanti yataḥ citer apratisaṃkramāyās tadākārāpattau satyāṃ svabuddhisaṃvedanaṃ bhavati citiḥ caitanyaṃ puruṣa ity arthaḥ sā cāpariṇāmitvāt apratisaṃkramā tasyāḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ api satyāś citeḥ tadākārāpattiḥ tad iti prakṛtaṃ cittaṃ pratyāmnāyate tasyākārāpattis tadākārāpattiḥ tasyāś cites tadākārāpattau satyāṃ svabuddhisaṃbedanaṃ bhavati svasya bauddhasya pratyayasya upalabdhir bhavati tad artham eva hi sā buddhiḥ śabdādipratyayarūpeṇ apariṇamate tad etat pratipādayati pratītya apariṇāminī hi bhoktṛ śaktiḥ dṛk śaktiḥ yathātrayākhyātā apratisaṃkramā ca satī pariṇāminy arthe bnauddhapratyaye pratisaṃkrānteva pratyayiviṣayatvāt tadvṛttim anupatantīvānupatantī draṣṭṛtvād upalabhamānā bauddhaḥ pratyayo jāyamāna eva tasyāḥ karmatām āpadyate taṃ bauddhaṃ pratyayaṃ vṛttim anupatanty upalabhamānā bhoktṛ śaktiḥ tasyāś ca prāptacaitanyopagraha sva rūpāyāḥ prāptaṃ caitanyopagraharūpaṃ puruṣopagraharūpaṃ yayā buddhivṛttyā samāsāditapāvakopagraharūpataptalohapiṇḍavat dṛśikarmatvād eva anukāramātratayā buddhivṛttisārūpyamātratayā buddhivṛttyaviśiṣṭā jñavṛttir iti jña evopalabdhir eva vṛttir iti ākhyāyate vṛttisārūpyam itaratra iti vyākhgyātam tathā pratyayāviśeṣo bhogaḥ iti prakhyāpitam bhoktṛbhogyabhede ca sati cittākārāpattir upapadyate na cāsati vyatirikte bhoktari cittasyaiva draṣṭṛdṛśyobhayābhāsatvam akasmād upakalpate tasmāt suṣṭhūcyate sāṅkhyayogādaya eva puruṣaṃ svaśabdenābhyupayantīti anye tu śabdāntareṇopayanto api tata eva bibhyati tatho ca uktam buddhivṛttyanukāramātratayā buddhāv eva jñavṛttir upalabhyate nānyatra iti na pātālaṃ no vivaraṃ girīṇāṃ naivāndhakāraḥ kukṣayo na udadhīnām evam ādīni na guhā yasyāṃ guhāyāṃ nihitaṃ brahma śāśvataṃ sā guhā na pātāchādīni kasyāṃ punar guhāyāṃ nihitam ity āha buddhāv eva guhāyāṃ vṛttim ātmākhyāṃ brahmākhyām aviśiṣṭam apṛthagbhūtāṃ buddhivṛttyaviśiṣṭāṃ vedayante vivekinaḥ kasmāt punaḥ kāraṇāt puruṣasya cittākārāpattiḥ tasyāṃ vā satyāṃ svabuddhisaṃvedanam kuto vaināśikānāṃ cittam eva grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ceti bhrāntir ity āha draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ cittaṃ sarvārtham drasṭā puruṣo dṛśyaṃ śabdādi tābhyām uparaktaṃ cittaṃ sarvārthaṃ puruṣasya bhogāpavargārthaṃ bhavati mano bhimantavyenārthena ayaskāntamaṇideśīyena viṣayeṇa uparaktaṃ svayaṃ ca viṣayatvāt puruṣasya viṣayiṇā puruṣeṇ asannihitena ātmīyayā vṛttyā mānasena pratyayena viṣayatayā abhisambaddham tad etac cittam ātmavṛttidvāreṇa puruṣeṇa sambandhād draṣṭuḥ svarūpopraktaṃ śabdādinā vā mantavyena uparaktam iti draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ cittam eva na puruṣaḥ draṣṭṛdrśyoparaktam ity asya vyākhyānaṃ karoti viṣayaviṣayinirbhāsaṃ cetanācetanasvarūpāpannam kathaṃ punaḥ svayam acetanaṃ sac cetanasvarūpāpannm iti na eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣeṇa nityasannidhānāc cetanam iva tad evāvivekibhiś cetanam ity ucyate na tathā viṣayāḥ nityam acetanātmakā hi te svatas tu vittam acetanam eva iti cetanācetanasvarūpāpannaṃ ity ucyate viṣayātmakam iva śabdādisvarūpamātram iva cety arthaḥ acetanaṃ cetanam iva puruṣasvarūpāpannam iva cety arthaḥ sphaṭikamaṇikalpaṃ yathā sphaṭikamaṇir alaktakādisannidhau tadākāratāṃ biharti tathā eva tat sarvārthaṃ cittam ucyate tasmāt anena cittasārūpyeṇa bhrāntāḥ kecit etat tu cittasārūpyaṃ vaiśeṣikāṇām pramohakāraṇam vaiśeṣikādayas tu cittasārūpyamāhendrajālavyāmohitacetasaḥ tad eva cittaṃ cetanam ity āhuḥ katham yasmān manaḥpruṣasaṃyogajaṃ caitanyaṃ guṇaḥ uddhedanīya iti manyate vaināśikebhyas tv ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ sthiram ekaṃ dharmiṇam icchantīti apare bauddhāḥ cit mātram eveddaṃ sarvam nāsti gavādir ghaṭādiś ca svākāreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ sarveṣāṃ pratyayasya sādhāraṇo lokaḥ iti svānubhavam apy apalapanti te evaṃ bhrāntāḥ sukumāratarabuddhayo vainācikā anukapmanīyāḥ kasmāt asti hi teṣāṃ bhrāntibījaṃ sarvarupākāranirbhāsaṃ cittam iti sanimittā hi teṣāṃ bhrāntiḥ na lokopāyatikānāṃ śūnyatvādinām iva nirbījā kevalajagadvañcanārthapravṛttatvāt tu na eteṣv anukampā kartavyā tasmād yuktam uktaṃ teṣāṃ varākāṇāṃ sabījabhrāntacetasāmanukampanīyam iti ke punar abhrāntā ity āha ssamādhiprajñāyām iti samādhiprajñāgrahaṇam abhrāntacittagrahaṇārtham vikṣiptacetaso hi bhrāntāḥ samādhiprajñāyām abhrānāyāṃ viśuddhāyāṃ vivekavatyāṃ prasannagambhīratarāyāṃ prajñeyo rthaḥ pratibimbībhūtaḥ nirmaladarpaṇamaṇḍala iva tasyāṃ samādhiprajñāyāṃ karaṇabhūtāyām ālambanībhūtatvād anyaḥ prajñātaḥ sakāśāj jātisvarūpakriyādibhir anyaḥ sa cet anyaḥ cittamātraṃ syāt kathaṃ prajñayā eva prajñārūpam avadhāryeta svātmani kriyāvirodhāt na hi kathañcid avadhāryeta tasmāt prajñāyāḥ anyo sāv arthaḥ saḥ yasyāṃ prajñāyāṃ pratibimbībhūto rtho yenāvadhāryate saḥ tasyāḥ prajñāyā ālambanībhūtāc cārthād anyaḥ kartṛkārakabhūtaḥ sa puruṣaḥ ity evaṃ grahītṛgrahaṇagrāhyasvarūpabhedāt kartṛkaraṇakarmabhedopapatteḥ na hi niravayavam ekam eva ekasmin kṣaṇew vastu kartṛ ca karma ca bhavati tato ye trayam apy etat jātitaḥ pravibhajante te samyagdarśanaḥ tair adhigataḥ pouruṣaḥ prāpta ity arthaḥ sāmarthyāt tu jñāta iti gamyate kutaś cāsti puruṣaś cittavyatiriktaḥ pūrvaṃ cittasya dṛśyatvena vyatiriktapuruṣasiddhir āpāditā tasya eva tu vittasya saṃhatykāritvenādhunā svāmisiddhuartham āha tadasaṅkhyeyavāsanācitram api parārthaṃ saṃhatyakāritvāt yady api tad eva cittam asaṃkhyeyābhir vāsanābhiḥ anādisamayābhiḥ citrīkṛtaṃ bhrāntikāraṇam uktaṃ tathāpi parā arthaṃ parasya bhogārtham eva iti pratijñāyate saṃhatyakāritvāt kāryakaraṇaviṣayādivyāpārāpekṣam arthasādhakatvāt saṃhatyakāritvam ataḥ saṃhatyakāritvāt gṛhādivat iti pārārthyaṃ cittasya na hiḥ kiṃcana loke saṃhatyakāri dṛṣṭaṃ svātham tasmāt saṃhatyakāriṇā cittena na svārthena bhavitavyam na hi sukhacittaṃ sukhārthaṃ sukhacittārthaṃ vā nāpi jñānacittaṃ jñānārthaṃ vā jñānacittārthaṃ vā kiṃ tarhi sukhacittaṃ jñānacittam api etad ubhayaṃ parārtham yaś ca bhogena sukhacittena jñānacittena ca apavarheṇārthenārthavān puruṣaḥ sa eva paraḥ na parasāmānyamātraṃ śarīram indriyāṇi viṣayā vā na hi vaināśīkaḥ sukhacittaṃ śarīrendriyaviṣayātham icchati tathā cecchann abhyupagataṃ virundhīta vijñānasya eva hi sukhāpavargābhyām arthitvam abhimanyate tasmāt ya eva śarīrendriyavijñānasya eva hi sukhāpavargābhyām arthitvam abhimanyate atasmāt ya eva śarīrendriyaviṣayavyatiriktaḥ puruṣo bhogāpavargābhyām arthavān anyo vijñānād abhyupagamanīyaḥ yadi yat kiṃcit parasāmānyamātram udāhared vaināśikaḥ yadi tu vaināśikaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇāṃ gṛhādīnāṃ devadattādisaṃhataparārthatvam iti vyāmohād abhimanyamānāaḥ kaṃcana viśiṣṭaṃ na param icchet evaṃ cen manvīta sa idaṃ vaktavyam yaḥ paraḥ śarīrendriyaviṣayapratyayānāṃ sāmānyam uta sarva eva iti kimeṣām anyatamaḥ kiṃ vā kaścid eva etebhyo bhinnajātīya iti na tāvat sāmānyam na hibhogāpavargārthenārthi sāmānyavastu vaināśiko bhyupaiti svasamayavirodhāt nāpi śarīra ādīni samastāni bhogāpavargābhyām arthīnīti vājddhati vijñānasantater eva bhogāpavargārthitvābhimanāt na cāpi jñānasantatir ity ekaṃ vastu santateḥ kṣaṇikatvam na cāpi santānasyāvastutayā śaśaviṣāṇakalpasya bhogāpavargābhyām arthitvam nāpi śarīrendriyādīnām anyatamatvam icchati vijñānavyatiriktānām ātmīyasamaye bhogāpavargārthitvānabhyupagamāt nāpi śarīrendriyāṇāṃ saṅghāto nāma vastuto bhavato vidyate yena cittaṃ saṃhataparārthaṃ prārthayethāḥ avastuno hi katham arthitvam nāpi śarīrendriyādibhyo nyaṃ saṃhatabhinnajātīyaṃ pratijānīṣe yadi bhinnajātīyaṃ bhogāpavargābhyām arthavantam adṛṣṭaṃ parikalpayethāh sa evāsmābhir uktaḥ para iti tasya ca saṃhatatve paratvaṃ dṛṣṭānātmavan na upakalpate pariśeṣāt tu asaṃhato bhogāpavargābhyām arthī para iti kiṃ cānyat saṃhataparārthaṃ cittam iti sādhayato rthinaḥ saṃhatasyānyasyānupapatteḥ svārtham eva cittam ity uktaṃ bhavati tathā ca sati bhavato dṛṣṭāntābhāvo bhyupagamavirodhaś ca tathā manvānasyānyad vāci hṛdaye cānyad aniśamyakāritvaṃ ca āpatati yena cakṣurādiparārthatvasādhanena viruddhatādoṣaḥ pratyākhyāyi teṣāṃ vijñānaparārthatvam iti ced vijñānasyāpi saṃhatvatvāt parārthatvaṃ prasādhitam atha vijñānasyāpi kṣaṇikatvād asaṃhatatvam iti cet na tasya vyatiriktadṛśyatvāt dharmamātrānabhyupagamāc ca kṣaṇikatvānabhyupagamāc cety etad api pratyavocāma tasmād ucyate yat kiṃcit parasāmānyamātraṃ svarūpeṇodāhared vaināśikaḥ sa sarvaḥ saṃhatyakāritvāt parārtha eva syāt na devadattādisaṃhatārthatvam ubhābhyām āvābhyām anabhyupagamāt tvam api vijñānavyatirekeṇa nānyam abhyupaiṣi vayam api puruṣavyatirekeṇa nānyārthatvam abhibāñchāmaḥ cijñānamātratvaṃ ca na upapadyata ity uktam ato yas tv asau paro viśeṣaḥ sa na saṃhatyakārī puruṣaḥ svārtha iti siddhaḥ tasmād asti bhoktā tasya svārthasya svena dṛśyena parārthena yannimittaḥ saṃyogaḥ tadviyogāt kaivalyam upakalpate guṇapuruṣa yogasyāvidyā nimittm uktam sā ca viśeṣadarśina ātmānaṃ vijijñāsamānasya vinivartate tannivṛttau ca liṅgam āha viśeṣadarśina ātmabhāvabhāvanānivṛttiḥ vyaktāvyaktasāmānyād viśiṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ asādhāraṇo viśeṣaḥ taṃ viśeṣaṃ vyaktāvyaktasāmānyāt pravivicya draṣṭuṃ śīlaṃ yasya sa viśeṣadarśī tasya ātmabhāvabhāvanā nivartate sā ca samyagdarśanābhimukhā kaivalyaprāpikarmanimittā kathaṃ punar ātmabhāvabhāvanā asyāstīti vijñāyata ity āha yathā prāvṛṣi tṛṇasyāṅkurodbhedena liṅgena tadbījasadbhāvo numīya gamya te tathā mokṣamārgaśravaṇena yasya romaharṣāśrupāto dṛśyate tatrāpy asti viśeṣadarśanabījasamapavargabhāgīyaṃ karmābhinirvartitam iti romaharṣāśrupātādiliṅgenānumīyate tasya viśeṣadarśinaḥ ātmabhāvabhāvanā kaivalyabhāgīyakarmanimittā svābhāvikī janmāntarakarmanimittā ihajanmāparihasthairyakāraṇā vā sā hy ācāryo padeśānapekṣā svābhāvikī pravartate tasya karmaṇas tādṛśasyābhāvāt idam uktam svabhāvadoṣāt aśuddhakarmayogāt eṣāṃ pūrvanpakṣe samyagdarśanatadupāyaviparyaye rucir bhavati aruciś ca nirṇaye samyagdarśane tatrātmabhāvabhāvanā kā punar ity āha ko ham āsaṃ katham aham āsaṃ kiṃsvid idaṃ kathaṃsvid idaṃ ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ kathaṃ bhaviṣyāmaḥ iti sā tu viśeṣadarśino nivartate yadviṣayā hi jijñāsā tasminn adhigate tadviṣayā jijñāsā vinivartate kutaḥ etad evam yataḥ cittasya evaiṣaḥ ke bhaviṣyāma ity ādiḥ citraḥ pariṇāmaḥ na puruṣasya puruṣatvasatyām avidyāyāṃ śuddhaś cittadharmair aprāmṛṣṭa iti yasmād evam ata evaṃ viśeṣadarśinaḥ tasyātmabhāvabhāvanā kuśalasya nirvartate yadā ca viśeṣadarśanam udapādi tadā vivekanimnaṃ kaivalyaprāgbhāraṃ cittaṃ yad asya cittaṃ viṣayanimnaṃ viṣayapravaṇam ajñānaprāgbhāram ajñānaniṣṭhaṃ saṃsārābhimukham āsīt tad asya viśeṣadarśinaḥ tadānīm anyathā bhavati kaivalyamrāgbhāraṃ vivekanimnam iti pratisnotovṛttir jñāyate tac chidreṣu pratyayāntarāṇi saṃskārebhyaḥ vivekanimnasya uttarottaravivekapravaṇacetasaḥ puruṣasya jñāninaḥ anyatākhyātipravāhādhirohiṇaḥ sattvapuruṣānyatāsrotaḥplāvinaḥ cittasya tacchidreṣu vivekapratyayapravāhāntareṣu pratyayāntarāṇi viparyayalakṣaṇāni asmīti vā mameti vā kkutaḥ tāni bhavantīty āha kṣīyamāṇakleśādibījasya cittasya pūrvopacitaviparītasaṃskārebhyaḥ pratyayāntarāṇi jāyante hānam eṣāṃ kleśavad uktam yathā kleśā dagdhabījabhāvā na parohasamarthā bhavantīti te pratiprasabaheyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ ity atroktam evaṃ jñānāgnidagdhabījabhāvāḥ asmi mametyādipratyayasaṃskārā na parohasamarthā bhavanti dagdhaśālibījavat pūrvasaṃskāro na pratyayaprasūrbhavatīty arthaḥ jñānasaṃskārās tu katham apratipakṣāḥ santaś cittam adhikāre na bīja yojayiṣyantīti te tu samyagdarśanasaṃskārāś cittādhikāraparisamāptim anuśerate jsahaivāśrayeṇāvasitaprayojanena cittena pralīyante na punaś cittam adhikārapravaṇaṃ kkurvanti adhikārahetor avidyāyāḥ pratipakṣatvāj jñānasya tyatra niṣphalatvāt na vintyante na hi svayaṃ patataḥ patanahetur anbeṣaṇīyaḥ vivekakhyātipravaṇāntaḥkaraṇasya brāhmāṇasya prasṃkhyāne apy akusīd asya sarvathāvivekakhyāter dharmamedhaḥ samādhiḥ sa yadā ayaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prasṃkhyāne vivekadarśanaśīlite apy akusīdaṅ avṛddhiko bhavati tato api prasaṃkhyānaprāsādaviśeṣād adhikaṃ na kiṃcit prārthayate apiśabdāt prasṃkhyāne api na prārthanā tatra Pi prasṃkhyāne viraktaḥ sarvathā sarveṇa prakāreṇa vivekakhyātir yasya sa sarvathāvivekakhyātir eva bhavati kleśasaṃskārabījakṣayāt nāsya śarīrādau śūnyeveśmanīvāsmi mameti vā jñānaprasādamātraikāyatanasya pratyayāntarāṇy utpadyante tadā sya brāhmāṇasya sarvathāvivekakhyāteḥ dharmamegho nāma samādhir bhavati kaivalyākhyaṃ paraṃ dharmaṃ varṣatīti dharmameghaḥ iti saṃjñā tataḥ kleśakarmanivṛttiḥ tasya dharmamedhanāmnaḥ samādheḥ samyagdarśanapākābhirūpasya lābhāt bhāvāt abidyādayaḥ kleśāḥ samūlakāṣaṃ kaṣitāḥ vāsanābhiḥ saha samastāḥ pralīnāḥ bhavanti kuśalākuśśalāś ca karmāśayāḥ samūlaghātaṃ hatā bhavanti mūlaiḥ kleśaiḥ sahocchinnā bhavanti kleśakarmanivṛttau jīvann eva vidvān mukto bhavati kasmāt evam yato viparyayaḥ mithyājñānaṃ bhavasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam na hi kṣīṇaviparyayaḥ kaścit kvacij jāto dṛśyate tadā sarvāvaraṇamalāpetasya jñānasyānantyāt jñeyam alpam tadā dharmamedhasamādhisamaye sarvaiḥ kleśakarmāvaraṇaiḥ rajastamojanmabhiḥ vimuktasya jñānasya sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātimātrasya bhavaty ānantyam tat katham iti tamasā na bhibhūtam anantaṃ jñānasattvaṃ tasya tiraskṛtarajomalasyānantasya nistaraṅgamahodadhideśīyasya nirahitasyāvikriyasya kathaṃ tad grahāṇasāmarthyam ityāha kvacid rajasā pravartitaṃ cittasattvam uddhāṭitaṃ vāyuneva mahāpayodamaṇḍalam āhataṃ cūcitaṃ grahaṇasamarthaṃ bhavvati svataḥ sattvasyāpravartanāt rajaso hiḥ pravṛttisāmarthyam iti tadāsya cittasya bhavaty ānantyam aśeṣajñeyaviṣayatvam ambaratalamadhyavartino jaladharanirodhanirgatasya sver iva tasya jñānasyānantyā aśeṣaviṣayatvāt jñeyam alpaṃ saṃpadyate yathā ākāśe khadyotaḥ iti yathā ākāśāpekṣayā khadyoto na kiṃcid evam etajjñānābhisamīkṣayā jñeyaṃ na kiṃcid iti paramārthajñānāvasthāyām aśeṣabiparyayatirodhāne sarvapuruṣārthaśūnyatā cety etatpradarśanārtham udāharaṇam āha yatredam uktam andho maṇim avindat dhyat tam anaṅgulirāvayat agrīvaḥ taṃ pratyamuñcat tamajihvo bhyapūjayat iti yathā andha ādīnāṃ maṇīvedhādikam asambhavad api viparyayeṇāndho maṇim avidhyad iti vyavahriyate tathā jñānajñeyasaṃvyavahāro api viparyayāvasthāyām eva viparyayābhāve tu sarvapuruṣārthaśūnyā eva guṇāḥ sampadyanta iti tataḥ kṛtārthānāṃ pariṇāmakramaparisamāptir guṇānām tataḥ dharmamedhasamādhisamudayāt kṛtārthāś cittaguṇāḥ sampadyante cittādhīnatvāc ca kāryakaraṇārambhiṇo api sattvādayaḥ kṛtārthā bhavanti samastasya puruṣārthasya kṛtatvāt eṣāṃ kṛtārthānāṃ guṇānāṃ janmamaraṇapra bhāva vāharūpaḥ pariṇāmakramaḥ parisamāpyate na hi kṛtabhogāpavargārthāḥ kṣaṇam api prayojanābhāvāt avasthātum utsahante pariṇāmakramaparisamāptir ity uktam atha ko yaṃ guṇakramo nāma yasya parisamāptir upavarṇitā tasyāyam adhigamopāya ucyate kṣaṇapratiyogī pariṇāmāparāntanirgrāhyaḥ kramaḥ kṣaṇaṃ prati yujyata iti kṣaṇapratiyogī kṣaṇāntaryātmā kṣaṇasyānantaratā kṣaṇānantaryaṃ tadātmā tatsvabhāvaḥ kṣaṇānantaryam eva kṣaṇatatkramayoḥ iti vyākhgyātam kiṃ punar asya grahaṇe liṅgam ity āha pariṇāmasyāparāntena vināśāvasthārūpeṇāvasānena liṅgena nigṛhyate saḥ kramaḥ katham aparāntena nirgrahaṇam iti ucyate na hy ananubhūtakramā kramam anavalambamānā kṣaṇe purāṇatā vastrasyānte vināśakāle bhavatīti na hi kadācidbhūtamātrasya eva vastrasya purāṇatā dṛśyate tasmāt purānatābhivyaktiliṅgenābhyūhyate yeneyaṃ purāṇatā vastrasyābhivyaktim upasaṃprāpitā sa kramaḥ tatra yadi labhāvasānatvam alabdhāvasānatvaṃ ca kramasya syāt tato yuktaṃ kṛtārthānāṃ pariṇāmakramaparisamāptir guṇānām iti vaktum tac ca labdhālabdhāvasānatvaṃ kramasya nityānityatve ghaṭate tatrānityeṣu vastrādiṣu kramo dṛṣṭaḥ na tu nityeṣu tataś ca guṇānāṃ nityānāṃ pariṇāmakramaprisamāptir ayuktā syād ity āśaṅkamāna āha nityeṣu ca kramo dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ sarvatra nety āha dvividheyaṃ nityatā pariṇāmanityatā guṇānāṃ kūṭasthanityatā puruṣasya iti nanu pariṇāmināṃ guṇānāṃ kathaṃ nityatā syād iti vravīti yasmin pariṇammāne tattvaṃ na vihanyate yasya yadrūpaṃ pramāṇena upalabdhaṃ tasya tat tattvam yadyasmin na vihanyate na vyabhicarati tad api nityam guṇānām api sukhaduḥkhamohātmatā prakāśakriyāsthitiśīlatā ca tattvaṃ na vihanyate tasmād ete api pariṇāmanityāḥ ubhayatra ca guṇāpuruṣeṣu tattvasyāvighātān nityatvam tato guṇeṣv api nityeṣu pariṇāmo dṛṣṭa iti labdhālabdhaprayavasānatvaṃ sthitam tatra guṇadharmeṣu mahadādisu pariṇāmāparāntanirgrāhyaḥ kramo labdhaparyavasānaḥ śarīrādiṣv api nityeṣu tu guṇeṣu dharmiṣv alabdhaparyavasānaḥ nityatvād eṣām kūṭasthanityeṣu svarūpamātrapratiṣṭheṣu muktapuruṣeṣu svarūpāstitā krameṇa evānubhūyate tena muktapuruṣeṣv asann apy anubhavadāreṇa śabdapṛṣṭhenāstikriyām upādāya vikalpitaḥ ity alabdhaparyavasāna eva paramārthataḥ puruṣeṣv apariṇāmitvān nāsti krama ity arthaḥ athāsya saṃsārasya sthityā pradhānarūpeṇa gagtyā vikārātmanā dvayaṃ ca guṇātmakam iti guṇeṣu ca vartamānasyāsti kramaparisamāptiḥ na vā ity avacanīyam etat asty eva ity avadhāraṇaṃ na śakyaṃ kartum nāpi nāsti eva iti kiṃ tu vibhajya kasyacid asti kasyāpi nāstīti vacanīyam eva katham asti praśna ekāntavacanīyaḥ apravibhajyāpi yathā sarvo jāto mariṣyati ajñānī iti nanu jñānavān api mariṣyaty eva ucyate ajñasya hi maraṇm ity abhimānaḥ na jñāninaḥ tathā ca uktam mithyā etad āhur mriyatīti mūḍhāḥ iti atha sarvo mṛtvā janiṣyata iti vibhajya vacanīyam etat ekāntānupapatteḥ katham pratyuditakhyātiḥ kṣīṇatṛṣṇaḥ kuśalo na janiṣyate itaraḥ ajñaḥ aniṣyate tathā manuṣyajātiḥ śreyasī eva na eva vā ity avacanīyaḥ praśnaḥ pravibhajya tu vacanīya eva katham paśūn uddiśya śreyasī bhavati devān ṛṣīṃś cādhikṛtya na śreyasī bhavati ayaṃ tv avacanīya evāpravibhajya sāmānyena praśnaḥ yathā saṃsāro yam antavān eva ity ananta eva iti vā bandhamokṣānupapatteḥ pravibhajya tu vacanīya eva yathā kuśalasyāsti saṃsāracakraparisamāptir netarasya iti anyatarāvadhāraṇe doṣaḥ saṃsāro ntavān evānanta eva iti vānyatarāvadhāraṇe doṣaḥ tasmād avyākaraṇīya evāyaṃ sāmānenāpravibhajya praśnaḥ yathā sarvo mṛtvā janiṣyate iti evaṃ manuṣyajātiḥ śreyasyeveti ca tasmāt suṣṭhūktaṃ kṛtārthānāṃ pariṇāmakramaparisamāptir guṇānām iti viśeṣaṇam guṇādhikāraparisamāptau kaivalyam uktam tatsvarūpam avadhāryate kaivalyaṃ prati vipratipatteḥ keṣāṃcid vijñānasantānasyātyantopaśamaḥ kaivalyam keṣāṃ cit tu navānām ātmaguṇānāṃ buddhīcchādveṣaprayatnasukhaduḥkhadharmādharmasaṃskārāṇām ucchedenācetanasya dravyamātrasya puruṣasyāvasthānam keṣāṃcid īśvarasāyujyam keṣāṃcit sarvajñatvādīśvaratulyadharmatvaprāptiḥ kaivalyam iti bhinnā matiḥ ihāpi vipratipattipraṇodāya kaivalyasvarūpam avadhāryate puruṣārthaśūnyānāṃ guṇānāṃ yaḥ pratiprasavaḥ pratisaṃsargaḥ svakāraṇe pratyastamaya ity arthaḥ pāryakaraṇātmakatayāpariṇatānām tat kaivalyaṃ puruṣasya kevalatvaṃ guṇair abhiśrībhāva ity arthaḥ svarūpapratiṣṭhā vā citiśktir iti buddhisattvānabhisaṃbandhinī yā puruṣasya citiśaktiḥ amiśrā kevalā tasyāḥ sadā tathā evāvasthānaṃ kevalāyāḥ bhāvaḥ kaivalyam nanu kaivalyasya ekatve kathaṃ vikalpaḥ kriyāyāṃ hi vikalpo na vastuni vastu svarūpasya bhedānupapatteḥ kaivalyam api vastu kathaṃ tadvikalpyata iti na eṣa doṣaḥ nimittanaimittakayoḥ prabhedopapatteḥ nimittanaimittkabhedopacarito api vikalpo rūpatā sā kāryakaraṇātmakānāṃ puruṣārthaśūnyānāṃ guṇānāṃ pratiasṃsargān nimittād apagacchatīti nimittam eva pratiprasavākhyaṃ kaivalyaśabdena upacaritaṃ pūrvam dvitīyaṃ tu guṇapratiprasavanimittabhāvi yat svarūpāvasthānaṃ puruṣasya guṇair amiśritatayā tat kaivalyam iti viśeṣaḥ guṇapuruṣāntarasvarūpatattvanirdhāraṇena tantrāntarīyatatvasvarūpanirākaraṇena ca kaivalyāntarāṇiniveditavyāni tatra oṅkāro maṅgalārthaḥ prayuktaḥ parameśvaranāmāṅkitamastakatayā tantrapracayārthaṃ śāntyarthaṃ vā vedāraṇyakavad iti om iti oṅkāro yasya vaktā samacarat phalaiḥ karma yasmād aśeṣaṃ niṣkarmakleśapāko ghaṭayati sakalaṃ yaḥ phalena kriyāṇām īśānām īśvaro yaḥ sthitibhavanidhanaprakriyāṇāṃ vidhātā dhyāya naḥ śuklimānaṃ vyapanudatu tarāṃ kṛṣṇimānaṃ sa kṛṣṇaḥ yātrākṛtas trijagatāṃ yad acintyaśaktileśām daśāhur iha mīnamukhāvatārān kleśudbhavatrividhatāpaparamparārtāḥ taṃ nāganāthaśayanaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmaḥ phaṇaratnaoghavidyoti pṛthivī dyunabhodiśe yogīndrāya phaṇīndrāya tatpatañjalaye namaḥ yogena cittasya padena vācāṃ malaṃ śarīrasya tu vaidyakena yo pākarot taṃ pravaraṃ munīnāṃ patañjaliṃ prāñjalir ānato smi sa jayati patañjalimuniḥ yena śreyo rthasārthasasyānām vihito harṣas tāpatritayahṛtā dharmameghena yas tatāna bhavamārgalaṅghināṃ kleśakarmamayadharmanuttaye dharmamedhamukhayogatoyadam taṃ patañjalim ṛṣiṃ praṇato smi vadanāhitapūrṇacandrakaṃ gurum īśānam abhūtibhūṣaṇam praṇamāmy
